sūta uvāca
īśānakalpavṛttāntamadhikṛtya mahātmanā
brahmaṇā kalpitaṃ pūrvaṃ purāṇaṃ laiṅgam uttamam
granthakoṭipramāṇaṃ tu śatakoṭi pravīstare
caturlakṣeṇa saṃkṣipte vyāsaiḥ sarvantareṣu vai
vyasteṣṭādaśadhā caiva brahmādau dvāparādiṣu
liṅgamekādaśaṃ proktaṃ mayā vyāsācchrutaṃ ca tat
asyaikādaśasāhasre granthamānamiha dvijāḥ
tasmātsaṃkṣepato vakṣye na śrutaṃ vistareṇa yat
caturlakṣeṇa saṃkṣipte kṛṣṇadvaipāyanena tu
atraikādaśasāhasraiḥ kathito liṅgasaṃbhavaḥ
sargaḥ prādhānikaḥ paścāt prākṛto vaikṛtāni ca
aṇḍasyāsya ca saṃbhūtiraṇḍasyāvaraṇāṣṭakam
aṇḍodbhavatvaṃ śarvasya rajoguṇasamāśrayāt
viṣṇutvaṃ kālarudratvaṃ śayanaṃ cāpsu tasya ca
prajāpatīnāṃ sargaś ca pṛthivyuddharaṇaṃ tathā
brahmaṇaś ca divārātramāyuṣo gaṇanaṃ punaḥ
divyaṃ ca mānuṣaṃ varṣamārṣaṃ vai dhrauvyameva ca
pitryaṃ pitṛāṇāṃsaṃbhūtidharmaścāśramiṇāṃ tathā
ākhyāṣṭakaṃ hi rudrasya kathitaṃ rodanāntare
brahmaviṣṇuvivādaś ca punarliṅgasya saṃbhavaḥ
śilādasya tapaścaiva vṛtrārerdarśanaṃ tathā
śilādaśakrasaṃvādaḥ padmayonitvameva ca
bhavasya darśanaṃ caiva tiṣyeṣvācāryaśiṣyayoḥ
vyāsāvatārāś ca tathā kalpamanvantarāṇi ca
kalpatvaṃ caiva kalpānāmākhyābhedeṣvanukramāt
kalpeṣu kalpe vārāhe vārāhatvaṃ hares tathā
punarliṅgodbhavaścaiva ṛṣimadhye pinākinaḥ
liṅgasyārādhanaṃ snānavidhānaṃ śaucalakṣaṇam
vārāṇasyāś ca mahātmyaṃ kṣetramāhātmyavarṇanam
bhuvi rudrālayānāṃ tu saṃkhyā viṣṇorgṛhasya ca
antarikṣe tathāṇḍe 'smin devāyatanavarṇanam
dakṣasya patanaṃ bhūmau punaḥ svārociṣe 'ntare
dakṣaśāpaś ca dakṣasya śāpamokṣastathaiva ca
kailāsavarṇanaṃ caiva yogaḥ pāśupatas tathā
saṃdhyāṃśakapramāṇaṃ ca saṃdhyāvṛttaṃ bhavasya ca
udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyātha putrotpādanameva ca
maithunātiprasaṅgena vināśo jagatāṃ bhayam
śāpaḥ satyā kṛto devānpurā viṣṇuṃ ca pālitam
grahaṇādiṣu kāleṣu snāpya liṅgaṃ phalaṃ tathā
pativratāyāścākhyānaṃ paśupāśavicāraṇā
pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ nivṛttyadhikṛtā tathā
vasiṣṭhatanayotpattirvāsiṣṭhānāṃ mahātmanām
munīnāṃ vaṃśavistāro rājñāṃ śaktervināśanam
sutaśoko vasiṣṭhasya arundhatyāḥ pralāpanam
snuṣāyāḥ preṣaṇaṃ caiva garbhasthasya vacas tathā
parāśarasyāvatāro vyāsasya ca śukasya ca
vināśo rākṣasānāṃ ca kṛto vai śaktisūnunā
devatāparamārthaṃ tu vijñānaṃ ca prasādataḥ
purāṇakaraṇaṃ caiva pulastyasyājñayā guroḥ
bhuvanānāṃ pramāṇaṃ ca grahāṇāṃ jyotiṣāṃ gatiḥ
jīvacchrāddhavidhānaṃ ca śrāddhārhāḥ śrāddhameva ca
nāndīśrāddhavidhānaṃ ca tathādhyayanalakṣaṇam
pañcayajñaprabhāvaś ca pañcayajñavidhis tathā
rajasvalānāṃ vṛttiś ca vṛttyā putraviśiṣṭatā
bhojyābhojyavidhānaṃ ca sarveṣāmeva varṇinām
narakāṇāṃ svarūpaṃ ca daṇḍaḥ karmānurūpataḥ
svarginārakiṇāṃ puṃsāṃ cihnaṃ janmāntareṣu ca
nānāvidhāni dānāni pretarājapuraṃ tathā
kalpaṃ pañcākṣarasyātha rudramāhātmyameva ca
śvetasya mṛtyoḥ saṃvādaḥ śvetārthe kālanāśanam
devadāruvane śaṃbhoḥ praveśaḥ śaṅkarasya tu
sudarśanasya cākhyānaṃ kramasaṃnyāsalakṣaṇam
śraddhāsāddhyotha rudrastu kathitaṃ brahmaṇā tadā
brahmaṇaḥ paramaṃ jñānamādātuṃ mīnatā hareḥ
sarvāvasthāsu viṣṇoś ca jananaṃ līlayaiva tu
rudraprasādādviṣṇoś ca jiṣṇoścaiva tu saṃbhavaḥ
manthānadhāraṇārthāya hareḥ kūrmatvamevaca
saṃkarṣaṇasya cotpattiḥ kauśikyāś ca punarbhavaḥ
yadūnāṃ caiva saṃbhūtiryādavatvaṃ hareḥ svayam
bālabhāve hareḥ krīḍā putrārthaṃ saṃkarārcanam
nārasya ca tathotpattiḥ kapāle vaiṣṇavāddharāt
bhūbhāranigrahārthe tu rudrasyārādhanaṃ hareḥ
devāsure purā labdho bhṛguśāpaś ca viṣṇunā
kṛṣṇatve dvārakāyāntu nilayo mādhavasya tu
labdho hitāya śāpastu durvāsasyānanāddhareḥ
vṛṣṇyandhakavināśāya śāpaḥ piṇḍāravāsinām
erakālābhato 'nyonyaṃ vivāde vṛṣṇivigrahaḥ
līlayā caiva kṛṣṇena svakulasya ca saṃhṛtiḥ
purāndhakāgnidakṣāṇāṃ śakrebhamṛgarūpiṇām
madanasyādidevasya brahmaṇaścāmarāriṇām
halāhalasya daityasya kṛtāvajñā pinākinā
viṣṇorvarāyudhāvāptis tathā rudrasya ceṣṭitam
hareḥ pitāmahasyātha śakrasya ca mahātmanaḥ
bhūmau rudrasya lokaṃ ca pātāle hāṭakeśvaram
tapasāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ caiva dvijānāṃ vaibhavaṃ tathā
ādhikyaṃ sarvamūrtīnāṃ liṅgamūrterviśeṣataḥ
liṅge 'sminnānupūrvyeṇa vistareṇānukīrtyate
etajjñātvā purāṇasya saṃkṣepaṃ kīrtayettu yaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge 'nukramaṇikāvarṇanaṃ nāma dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
aliṅgo liṅgamūlaṃ tu avyaktaṃ liṅgamucyate
aliṅgaḥ śiva ityukto liṅgaṃ śaivamiti smṛtam
aguṇaṃ dhruvamakṣayyamaliṅgaṃ śivalakṣaṇam
gandhavarṇarasairyuktaṃ śabdasparśādilakṣaṇam
jagadyoniṃ mahābhūtaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ dvijottamāḥ
vigraho jagatāṃ liṅgamāliṅgādabhavatsvayam
saptadhācāṣṭadhā caiva tathaikādaśadhā punaḥ
liṅgānyaliṅgasya tathā māyayā vitatāni tu
tebhyaḥ pradhānadevānāṃ trayamāsīcchivātmakam
ekenaiva hṛtaṃ viśvaṃ vyāptaṃ tvevaṃ śivena tu
aliṅgaṃ caiva liṅgaṃ ca liṅgāliṅgāni mūrtayaḥ
aliṅgī bhagavān bījī sa eva parameśvaraḥ
bījaṃ yoniś ca nirbījaṃ nirbījo bījamucyate
bījayonipradhānānām ātmākhyā vartate tviha
viśuddhoyaṃ tathā rudraḥ purāṇe śiva ucyate
śivena dṛṣṭā prakṛtiḥ śaivī samabhavaddvijāḥ
sargādau sā guṇairyuktā purāvyaktā svabhāvataḥ
avyaktādiviśeṣāntaṃ viśvaṃ tasyāḥ samucchritam
viśvadhātrī tvajākhyā ca śaivī sā prakṛtiḥ smṛtā
tāmajāṃ lohitāṃ śuklāṃ kṛṣṇāmekā bahuprajām
janitrīmanuśete sma juṣamāṇaḥ svarūpiṇīm
tāmevājāmajo 'nyastu bhuktabhogāṃ jahāti ca
ajā janitrī jagatāṃ sājena samadhiṣṭhitā
prādurbabhūva sa mahān puruṣādhiṣṭhitasya ca
ajājñayā pradhānasya sargakāle guṇaistribhiḥ
sisṛkṣayā codyamānaḥ praviśyāvyaktamavyayam
vyaktasṛṣṭiṃ vikurute cātma nādhiṣṭhito mahān
mahatastu tathā vṛttiḥ saṃkalpādhyavasāyikā
tenaiva cāvṛtaḥ samyagahaṅkārastamodhikaḥ
ahaṅkārācchabdamātraṃ tasmādākāśamavyayam
saśabdamāvṛṇotpaścādākāśaṃ śabdakāraṇam
tanmātrādbhūtasargaś ca dvijāstvevaṃ prakīrtitaḥ
sparśamātraṃ tathākāśāttasmādvāyur mahānmune
tasmācca rūpamātraṃ tu tatogniś ca rasastataḥ
rasādāpaḥ śubhāstābhyo gandhamātraṃ dharā tataḥ
āvṛṇoddhi tathākāśaṃ sparśamātraṃ dvijottamāḥ
āvṛṇodrūpamātraṃ tu vāyurvāti kriyātmakaḥ
āvṛṇodrasamātraṃ vai devaḥ sākṣādvibhāvasuḥ
āvṛṇvānā gandhamātramāpaḥ sarvarasātmikāḥ
kṣmā sā pañcaguṇā tasmādekonā rasasaṃbhavāḥ
triguṇo bhagavānvahnirdviguṇaḥ sparśa saṃbhavaḥ
pañca buddhīndriyāṇyasya pañca karmedriyāṇi tu
śabdādīnāmavāptyarthaṃ manaścaivobhayātmakam
mahadādiviśeṣāntā hyaṇḍamutpādayanti ca
jalabudbudavattasmādavatīrṇaḥ pitāmahaḥ
aṇḍaṃ daśaguṇenaiva vāriṇā prāvṛtaṃ bahiḥ
āpo daśaguṇenaiva tadbrāhye tejasā vṛtāḥ
tejo daśaguṇenaiva bāhyato vāyunā vṛtam
vāyurdaśaguṇenaiva bāhyato nabhasā vṛtaḥ
ākāśenāvṛto vāyurahaṅkāreṇa śabdajaḥ
mahatāśabdaheturvai pradhānenāvṛtaḥ svayam
saptāṇḍāvaraṇānyāhustasyātmā kamalāsanaḥ
koṭikoṭiyutānyatra cāṇḍāni kathitāni tu
sṛṣṭāḥ pradhānena tadā labdhvā śaṃbhostu saṃnidhim
ādikartā ca bhūtānāṃ saṃhartā paripālakaḥ
tasmānmaheśvaro devo brahmaṇodhipatiḥ śivaḥ
sadāśivo bhavo viṣṇurbrahmā sarvātmako yataḥ
ekadaṇḍe tathā lokā ime kartā pitāmahaḥ
prākṛtaḥ kathitastveṣa puruṣādhiṣṭhito mayā
sargaścābuddhipūrvastu dvijāḥ prāthamikaḥ śubhaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge prākṛtaprāthamikasargakathanaṃ nāma tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
sargasya tādṛśī rātriḥ prākṛtasya samāsanaḥ
divā sṛṣṭiṃ vikurute rajanyāṃ pralayaṃ vibhuḥ
divā vikṛtayaḥ sarve vikārā viśvadevatāḥ
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve tiṣṭhantyanye maharṣayaḥ
ahastu tasya vaikalpo rātristādṛgvidhā smṛtā
catvāri tu sahasrāṇi vatsarāṇāṃ kṛtaṃ dvijāḥ
tāvacchatī ca vai saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca kṛtasya tu
triśartā dviśatī saṃdhyā tathā caikaśatī kramāt
aṃśakaḥ ṣaṭśataṃ tasmātkṛtasaṃdhyāṃśakaṃ vinā
tretādvāparatiṣyāṇāṃ kṛtasya kathayāmi vaḥ
nimeṣapañcadaśakā kāṣṭhā svasthāsya suvratāḥ
martyasya cākṣṇostamyāś ca tatastriṃśatikā kalā
kalātriṃśatiko viprā muhūrta iti kalpitaḥ
muhūrtapañcadaśikā rajanī tādṛśaṃ tvahaḥ
pitrya rātryahanī māsaḥ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ
kṛṣṇapakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī
triṃśadye mānuṣā māsāḥ pitryo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ
śatāni trīṇi māsānāṃ ṣaṣṭyā cāpyadhikāni vai
pitryaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa vibhāvyate
mānupeṇaiva mānana varṣāṇāṃ yacchataṃ bhavet
pitaṇāṃ trīṇi varṣāṇi saṃkhyātānīha tāni vai
daśa vai dvyadhikā māsāḥ vitṛsaṃkhyeha saṃsmṛtā
laukikenaiva mānena abdo yo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ
divye rātryahanī varṣaṃ pravi bhāgastayoḥ punaḥ
ahastatrodagayanaṃ rātriḥ syāddakṣiṇāyanam
ete rātryahanī divye prasaṃkhyāte viśeṣataḥ
triṃśadyāni tu varṣāṇi divyo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ
mānuṣaṃ tu śataṃ viprā divyamāsāstrayastu te
daśa caiva tathāhāni divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ
trīṇi varṣaśatanyena ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇi yāni tu
divyaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitaḥ
triṇi varṣasahasrāṇi mānuṣāṇi pramāṇataḥ
triṃśadanyāni varṣāṇi mataḥ saptarṣivatsaraḥ
nava yāni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu
ṣaṭtriśattu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu
varṣāṇāṃ tacchataṃ jñeyaṃ divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ
trīṇyeva niyutānyāhurvarṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu
ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi saṃkhyātāni tu saṃkhyayā
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu prāhuḥ saṃkhyāvido janāḥ
pūrvaṃ kṛtayugaṃ nāma tatastretā vidhīyate
dvārapaś ca kaliścaiva yugānyetāni suvratāḥ
atha saṃvatsarā dṛṣṭā mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānyāsaṃścaturdaśa ca saṃkhyayā
catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi tathānyāni kṛtaṃ yugam
tathā daśasahasrāṇāṃ varṣāṇāṃ śatasaṃkhyayā
aśītiś ca sahasrāṇi kālasretāyugasya ca
saptaiva niyutānyāhurvarṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu
viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi kālastu dvāparasya ca
tathā śatasahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ trīṇi saṃkhyayā
ṣaṣṭhiścaiva sahasrāṇi kālaḥ kaliyugasya tu
evaṃ caturyugaḥ kāla ṛte saṃdhyāṃśakātsmṛtaḥ
niyutānyeva ṣaṭtriṃśanniraṃśāni tu tāni vai
catvāriṃśattathā trīṇī niyutānīha saṃkhyayā
viṃśatiś ca sahasrāmi saṃdhyāṃśaś ca caturyugaḥ
evaṃ caturyugākhyānāṃ sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ
manvantarasya saṃkhyā ca varṣāgreṇa prakīrtitā
triṃśatkoṭyastu varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣeṇa dvijottamāḥ
saptaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutānyadhikāni tu
viṃśatiś ca sahasrāṇi kāloyamadhikaṃ vinā
manvantarasya saṃkhyaiṣā laiṅgesminkīrtitā dvijāḥ
niśānte sṛjate lokān naśyante niśi jantavaḥ
tatra vaimānikānāṃ tu aṣṭāviṃśatikoṭayaḥ
manvantareṣu vai saṃkhyā sāṃtareṣu yathātathā
trīṇi koṭiśatānyāsan koṭyo dvinavatis tathā
kalpetī'te tu vai viprāḥ sahasrāṇāṃ tu saptatiḥ
punastathāṣṭasāhasraṃ sarvatraiva samāsataḥ
koṭīnāṃ dve sahasre tu aṣṭau koṭiśatāni tu
dviṣāṣṭiś ca tathā koṭyo niyutāni ca saptatiḥ
varṣāṇāmaṣṭasāhasraṃ brāhmaṃ vai brahmaṇo yugam
savanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu trividhaṃ triguṇaṃ tathā
brahmaṇastu tathā proktaḥ kālaḥ kālātmanaḥ prabho
ṛturvahnirhavyavāhaḥ sāvitraḥ śuddha eva ca
uśikaḥ kuśikaścaiva gāndhāro muni sattamāḥ
ṛṣabhaś ca tathā ṣaḍjo majjālīyaś ca madhyamaḥ
vairājovai niṣādaś ca mukhyo vai meghavāhanaḥ
pañcamāścitrakaścaiva ākūtirjñāna eva ca
manaḥ sudarśo bṛṃhaś ca tathā vai śvetalohitaḥ
raktaś ca pītavāsāś ca asitaḥ sarvarūpakaḥ
evaṃ kalpāstu saṃkhyātā brahmaṇo 'vyaktajanmanaḥ
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇi kalpānāṃ munisattamāḥ
gatāni tāvaccheṣāṇi aharniśyāni vai punaḥ
parānte vai vikārāṇi vikāraṃ yānti viśvataḥ
vikārasya śivasyājñāvaśenaiva tu saṃhṛtiḥ
sādharmyeṇāvatiṣṭhete pradhānapuruṣāvubhau
guṇānāṃ caiva vaiṣamye viprāḥ sṛṣṭiriti smṛtā
sāmye layo guṇānāṃ tu tayorheturmaheśvaraḥ
līlayā devadevena sargāstvīdṛgvidhāḥ kṛtāḥ
asaṃkhyātāś ca saṃkṣepāt pradhānādanvadhiṣṭhitāt
asaṃkhyātāś ca kalpākhyā hyasaṃkhyatāḥ pitāmahāḥ
harayaścāpyasaṃkhyātās tv eka eva maheśvaraḥ
pradhānādipravṛttāni līlayā prākṛtāni tu
aprākṛtasya tasyādirmadhyāntaṃ nāsti cātmanaḥ
pitāmahasyātha paraḥ parārdhadvayasaṃmitaḥ
divā sṛṣṭaṃ tu yatsarvaṃ niśi naśyati cāsya tat
rātrau caikārṇave brahma naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame
suṣvāpāṃbhāsi yastasmānnārāyaṇa iti smṛtaḥ
śarvaryante prabuddho vai dṛṣṭvā śūnyaṃ carācaram
sraṣṭuṃ tadā matiṃ cakre brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ
udakairāplutāṃ kṣmāṃ tāṃ samādāya sanātanaḥ
pūrvavatsthāpayāmāsa vārāhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ
nadīnadasamudrāṃś ca pūrvavaccākarotprabhuḥ
dharāyāṃ socinotsarvān girīn dagdhān purāgninā
bhūrādyāṃścaturo lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat
sraṣṭuṃ ca bhagavāṃścakre tadā sraṣṭā punarmatim
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sṛṣṭiprāraṃbhavarṇanaṃ nāma caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
yadā sraṣṭuṃ matiṃ cakre mohaścāsīnmahātmanaḥ
tamo moho mahāmo hastāmisraścāndhasaṃjñitaḥ
avidyā pañcadhā hyeṣā prādurbhūtā svayaṃbhuvaḥ
asādhaka iti smṛtvā sargo mukhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ
abhyamanyata so 'nyaṃ vai nagā mukhyodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ
arvāksroto 'nugrahaś ca tathā bhūtādikaḥ punaḥ
saptamo mānuṣo viprā aṣṭamo 'nugrahaḥ smṛtaḥ
navamaścaiva kaumāraḥ prākṛtā vaikṛtāstvime
purastādasṛjaddevaḥ sanandaṃ sanakaṃ tathā
sanātanaṃ muniśreṣṭhā naiṣkarmyeṇa gatāḥ param
dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so 'sṛjadyogavidyayā
navaite brahmaṇaḥ putrā brahmajñā brāhmaṇottamāḥ
brahmavādina evaite brahmaṇaḥ sadṛśāḥ smṛtāḥ
ṛbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca sasarjādau sanātanaḥ
vakṣye bhāryākulaṃ teṣāṃ munīnāmagrajanmanām
samāsato muniśreṣṭhāḥ prajāsaṃbhūtimeva ca
śatarūpāṃ tu vai rājñiṃ virājamasṛjatprabhuḥ
svāyaṃbhuvāttu vai rājñī śatarūpā tvayonijā
lebhe putradvayaṃ puṇyā tathā kanyādvayaṃ ca sā
uttānapādo hyavaro dhīmāñjyeṣṭhaḥ priyaṃvrataḥ
jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā tvākūtiḥ prasūtiścānujā smṛtā
upayeme tadākūtiṃ rucirnāma prajāpatiḥ
prasūtiṃ bhagavāndakṣo lokadhātrīṃ ca yoginīm
dakṣiṇāsahitaṃ yajñamākūtiḥ suṣuve tathā
dakṣiṇājanayāmāsa divyā dvādaśa putrikāḥ
prasūtiḥ suṣuve dakṣāccaturviśatikanyakāḥ
śraddhāṃ lakṣmīṃ dhṛtiṃ puṣṭiṃ tuṣṭiṃ medhāṃ kriyāṃ tathā
buddhi lajjāṃ vapuḥśāntiṃ siddhiṃ kīrti mahātapāḥ
khyātiṃ śānti ca saṃbhūtiṃ smṛitṃ prītiṃ kṣamāṃ tathā
sannatiṃ cānasūyāṃ ca ūrjāṃ svāhāṃ surāraṇim
svadhāṃ caiva mahābhāgāṃ pradadau ca yathākramam
śraddhādyāścaiva kīrtyantāstrayodaśa sudārikāḥ
dharmaṃ prajāpatiṃ jagmuḥ patiṃ paramadurlabhāḥ
upayeme bhṛgurdhīmān khyātiṃ tāṃ bhārgavāraṇim
saṃbhūtiṃ ca marīcistu smṛtiṃ caivāṅgirā muniḥ
prītiṃ pulastyaḥ puṇyātmā kṣamāṃ tāṃ pulaho muniḥ
kratuś ca saṃnatiṃ dhīmānatristāṃ cānasūyakām
ūrjāṃ vasiṣṭho bhagavānvariṣṭho vārijekṣaṇām
vibhāvasus tathā svāhāṃ svadhāṃ vai pitaras tathā
putrīkṛtā satī yā sā mānasī śivasaṃbhavā
dakṣema jagatāṃ dhātrī rudramevāsthitā patim
ardhanālīśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā sargādau kanakāṇḍajaḥ
vibhajasveti cāhādau yadā jātā tadābhavat
tasyāścaivāṃśajāḥ sarvāḥ striyastribhuvane tathā
ekādaśāvidhā rudrāstasya cāṃśodbhavās tathā
strīliṅgamakhilaṃ sā vai pulliṅgaṃ nīlalohitaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān brahmā dakṣamālokya suvratām
bhajasva dhātrīṃ jagatāṃ mamāpi ca tavāpi ca
praśastā tava kānteyaṃ syāt putrī viśvamātṛkā
tasmāt putrī satī nāmnā tavaiṣā ca bhaviṣyati
labdhvā putrīṃ dadau sākṣāt satīṃ rudrāya sādaram
dharmasya patnyaḥ śraddhādyāḥ kīrtitā vai trayodaśa
śrutastu daṇḍaḥ samayo bodhaścaiva mahādyutiḥ
kṣemaṃ sukhaṃ yaśaścaiva dharmaputrāś ca tāsu vai
dharmasya vai kriyāyāṃ tu daṇḍaḥ samaya eva ca
bhṛgupatnī ca suṣuve khyātirviṣṇoḥ priyāṃ śriyam
dhātāraṃ ca vidhātāraṃ merorjāmātarau sutau
prabhūtirnāma yā patnī marīceḥ suṣuve sutau
pūrṇamāsaṃ tu mārīcaṃ tataḥ kanyācatuṣṭayam
tuṣṭirjyeṣṭhā ca vai dṛṣṭiḥ kṛṣiścāpacitis tathā
kṣamā ca suṣuve putrān putrīṃ ca pulahācchubhām
kardamaṃ ca varīyāṃsaṃ sahiṣṇuṃ munisattamāḥ
tathā kanakapītāṃ sa pīvarīṃ pṛthivīsamām
prītyāṃ pulastyaś ca tathā janayāmāsa vai sutān
dattorṇaṃ vedabāhuṃ ca putrīṃ cānyāṃ dṛṣadvatīm
putrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭisāhasraṃ saṃnatiḥ suṣuve śubhā
kratostu bhāryā sarve te vālakhilyā iti śrutāḥ
sinīvālīṃ kuhūṃ caiva rākāṃ cānumatiṃ tathā
smṛtiś ca suṣuve patnī muneścāṅgirasas tathā
atrerbhāryānasūyā vai suṣuve ṣaṭprajāstu yāḥ
tāsvekā kanyakā nāmnā śrutuḥ sā sūnupañcakam
somaś ca vai śrutiḥ ṣaṣṭhī pañcātreyāstu sūnavaḥ
ūrjā vasiṣṭhādvai lebhe sutāṃś ca sutavatsalā
jyāyasī puṇḍarīkākṣānvāsiṣṭhānvaralocanā
rajaḥ suhotro bāhuś ca savanaścānaghas tathā
yaścābhimānā bhagavān bhavātmā paitāmaho vahnirasuḥ prajānām
svāhā ca tasmātsuṣuve sutānāṃ trayaṃ trayāṇāṃ jagatāṃ hitāya
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge prajāsṛṣṭivarṇanaṃ nāma pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
pavamānaḥ pāvakaś ca śuciragniś ca te smṛtāḥ
nirmarthyaḥ pavamānastu vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ
śuciḥ saurastu vijñeyaḥ svāhāputrāstrayastu te
putraiḥ pautraistvihaiteṣāṃ saṃkhyā saṃkṣepataḥ smṛtā
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve sarve rudrātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ
ayajvānaś ca yajvānaḥ pitaraḥ prītimānasāḥ
āgniṣvāttāś ca yajvānaḥ śeṣā barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ
menāṃ tu mānasīṃ teṣāṃ janayāmāsa vai svadhā
āgniṣvāttātmajā menā mānasī lokaviśrutā
asūta menā mainākaṃ kraiñcaṃ tasyānujāmumām
gaṅgāṃ haimavatīṃ jajñe bhavāṅgāśleṣapāvanīm
dharaṇīṃ janayāmāsa mānasīṃ yajñayājinīm
pitaro 'mṛtapāḥ proktāsteṣāṃ caiveha vistaraḥ
ṛṣīṇāṃ ca kulaṃ sarvaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ tatsuvistaram
vadāmi pṛthagadhyāyasaṃsthitaṃ vastadūrdhvataḥ
dākṣāyaṇi sati yātā pārśvaṃ rudrasya pārvatī
paścāddakṣaṃ vinindyaiṣā patiṃ lebhe bhavaṃ tathā
tāṃ dhyātvā vyasṛjadrudrānanekānnīlalohitaḥ
yācito muniśārdūlā brahmaṇā prahasan kṣaṇāt
tāndṛṣṭvā vividhātrudrānnirmalānnīlalohitān
jarāmaraṇanirmuktān prāha rudranpitāmahaḥ
namo 'stu vo mahādevāstrinetrā nīla lohitāḥ
sarvajñāḥ sarvagā dīrghā hrasvā vāmanakāḥ śubhāḥ
hiraṇyakeśā dṛṣṭighnā nityā buddhāś ca nirmalāḥ
nirdvandvā vītarāgāś ca viśvātmāno bhavātamajāḥ
evaṃ stutvā tadā rudrātrudraṃ cāha bhavaṃ śivam
pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tadā bhagavānkanakāṇḍajaḥ
mṛtyuhīnā vibho sraṣṭuṃ mṛtyuyuktāḥ sṛja prabho
tatastamāha bhagavānna hi me tādṛśī sthitiḥ
sa tvaṃ sṛja yathākāmaṃ mṛtyuyuktāḥ prajāḥ prabho
labdhvā sasarja sakalaṃ śaṅkarācca turānanaḥ
śaṅkaro 'pi tadā rudraurnivṛttātmā hyadhiṣṭhitaḥ
sthāṇutvaṃ tasya vai viprāḥ śaṅkarasya mahātmanaḥ
niṣkalasyātmanaḥ śaṃbhoḥ svecchādhṛtaśarīriṇaḥ
śaṃ rudraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ karoti ghṛṇayā yataḥ
śaṅkaraścāprayatnena tadātmā yoga vidyayā
aṇostu viṣayatyāgaḥ saṃsārabhayataḥ kramāt
vairāgyājjāyate puṃso virāgo darśanāntare
vimikhyo viguṇatyāgo vijñānasyāvicārataḥ
tasya cāsya ca saṃdhānaṃ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ
dharmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ śaṅkarād iha
sa eva śaṅkaraḥ sākṣāt pinākī nīlalohitaḥ
ye śaṅkarāśritāḥ sarve mucyante te na saṃśayaḥ
na gacchantyeva narakaṃ pāpiṣṭhā api dāruṇam
āśritāḥ śaṅkaraṃ tasmātprāpnuvanti ca śaśvatam
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
māyāntāścaiva ghorādya hyaṣṭaviṃśatireva ca
koṭayo narakāṇāṃ tu pacyante tāsu pāpinaḥ
anā śritāḥ śivaṃ rudrāṃ śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam
āśrayaṃ sarvabhūtānāmavyayaṃ jagatāṃ patim
puruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam
tamasā kālarudrākhyaṃ rajasā kanakāṇḍajam
karmaṇākarmaṇā vāpi śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ
prabhāvaṃ śaṅkarasyādyaṃ saṃkṣepātsarvadarśinaḥ
yoginaḥ sarvatattvajñāḥ paraṃ vairāgyamāsthitāḥ
prāṇāyāmādibhiścāṣṭasādhanaiḥ sahacāriṇaḥ
karuṇādiguṇopetāḥ kṛtvāpi vividhāni te
prasādājjāyate jñānaṃ jñānādyogaḥ pravartate
yogena jāyate muktiḥ prasādādākhilaṃ tataḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
prasādā dyādi vijñānaṃ svarūpaṃ vaktumarhasi
divyaṃ māheśvaraṃ caiva yogaṃ yogavidāṃ vara
kathaṃ karoti bhagavān cintayā rahitaḥ śivaḥ
prasādaṃ yogamārgeṇa kasminkāle nṛṇāṃ vibhuḥ
romaharṣaṇa uvāca
devānāṃ ca ṛṣīṇāṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ saṃnidhau purā
śailādinā tu kathitaṃ śṛṇvantu brahmasūnave
vyāsāvatārāṇi tathā dvāparānte ca suvratāḥ
yogācāryāvatārāṇi tathā tiṣye tu śūlinaḥ
tatratatra vibhoḥ śiṣyāścātvāraḥ śamabhājanāḥ
praśīṣyā bahavasteṣāṃ prasīdatyevamīśvaraḥ
evaṃ kramāgataṃ jñānaṃ mukhādeva nṛṇāṃ vibhoḥ
vaiśyāntaṃ brāhmaṇādyaṃ hi ghṛṇayā cānurūpataḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
dvāparedvāpare vyāsāḥ ke vai kutrāntareṣu vai
sūta uvāca
śṛṇvantu kalpe vārāhe dvijā vaivasvatāntare
vyāsāṃś ca sāṃprataṃ rudrāṃs tathā sarvāntareṣu vai
vedānāṃ ca purāṇānāṃ tathā jñānapradarśakān
yathākramaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvāvarteṣu sāpratam
kratuḥ satyo bhārgavaś ca aṅgirāḥ savitā dvijāḥ
mṛtyuḥ śatakraturdhīmān vasiṣṭho munipuṅgavaḥ
sārasvatastridhāmā ca trivṛto munipuṅgavaḥ
śatatejāḥ svayaṃ dharmo nārāyaṇa iti śrutaḥ
tarakṣuścāruṇirdhīmāṃs tathā devaḥ gṛtañjayaḥ
vācaḥśravāḥ muniḥ sākṣāttathā śuṣmāyaṇiḥ śuciḥ
tṛṇābindurmunī rukṣaḥ śaktiḥ śākteya uttaraḥ
jātūkarṇyo hariḥ sākṣātkṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ
vyāsāstvete ca śṛṇvantu kalau yogeśvarān kramāt
asaṃkhyātā hi kalpeṣu vibhoḥ sarvāntareṣu ca
kalau rudrāvatārāṇāṃ vyāsānāṃ kila gauravāt
avatārān pravakṣyāmi tathā sarvāntareṣu vai
ṛṣa ūcuḥ
manvantarāṇi vārāhe vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam
romaharṣaṇa uvāca
manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvastvādyastataḥ svārociṣo dvijāḥ
uttamastāmasaścaiva raivatāścākṣuṣas tathā
vaivasvataś ca sāvarṇir dharmaḥ sāvarṇikaḥ punaḥ
piśaṅgaścāpiśaṅgābhaḥ śabalo varṇakas tathā
aukārāntā akārādyā manavaḥ parīkīrtitāḥ
śvetaḥ pāṇḍus tathā raktastāmrāḥ patiś ca kāpilaḥ
kṛṣṇaḥ śyāmas tathā dhūmraḥ sudhūmraś ca dvijottamāḥ
apiśaṅgaḥ piśaṅgaś ca trivarṇaḥ śabalas tathā
kālandhurastu kathitā varmato manavaḥ śubhāḥ
svarātmānaḥ samākhyātāścāntareśāḥ samāsataḥ
vaivasvata ṛkārastu manuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sureśvaraḥ
samatīteṣu kalpeṣu tathā cānāgateṣu vai
vārāhaḥ sāṃprataṃ jñeyaḥ saptamāntarataḥ kramāt
yogāvatārāṃś ca vibhoḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ saṃtatis tathā
saṃprekṣya sarvakāleṣu tathāvartteṣu yoginām
ādye śvetaḥ kalau rudrāḥ sutāro madanas tathā
suhotraḥ kaṅkaṇaścaiva logākṣirmunisattamāḥ
jaigīṣavyo mahātejā bhagavān dadhivāhanaḥ
ṛṣabhaś ca munirdhīmānugraścatriḥ subālakaḥ
vedaśīrṣaś ca gokarṇo guhāvāsī śikhaṇḍabhṛt
jaṭā mālyaṭṭahāsaś ca dāruko lāṅgalī tathā
mahākāyamuniḥ śūlī daṇḍī muṇḍīśvaraḥ svayam
sahiṣṇuḥ somaśarmā ca nakulīśo jagadguruḥ
yogācāryāvatārā ye sarvāvarteṣu suvratāḥ
vyāsāścaivaṃ muniśreṣṭhā dvāparedvāpare tvime
yogeśvarāṇāṃ catvāraḥ śiṣyāḥ pratyekamavyayāḥ
śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaṇḍī ca śvetāśvaḥ śvetalohitaḥ
dundubhiḥ śatarūpaś ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃs tathā
viśākeś ca vikeśaś ca vipāśaḥ pāpanāśanaḥ
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca sudhāmā virajās tathā
śaṅkhapā dvairajaścaiva meghaḥ sārasvatas tathā
suvāhano muniśreṣṭho meghavāho mahādyutiḥ
kapilaścāsuriścaiva tathā pañcāśikho muniḥ
vālkalaś ca mahāyogī dharmātmāno mahaujasaḥ
parāśaraś ca gargaś ca bhārgavaścāṅgirās tathā
balabandhuniṃrāmitraḥ ketuśṛṅgastapodhanaḥ
laṃbodaraś ca laṃbaś ca laṃbākṣo laṃbakeśakaḥ
sudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vāsiṣṭho virajās tathā
atrirdevasadaścaiva śravaṇo 'tha śraviṣṭhakaḥ
kuṇiś ca kuṇibāhuś ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ
kaśyapopyuśanāścaiva cyavano 'tha bṛhaspatiḥ
vācaḥśravāḥ sudhakiś ca śyāvāśvaś ca yatīśvaraḥ
hiraṇya nābhaḥ kauśalyo logākṣiḥ kuthumis tathā
plakṣo dālbhyāyāṇiścaiva ketumān gopanas tathā
bhallāvī madhupiṅgaś ca śvetaketustāponidhiḥ
śālihotrogniveśaś ca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ
chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaś ca kuṃbhaścaiva pravāhaṅkaḥ
ulūko vidyutaścaiva maṇḍūko hyāśvalāyanaḥ
akṣapādaḥ kumāraś ca uluko vatsa eva ca
śiṣyāstvete mahātmānaḥ sarvāvarteṣu yoginām
vimalā brahmabhūyiṣṭhā jñānayogaparāyaṇāḥ
ete pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ
śiṣyāḥ praśiṣyāścaiteṣāṃ śataśotha sahasraśaḥ
prāpya pāśupataṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ
devādayaḥ piśācāntāḥ paśavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
teṣāṃ patitvātsarveśo bhavaḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ
tena praṇīto rudreṇa paśūnāṃ patinā dvijāḥ
yogaḥ pāśupato jñeyaḥ parāvaravibhūtaye
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge manuvyāsa yogeśvaratacchiṣyakathanaṃ nāma saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
saṃkṣepataḥ pravakṣyāmi yogasthānāni sāṃpratam
kalpitāni śivenaiva hitāya jagatāṃ dvijāḥ
prasādasya svarūpaṃ yatsvasaṃvedyaṃ dvijottamāḥ
vaktuṃ na śakyaṃ brahmādyaiḥ kramaśo jāyate nṛṇām
yogaśabdena nirvāṇaṃ māheśaṃ padamucyate
tasya heturṛṣerjñānaṃ jñānaṃ tasya prasādataḥ
jñānena nirdahetpāpaṃ nirudhya viṣayān sadā
sādhanānyaṣṭadhā cāsya kathitānīha siddhaye
tṛtīyamāsanaṃ proktaṃ prāṇāyāmastataḥ param
pratyāhāraṃ pañcamo vai dhāraṇā ca tataḥ parā
dhyānaṃ saptamamityuktaṃ samādhistvaṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ
ahiṃsā prathamo heturyamasya yamināṃ varāḥ
niyamasyāpi vai mūlaṃ yama eva na saṃśayaḥ
ātmavatsarvabhūtānāṃ hitāyaiva pravartanam
ahiṃsaiṣā samākhyātā yā cātmajñānasiddhidā
dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ cānubhitaṃ svānubhūtaṃ yathārthataḥ
nāślīlaṃ kīrtayedevaṃ brāhmaṇānāmiti śrutiḥ
anādānaṃ parasvānāmāpadyapi vicārataḥ
manasā karmaṇā vācā tadasteyaṃ samāsataḥ
maithunasyāpravṛttirhi manovākkāyakarmaṇā
brahmacaryamiti proktaṃ yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām
iha vaikhānasānāṃ ca vidārāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ
sadārāṇāṃ gṛhasthanāṃ tathaiva ca vadāmi vaḥ
svadāre vidhivatkṛtvā nivṛttiścānyataḥ sadā
manasā karmaṇā vācā brahmacaryamiti smṛtam
medhyā svanārā saṃbhogaṃ kṛtvā snānaṃ samācaret
evaṃ gṛhastho yuktātmā brahmacārī na saṃśayaḥ
vidhinā yādṛśī hiṃsā sātva hiṃsā iti smṛtā
striyaḥ sadā parityājyāḥ saṃgaṃ naiva ca kārayet
kuṇapeṣu yathā citta tathā kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ
viṇmūtrotsargakāleṣu bahirbhūmau yathā matiḥ
tathā kāryā ratau cāpi svadāre cānyataḥ kutaḥ
aṅgārasadṛśī nārī ghṛtakuṃbhasamaḥ pumān
tasmānnariṣu saṃsargaṃ dūrataḥ parivarjayet
bhogena tṛptirnaivāsti viṣayāṇāṃ vicārataḥ
tasmādvirāgaḥ kartavyo manasā karmaṇā girā
na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānāmupabhogena śāmyati
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate
tasmāttyāgaḥ sadā kāryastvamṛtatvāya yoginā
tyogenaivāmṛtatvaṃ hi śrutismṛtividāṃ varāḥ
karmaṇā prajayā nāsti dravyeṇa dvijasattamāḥ
tasmādvirāgaḥ kartavyo manovākkāyakarmaṇā
yamāḥ saṃkṣepataḥ proktā niyamāṃś ca vadāmi vaḥ
śaucamijyā tapo dānaṃ svādhyāyopasthanigrahaḥ
vratopavāsamaunaṃ ca snānaṃ ca niyamā daśa
niyamaḥ syādanīhā ca śaucaṃ tuṣṭistapas tathā
japaḥ śivapraṇīdhānaṃ padmakādyaṃ tathāsanam
bāhyamābhyantaraṃ proktaṃ śaucamābhyantaraṃ varam
bāhyaśaucena yuktaḥ saṃs tathā cābhyantaraṃ caret
āgneyaṃ vāruṇaṃ brāhmaṃ kartavyaṃ śivapūjakaiḥ
snānaṃ vidhānataḥ samyak paścādābhyaṃ taraṃ caret
ādehāntaṃ mṛdālipya tīrthatoyeṣu sarvadā
śaivalā jhaṣakā matsyāḥ sattvā matsyopajīvinaḥ
sadāvagādyaḥ salile viśuddhāḥ kiṃ dvijottamāḥ
tasmādābhyantaraṃ śaucaṃ sadā kāryaṃ vidhānataḥ
ātmajñānāṃbhasi snātvā sakṛdālipya bhāvataḥ
suvairāgyamṛdā śuddhaḥ śaucamevaṃ prakīrtitam
śuddhasya siddhayo dṛṣṭā naivāśuddhasya siddhayaḥ
nyāyenāgatayā vṛttyā saṃtuṣṭo yastu suvrataḥ
saṃtoṣastasya satatamatītārthasya cāsmṛtiḥ
cāndrāyaṇādinipuṇasya pāṃsi suśubhāni ca
svādhyāyastu japaḥ proktaḥ praṇavasya tridhā smṛtaḥ
vācikaścādhamo mukhya upāṃśuścottamottamaḥ
mānaso vistareṇaiva kalpe pañcākṣare smṛtaḥ
tathā śivapraṇīdhānaṃ manovākkāyakarmaṇā
śivajñānaṃ gurorbhaktiracalā supratiṣṭhitā
nigraho hyapahṛtyāśu prasaktānīndriyāṇi ca
viṣayeṣu samāsena pratyāhāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
cittasya dhāraṇā proktā sthānabandhaḥ samāsataḥ
tasyāḥ svāsthyena dhyānaṃ ca samādhiś ca vicārataḥ
samādhiḥ sarvahetuś ca prāṇāyāma iti smṛtaḥ
prāṇāpānanirodhastu prāṇāyāmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
prāṇāyāmasya mānaṃ tu mātrādvādaśakaṃ smṛtam
nīco dvādaśamātrastu uddhāto dvādaśaḥ smṛtaḥ
mukhyastu yastriruddhātaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśanmātra ucyate
romāñcadhvanisaṃviddhasvāṅgamo ṭanakaṃpanam
bhramaṇaṃ svedajanyā sā saṃvinmūrcchā bhavedyadā
tadottamottamaḥ proktaḥ praṇāyāmaḥ suśobhanaḥ
ibho vā śarabho vāpi durādharṣo 'tha kesarī
tathā samariṇo 'svastho durādharṣaś ca yoginām
yathaiva mṛgarāḍ nāgaḥ śarabho vāpi durmadaḥ
kālāntaravaśādyogāddamyate paramādarāt
manovākkāyajān doṣān karturdehaṃ ca rakṣati
saṃyuktasya tathā samyakprāṇāyāmena dhīmataḥ
doṣāttasmācca naśyanti niśvāsastena jīryate
prāṇāyāmena sidhyanti divyāḥ śāntyādayaḥ kramāt
śāntiḥ praśāntirdīptiś ca prasādaś ca tathā kramāt
ādau catuṣṭayasyeha proktā śāntiriha dvijāḥ
sahajāgantukānāṃ ca pāpānāṃ śāntīrucyate
praśāntiḥ saṃyamaḥ samyagvacasāmiti saṃsmṛtā
prakāśo dīptirityuktaḥ sarvataḥ sarvadā dvijāḥ
prasāda iti saṃproktaḥ svānte tviha catuṣṭaye
prāṇo 'pānaḥ samānaś ca udāno vyāna eva ca
nāgaḥ kūrmastu kṛkalo devadatto dhanañjayaḥ
eteṣāṃ yaḥ prasādastu marutāmiti saṃsmṛtaḥ
prayāṇaṃ kurute tasmādvāyuḥ prāṇa iti smṛtaḥ
apānayatyapānastu āhārādīn krameṇa ca
vyāno vyānāmayatyaṅgaṃ vyādhyādīnāṃ prakopakaḥ
udvejayati marmāṇi udāno 'yaṃ praṅkīrtitaḥ
samaṃ nayati gātrāṇi samānaḥ pañca vāyavaḥ
udgāre nāga ākhyātaḥ kūrma unmīlane tu saḥ
kṛkalaḥ kṣutakāyaiva devadatto vijṛṃbhaṇe
dhanañjayo mahāghoṣaḥ sarvagaḥ sa mṛte 'pi hi
iti yo daśavāyūnāṃ prāṇāyāmena sidhyati
prasādo 'sya turīyā tu saṃjñā viprāścatuṣṭaye
khyātiḥ saṃvīttataḥ paścādīśvaro matireva ca
buddheretāḥ dvijāḥ saṃjñā mahataḥ parikīrtitāḥ
asyā buddheḥ prasādastu prāṇāyāmena siddhyati
visvaro visvarībhāvo dvandvānāṃ munisattamāḥ
agrajaḥ sarva tattvānāṃ mahānyaḥ parimāṇataḥ
yatpramāṇaguhā prajñā manastu manute yataḥ
bṛhatvādbṛṃhaṇatvācca brahmā brahmavidāṃvarāḥ
sarvakarmāṇi bhogārthaṃ yaccinoti citiḥ smṛtā
khyāyate yattviti khyātir jñānādibhir anekaśaḥ
sarvatattvādhipaḥ sarvaṃ vijānāti yadīśvaraḥ
asyā buddheḥ prasādastu prāṇāyāmena siddhyati
doṣānvinirdahetsarvān prāṇāyāmādasau yamī
pātakaṃ dhāraṇābhistu pratyāhāreṇa nirdahet
viṣayānviṣavaddhyātvā dhyānenānīśvarān guṇān
samādhinā yatiśreṣṭhāḥ prajñāvṛddhiṃ vivardhayet
sthānaṃ labdhvaiva kurvīta yogāṣṭāṅgāni vai kramāt
agnyabhyāse jale vāpi śuṣkaparṇacaye tathā
jantuvyāpte śmaśāne ca jīrṇagoṣṭe catuṣpathe
nācareddehabādhāyāṃ daurmanasyādisaṃbhave
darpaṇodarasaṃkāśe kṛṣṇāgarusudhūpite
nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇe vitānopari śobhite
samāsanastho yogāṅgānyabhyaseddhṛṣitaḥ svayam
praṇipatya guruṃ paścādbhavaṃ devīṃ vināyakam
yogīśvarān saśiṣyāṃś ca yogaṃ yuñjīta yogavit
āsanaṃ svastikaṃ badhvā padmamardhāsanaṃ tu vā
samajānus tathā dhīmānekajānurathāpivā
samaṃ dṛḍhāsano bhūtvā saṃhṛtya caraṇāvubhau
saṃvṛtāsyopabaddhākṣa uro viṣṭabhya cāgrataḥ
pārṣṇibhyāṃ vṛṣaṇau rakṣaṃs tathā prajananaṃ punaḥ
kiñcidunnāmitaśira dantairdantānna saṃspṛśet
saṃprekṣya nāsikāgrāṃ svaṃ diśaścānavalo kayan
oṅkāravācyaṃ paramaṃ śuddhaṃ dīpaśikhākṛtim
dhyāyedvai puṇḍarīkasya karṇikāyāṃ samāhitaḥ
tryaṅgule cāṣṭakoṇaṃ vā pañcakoṇamathāpi vā
trikoṇaṃ ca tathāgneyaṃ saumyaṃ sauraṃ svaśaktibhiḥ
āgneyaṃ ca tataḥ sauraṃ saumyamevaṃ vidhānataḥ
agneradhaḥ prakalpyaivaṃ dharmādīnāṃ catuṣṭayam
guṇatrayaṃ krameṇaiva maṇḍalopari bhāvayet
nābhau vātha gale vāpi śrūmadhye vā yathāvidhi
lalāṭa phalikāyāṃ vā mūrdhni dhyānaṃ samācaret
dbidale ṣoḍaśāre vā dvādaśāre krameṇa tu
daśāre vā ṣaāḍasre vā caturasre smarecchivam
dvādaśādityasaṃkāśe candrabiṃbasame 'pi vā
āgnivarṇe 'tha vā vidyudvalayābhe samāhitaḥ
nīlalohitabiṃbe vā yogī dhyānaṃ samabhya set
maheśvaraṃ hṛdi dhyāyennābhipadme sadāśivam
candracūḍaṃ lalāṭe tu śrūmadhye śaṅkaraṃ svayam
divye ca śāśvatasthāne śivadhyānaṃ samabhyaset
nirmalaṃ niṣkalaṃ brahma suśāntaṃ jñānarūpiṇam
alakṣaṇamanirdeśyamaṇoralpataraṃ śubham
kaivalyaṃ caiva nirvāṇaṃ niḥśreyasamanūpamam
mahānandaṃ parānandaṃ yogānandamanāmayam
heyopādeyarahitaṃ sūkṣmātsūkṣmataraṃ śivam
atīndriyamanābhāsaṃ paraṃ tattvaṃ parātparam
nābhau sadāśivaṃ cāpi sarvadevātmakaṃ vibhum
dehamadhye śivaṃ devaṃ śuddhajñānamayaṃ vibhum
kanyasenaiva mārgeṇa codghātenāpi śaṅkaram
dvātrīṃśadrecayeddhīmān hṛdi nābhau samāhitaḥ
recakaṃ pūrakaṃ tyaktvā kuṃbhakaṃ ca dvijottamāḥ
ānandaṃ brahmaṇo vidvān sākṣātsamarase sthitaḥ
dhāraṇā dvādaśāyāmā dhyānaṃ dvādaśa dhāraṇam
dhyānaṃ dvādaśakaṃ yāvatsamādhi rabhidhīyate
athavā jñānināṃ viprāḥ saṃparkādeva jāyate
prayatnādvā tayostulya cirādvā hyacirāddvijāḥ
yogāntarāyāsta syātha jāyante yuñjataḥ punaḥ
iti śrīliṅge mahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge 'ṣṭāṅgayoganirūpaṇaṃ nāmāṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
ālasyaṃ prathamaṃ paścādvyādhipīḍā prajāyate
pramādaḥ saṃśayasthāne cittasyehānavasthitiḥ
aśraddhādarśanaṃ bhrāntirduḥkhaṃ ca trividhaṃ tataḥ
daśadhābhiprajāyante muneryogāntarāyakāḥ
ālasyaṃ cāpravṛttiś ca gurutvātkāyācittayoḥ
vyādhayo dhātuvaiṣamyāt karmajā doṣajās tathā
pramādastu samāvestu sādhanānā mabhāvanam
idaṃ vetyubhayaspṛktaṃ vijñānaṃ sthānasaṃśayaḥ
aśraddhābhāvarahitā vṛttirvai sādhaneṣu ca
sādhye cittasya hi gurau jñānācāraśivādiṣu
anātmanyātmavijñānamajñānāttasya saṃnidhau
icchāvighātātsaṃkṣobhaścetasastadudāhṛtam
tamasā rajasā caiva saṃspṛṣṭaṃ durmanaḥ smṛtam
haṭhātsvīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā yogyāyogya vivekataḥ
pranaṣṭeṣvantarāyeṣu dvijāḥ paścāddhi yoginaḥ
pratibhā prathamā siddhirdvitīyā śravaṇā smṛtā
vārtā tṛtīyā viprendrāsturīyā ceha darśanā
āsvādā pañcamī proktā vedanā ṣaṣṭhikā smṛtā
svalpaṣaṭsiddhisaṃtyāgātsiddhidāḥ siddhayo muneḥ
sūkṣme vyavahitetīte viprakṛṣṭe tvanāgate
sarvatra sarvadā jñānaṃ pratibhānukrameṇa tu
śravaṇātsarvaśabdānāmaprayatnena yoginaḥ
hrasvadīrghaplutādīnāṃ guhyānāṃ śravaṇādapi
sparśasyādhigamo yastu vedanā tūpapāditā
darśanāddivyarūpāṇāṃ darśanaṃ cāprayatnataḥ
vārtā ca divyagandhānāṃ tanmātrā buddhisaṃvidā
jagatyasmin hi dehasthaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ samam
aupasagiṅkameteṣu guṇeṣu guṇitaṃ dvijāḥ
paiśāce pārthivaṃ cāpyaṃ rākṣasānāṃ pure dvijāḥ
yākṣe tu taijasaṃ proktaṃ gāndharve śvasanātmakam
ādye cāṣṭau dvitīye ca tathā ṣoḍaśarūpakam
catvāriṃśat pañcame tu bhūtamātrātmakaṃ smṛtam
tathāṣṭacatvāriṃśacca ṣaṭpañcāśattathaiva ca
catuḥ ṣaṣṭiguṇaṃ brāhmaṃ labhate dvijasattamāḥ
sthūlatā hrasvatā bālyaṃ vārdhakyaṃ yauvanaṃ tathā
nānājātisvarūpaṃ ca caturbhir dehadhāraṇam
pārthivāṃśaṃ vinā nityaṃ surabhir gandhasaṃyutaḥ
etadaṣṭaguṇaṃ proktamaiśvaryaṃ pārthivaṃ mahat
tattadrasānvitaṃ tasya trayāṇāṃ dehadhāraṇam
bhāṇḍaṃ vinātha hastena jalapiṇḍasya dhāraṇam
agninigrahaṇaṃ haste smṛtimātreṇa cāgamaḥ
bhasmībhūtavinirmāṇaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ sakāmataḥ
dvābhyāṃ rūpaviniṣpattirvinā taistribhir ātmanaḥ
caturviṃśātmakaṃ hyetattaijasaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
manogatitvaṃ bhūtānāmantarnivasanaṃ tathā
laghutvaṃ ca gurutvaṃ ca pāṇibhyāṃ vāyudhāraṇam
chāyāvihīnaniṣpattirindriyāṇāṃ ca darśanam
dūre ca śabdagrahaṇaṃ sarvaśabdā vagāhanam
tanmātraliṅgagrahaṇaṃ sarvaprāṇinidarśanam
yatākāmopalabdhiś ca yathākāma vinirgamaḥ
kāmānurūpanirmāṇaṃ vaśitvaṃ priyadarśanam
saṃsāradarśanaṃ caiva mānasaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam
chedanaṃ tāḍanaṃ bandhaṃ saṃsāraparivartanam
sarvabhūtaprasādaś ca mṛtyukālajayas tathā
prājāpatyamidaṃ proktamāha ṅkārikamuttamam
akāraṇajagatsṛṣṭistathānugraha eva ca
asādṛśyamidaṃ vyaktaṃ nirmāṇaṃ ca pṛthakpṛthak
etāvattattvamityuktaṃ prādhānyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padam
brahmaṇā tadguṇaṃ śakyaṃ vettumanyairna śakyate
vidyate tatparaṃ śaivaṃ viṣṇunā nāvagamyate
asaṃkhyeyaguṇaṃ śuddhaṃ ko jānīyācchivātmakam
vyutthāne siddhayaścaitā hyupasargāś ca kīrtitāḥ
nāśātiśayatāṃ jñātvā viṣayeṣu bhayeṣu ca
vaitṛṣṇyaṃ puruṣe khyātaṃ guṇavaitṛṣṇyamucyate
vairāgyeṇaiva saṃtyājyāḥ siddhayaścaupasargikāḥ
athavānugrahārthaṃ ca līlārthaṃ vā tadā muniḥ
kvacidbhūmiṃ parityajya hyākāśe krīḍate śriyā
udgirecca kvacidvedān sūkṣmānarthān samāsataḥ
kvaciddaṇḍakabandhaṃ tu kuryādhdandhaṃ sahasraśaḥ
mṛgapakṣisamūhasya rutajñānaṃ ca vindati
bahunātra kimuktena vijñānāni sahasraśaḥ
abhyāsenaiva vijñānaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca sthiraṃ bhavet
tejorūpāṇi sarvāṇi sarvaṃ paśyati yogavit
devabiṃbānyanekāni vimānāni sahasraśaḥ
paśyati brahmaviṣṇvīndrayamāgnivaruṇādikān
grahanakṣatratārāś ca bhuvanāni sahasraśaḥ
pātālatalasaṃsthāś ca samādhisthaḥ sa paśyati
prasādāmṛtapūrṇena sattvapātrasthitena tu
tamo nihatya puruṣaḥ paśyāti hyatmanīśvaram
tasya prasādāddharmaś ca aiśvaryaṃ jñānameva ca
vairāgyamapavargaś ca nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
na śakyo vistaro vaktuṃ varṣāṇāmayutairapi
yoge pāśupate niṣṭhā sthātavyaṃ ca munīśvarāḥ
iti śrīliṅgapurāṇe pūrvabhāge yogāntarāyakathanaṃ nāma navamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
satāṃ jitātmanāṃ sākṣāddvijātīnāṃ dvijottamāḥ
dharmajñānāṃ ca sādhūnāmācāryāṇāṃ śivatmanām
dayāvatāṃ dvijaśreṣṭhās tathā caiva tapasvinām
saṃnyāsināṃ viraktānāṃ jñānināṃ vaśagātmanām
dānināṃ caiva dāntānāṃ trayāṇāṃ satyavadinām
alubdhānāṃ sayogānāṃ śruti smṛtividāṃ dvijāḥ
śrautasmārtāviruddhānāṃ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ
sāyujyaṃ brahmaṇo yāti tena saṃtaḥ pracakṣate
daśātmake ye viṣaye sādhane cāṣṭalakṣaṇe
na krudhyānti na hṛṣyanti jitātmānastu te smṛtāḥ
sāmānyeṣu ca dravyeṣu tathā vaiśeṣikeṣu ca
brahmakṣatraviśe yasmādyuktāstasmāddvijātayaḥ
varṇāśrameṣu yuktasya svargādisukhakāriṇaḥ
vidyāyāḥ sādhanātsādhubrahmacārī gurorhitaḥ
kriyāṇāṃ sādhanāccaiva gṛhasthaḥ sādhurucyate
sādhanāttapaso 'raṇye sādhurvaikhānasaḥ smṛtaḥ
yatamāno yatiḥ sādhuḥ smṛto yogasya sādhanāt
evamāśramadharmāṇāṃ sādhanātsādhavaḥ smṛtāḥ
kuśalakuśalaṃ karma dharmādharmāviti smṛtau
dhāraṇārthe mahān hyeṣa dharmaśabdaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
atreṣṭaprāpako dharma ācāryairupadiśyate
adharmaścāniṣṭaphalo hyācaryairupadiśyate
vṛddhāścālolupāścaiva ātmavanto hyadāṃbhikāḥ
samyagvinītā ṛjavastānācāryanpracakṣate
ācinoti ca śāstrārthānācāryastena cocyate
vijñeyaṃ śravaṇācchrautaṃ smaraṇātsmārtamucyate
ijyā vedātmakaṃ śrautaṃ smārtaṃ varṇāśramātmakam
dṛṣṭvānurūpamarthaṃ yaḥ pṛṣṭo naivāpi gūhati
yathādṛṣṭapravādastu satyaṃ laiṅge 'tra paṭhyate
ahiṃsā sarvataḥ śāntistapa ityabhidhīyate
ātmavatsarvabhūteṣu yo hitāyāhitāya ca
vartate tvasakṛddhṛttiḥ kṛtsnā hyeṣā dayā smṛtā
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ dravyaṃ nyāyenaivāgataṃ kramāt
tattadguṇavate deyaṃ dātustaddānalakṣaṇam
kāruṇyātsarvabhūtebhyaḥ saṃvibhāgastu madhyamaḥ
śrutismṛtibhyāṃ vihito dharmo varṇāśramātmakaḥ
śiṣṭācārāviruddhaś ca sa dharmaḥ sādhurucyate
māyākarmaphalatyāgī śivātmā parir ketataḥ
ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā indriyāṇīha yasya vai
anudvigno hyaniṣṭeṣu tatheṣṭānnābhinandati
prītitāpaviṣādebhyo vinivṛttirviraktatā
saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇāṃ nyāsaḥ kṛtānāmakṛtaiḥ saha
kuśalakuśalānāṃ tu prahāṇaṃ nyāsa ucyate
cetanācetanānyatva vijñānaṃ jñānamucyate
evaṃ tu jñānayuktasya śraddhāyuktasya śaṅkaraḥ
prasīdati na saṃdeho dharmaścāyaṃ dvijottamāḥ
jñānamadhyāpanaṃ homo dhyānaṃ yajñastapaḥ śrutam
cāndrāyaṇasahasraiś ca prājāpatyaśatais tathā
māsopavāsai ścānyairvā bhaktirmunivarottamāḥ
bhaktānāṃ darśanādeva nṛṇāṃ svargādayo dvijāḥ
brahmaviṣṇusuredrāṇāṃ tathānyeṣāmapi sthitiḥ
bhavena ca tathā proktaṃ saṃprekṣyomāṃ pinākinā
devyai devena madhuraṃ vārāṇasyāṃ purā dvijāḥ
avimukte samāsīnā rudreṇa paramātmanā
rudrāṇī rudramāhedaṃ labdhvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm
śrīdevyuvāca
kena vaśyo mahādeva pūjyo dṛśyastvamīśvaraḥ
sūta uvāca
niśamya vacanaṃ tasyās tathā hyālokya vārvatīm
āha bālendutilakaḥ pūrṇenduvadanāṃ hasan
smṛtvātha menayā patnyā girergāṃ kathitāṃ purā
devī labdhā purī ramyā tvayā yatpraṣṭumarhasi
sthānārthaṃ kathitaṃ mātrā vismṛteha vilāsini
purā pitāmahenāpi pṛṣṭaḥ praśravatāṃ vare
yathā tvayādya vai pṛṣṭo draṣṭuṃ brahmatmakaṃ tvaham
śvete śvetena varṇena dṛṣṭvā kalpe tu māṃ śubhe
sadyojātaṃ tathā rakte raktaṃ vāmaṃ pitāmahaḥ
pīte tatpuruṣaṃ pītamaghore kṛṣṇamīśvaram
īśānaṃ viśvarūpākhyo viśvarūpaṃ tadāha mām
pitāmaha uvāca
dṛṣṭo mayā tvaṃ gāyatryā devadeva maheśvara
kena vaśyo mahādeva dhyeyaḥ kutra ghṛṇānidhe
dṛśyaḥ pūjyas tathā devyā vaktumarhasi śaṅkara
śrībhagavānuvāca
dhyeyo liṅge tvayā dṛṣṭe viṣṇunā payasāṃ nidhau
pūjyaḥ pañcāsyarūpeṇa pavitraiḥ pañcabhi rdvijaiḥ
bhavabhaktyādya dṛṣṭohaṃ tvayāṇḍaja jagadguro
sopi māmāha bhāvārthaṃ dattaṃ tasmai mayā purā
bhāvaṃ bhāvena deveśi dṛṣṭavānmāṃ hṛdīśvaram
tasmāttu śraddhayā vaśyo dṛśyaḥ śreṣṭhagireḥ sute
pūjyo liṅge na saṃdehaḥ sarvadā śraddhayā dvijaiḥ
śraddhā dharmaḥ paraḥ sūkṣmāḥ śraddhā jñānaṃ hutaṃ tapaḥ
śraddhā svargaś ca mokṣaś ca dṛśyohaṃ śraddhayā sadā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge bhaktibhāvakathanaṃ nāma daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ vai dṛṣṭavānbrahmā sadyojātaṃ maheśvaram
vāmadevaṃ mahātmānaṃ purāṇa puruṣottamam
sūta uvāca
ekonatriṃśakaḥ kalpo vijñeyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ
tasmiṃstatparamaṃ dhyānaṃ dhyāyato brahmaṇastadā
utpannastu śikhāyuktaḥ kumāraḥ śvetalohitaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā puruṣaṃ śrīmānbrahmā vai viśvatomukhaḥ
hṛdi kṛtvā mahātmānaṃ brahmarūpiṇamīśvaram
dhyānayogātparaṃ jñātvā vavande devamīśvaram
tatosya pārśvataḥ śvetāḥ prādurbhūtā mahāyaśāḥ
śiṣyāste vai mahātmāno yaistadbrahma sadāvṛtam
tasyāgre śvetavarṇābhaḥ śveto nāma mahāmuniḥ
prapannāḥ parayā bhaktyā gṛṇanto brahma śāśvatam
tasmādviśveśvaraṃ devaṃ ye prapadyanti vai dvijāḥ
prāṇāyāmaparā bhūtvā brahmatatpara mānasāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sadyojātamāhatmyaṃ nāmaikādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
dhyāyataḥ putrakāmasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
prādurbhūto mahātejāḥ kumāro raktabhūṣaṇaḥ
sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmānaṃ kumāraṃ raktavāsasam
paraṃ dhyānaṃ samāśritya bubudhe devamīśvaram
tathā stuto mahādevo brahmaṇā parameśvaraḥ
dhyāyatā putrakāmena yasmāttehaṃ pitāmaha
dṛṣṭaḥ paramayā bhaktyā stutaś ca brahmapurvakam
vetsyase māṃ prasaṃkhyātaṃ lokadhātāramīśvaram
tatastasya mahātmānaścatvāraste kumārakāḥ
saṃbabhūvurmahātmāno viśuddhā brahmavarcasaḥ
virajāś ca vibāhuś ca viśoko viśvabhāvanaḥ
brahmaṇyā brahmaṇastulyā vīrā adhyavasāyinaḥ
raktāṃbaradharāḥ sarve raktamālyānulepanāḥ
raktakuṅkumaliptāṅgā raktabhasmānulepanāḥ
gṛṇantaś ca mahātmāno brahma tadvāmadaivikam
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā
dharmopadeśamakhilaṃ kṛtvā te brahmaṇaḥ priyāḥ
yepi cānye dvijaśreṣṭhā yuñjānā vāmamīśvaram
prapaśyanti mahādevaṃ tadbhaktāsta tparāyaṇāḥ
te sarve pāpanirmuktā vimalā brahmacāriṇaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vāmadevamāhātmyaṃ nāma dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
ekatriṃśattamaḥ kalpaḥ pītavāsā iti smṛtaḥ
brahma yatra mahābhāgaḥ pītavāsā babhūva ha
dhyāyataḥ putrakāmasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
prādurbhūto mahātejāḥ kumāraḥ pītavastradhṛk
pītagandhānuliptāṅgaḥ pītamālyāṃbaro yuvā
hemayajñopavītaś ca pītoṣṇīṣo mahābhujaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā dhyānasaṃyukto brahmā lokamaheśvaram
manasā lokadhātāraṃ prapede śaraṇaṃ vibhum
tato dhyānagatastatra brahmā māheśvarīṃ varām
gāṃ viśvarūpāṃ dadṛśe maheśvaramukhāccyutām
catuṣpadāṃ caturvaktrāṃ caturhastāṃ catuḥstanīm
caturnetrāṃ catuḥśṛṅgīṃ caturdaṃṣṭrāṃ caturmakhīm
dvātriṃśadguṇasaṃyuktāmī śvarīṃ sarvatomukhām
sa tāṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātejā mahādevīṃ maheśvarīm
matīḥ smṛtirbuddhiriti gāyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
ehyehīti mahādevī sātiṣṭhatprāñjalirvibhum
viśvamāvṛtya yogena jagatsarvaṃ vaśīkuru
atha tāmāha deveśo rudrāṇī tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
brāhmaṇānāṃ hitārthāya paramārthā bhaviṣyasi
tathaināṃ putrakāmasya dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
pradadau devadeveśaḥ catuṣpādāṃ jagadguruḥ
tatastāṃ dhyānayogena viditvā parameśvarīm
gāyatrīṃ tu tato raudrīṃ dhyātvā brahmanuyantritaḥ
ityetāṃ vaidīkīṃ vidya raudrīṃ gāyatrimīritām
japitvā tu mahādevīṃ brahmā lokanamaskṛtām
aiśvaryaṃ jñānasaṃpattiṃ vairāgyaṃ ca dadau prabhuḥ
tatosya pārśvato divyāḥ pradurbhūtāḥ kumārakāḥ
pītamālyāṃbaradharāḥ pītasraganulepanāḥ
pītābhoṣṇīṣaśirasaḥ pītāsyāḥ pītamūrdhajāḥ
yogātmānasta pohlādāḥ brāhmaṇānāṃ hitaiṣiṇaḥ
dharmayogabalopetā munīnāṃ dīrghasattraṇām
upadiśya mahāyogaṃ praviṣṭāste maheśvaram
anyopi niyatātmāno dhyānayuktā jitendriyāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge tatpuruṣamāhātmyaṃ nāma trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
sraṣṭukāmaḥ prajā brahmā cintayāmāsa duḥkhitaḥ
kṛṣṇaḥ samabhava dvarṇo dhyāyataḥ paramoṣṭhinaḥ
athāpaśyanmahātejāḥ prādurbhūtaṃ kumārakam
kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ mahāvīryaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā
kṛṣṇāṃbaradharoṣṇīṣaṃ kṛṣṇayajñopavītinam
kṛṣṇena maulinā yuktāṃ kṛṣṇasraganulepanam
sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmānamaghoraṃ ghoravikramam
vavande devadeveśamadbhutaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalam
prāṇāyāmaparaḥ śrīmān hṛdi kṛtvā maheśvaram
tathā vai dhyāyamānasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
athāsya pārśvataḥ kṛṣṇāḥ kṛṣṇasraganulepanāḥ
catvārastu mahātmānaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ kumārakāḥ
kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇaśikhaścaiva kṛṣṇāsyaḥ kṛṣṇavastradhṛk
upāsitvā mahāyogaṃ śiṣyebhyaḥ pradaduḥ punaḥ
yogena yogasaṃ pannāḥ praviśya manasā śivam
amalaṃ nirguṇaṃ syānaṃ praviṣṭā viśvamīśvaram
evametena yogena yepi cānye manīṣiṇaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge aghorotpattivarṇanaṃ nāma caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
tatastāsmin gate kalpe kṛṣṇavarṇe bhayānake
tuṣṭāva devadeveśaṃ brahmā taṃ brahmarūpiṇam
anugṛhya tatastuṣṭo brahmāṇa mavadaddharaḥ
anenaiva tu rūpeṇa saṃharāmi na saṃśayaḥ
brahmahatyādikān ghorāṃstathānyānapi pātakān
hīnāṃścaiva mahābhāga tathaiva vividhānyapi
mānasāniṃ sutīkṣṇāni vācikāni pitāmaha
kāyikāni sumiśrāṇi tathā prāsaṃgikāni ca
buddhipūrvaṃ kṛtānyeva sahajāgantukāni ca
mātṛdehotthatānyevaṃ pitṛdehe ca pātakam
saṃharāmi na saṃdehaḥ sarvaṃ pātakajaṃ vibho
caturguṇaṃ buddhipūrve krodhādaṣṭaguṇaṃ smṛtam
vīrahā lakṣamātreṇa bhrūṇahā koṭimabhyaset
mātṛhā niyutaṃ japtvā śuddhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
goghnaścaiva kṛtaghnaś ca strīghnaḥ pāpayuto naraḥ
asnātāśī sahasreṇa ajapī ca tathā dvijaḥ
ahutāśī sahasreṇa adātā ca viśuddhyāti
brāhmaṇasvāpahartā ca svarṇasteyī narādhamaḥ
niyutaṃ mānasaṃ japtvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
gurutalpa rato vāpi mātṛghno vā narādhamaḥ
saṃparkātpāpināṃ pāpaṃ tatsamaṃ paribhāṣitam
saṃsargātpātakī lakṣaṃ japedvai mānasaṃ dhiyā
upāṃśu yaccaturdhā vai vācikaṃ cāṣṭadhā japet
pātakādardhameva syādupapātakināṃ smṛtam
tadardhaṃ kevale pāpe nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
kṛtvā caja gurutalpaṃ pāpakṛdbrāhmaṇo yadi
rudragāyatriyā grāhyaṃ gomūtraṃ kāpilaṃ dvijāḥ
tejosi śuktamityājyaṃ kāpilaṃ saṃharedbudhaḥ
āpyāyasveti ca kṣīraṃ dadhiktāvṇeti cāharet
gavyaṃ dadhi navaṃ sākṣātkāpilaṃ vai pitāmaha
ekasthāṃ hemapātre vā kṛtvāghoreṇa rājate
tāmre vā padmapātre vā pālāśe vā dale śubhe
sakūrcaṃ sarvaratnāḍhyaṃ kṣiptvā tatraiva kāñcanam
japellakṣamaghorākhyaṃ hutvā caiva ghṛtādibhiḥ
hutvāvoreṇa deveśaṃ snātvāghoreṇa vai dvijāḥ
aṣṭadroṇaghṛtenaiva snāpya paścādviśodhya ca
ahorātroṣitaḥ snātaḥ pibetkūrcaṃ śivāgrataḥ
evaṃ kṛtvā kṛtaghno 'pi brahmahā bhrūṇahā tathā
vīrahā guruvātī ca mitraviśvāsaghātakaḥ
madyapo vṛṣalīsaktaḥ paradāravidharṣakaḥ
brahmasvahā tathā goghno mātṛhā pitṛhā tathā
tathānyāni ca pāpāni mānasāni dvijo yadi
vācikāni tathānyāni kāyikāni sahasraśaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge 'ghoreśamahātmyaṃ pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
athānyo brahmaṇaḥ kalpo vartate munipuṅgavāḥ
viśvarūpa iti khyāto nāmataḥ paramādbhutaḥ
vinivṛtte tu saṃhāre punaḥ sṛṣṭe carācare
brahmaṇaḥ putrakāmasya dhyāyataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
prādurbhūtā mahānādā viśvarūpā sarasvatī
viśvamālyāṃbaradharā viśvayajñopavītinī
viśvoṣṇīṣā viśvagandhā viśvamātā mahoṣṭhikā
tathāvidhaṃ sa bhagavānīśānaṃ parameśvaram
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
atha taṃ manasā dhyātvā yuktātmā vai pitāmahaḥ
vavande devamīśānaṃ sarveśaṃ sarvagaṃ prabhum
namostu sarvavidyānāmīśāna parameśvara
namostu sarvabhūtānāmīśāna vṛṣavāhana
oṅkāramūrte deveśa sadyojāta namonamaḥ
vāmadeva namastubhyaṃ jyeṣṭhāya varadāya ca
namo vikaraṇāyaiva kālavarṇāya varṇine
balāya balināṃ nityaṃ sadā vikaraṇāya te
sarvabhūteśvareśāya bhūtānāṃ damanāya ca
vāmadevāya vāmāya namastubhyaṃ mahātmane
jyeṣṭhāya caiva śreṣṭhāya rudrāya varadāya ca
śrāvayedvā dvijān śrāddhe sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
evaṃ dhyānagataṃ tatra praṇamantaṃ pitāmaham
uvāca bhagavānīśaḥ prītohaṃ te kimicchasi
tatastu praṇato bhūtvā vāgviśuddhaṃ maheśvaram
uvāca bhagavān rudraṃ prītaṃ prītena cetasā
yadidaṃ viśvarūpaṃ te viśvagauḥ śreyasīśvarī
kaiṣā bhagavatī devī catuṣpādā caturmukhī
catuḥśṛṅgī caturvattrā caturdaṃṣṭrā catuḥstanī
caturhastā caturnetrā viśvarūpā kathaṃ smṛtā
kiṃnāmagotrā kasyeyaṃ kiṃvīryā cāpi karmataḥ
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ
prāha devavṛṣaṃ brahmā brahmāṇaṃ cātmasaṃbhavam
rahasyaṃ sarvamantrāṇāṃ pāvanaṃ puṣṭivardhanam
śṛṇuṣvaitatparaṃ guhyamādisarge yathā tathā
tvattaḥ parataraṃ deva viṣṇunā tatpadaṃ śubham
vaikuṇṭhena viśuddhena mama vāmāṅgajena vā
śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāmatītā ye svayaṃbhuvaḥ
purastāttava deveśa tacchṛṇuṣva mahāmate
māṇḍavyagotrastapasā mama putratvamāgataḥ
tvayi yogaṃ ca sāṃkhyaṃ ca tapovidyāvidhikriyāḥ
ṛtaṃ satyaṃ dayā brahma ahiṃsā sanmatiḥ kṣamā
dhyānaṃ dhyeyaṃ damaḥ śāntirvidyāvidyā matirdhṛtiḥ
kāntirnitiḥ prathā medhā lajjā dṛṣṭiḥ sarasvatī
tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ kriyā caiva prasādaś ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ
dvātriṃśatsuguṇā hyeṣā dvātriṃśākṣarasaṃjñayā
viṣṇorbhagavataścāpi tathānyeṣāmapi prabho
saiṣā bhagavatī devī matprasūtiḥ pratiṣṭhitā
caturmukhī jagadyoniḥ prakṛtirgauḥ pratiṣṭhitā
gaurī māyā ca vidyā ca kṛṣṇā haimavatīti ca
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiścaiva yāmāhustattvacintakāḥ
ajāmekāṃ lohitāṃ śuklakṛṣṇāṃ viśvaprajāṃ sṛjamānāṃ sarūpām
ajohaṃ māṃ viddhi tāṃ viśvarūpaṃ gāyatrīṃ gāṃ viśvarūpāṃ hi buddhyā
tataś ca pārśvagā devyāḥ sarvarūpakumārakāḥ
jaṭī muṇḍī śikhaṇḍi ca ardhamuṇḍaś ca jajñire
dharmopadeśamakhilaṃ kṛtvā yogamayaṃ dṛḍham
śiṣṭāś ca niyatātmānaḥ praviṣṭā rudramīśvaram
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge īśānamāhātmyakathanaṃ nāma ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ sadyādīnāṃ samudbhavaḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ liṅgamabhūlliṅge samabhyarcyaḥ sa śaṅkaraḥ
kiṃ liṅgaṃ kas tathā liṅgī sūta vaktumihārhasi
romaharṣaṇa uvāca
evaṃ devāś ca ṛṣayaḥ praṇipatya pitāmaham
apṛcchan bhagavāṃlliṅgaṃ kathamāsīditi svayam
kiṃ liṅgaṃ kas tathā liṅgī sopyāha ca pitāmahaḥ
pitāmaha uvāca
pradhānaṃ liṅgamākhyātaṃ liṅgī ca parameśvaraḥ
rakṣārthamaṃbudhau mahyaṃ viṣṇostvāsītsurottamāḥ
sthitikāle tadā pūrṇe tataḥ pratyāhṛte tathā
śuṣke ca sthāvare sarve tvanāvṛṣṭyā ca sarvaśaḥ
paśavo mānuṣā vṛkṣāḥ piśācāḥ piśitāśanāḥ
gandharvādyāḥ krameṇaiva nirdagdhā bhānubhānubhiḥ
suṣvāpāṃbhasi yogātmā nirmalo nirupaplavaḥ
sahasraśīrṣā viśvātmā sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt
hiraṇyagarbho rajasā tamasā śaṅkaraḥ svayam
kālātmā kālānābhastu śuklaḥ kṛṣṇastu nirguṇaḥ
nārāyaṇo mahābāhuḥ sarvātmā sadasanmayaḥ
tathābhūtamahaṃ dṛṣṭvā śayānaṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam
tadā hastaprahāreṇa tīvreṇa sa dṛḍhena tu
prabuddhohīyaśayanātsamāsīnaḥ kṣaṇaṃ vaśī
māmagre saṃsthitaṃ bhāsādhyāsito bhagavān hariḥ
āha cotthāya bhagavān hasanmāṃ madhuraṃ sakṛt
svāgataṃsvāgataṃ vatsa pitāmaha mahādyute
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā smitapūrvaṃ surarṣabhāḥ
bhāṣase vatsavatseti sargasaṃhārakāraṇam
māmihāntaḥ smitaṃ kṛtvā guruḥ śiṣyamivānagha
kartāraṃ jagatāṃ sākṣātprakṛteś ca pravartakam
sanātanamajaṃ viṣṇuṃ viriñciṃ viśvasaṃbhavam
viśvātmānaṃ vidhātāraṃ dhātāraṃ paṅkajekṣaṇam
bhartā hartā bhavānaṅgādavatīrṇo mamāvyayāt
vismṛto 'si jagannāthaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam
puruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam
viṣṇumacyutamīśānaṃ viśvasya prabhavodbhavam
tavāparādho nāstyatra mama māyākṛtaṃ tvidam
ahameva paraṃ jyotiḥ paramātmā tvahaṃ vibhuḥ
yadyadṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ sarvaṃ jagatyasmiṃścarācaram
mayā sṛṣṭaṃ purāvyaktaṃ caturviśatikaṃ svayam
nityāntā hyaṇavo baddhāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ krodhodbhavādayaḥ
prasādāddhi bhavānaṇḍānyanekānīha līlayā
sṛṣṭā buddhirmayā tasyāmahaṅkārastridhā tataḥ
tanmātrāpañcakaṃ tasmānmanaḥ ṣaṣṭhendriyāṇi ca
ākāśādīni bhūtāni bhautikāni ca līlayā
āvayoścābhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam
vivādaśamanārthaṃ hi prabodhārthaṃ ca bhāsvaram
jvālāmālāsahasrāḍhyaṃ kālānalaśatopamam
mohitaṃ prāha māmatra parikṣāvo 'gnisaṃbhavam
evaṃ vyāhṛtya viśvātmā svarūpamakarottadā
vārāhamahamapyāśu haṃsatvaṃ prāptavānsurāḥ
tadāprabhṛti māmāhurṃhasaṃ haṃso virāḍiti
haṃsahaṃseti yo brūyānmāṃ haṃsaḥ sa bhaviṣyati
suśveto hyanalākṣaś ca viśvataḥ pakṣasaṃyutaḥ
manonilajavo bhūtvā gatohaṃ cordhvataḥ surāḥ
nārāyaṇopi viśvātmā nīlāñjanacayopamam
daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ śatayojanamāyatam
meruparvatavarṣmāṇaṃ gauratīkṣṇāgradaṃṣṭriṇam
kālādityasamābhāsaṃ dīrghaghoṇaṃ mahāsvaram
hrasvapādaṃ vicitrāṅgaṃ jaitraṃ dṛḍhamanaupamam
vārāhamasitaṃ rūpamāsthāya gatavānadhaḥ
evaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu tvaranviṣṇuradhogataḥ
nāpaśyadalpamapyasya mūlaṃ liṅgasya sūkaraḥ
śrānto hyadṛṣṭvā tasyāntamahaṅkārādadhogataḥ
tathaiva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śrāntaḥ saṃtrastalocanaḥ
samāgato mayā sārdhaṃ praṇipatya mahāmanāḥ
māyayā mohitaḥ śaṃbhostasthau saṃvignamānasaḥ
pṛṣṭhataḥ pārśvataścaiva cāgrataḥ parameśvaram
praṇipatya mayā sārdhaṃ sasmāra kimidaṃ tviti
tadā samabhavattatra nādo vai śabdalakṣaṇaḥ
omomiti suraśreṣṭhāḥ suvyaktaḥ plutalakṣaṇaḥ
liṅgasya dakṣiṇe bhāge tadāpaśyatsanātanam
ādyavarṇamakāraṃ tu ukāraṃ cottare tataḥ
makāraṃ madhyataścaiva nādāntaṃ tasya comiti
sūryamaṇḍalavaddṛṣṭvā varṇamādyaṃ tu dakṣiṇe
uttare pāvakaprakhyamukāraṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
śītāṃśumaṇḍalaprakhyaṃ makāraṃ madhyamaṃ tathā
turīyātītamamṛtaṃ niṣkalaṃ nirupaplavam
nirdvandvaṃ kevalaṃ śūnyaṃ bāhyābhyantaravarjitam
ādimadhyāntarahitamānandasyāpi kāraṇam
mātrāstisrastvardhamātraṃ nādākhyaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam
ṛgyajuḥsāmavedā vai mātrārūpeṇa mādhavaḥ
vedaśabdebhya eveśaṃ viśvātmānamacintayat
tadābhavadṛṣirveda ṛṣeḥ sāratamaṃ śubham
tenaiva ṛṣiṇā viṣṇurjñātavānparameśvaram
aprāpya taṃ nivartante vācyastvekākṣareṇa saḥ
ekākṣareṇa tadvācyamṛtaṃ paramakāraṇam
ekākṣarādakārākhyo bhagavānkanakāṇḍajaḥ
ekākṣarādukārākhyo hariḥ paramakāraṇam
ekākṣarānmakārākhyo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
makārākhyo vibhurvījī hyakāro bījamucyate
ukārākhyo hariryoniḥ pradhānapuruṣeśvaraḥ
bījī ca bījaṃ tadyonirnādākhyaś ca maheśvaraḥ
bījī vibhajya cātmānaṃ svecchāyā tu vyavasthitaḥ
asya liṅgādabhūdbījamakāro bījīnaḥ prabhoḥ
sauvarṇamabhavaccāṇḍam āveṣṭyādyaṃ tadakṣaram
anekābdaṃ tathā cāpsu divyamaṇḍaṃ vyavasthitam
aṇḍamapsu sthitaṃ sākṣādādyākhyeneśvareṇa tu
tasyāṇḍasya śubhaṃ haimaṃ kapālaṃ corddhvasaṃsthitam
jajñe yaddyaustadaparaṃ pṛthivī pañcalakṣaṇā
tasmādaṇḍodbhavo jajñe tvakārākhyaścaturmukhaḥ
sa sraṣṭā sarvalokānāṃ sa eva trividhaḥ prabhuḥ
evamomomiti proktamityāhuryajuṣāṃ varāḥ
yajuṣāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā ṛcaḥ sāmāni sādaram
tato vijñāya deveśaṃ yathāvacchrutisaṃbhavaiḥ
āvayoḥ stutisaṃtuṣṭo liṅge tasminnirañjanaḥ
divyaṃ śabdamayaṃ rūpamāsthāya prahasan sthitaḥ
akārastasya mūrddhā tu lalāṭaṃ dīrghamucyate
ikāro dakṣiṇaṃ netramīkāro vāmalocanam
ukāro dakṣiṇaṃ śrotramūkāro vāmamucyate
ṛkāro dakṣiṇaṃ tasya kapolaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
vāmaṃ kapolam ṝkāro ḷ ḹ nāsāpuṭe ubhe
ekāramoṣṭhamūrddhvaś ca ekārastvadharo vibhoḥ
kādipañcākṣarāṇyasya pañca hastāni dakṣiṇe
cādipañcākṣarāṇyevaṃ pañca hastāni vāmataḥ
ṭādipañcākṣaraṃ pādastādipañcākṣaraṃ tathā
pakāramudaraṃ tasya phakāraḥ pārśvamucyate
bakāro vāmapārśvaṃ vai bhakāraṃ skandhamasya tat
makāraṃ hṛdayaṃ śaṃbhormahādevasya yogīnaḥ
yakārādisakārāntaṃ vibhorvai sapta dhātavaḥ
hakāra ātmarūpaṃ vai kṣakāraḥ krodha ucyate
taṃ dṛṣṭvā umayā sārddhaṃ bhagavantaṃ maheśvaram
praṇamya bhagavān viṣṇuḥ punaścāpaśyadūrddhvataḥ
oṅkāraprabhavaṃ mantraṃ kalāpañcaka saṃyutam
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ subhāṣṭatriṃśadakṣaram
gāyatrīprabhavaṃ mantraṃ haritaṃ vaśyakārakam
caturviṃśativarṇāḍhyaṃ catuṣkalamanuttamam
atharvamasitaṃ mantraṃ kalāṣṭakasamāyutam
yajurvedasamāyuktaṃ pañcatriṃśacchubhākṣaram
kalāṣṭakasamāyuktaṃ suśvetaṃ śāntikaṃ tathā
trayodaśakalāyuktaṃ bālādyaiḥ saha lohitam
samodbhavaṃ jagatyādyaṃ vṛddhisaṃhārakāraṇam
varṇāḥ ṣaḍadhikāḥ ṣaṣṭirasya mantravarasya tu
pañca mantrāṃs tathā labdhvā jajāpa bhagavān hariḥ
atha dṛṣṭvā kalāvarṇamṛgyajuḥsāmarūpiṇam
īśānamīśamukuṭaṃ puruṣāsyaṃ purātanam
aghorahṛdayaṃ hṛdyaṃ vāmaguhyaṃ sadāśivam
sadyaḥ pādaṃ mahādevaṃ mahābhogīndrabhūṣaṇam
viśvataḥ pādavadanaṃ viśvatokṣikaraṃ śivam
tuṣṭāva punariṣṭābhir vāgbhir varadamaśviram
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge liṅgodbhavo nāma saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
ekākṣarāya rudrāya akārāyātmarūpiṇe
ukārāyādidevāya vidyādehāya vai namaḥ
tṛtīyāya makārāya śivāya paramātmane
sūryāgnisomavarṇāya yajamānāya vai namaḥ
agnaye rudrarūpāya rudrāṇāṃ pataye namaḥ
śivāya śivamantrāya sadyojātāya vedhase
vāmāya vāmadevāya varadāyāmṛtāya te
aghorāyātighorāya sadyojātāya raṃhase
īśānāya śmaśānāya ativegāya vegine
namostu śrutipādāya ūrdhvaliṅgāya liṅgine
hemaliṅgāya hemāya vāriliṅgāya cāṃbhase
śivāya śiva liṅgāya vyāpine vyomavyāpine
pṛthivyai cāntarikṣāya pṛthivīvyāpine namaḥ
anantāya virupāya anantānāmayāya ca
śāśvatāya variṣṭhāya vārigarbhāya yogine
acetanāya cintyāya cetanāyāsahāriṇe
arūpāya surūpāya anaṅgāyāṅgahāriṇe
śvetāya śvetavarṇāya tuhinādricarāya ca
suśvetāya suvaktrāya namaḥ śvetaśikhāya ca
śvetāsyāya mahāsyāya namaste śvetalohita
sutārāya viśiṣṭāya namo dundubhine hara
śatarūpa virupāya namaḥ ketumate sadā
ṛddhiśokaviśokāya pinākāya kapardine
vipāśāya supāśāya namaste pāśanāśine
suhotrāya haviṣyāya subrahmaṇyāya sūriṇe
kaṅkāya kaṅkarūpāya kaṅkaṇīkṛtapannaga
sanatkumāra sāraṅgamāraṇāya mahātmane
lokākṣiṇe tridhāmāya namo virajase sadā
śaṅkhapālāya śaṅkhāya rajase tamase namaḥ
suvāhāya vivāhāya vivādavaradāya ca
namaḥ śivāya rudrāya pradhānāya namonamaḥ
saṃsārāya namastubhyaṃ namaḥ saṃsārahetave
mokṣāya mokṣarūpāya mokṣakartre namonamaḥ
ātmane ṛṣaye tubhyaṃ svāmine viṣṇave namaḥ
namo bhagavate tubhyaṃ nāgānāṃ pataye namaḥ
oṅkārāya namastubhyaṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ
sarvāya ca namastubhyaṃ namo nārāyaṇāya ca
mahādevāya devānāmīśvarāya namo namaḥ
śarvāya ca namastubhyaṃ satyāya śamanāya ca
brahmaṇe caiva bhūtānāṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ
mahātmane namastubhyaṃ prajñārūpāya vai namaḥ
citaye citirūpāya smṛtirūpāya vai namaḥ
jñānāya jñānagamyāya namaste saṃvide sadā
śikharāya namastubhyaṃ nalikaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ
ardhanārīśarīrāya avyaktāya namonamaḥ
ekādaśavibhedāya sthāṇave te namaḥ sadā
namaḥ somāya sūryāya bhavāya bhavahāriṇe
yaśaskarāya devāya śaṅkarāyeśvarāya ca
namoṃbikādhipataye umāyāḥ pataye namaḥ
nīlakeśāya vittāya śitikaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ
kapardine namastubhyaṃ nāgāṅgābharaṇāya ca
vṛṣārūḍhāya sarvasya hartre kartre namonamaḥ
vīrarāmātirāmāya rāmanāthāya te vibho
namo rājā dhirājāya rājñāmadhigatāya te
namaḥ pālādhipataye pālāśākṛntate namaḥ
namaḥ keyūrabhūṣāya gopate te namonamaḥ
namaḥ śrīkaṇṭhanāthāya namo likucapāṇaye
sāraṅgāya namastubhyaṃ rājahaṃsāya te namaḥ
sarpakuṇḍalamālāya kaṭisūtrīkṛtāhine
virarāmeti saṃstutvā brahmaṇā sahito hariḥ
etatstotravaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam
yaḥ paṭhecchrāvayedvāpi brāhmaṇān vedapāragān
tasmājjapetpaṭhennityaṃ śrāvayedbrāhmaṇāñchubhān
sarvapāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ viṣṇunā paribhāṣitam
iti liṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge viṣṇustavo nāmāṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
paśyatāṃ māṃ mahādevaṃ bhayaṃ sarvaṃ vimucyatām
yuvāṃ prasūtau gātrābhyāṃ mama pūrvaṃ mahābalau
ayaṃ me dakṣiṇe pārśve brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
vāme pārśve ca me viṣṇurviśvātmā hṛdayodbhavaḥ
evamuktvā tu taṃ viṣṇuṃ karābhyāṃ parameśvaraḥ
pasparśa subhagābhyāṃ tu kṛpayā tu kṛpānidhiḥ
tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanasā praṇipatya maheśvaram
prāha nārāyaṇo nāthaṃ liṅgasthaṃ liṅgavarjitam
devaḥ pradattavān devāḥ svātmanyavyabhicāriṇīm
brahmaṇe viṣṇave caiva śraddhāṃ śītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ
jānubhyāmavanīṃ gatvā punarnārāyaṇaḥ svayam
praṇipatya ca viśveśaṃ prāha mandataraṃ vaśī
ihāgato bhavān yasmādvivādaśamanāya nau
praṇipatya sthitaṃ mūrdhnā kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ smayan
śrīmahādeva uvāca
pralayasthitisargāṇāṃ kartā tvaṃ dharaṇīpate
tridhā bhinno hyahaṃ viṣṇo brahmaviṣṇubhavākhyayā
sargarakṣālayaguṇairniṣkalaḥ parameśvaraḥ
saṃmohaṃ tyaja bho viṣṇo pālayainaṃ pitāmaham
tadā drakṣyasi māṃ caivaṃ sopi drakṣyati padmajaḥ
tadāprabhṛti lokeṣu liṅgārccā supratiṣṭhitā
liṅgavedī mahādevī liṅgaṃ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ
sa yāti śivatāṃ vipro nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge viṣṇuprabodho nāmaikonāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
bhavaṃ ca dṛṣṭavāṃstena brahmaṇā puruṣottamaḥ
etatsarvaṃ viśeṣeṇa sāṃprataṃ vaktumarhasi
sūta uvāca
āsīdekārṇavaṃ ghoramavibhāgaṃ tamomayam
jīmūtāṃbho 'mbujākṣaś ca kiriṭī śrīpatirhariḥ
nārāyaṇamukhodgīrṇasarvātmā puruṣottamaḥ
aṣṭabāhurmahāvakṣā lokānāṃ yonirucyate
evaṃ tatra śayanena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
ātmārāmeṇa krīḍārthaṃ līlayākliṣṭakarmaṇā
śatayojanavistīrṇaṃ taruṇādityasannibham
vajradaṇḍaṃ mahotsedhaṃ nābhyāṃ sṛṣṭaṃ tu puṣkaram
tasyaivaṃ krīḍamānasya samīpaṃ devamīḍhuṣaḥ
caturvaktro viśālākṣaḥ samāgamya yadṛcchayā
krīḍamānaṃ ca padmena dṛṣṭvā brahmā śubhekṣaṇam
provāca ko bhavāñchete hyāśrito mavyamaṃbhasām
atha tasyācyutaḥ śrutvā brahmaṇastu śubhaṃ vacaḥ
dyaurantarikṣaṃ bhūścaiva paraṃ padamahaṃ bhuvaḥ
tamevamuktvā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ punarathābravīt
kastvaṃ khalu samāyātaḥ samīpaṃ bhagavānkutaḥ
kva vā bhūyaś ca gantavyaṃ kaś ca vā te pratiśrayaḥ
evaṃ bruvantaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ pratyuvāca pitāmahaḥ
māyayā mohitaḥ śaṃbhoravijñāya janārdanam
māyayā mohitaṃ devamavijñātaṃ mahātmanaḥ
yathā bhavāṃstathaivāhamādikartā prajāpatiḥ
savismayaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā brahmaṇo lokatantriṇaḥ
anujñātaś ca te nātha vaikuṇṭho viśvasaṃbhavaḥ
kautūhalānmahāyogī praviṣṭo brahmaṇo mukham
imānaṣṭādaśa dvīpānsasamudrān saparvatān
praviśya sumahātejāścāturvarṇyasamākulān
brahmaṇastūdare dṛṣṭvā sarvānviṣṇurmahābhujaḥ
aṭitvā vividhāṃllokān viṣṇurnānāvidhāśrayān
tato varṣasahasrānte nāntaṃ hi dadṛśo yadā
nārāyaṇo jagaddhātā pitāmahamathābravīt
bhagavānādiraṅkaś ca madhyaṃ kālo diśo nabhaḥ
evamuktvābravīdbhūyaḥ pitāmahamidaṃ hariḥ
bhagavānevamevāhaṃ śāśvataṃ hi mamodaram
tataḥ prāhlādinīṃ vāṇīṃ śrutvā tasyābhinandya ca
śrīpaterudaraṃ bhūyaḥ praviveśa pitāmahaḥ
paryaṭitvā tu devasya dadṛśe 'ntaṃ na vai hareḥ
jñātvā gatiṃ tasya pitāmahasya dvārāṇi sarvāṇi pidhāya viṣṇuḥ
tato dvārāṇi sarvāṇi pihitāni samīkṣya vai
sūkṣmaṃ kṛtvātmano rūpaṃ nābhyāṃ dvāramavindata
padmasūtrānusārema cānvapaśyatpitāmahaḥ
ujjahārātmano rūpaṃ puṣkarāccaturānanaḥ
brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavāñjagadyoniḥ pitāmahaḥ
kutopyaparimeyātmā bhūtānāṃ prabhuriśvaraḥ
śūlapāṇirmahādevo hemavīrāṃbaracchadaḥ
śīghraṃ vikramatastasya padbhyamākraāntapīḍitāḥ
udbhūtāstūrṇamākāśe pṛthulāstoyabindavaḥ
atyuṣṇaścātiśatiś ca vāyustatra vavau punaḥ
taddṛṣṭvā mahadāścaryaṃ brahmā viṣṇumabhāṣata
abbindavaś ca śītoṣṇāḥ kaṃpayantyaṃbujaṃ bhṛśam
etanme saṃśayaṃ brūhi kiṃ vā tvanyaccikīrṣasi
śrutvāpratimakarmā hi bhagavānasurāntakṛt
kiṃ nu khalvatra me nābhyāṃ bhūtamanyatkṛtālayam
kiṃ mayā ca kṛtaṃ deva yanmāṃ priyamanuttamam
bhāṣase puruṣaśreṣṭha kimarthaṃ brūhi tattvataḥ
evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ deveśaṃ lokayātrānugaṃ tataḥ
pratyuvācāmbujābhākṣaṃ brahmā vedanidhiḥ prabhuḥ
yo 'sau tavodaraṃ pūrvaṃ praviṣṭo 'haṃ tvadicchayā
yathā mamodare lokāḥ sarve dṛṣṭāstvayā prabho
tathaiva dṛṣṭāḥ kārtsnyena mayā lokāstavodare
tvayā matsarabhāvena māṃ vaśīkartumicchatā
āśu dvārāṇi sarvāṇi pihitāni samantataḥ
mābhūtte manaso 'lpopi vyāghāto 'yaṃ kathañcana
ityeṣānugatirviṣṇo kāryāṇāmaupasarpiṇī
yanmayānantaraṃ kāryaṃ brūhi kiṃ karavāṇyaham
tataḥ paramameyātmā hiraṇyakaśipo ripuḥ
anavadyāṃ priyāmiṣṭāṃ śivāṃ vāṇīṃ pitāmahāt
na hyevamīdṛśaṃ kāryaṃ mayādhyavasitaṃ tava
tvāṃ bodhayitukāmena krīḍāpūrvaṃ yadṛcchayā
āśu dvārāṇi sarvāṇi ghāṭitāni mayātmanaḥ
na te 'nyathāvagantavyaṃ mānyaḥ pūjyaś ca me bhavān
sarvaṃ marṣaya kalyāṇa yanmayāpakṛtaṃ tava
nāhaṃ bhavantaṃ śaknomi soḍhuṃ tejomayaṃ gurum
sa tvaṃ ca no mahāyogī tvamīḍyaḥ praṇavātmakaḥ
adyaprabhṛti sarveśaḥ śvetoṣṇīṣavibhūṣitaḥ
tataḥ sa bhagavāndevo varaṃ datvā kirīṭine
evaṃ bhavatu cetyuktvā prītātmā gatamatsaraḥ
pratyā saṃnamathāyāntaṃ bālārkābhaṃ mahānanam
bhavamatyadbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā nārāyaṇamathābravīt
aprameyo mahāvaktro daṃṣṭrī dhvastaśiroruhaḥ
daśabāhustrisūlāṅko nayanairviśvataḥ sthitaḥ
lokaprabhuḥ svayaṃ sākṣādvikṛto muñjamekhalī
kaḥ khalveṣa pumān viṣṇo tejorāśirmahādyutiḥ
vyāpya sarvā diśo dyāṃ ca ita evābhivartate
vegena mahatākāśepyutthitāś ca jalaśayāḥ
ghrāṇajena ca vātena kaṃpyamānaṃ tvayā saha
samāgato bhavānīśo hyanādiścāntakṛtprabhuḥ
bhavānahaṃ ca stotreṇa upatiṣṭhāva godhvajam
tataḥ kruddho 'mbujābhākṣaṃ brahmā provāca keśavam
brahmāṇaṃ lokakartāraṃ māṃ na vetsi sanātanam
tasya tatkrodhajaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā harirabhāṣata
mā maivaṃ vada kalyāṇa parivādaṃ mahātmanaḥ
heturasyātha jagataḥ purāṇapuruṣo 'vyayaḥ
bījī khalveṣa bījānāṃ jyotirekaḥ prakāśate
bālakrīḍanakairdevaḥ krīḍate śaṅkaraḥ svayam
mama caitāni nāmāni nityaṃ prasavadharmiṇaḥ
yaḥ kaḥ sa iti duḥkhārtairdṛśyate yatibhiḥ śivaḥ
eṣa bījī bhavānbījamahaṃ yoniḥ sanātanaḥ
sa evamukto viśvātmā brahmā viṣṇumapṛcchata
bhavān yonirahaṃ bījaṃ kathaṃ bījī maheśvaraḥ
jñātvā ca vividhotpattiṃ brahmaṇo lokatantriṇaḥ
imaṃ paramasādṛśyaṃ praśramabhyavadaddhariḥ
mahataḥ paramaṃ dhāma śivamadhyātmināṃ padam
mama yonau samāyuktaṃ tadbījaṃ kālaparyayāt
hiraṇmayamakūpāre yonyāmaṇḍamajāyata
śatāni daśavarṣāṇā maṇḍamapsu pratiṣṭhitam
kapālamekaṃ dyaurjajñe kapālamaparaṃ kṣitiḥ
ātārārkedunakṣatraṃ śūnyaṃ lokamavekṣya ca
priyadarśanāstu yatayo yatīnāṃ pūrvajās tava
bhuvanānalasaṃkāśāḥ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇāḥ
śrīmānsanatkumāraś ca ṛbhuścaivordhva retasau
utpannāḥ samakālaṃ te buddhyātīndriyadarśanāḥ
utpannāḥ pratibhātmāno jagatāṃ sthitihetavaḥ
nārapsyante ca karmāṇi tāpatrayavivarjitāḥ
alpasaukhyaṃ bahukleśaṃ jarāśokasamanvitām
jīvanaṃ maraṇaṃ caiva saṃbhavaś ca punaḥ punaḥ
viditvā cāgamaṃ sarvamavaśyaṃ bhavitavyatām
ṛbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca dṛṣṭvā tava vaśe sthitau
trayastu trīn guṇān hitvā cātmajāḥ sanakādayaḥ
tatasteṣu pravṛtteṣu sanakādiṣu vai triṣu
bhaviṣyasi vimūḍhastvaṃ māyayā śaṅkarasya tu
evaṃ kalpe tu vaivṛtte saṃjñā naśyati te 'nagha
kalpe śeṣāṇi bhūtāni sūkṣmāṇi pārthivāni ca
sarveṣāṃ hyaiśvarī māyā jāgṛtiḥ samudāhṛtā
jñātvā ceśvarasadbhāvaṃ jñātvā māmaṃbujekṣaṇam
mahādevaṃ mahābhūtaṃ bhūtānāṃ varadaṃ prabhum
tvāṃ ca māṃ caiva saṃkruddho niḥśvāsānnirdahedayam
evaṃ jñātvā mahāyogamabhyuttiṣṭhanmahābalam
ahaṃ tvāmagrataḥ kṛtvā stoṣyāmyanalasaprabham
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge brahmaprabodhanaṃ nāma viṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
brahmaṇamagrataḥ kṛtvā tataḥ sa garuḍadhvajaḥ
viṣṇuruvāca
namaḥ kṣetrādhipataye bījine śūline namaḥ
sumeṇḍhrāyārcyameṇḍhrāya daṇḍine rūkṣaretase
namo jyeṣṭhāya śreṣṭhāya pūrvāya prathamāya ca
namo mānyāya pūjyāya sadyojātāya vai namaḥ
gahvarāya ghaṭeśāya vyomacīrāṃbarāya ca
namaste hyasmadādīnāṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
vedānāṃ prabhave caiva smṛtīnāṃ prabhave namaḥ
prabhave karmadānānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
namo dhruvanibaddhānāmṛṣīṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
ṛkṣāṇāṃ prabhave tubhyaṃ grahāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
vaidyutāśanimeghānāṃ garjitaprabhave namaḥ
mahodadhīnāṃ prabhave dvīpānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
adrīṇāṃ prabhave caiva varṣāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
namo nadīnāṃ prabhave nadānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
mahauṣadhīnāṃ prabhave vṛkṣāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
dharmavṛkṣāya dharmāya sthitīnāṃ prabhave namaḥ
namo rasānāṃ prabhave ratnānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
kṣaṇānāṃ prabhave caiva lavānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
ahorātrārdhamāsānāṃ māsānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
ṛtūnāṃ prabhave tubhyaṃ saṃkhyāyāḥ prabhave namaḥ
namaḥ purāṇaprabhave sargāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
kalpodayanibandhānāṃ vātānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
mantrāṇāṃ prabhave tubhyaṃ mantrādhipataye namaḥ
pitṝṇāṃ pataye caiva paśūnāṃ pataye namaḥ
vāgvṛṣāya namastubhyaṃ purāṇavṛṣabhāya ca
namaḥ paśūnāṃ pataye govṛṣendradhvajāya ca
prajāpatīnāṃ pataye siddhīnāṃ pataye namaḥ
daityadānavasaṃghānāṃ rakṣasāṃ pataye namaḥ
gandharvāṇāṃ ca pataye yakṣāṇāṃ pataye namaḥ
garuḍoragasarpāṇāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ pataye namaḥ
sarvaguhyapiśācānāṃ guhyādhipataye namaḥ
gokarṇāya ca goptre ca śaṅkukarṇāya vai namaḥ
varāhāyāprameyāya ṛkṣāya virajāya ca
namo surāṇāṃ pataye gaṇānāṃ pataye namaḥ
aṃbhasāṃ pataye caiva ojasāṃ pataye namaḥ
namostu lakṣmīpataye śrīpāya kṣitipāya ca
balābalasamūhāya akṣobhyakṣobhaṇāya ca
dīptaśṛṅgaikaśṛṅgāya vṛṣabhāya kakudmine
atītāya bhaviṣyāya vartamānāya vai namaḥ
suvarcase ca vīryāya śūrāya hyajitāya ca
varadāya vareṇyāya puruṣāya mahātmane
namo bhavāya devāya ijyāya yājakāya ca
pratyudīrṇāya dīptāya tattvāyātiguṇāya ca
namaḥ pāśāya śastrāya namastvābharaṇāya ca
hutāya upahūtāya prahutaprāśitāya ca
namostviṣṭāya pūrtāya agniṣṭomadvijāya ca
sadasyāya namaścaiva dakṣiṇāvabhṛthāya ca
ahiṃsāyāpralobhāya paśumantrauṣadhāya ca
namaḥ puṣṭipradānāya suśīlāya suśīline
atītāya bhaviṣyāya vartamānāya te namaḥ
suvarcase ca vīryāya śūrāya hyajitāya ca
varadāya vareṇyāya puruṣāya mahātmane
namaścendriyapatrāṇāṃ lelihānāya sragviṇe
viśvāya viśvarūpāya viśvataḥ śirase namaḥ
sarvataḥ pāṇipādāya rudrāyāpratimāya ca
namaḥ siddhāya medhyāya iṣṭāyejyāparāya ca
suvīrāya sughorāya akṣobhyakṣobhaṇāya ca
suprajāya sumedhāya dīptāya bhāskarāya ca
namo buddhāya śuddhāya vistṛtāya matāya ca
namaḥ sthūlāya sūkṣmāya dṛśyādṛśyāya sarvaśaḥ
namaste vakrakeśāya ūruvakṣaḥśikhāya ca
virupākṣāya liṅgāya piṅgalāya mahaujase
vṛṣṭighnāya namaścaiva namaḥ saumyekṣaṇāya ca
namo dhūmrāya śvetāya kṛṣṇāya lohitāya ca
piśitāya piśaṅgāya pītāya ca niṣaṅgiṇe
namaste saviśeṣāya nirviśeṣāya vai namaḥ
nama ījyāya pūjyāya upajīvyāya vai namaḥ
namaḥ kṣemyāya vṛddhāya vatsalāya namonamaḥ
namo bhūtāya satyāya satyāsatyāya vai namaḥ
mahāsaṃdhyābhravarṇāya cārudīptāya dīkṣiṇe
apramāṇāya sarvāya avyayāyāmarāya ca
namo rūpāya gandhāya śāśvatāyākṣatāya ca
purastādbṛṃhate caiva vibhrāntāya kṛtāya ca
tarkyātarkyaśarīrāya baline raṃhasāya ca
sikatyāya pravāhyāya sthitāya prasṛtāya ca
sumedhase kulālāya namaste śaśikhaṇḍine
cekitānāya tuṣṭāya namaste nihitāya ca
namaḥ kṣāntāya dāntāya vajrasaṃhananāya ca
rakṣoghnāya viṣaghnāya śitikaṇṭhordhvamanyave
lelihāya kṛtāntāya tigmāyudhadharāya ca
anāmayāya sarvāya mahākālāya vai namaḥ
praṇavapraṇaveśāya bhaganetrāntakāya ca
mṛgavyādhāya dakṣāya dakṣayajñāntakāya ca
sarvabhūtātmabhūtāya sarveśāti śayāya ca
pūṣadantavināśāya bhaganetrāntakāya ca
kāmadāya variṣṭhāya kāmāṅgadahanāya ca
daityānāmantakeśāya daityāktandakarāya ca
himaghnāya ca tīkṣṇāya ārdracarmadharāya ca
śmaśānaratinityāya namostūlmukadhārīṇe
namaste prāṇapālāya muṇḍamālādharāya ca
prahīṇaśokairvividhairbhūtaiḥ parivṛtāya ca
naranārīśarīrāya devyāḥ priyakarāya ca
jaṭine muṇḍine caiva vyālayajñopavītine
namo 'stu nṛtyaśīlāya upanṛtyapriyāya ca
manyave gītaśīlāya munibhir gāyate namaḥ
kaṭakaṭāya tigmāya apriyāya priyāya ca
vibhīṣaṇāya bhīṣmāya bhagapramathanāya ca
siddhasaṃghānugītāya mahābhāgāya vai namaḥ
namo muktāṭṭahāsāya kṣveḍitāsphoṭitāya ca
namo mṛḍāya śvasate dhāvate 'dhiṣṭhite namaḥ
valgate krīḍate caiva laṃbodaraśarīriṇe
namo 'kṛtyāya kṛtyāya muṇḍāya kīkaṭāya ca
nama unmattadehāya kiṅkiṇīkāya vai namaḥ
namo vikṛtaveṣāya krūrāyāmarṣaṇāya ca
aprameyāya goptre ca dīptāyānirguṇāya ca
vāmapriyāya vāmāya cūḍāmaṇidharāya ca
sarveṣāṃ siddhiyogānāmadhiṣṭhānaṃ tavodaram
madhye 'ntarikṣaṃ vistīrṇaṃ tārāgaṇavibhūṣitam
svāteḥ patha ivābhāti śrīmān hārastavorasi
diśo daśabhujāstubhyaṃ keyūrāṅgadabhūṣitāḥ
vistīrṇapariṇāhaś ca nīlāñjanacayopamaḥ
kaṇṭhaste śobhate śrīmān hemasūtravibhūṣitaḥ
daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ durdharṣamanaupamyaṃ mukhaṃ tathā
padmamālākṛtoṣṇīṣaṃ śiro dyauḥ śobhate 'dhikam
akṣarāntaraniṣpandādguṇānetānvidurbudhāḥ
pureśayo guhāvāsī khecaro rajanīcaraḥ
hayaśīrṣā payodhātā vidhātā bhūtabhāvanaḥ
bṛhadratho bhīmakarmā bṛhatkīrtirdhanañjayaḥ
ghaṇṭāpriyo dhvajī chatrī pinākī dhvajivipatiḥ
kavacī pāṭṭiśī khaṅgī dhanurhastaḥ paraśvadhī
tvāṃ prasādya purāsmābhir dviṣanto nihatā yudhi
āgniḥ sadārṇavāṃbhastvaṃ pibannapi na tṛpyase
krodhākāraḥ prasannātmā kāmadaḥ kāmagaḥ priyaḥ
brahmacāri cāgādhaś ca brahmaṇyaḥ śiṣṭapūjitaḥ
devānām akṣayaḥ kośas tvayā yajñaḥ prakalpitaḥ
bhavānīśo 'nādimāṃstvaṃ ca sarvalokānāṃ tvaṃ brahmakartādisargaḥ
sāṃkhyāḥ prakṛteḥ paramaṃ tvāṃ viditvā kṣīṇadhyānāstvāmamṛtyuṃ viśanti
yogāś ca tvāṃ dhyāyino nityasiddhaṃ jñātamvā yogān saṃtyajante punastān
kīrtitaṃ tava māhātmyam apārasya mahātmanaḥ
sūta uvāca
śrāvayedvā dvijān vidvān śṛṇuyādvā samāhitaḥ
aśvamedhāyutaṃ kṛtvā yatphalaṃ tadavāpnuyāt
pāpācāro 'pi yo martyaḥ śṛṇuyācchivasannidhau
śrāddhe vā daivike kārye yajñe vāvabhṛthāntike
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge brahmaviṣṇustutirnāmaikaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
atyantāvanatau dṛṣṭvā madhupiṅgāyatekṣaṇaḥ
umāpatirvirūpākṣo dakṣayajñavināśanaḥ
pinākī khaṇḍaparaśuḥ suprītastu trilocanaḥ
tataḥ sa bhagavāndevaḥ śrutvā vāgamṛtaṃ tayoḥ
jānannapi mahādevaḥ kriḍāpūrvamathābravīt
sametāvaṃbujābhakṣāv asmin ghore mahāplave
tāvūcaturmahātmānau saṃnirīkṣya parasparam
vibho rudra mahāmāya icchayā vāṃ kṛtau tvayā
uvāca bhagavāndevo madhuraṃ ślakṣṇayā girā
bho bho hiraṇya garbha tvāṃ tvāṃ ca kṛṣṇa bravīmyaham
prīto 'hamanayā bhaktyā śāśvatākṣarayuktayā
yuvābhyāṃ kiṃ dadāmyadya varāṇāṃ varamīpsitam
athovāca mahābhāgo viṣṇurbhavamidaṃ vacaḥ
tadevaṃ svasti te vatsa gamiṣyāmyaṃbujekṣaṇa
evamuktvā tu bhagavān brahmāṇaṃ cāpi śaṅkaraḥ
anugṛhyāspṛśaddevo brahmāṇaṃ parameśvaraḥ
karābhyāṃ suśubhābhyāṃ ca prāha hṛṣṭataraḥ svayam
evamuktvā tu bhagavāṃstatontardhānamīśvaraḥ
avāpya saṃjñāṃ govindāt padmayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ
prajāḥ sraṣṭumanāścakre tapa ugraṃ pitāmahaḥ
tato dīrgheṇa kālena duḥkhātkrodho hyajāyata
krodhāviṣṭasya netrābhyāṃ prāpatannaśrubindavaḥ
mahābhāgā mahāsattvāḥ svastikairapyalaṅkṛtāḥ
prakīrṇakeśāḥ sarpāste prādurbhūtā mahā viṣāḥ
sarpāṃstānagrajāndṛṣṭvā brahmātmānamanindayat
lokavaināśikī jajñe ādā veve prajā mama
tasya tīvrābhavanmūrcchā krodhāmarṣasamudbhavā
mūrcchābhiparitāpena jahau prāṇānprajāpatiḥ
tasyāpratimavīryasya dehātkāruṇyapūrvakam
ye rudrāste khalu prāṇā ye prāṇāste tadātmakāḥ
prāṇāḥ prāṇavatāṃ jñeyāḥ sarvabhūteṣvavasthitāḥ
prāṇāṃstasya dadau bhūyastriśūlī nīlalohitaḥ
praṇamya saṃsthito 'paśyadgāyatryā viśvamīśvaram
sarvalokamayaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā stutvā pitāmahaḥ
uvāca vacanaṃ śarvaṃ sadyāditvaṃ kathaṃ vibho
iti śrīlaṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge rudrotpattivarṇanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
brahmarūpī prabodhārthaṃ brahmāṇaṃ prāha sasmitam
śvetoṣṇīṣaḥ śvetamālyaḥ śvetāṃbaradharaḥ sitaḥ
śvetāsthiḥ śvetaromā ca śvetāsṛk śvetalohitaḥ
matprasūtā ca deveśī śvetāṅgā śvetalohitā
śvetavarṇā tadā hyāsīdgāyatrī brahmasaṃjñitā
vijñātaḥ svena tapasā sadyojātatvamāgataḥ
tasmādguhyatvamāpannaṃ ye vetsyāṃ ti dvijātayaḥ
yadā caiva punastvāsīllohito nāma nāma taḥ
tadā lohitamāṃsāsthilohitakṣīrasaṃbhavā
lohitākṣī stanavatī gāyatrī gauḥ prakīrtitā
latrāpi ca mahāsattva tvayāhaṃ niyatātmanā
tataś ca vāmadeveti khyātiṃ yāto 'smi bhūtale
ye cāpi vāmadeva tvāṃ jñāsyantīha dvijātayaḥ
matprasūtā ca deveśī pītāṅgī pītalohitā
pītavarṇā tadā hyasīdgāyatrī brahmasaṃjñitā
yasmādahaṃ tairvijñāto yogatatparamānasaiḥ
tatra tatpuruṣatvena vijñāto 'haṃ tvayā punaḥ
ye māṃ rudraṃ ca rudrāṇīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram
vetsyanti tapasā yuktā vimalā brahmasaṃgatāḥ
yadāhaṃ punarevāsaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇo bhayānakaḥ
matkṛtena ca varṇena saṃkalpaḥ kṛṣṇa ucyate
tatrāhaṃ kālasaṃkāśaḥ kālo lokaprakālakaḥ
matprasūtā ca gāyatrī kṛṣṇāṅgī kṛṣṇalohitā
kṛṣṇarūpā ca deveśa tadāsīdbrahmasaṃjñitā
teṣāmaghoraḥ śāntaś ca bhaviṣyāmyahamavyayaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ tvayā jñātaḥ parameṇa samādhinā
viśvarūpā ca saṃvṛttā gāyatrī lokadhāriṇī
tasmin viśvatvam āpannaṃ ye māṃ vetsyānti bhūtale
teṣāṃ śivaś ca saumyaś ca bhaviṣyāmi sadaiva hi
yasmācca viśvarūpo vai kalpo 'yaṃ samudāhṛtaḥ
viśvarūpā tathā ceyaṃ sāvitrī samudāhṛtā
sarvarūpā tathā ceme saṃvṛttā mama putrakāḥ
catvāraste mayā khyātāḥ putra vai lokasaṃmatāḥ
yasmācca sarvavaṇatvaṃ prajānāṃ ca bhaviṣyati
mokṣo dharmastathārthaś ca kāmaśceti catuṣṭayam
bhūtagrāmāś ca catvāra āśramāś ca tathaiva ca
dharmasya pādāścatvāraścatvāro mama putrakāḥ
aṣṭākṣarasthito lokaḥ sthānesthāne tadakṣaram
bhūrbhuvaḥ svarmahaścaiva pādāścatvāra eva ca
viṣṇulokaḥ smṛtaṃ sthānaṃ punarāvṛttidurlabham
rudralokaḥ smṛtastasmātpadaṃ tadyogināṃ śubham
nirmamā nirahaṅkārāḥ kāmakrodha vivirjitāḥ
drakṣyanti taddvijā yuktā dhyānatatparamānasāḥ
yasmāccatuṣpadā hyeṣā tvayā dṛṣṭā sarasvatī
pādāntaṃ viṣṇu lokaṃ vai kaumāraṃ śāntamuttamam
aumaṃ māheśvaraṃ caiva tasmāddṛṣṭā catuṣpadā
tasmāttu paśavaḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti catuṣpadāḥ
tataścaiṣāṃ bhaviṣyanti catvāraste payodharāḥ
jīvaḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ brahman punaḥ pītastanāḥ smṛtāḥ
tasmātsomamayaṃ caiva amṛtaṃ jīvasaṃjñitam
catuṣpādā bhaviṣyanti śvetatvaṃ cāsya tena tat
yasmāccaiva kriyā bhūtvā dvipadā ca maheśvarī
dṛṣṭā punastathaivaiṣā sāvitrī lokabhāvinī
tasmācca dvipadāḥ sarve dvistanāś ca narāḥ śubhāḥ
tasmācceyamajā bhūtvā sarvavarṇā maheśvarī
yā vai dṛṣṭā mahāsattvā sarvabhūtadharā tvayā
tasmācca viśvarūpatvaṃ prajānāṃ vai bhaviṣyati
ajaścaiva mahātejā viśvarūpo bhaviṣyati
amogharetāḥ sarvatra mukhe cāsya hutāśanaḥ
tasmātsarvagato medhyaḥ puśurūpī hutāśanaḥ
tapasā bhīvitātmāno ye māṃ drakṣyanti vai dvijāḥ
rajastamobhyāṃ nirmuktāstyaktvā mānuṣyakaṃ vapuḥ
praṇamya prayato bhūtvā punarāha pitāmahaḥ
viśvātmānaṃ hi sarvaṃ tvāṃ gāyatryāstava ceśvara
tasmādvidvān hi viśvatvamasyāścāsya mahātmanaḥ
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ vacanād brahyaṇaḥ prabhoḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge trayoviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
punaḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ rudramāha prajāpatiḥ
viśvarūpa mahābhāga kasminkāle maheśvara
kasyāṃ vā yugasaṃbhūtyāṃ drakṣyantīha dvajatayaḥ
namaste vai mahādeva śakyo draṣṭuṃ dvijātibhiḥ
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śarvaḥ saṃprekṣya taṃ puraḥ
smayanprāha mahādevo ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃ bhavaḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
na śakyaṃ mānavairdraṣṭumṛte dhyānādahaṃ tviha
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya ca
tadāhaṃ brāhmaṇārthāya kalau tasmin yugāntike
bhaviṣyāmi śikhāyuktaḥ śveto nāma mahāmuniḥ
tatra śiṣyāḥ śikhāyuktā bhaviṣyanti tadā mama
śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaścaiva śvetāsyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ
catvārastu mahātmāno brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
tataste brahmabhūyiṣṭhā dṛṣṭvā brahmagatiṃ parām
matsa mīpaṃ gamiṣyanti dhyānayogaparāyaṇāḥ
tadā lokahitārthāya sutāro nāma nāmataḥ
bhaviṣyāmi kalau tasmin śiṣyānugrahakāmyayā
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā nāmataḥ parikīrtitāḥ
dundubhiḥ śatarūpaś ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃstadā
prāpya yogaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ sthāpya brahma ca bhūtale
tṛtīye dvāpare caiva yadā vyāsastu bhārgavaḥ
vikośaś ca vikeśaś ca vipāśaḥ śāpanāśanaḥ
caturthe dvāpare caiva yadā vyāso 'ṅgirāḥ smṛtaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi suhotro nāma nāmataḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrāścatvāropi tapodhanāḥ
dvijaśreṣṭhā bhaviṣyanti yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ
prāpya yogagatiṃ sūkṣmāṃ vimalā dagdha kilbiṣāḥ
tadā cāpi bhaviṣyāmi kaṅko nāma mahātapāḥ
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ yogātmaikakalāgatiḥ
catvārastu mahābhāgā vimalāḥ śuddhayonayaḥ
śiṣyā mama bhaviṣyanti yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ
vibhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca nirmamā nirahaṅkṛtāḥ
parīvarte punaḥ ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyurvyāso yadā vibhuḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi logākṣīrnāma nāmataḥ
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā yogātmānā dṛḍhavratāḥ
bhaviṣyanti mahābhāgāścatvāro lokasaṃmatāḥ
sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṅkhapādraja eva ca
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve vai dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
vibhunāmā mahātejāḥ prathitaḥ pūrvajanmani
jaigīṣavyo vibhuḥ khyātaḥ sarveṣāṃ yogināṃ varaḥ
sārasvataś ca meghaś ca meghavāhaḥ suvāhanaḥ
tepi tenaiva mārgeṇa dhyānayogaparāyaṇāḥ
gamiṣyānti mahātmāno rudralokaṃ nirāmayam
vasiṣṭhaścāṣṭame vyāsaḥ parīvarte bhaviṣyati
yadā tadā bhaviṣyāmi nāmnāhaṃ dadhivāhanaḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ
bhaviṣyanti mahāyogā yeṣāṃ nāsti samo bhuvī
kapilaścāsuriścaiva tathā pañcaśikho muniḥ
bāṣkalaś ca mahāyogī dharmātmāno mahaujasaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ jñānino dagdhākilbiṣāḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi ṛṣabho nāma nāmataḥ
parāśaraś ca gargaś ca bhārgavāṅgirasau tadā
bhaviṣyanti mahātmāno brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
sarve tapobalotkṛṣṭāḥ śāpānugrahakovidāḥ
daśame dvāpare vyāsaḥ tripādvai nāma nāmataḥ
yadā bhaviṣyate viprastadāhaṃ bhavitā muniḥ
nāmnā bhṛgostu śikharaṃ prathitaṃ devapūjitam
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti dṛḍhavratāḥ
yogātmāno mahātmānastapoyogasamanvitāḥ
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti tapasā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi gaṅgādvāre kalau tathā
ugro nāma mahātejāḥ sarvalokeṣu viśrutaḥ
laṃbodaraś ca laṃbākṣo laṃbakeśaḥ pralaṃbakaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te
dvādaśe parivarte tu śatatejā yadā muniḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi kalāviha yugāntike
haitukaṃ vanamāsādya atrirnāmnā pariśrutaḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhasmasnānānulepanāḥ
bhaviṣyanti mahāyogā rudralokaparāyaṇāḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te
dharmo nārāyaṇo nāma vyāsastu bhavitā yadā
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi vālirnāma mahāmuniḥ
sudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vāsiṣṭho virajāsta thā
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te
tatrāpi punarevāhaṃ bhaviṣyāmi yugāntike
vaṃśe tvaṅgirasāṃ śreṣṭhe gautamo nāma nāmataḥ
bhaviṣyati mahāpuṇyaṃ gautamaṃ nāma tadvanam
atrirdevasadaścaiva śravaṇo 'tha śraviṣṭhakaḥ
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve yogasamanvitāḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi nāmnā vedaśirā dvijaḥ
bhaviṣyati mahāvīryaṃ vedaśīrṣaś ca parvataḥ
himavatpṛṣṭhamāsādya sarasvatyāṃ nagottame
kuṇiś ca kuṇibāhuś ca kuśarīraḥ kunetra kaḥ
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve te dyūrdhvaretasaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ
vyāso yuge ṣoḍaśe tu yadā devo bhaviṣyati
tatra yogapradānāya bhaktānāṃ ca yatātmanām
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi gokarṇo nāma nāmataḥ
bhaviṣyati supuṇyaṃ ca gokarṇaṃ nāma tadvanam
kāśyapo hyuśanāścaiva cyavanotha bṛhaspatiḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ gantāro rudrameva hi
yadā bhaviṣyati vyāso nāmnā devakṛtaṃ jayaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi guhāvāsīti nāmataḥ
siddhakṣetraṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati mahālayam
tatrāpi mama te putrā yogajñā brahmavādinaḥ
bhaviṣyanti mahātmāno nirmamā nirahaṅkṛtāḥ
teṣāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu śiṣyāṇāṃ dhyānayoginām
bhaviṣyanti tadā kāle sarve te dhyānayuñjakāḥ
yogābhyāsaratāścaiva hṛdi kṛtvā maheśvaram
mahālaye padaṃ nyastaṃ dṛṣṭvā yānti śivaṃ padam
dhyāne manaḥ samādhāya vimalāḥ śuddhabuddhayaḥ
mama prasādādyāsyanti rudralokaṃ gatajvarāḥ
gatvā mahālayaṃ puṇyaṃ dṛṣṭvā māheśvaraṃ padam
tīrṇastārayate janturdaśa pūrvāndaśottarān
ātmānamekaviṃśaṃ tu tārayitvā mahālaye
mama prasādādyāsyanti rudralokaṃ gatajvarāḥ
tadā ṛtañjayo nāma vyāsastu bhavitā muniḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi śikhaṇḍi nāma nāmataḥ
śikhaṇḍino vanaṃ cāpi yatra siddhaniṣevitam
vācaśravā ṛcakiś ca śyāvāśvaś ca yatīśvaraḥ
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve te vedapāragāḥ
prapya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃvṛtāḥ
vyāsastu bhavitā nāmnā bharadvājo mahāmuniḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi jaṭāmālī ca nāmataḥ
hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo lokākṣī kuthumis tathā
īśvarā yogadharmāṇaḥ sarve te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi aṭṭahāsastu nāmataḥ
aṭṭahāsapriyāścaiva bhaviṣyanti tadā narāḥ
tatraiva himavatpṛṣṭhe aṭṭahāso mahāgiriḥ
devadānavaṃ yakṣendrasiddhyacāraṇasevitaḥ
yogātmāno mahātmāno dhyāyino niyatavratāḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ
vācaśravāḥ smṛto vyāso yadā sa ṛṣisattamaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi dāruko nāma nāmataḥ
tasmādbhaviṣyate puṇyaṃ devadāru vanaṃ śubham
plakṣo dārbhāyaṇiścaiva ketumān gautamas tathā
yogātmāno mahātmāno niyatā ūrdhvaretasaḥ
naiṣṭhikaṃ vratamāsthāya rudralokāya te gatāḥ
dvāviṃśe parivarte tu vyāsaḥ śuṣmāyaṇo yadā
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi vārāṇasyāṃ mahāmuniḥ
nāmnā vai lāṅgalī bhīmo yatra devāḥ savāsavāḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti sudhārmikāḥ
bhallavī madhupiṅgaś ca śvetaketuḥ kuśas tathā
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ tepi dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ
vimalā brahmabhūyiṣṭhā rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ
parivarte trayoviṃśe tṛṇabinduryadā muniḥ
vyāso hi bhavitā brahmaṃstadāhaṃ bhavitā punaḥ
śveto nāma mahākāyo muniputrastu dhārmikaḥ
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā bhaviṣyanti tapasvinaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gataḥ
parivarte caturviṃśe vyāso ṛkṣo yadā vibho
śūlī nāma mahāyogī naimiṣe devavandite
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ
śālihotrogniveśaś ca yuva nāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ
te 'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ
pañcaviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate
vāsiṣṭhastu yadā vyāsaḥ śaktirnāmnā bhaviṣyati
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi daṇḍī muṇḍīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaś ca kubhāṇḍaś ca pravāhakaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogamamṛtatvāya te gatāḥ
paḍviṃśe parivarte tu yadā vyāsaḥ parā śaraḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi sahiṣṇurnāma nāmataḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti sudhārmikāḥ
ulūko vidyutaścaiva śaṃbūko hyāśvalāyanaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yugaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ
jātūkarṇyo yadā vyāso bhaviṣyati tapodhanaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi somaśarmā dvijottamaḥ
prabhāsatīrthamāsādya yogātmā yogaviśrutaḥ
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ
akṣapādaḥ kumāraś ca ulūko vatsa eva ca
yogātmāno mahātmāno vimalāḥ śuddhabuddhayaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ tato gatāḥ
aṣṭāviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate
parāśarasutaḥ śrīmān viṣṇurlokapitāmahaḥ
