rāmasya ca tathānyeṣāṃ vṛṣṇīnāmapi suvrataḥ
dravyābhāvātsvaṃyaṃ pārtho bhrātṛbhiś ca divaṃ gataḥ
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ kṛṣṇasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
ityetatsomavaṃśānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ caritaṃ dvijāḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi brāhmaṇān śrāvayedapi
sa yāti vaiṣṇavaṃ lokaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge somavaṃśānukīrtanaṃ nāmaikonasaptatitamo 'dhyacāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
ādisargastvayā sūta sūcito na prakāśitaḥ
sūta uvāca
maheśvaro mahādevaḥ prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca
paratve saṃsthito devaḥ paramātmā munīśvarāḥ
avyaktaṃ ceśvarāttasmādabhavatkāraṇaṃ param
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiśceti yadāhustattvacintakāḥ
jagadyoniṃ mahābhūtaṃ paraṃ brahma sanātanam
vigrahaḥ sarvabhūtānāmīśvarājñāpracoditam
anādyantamajaṃ sūkṣmaṃ triguṇaṃ prabhavāvyayam
asyātmanā sarvamidaṃ vyāptaṃ tvāsīcchivecchayā
sargakāle pradhānasya kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitasya vai
guṇabhāvādvyajyamāno mahānprādurbabhūvaha
sūkṣmeṇa mahatā cātha avyaktena samāvṛtam
mano mahāṃstu vijñeyamekaṃ tatkāraṇaṃ smṛtam
samutpannaṃ liṅgamātraṃ kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitaṃ hi tat
dharmādīni ca rūpāṇi lokatattvārthahetavaḥ
mahān sṛṣṭiṃ vikurute codyamānaḥ sisṛkṣayā
mano mahānmatirbrahma pūrbuddhiḥ khyātirīśvaraḥ
prajñā citiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃvidviśveśaśceti sa smṛtaḥ
manute sarvabhūtānāṃ yasmācceṣṭā phalaṃ tataḥ
tattvānā magrajo yasmānmahāṃś ca parimāṇataḥ
viśeṣebhyo guṇebhyopi mahāniti tataḥ smṛtaḥ
puruṣo bhogasaṃbandhāttena cāsau matiḥ smṛtaḥ
bṛhattvātbṛṃhaṇatvācca bhāvānāṃ sakalaśrayāt
yaḥ pūrayati yasmācca kṛtsnāndevānanugrahaiḥ
budhyate puruṣaścātra sarvān bhāvān hitaṃ tathā
bhogasya jñānaniṣṭhatvāttena khyātiriti smṛtaḥ
khyāyate tadguṇairvāpi jñānādibhir anekaśaḥ
tasmācca mahataḥ saṃjñā khyātirityabhidhīyate
sākṣātsarvaṃ vijānāti mahātmā tena ceśvaraḥ
yasmājjñānānugaścaiva prajñā tena sa ucyate
jñānādini ca rūpāṇi bahukarmaphalāni ca
vartamānavya tītāni tathaivānāgatānyapi
kṛtsnaṃ ca vindate jñānaṃ yasmānmāhātmyamuttamam
jānāterjñānamityāhurbhagavān jñānasaṃnidhiḥ
bandhanādiparībhāvādīśvaraḥ procyate budhaiḥ
vyākhyātaṃ tattvabhāvajñairdevasadbhāvacetakaiḥ
mahānsṛṣṭiṃ vikurute codyamānaḥ sisṛkṣayā
mahatā ca vṛtaḥ sargo bhūtādirbāhmatastu saḥ
tasmādeva tamodriktādahaṅkārādajāyata
bhūtādistu vikurvāṇaḥ śabdamātraṃ sasarja ha
ākāśaṃ suṣiraṃ tasmādutpannaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam
ākāśaṃ śabdamātraṃ tu sparśamātraṃ samāvṛṇot
vāyuścāpi vikurvāṇo rūpamātraṃ sasarja ha
sparśamātrastu vai vāyū rūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot
jyotiścāpi vikurvāṇaṃ rasamātraṃ sasarja ha
rasamātrāstu tā hyāpo rūpamātrognirāvṛṇot
saṃghāto jāyate tasmāttasya gandho guṇo mataḥ
tasmiṃstasmiṃś ca tanmātraṃ tena tanmātratā smṛtā
aviśeṣavācakatvād aviśeṣās tatas tu te
praśāntaghoramūḍhatvādaviśeṣāstataḥ punaḥ
vaikārikādahaṅkārātsattvodriktāttu sāttvikāt
sādhakānīndriyāṇi syurdevā vaikā rikā daśa
śrotraṃ tvak cakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā caiva pañcamī
śabdādīnāmavāptyarthaṃ buddhiyuktāni tāni vai
ākāśaṃ śabdamātraṃ ca sparśamātraṃ samāviśat
rūpaṃ tathaiva viśataḥ sabdasparśa guṇāvubhau
saśabdasparśarūpaṃ ca rasamātraṃ samāviśat
tasmāccaturgumā āpo vijñeyāstu rasātmikāḥ
śabdasparśaṃ ca rūpaṃ ca raso vai gandhamāviśat
saṃgatā gandhamātreṇa āviśanto mahīmimām
tasmātpañcaguṇā bhūmiḥ sthūlā bhūteṣu śasyate
śāntā ghorāś ca mūḍhāś ca viśeṣāstena te smṛtāḥ
bhūmerantastvidaṃ sarvaṃ lokālokācalāvṛtam
viśeṣāścendriyagrāhyā niyatatvācca te smṛtāḥ
teṣāṃ yāvacca tadyacca yacca tāvadguṇaṃ smṛtam
pṛthivyāmeva taṃ vidyādapāṃ vāyoś ca saṃśrayāt
puruṣādhiṣṭhitatvācca avyaktānugraheṇa ca
mahā dayo viśeṣāntā hyaṇḍamutpādayanti te
adbhir daśaguṇābhistu bāhyatoṇḍaṃ samāvṛtam
āpo daśaguṇenaitāstejasā bāhyato vṛtāḥ
tejo daśaguṇenaiva vāyunā bāhyato vṛtam
vāyurdaśaguṇenaiva bāhyato nabhasā vṛtaḥ
ākāśonāvṛto vāyuḥ khaṃ tu bhūtādināvṛtam
bhūtādirmahatā cāpi avyaktenāvṛto mahān
śarvaścāṇḍakapālastho bhavaścāṃbhasi suvratāḥ
bhīmaścāvanimadhyastho hyahaṅkāre maheśvaraḥ
buddhau ca bhagavānīśaḥ sarvataḥ parameśvaraḥ
etairāvaraṇairaṇḍaṃ saptabhiḥ prākatairvṛtam
etā āvṛtya cānyonyamaṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ
ādhārādheyabhāvena vikārāste vikāriṣu
aṇḍājjajñe sa eveśaḥ puruṣorkasamaprabhaḥ
tasya vāmāṅgajo viṣṇuḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ
lakṣmyā devyā hyabhūddeva icchayā parameṣṭhinaḥ
dakṣiṇāṅgabhavo brahmā sarasvatyā jagadguruḥ
yattu sṛṣṭau prasaṃkhyātaṃ mayā kālāntaraṃ dvijāḥ
etatkālāntaraṃ jñeyamaharvai pārameśvaram
rātriścaitāvatī jñeyā parameśasya kṛtsnaśaḥ
ahastasya tu yā sṛṣṭiḥ rātriś ca pralayaḥ smṛtaḥ
upacārastu kriyate lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
indriyāṇīndriyārthāś ca mahābhūtāni pañca ca
tasmātsarvāṇibhūtāni buddhiś ca saha daivataiḥ
ahastiṣṭhanti sarvāṇi parameśasya dhīmataḥ
sādharmyeṇāvatiṣṭhete pradhānapuruṣāvubhau
guṇasāmye layo jñeyo vaiṣamye sṛṣṭirucyate
upāsya rajanīṃ kṛtsnāṃ parāṃ māheśvarīṃ tathā
kṣobhayāmāsa yogena pareṇa parameśvaraḥ
pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ caiva praviśya sa maheśvaraḥ
maheśvarāttrayo devā jajñire jagadīśvarāt
śāśvatāḥ paramā guhyaḥ sarvātmānaḥ śarīreṇaḥ
kṣaṇaṃ viyogo na hyeṣāṃ na tyajanti parasparam
īśvarastu paro devo viṣṇuś ca mahataḥ paraḥ
paraḥ sa puruṣo jñeyaḥ prakṛtiḥ sā parā smṛtā
anupravṛttastu mahāṃstadenāṃ cirastiratvādviṣayaṃ śriyaḥ svayam
īśvarādhiṣṭhitātpūrvaṃ tasmātsadasadātmakāt
tejasāpratimo dhīmānavyaktaḥ saṃprakāśakaḥ
brahmā ca bhagavāṃstasmāccaturvaktraḥ prajāpatiḥ
saṃsiddhaḥ kāryakāraṇe tathā vai samavartata
apratīpena jñānena aiśvaryeṇa samanvitaḥ
dharmeṇa cāpratīṣena vairāgyeṇa ca te 'nvitāḥ
avyaktāj jāyate teṣāṃ manasā yad yad īhitam
vaśīkṛtatvāttraiguṇyaṃ sāpekṣatvātsvabhāvataḥ
sahasramūrdhā puruṣastisro 'vasthāḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ
puruṣatve hyudāsīnastisrāvesthāḥ prajāpateḥ
puruṣaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo rūpaṃ tatparamātmanaḥ
maheśvaraḥ śarīrāṇi karoti vikaroti ca
nānākṛtikriyārūpanāmavanti svalīlayā
maheśvaraḥ śarīrāṇi karoti vikaroti ca
yaccāsya satataṃ bhāvastasmādātmā nirucyate
ṛṣiḥ sarvagatatvācca śarīrī sosya yatprabhuḥ
svāmitvamasya yatsarvaṃ viṣṇuḥ sarvapraveśanāt
bhagavān bhagavadbhāvānnirmalatvācchivaḥ smṛtaḥ
paramaḥ saṃprakṛṣṭatvādavanādomiti smṛtaḥ
sarvajñaḥ sarvavijñānātsarvaḥ sarvamayo yataḥ
āditvādādidevosāvajātatvādajaḥ smṛtaḥ
pāti yasmātprajāḥ sarvāḥ prajāpati riti smṛtaḥ
deveṣu ca mahāndevo mahādevastataḥ smṛtaḥ
sarvagatvācca devānāmavaśyatvācca īśvaraḥ
bṛhattvācca smṛto brahmā bhūtatvādbhūta ucyate
kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetravijñānādekatvātkevalaḥ smṛtaḥ
yasmātpuryāṃ sa śete ca tasmātpūruṣa ucyate
anāditvācca pūrvatvātsvayaṃbhūriti saṃsmṛtaḥ
yājyatvāducyate yajñaḥ kavirvikraāntadarśanāt
kramaṇaḥ kramaṇīyatvātpālakaścāpi pālanāt
āditya saṃjñaḥ kapilo hyagrahogniriti smṛtaḥ
na śakyaḥ parisaṃkhyātumapi varṣaśatairapi
kālasaṃkhyāvivṛttasya parārdho brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇi aharbhūtāni yāni vai
samatītāni kalpānāṃ tāvaccheṣāḥ pare tu ye
prathamaḥ sāṃpratasteṣāṃ kalpoyaṃ vartate dvijāḥ
atītā vartamānāś ca bhaviṣyā ye ca vai punaḥ
tairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā saparvatā
pūrṇaṃ yugasahasraṃ vai paripālyā maheśvaraiḥ
prajābhistapasā caiva teṣāṃ śṛṇuta vistaram
manvantareṇa caikena sarvāṇyevāntarāṇi ca
atītāni ca kalpāni sodarkāṇi sahānvayaiḥ
anāgateṣu tadvacca tarkaḥ kāryo vijānatā
śāntatāraikanīresminna prājñāyata kiñcana
ekārṇave tadā tasminnaṣṭe stāvarajaṅgame
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣo rukmavarṇas tvatīndriyaḥ
brahmā nārāyaṇākhyastu suṣvāpa salile tadā
imaṃ codāharantyatra ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati
āpo nārāś ca sūnava ityapāṃ nāma śuśrumaḥ
āpūrya tābhir ayanaṃ kṛtavānātmano yataḥ
apsu śete yatastasmāttato nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
niśāyāmiva khadyotaḥ prāvṛṭkāle tatastu saḥ
tatas tu salile tasmin vijñāyāntargatāṃ mahīm
anumānādasaṃ mūḍho bhūmeruddharaṇaṃ punaḥ
akarotsa tanūmanyāṃ kalpādiṣu yathāpurā
salilenāplutāṃ bhūmiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa tu samantataḥ
kiṃnu rūpamahaṃ kṛtvā uddhareyaṃ mahīmimām
jalakrīḍānusadṛśaṃ vārāhaṃ rūpamāviśat
adhṛṣyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ vāṅmayaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam
pṛthivyuddharaṇārthāya praviveśa rasātalam
adbhiḥ saṃchāditāṃ bhūmiṃ sa tāmāśu prajāpatiḥ
upagamyojjahāraināmāpaścāpi samāviśat
sāmudrā vai samudreṣu nādeyāś ca nadīṣu ca
rasātalatale magnāṃ rasātalapuṭe gatām
prabhurlokahitārthāya daṃṣṭrayābhyujjahāra gām
tataḥ svasthānamānīya pṛthivīṃ pṛtivīdharaḥ
mumoca pūrvavādasau dhārayitvā dharādharaḥ
tata utkṣipta tāṃ devo jagataḥ sthāpanecchayā
pṛthivyāḥ pravibhāgāya manaścakrembujekṣaṇaḥ
pṛthivīṃ ca samāṃ kṛtvā pṛthivyāṃ socinodgirīn
prāksarge dahyamāne tu tadā saṃvartakāgninā
tenāgninā viśīrṇāste parvatā bhūrivistarāḥ
śaityādekārṇave tasmin vāyunā tena saṃhatāḥ
tadācalatvādacalāḥ parvabhiḥ parvatāḥ smṛtāḥ
tatasteṣu vikīrṇeṣu koṭiśo hi giriṣvatha
viśvakarmā vibhajate kalpādiṣu punaḥ punaḥ
sasamudrāmimāṃ pṛthvīṃ saptadvīpāṃ saparvatām
bhūrādyāṃś ca turo lokānpunaḥ sotha vyakalpayat
brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavānsisṛkṣurvividhāḥ prajāḥ
sasarja sṛṣṭiṃ tadrūpāṃ kalpādiṣu yathāpurā
tamomoho mahāmohastāmisraścāndhasaṃjñitaḥ
avidyā pañcaparvaiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ
pañcadhāvasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyataḥ sobhimāninaḥ
saṃvṛtastamasā caiva bījāṅkuravadāvṛtaḥ
bahirantaścāprakāśastabdho niḥsaṃjña eva ca
yasmātteṣāṃ vṛtā buddhirduḥkhāni karaṇāni ca
tasmātte saṃvṛtātmāno nagā mukhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
mukhyasargaṃ tathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā brahmā hyasādhakam
tasmāt tiryakpravṛttaḥ sa tiryaksrotās tataḥ smṛtaḥ
paśvādayaste vikhyātā utpathagrāhiṇo dvijāḥ
te sukhaprītibahulā bahirantaś ca saṃvṛtāḥ
prakāśābahirantaś ca ūrdhvasrotobhavāḥ smṛtāḥ
te sattvasya ca yogena sṛṣṭāḥ sattvodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ
prakāśādbrahirantaś ca ūrdhvasrotodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ
te ūrdhvasrotaso jñeyāstuṣṭātmāno budhaiḥ smṛtāḥ
ūrdhvasrotaḥsusṛṣṭeṣu deveṣu varadaḥ prabhuḥ
prādurāsīttadā vyaktādarvāksrotāstu sādhakaḥ
te ca prakāśabahulāstamaḥ pṛktā rajodhikāḥ
tasmātte duḥkhabahulā bhūyobhūyaś ca kāriṇaḥ
saṃvṛtā bahirantaś ca manuṣyāḥ sādhakāś ca te
lakṣaṇaistārakādyaiste hyaṣṭadhā tu vyavastitāḥ
viparyayeṇa śaktyā ca siddhyā tuṣṭyā tathaiva ca
sthāvareṣu viparyāsaḥ stiryagyoniṣu śaktitaḥ
siddhātmāno manuṣyāstu ṛṣideveṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargo vaikṛto 'navamaḥ smṛtaḥ
bhūtādikānāṃ bhūtānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ sa ucyate
nivṛttaṃ vartamānaṃ ca teṣāṃ jānanti vai punaḥ
bhūtādikānāṃ bhūtānāṃ saptamaḥ sarga eva ca
te 'parigrāhiṇaḥ sarve saṃvibhāgaratāḥ punaḥ
svādanāścāpyaśīlāś ca jñeyā bhūtādikāś ca te
viparyayeṇa bhūtādiraśaktyā ca vyavasthitaḥ
tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyastu bhūtasargaḥ sa ucyate
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃbhūto buddhipūrvakaḥ
mukhyasargaścaturthaś ca mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ
tatorvāksrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ
aṣṭamo 'nugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttvikastāmasaś ca saḥ
pañcaite vaikṛtāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtāstu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ
prākṛto vaikṛtaścaiva kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ
abuddhipūrvakāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtāstu traya smṛtāḥ
caturdhāvasthitaḥ sotha sarvabhūteṣu kṛtsraśaḥ
ityete prākṛtāścaiva vaikṛtāś ca navasmṛtāḥ
parasparānuraktāś ca kāraṇaiś ca budhaiḥ smṛtāḥ
agre sasarja vai brahmā mānasānātmanaḥ samān
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca dvāvetāvūrdhvaretasau
vyatīte tvaṣṭame kalpe purāṇau lokasākṣiṇau
tau vārāhe tu bhūrloke tejaḥ saṃkṣipya dhiṣṭhitau
tāvubhau mokṣakarmāṇāvāropyātmānamātmani
prajāṃ dharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca tyaktvā vairāgyamāsthitau
sanandaṃ sanakaṃ caiva vidvāṃsaṃ ca sanātanam
saṃbuddhāścaiva nānātve apravṛttāś ca yoginaḥ
asṛṣṭvaiva prajāsargaṃ pratisargaṃ gatāḥ punaḥ
tatasteṣu vyatīteṣu tatonyānsādhakānsutān
mānasānasṛjadbrahma punaḥ sthānābhimāninaḥ
ābhūtasaṃplavāvasthā yairiyaṃ vidhṛtā mahī
āpogniṃ pṛthivīṃ vāyumantarikṣaṃ divaṃ tathā
samudrāṃś ca nadīścaiva tathā śailavanaspatīn
oṣadhīnāṃ tathātmāno vallīnāṃ vṛkṣavīrudhām
latāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ kalāścaiva muhūrtāḥ saṃdhirātryahān
ardhamāsāṃś ca māsāṃś ca ayanābdayugāni ca
sthānābhimāninaḥ sarve sthānākhyāścaiva te smṛtāḥ
devānṛṣīṃś ca mahato gadatastānnabodhata
dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca sosajanmānasānnava
nava brahmāṇa ityete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ
teṣāṃ brahmātmakānāṃ vai sarveṣāṃ brahmavādinām
sthānāni kalpayāmāsa pūrvavatpadmasaṃbhavaḥ
sosṛjadvyavasāyāttu dharmaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ
mānasaś ca rucirnāma vijajñe brahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ
prāṇādbrahmāsṛjaddakṣaṃ cakṣurbhyāṃ ca marīcinam
bhṛgustu hṛdayājjajñe ṛṣiḥ salila janmanaḥ
śirasoṅgirasaścaiva śrotrādatriṃ tatāsṛjat
pulastyaṃ ca tathodānādvyānācca pulahaṃ punaḥ
samānajo vasiṣṭhaś ca apānānnirmame kratum
ityete brahmaṇaḥ putrā divyā ekādaśā smṛtāḥ
dharmādayaḥ prathamajāḥ sarve te brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ
bhṛgvādayastu te sṛṣṭā navaite brahmavādinaḥ
gṛhamedhinaḥ purāṇās te dharmas taiḥ saṃpravartitaḥ
teṣāṃ dvādaśa te vaṃśā divyā devaguṇānvitāḥ
kriyāvantaḥ prajāvanto maharṣibhir alaṅkṛtāḥ
ṛbhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca dvāvetāvūrdhvaretasau
vyatītetvaṣṭame kalpe purāṇau lokasākṣiṇau
virājetāmubhau loke tejaḥ saṃkṣipya dhiṣṭhitau
tāvubhau yogakarmāmāvāropyātmānamātmani
prajāṃ dharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca tyaktvā vairāgyamāsthitau
tasmātsanatkumāroti nāmāsyeha pratiṣṭhitam
tatobhidhyāyatastasya jajñire mānasāḥ prajāḥ
taccharīrasamutpannaiḥ kāryaistaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ saha
kṣetrajñāḥ samavartanta gātrebhyastasya dhīmataḥ
tato devāsurapitṝn mānuṣāṃś ca catuṣṭayam
sisṛkṣuraṃbhāsyetāni svamātmānamayūyujat
tatosya jaghanātpūrvamasurā jajñire sutāḥ
asuḥ prāṇaḥ smṛto viprastajjanmānastatosurāḥ
yayā sṛṣṭāsurāḥ sarve tāṃ tanuṃ sa vyapohata
sā tamobahulā yasmāttato rātrirniyāmikā
āvṛtāstamasā rātrau prajāstasmātsvapantyuta
sṛṣṭvāsurāṃstataḥ so vai tanumanyāmagṛhṇata
avyaktāṃ sattvabahulāṃ tatastāṃ sobhyapūjayat
tatastāṃ yuñjatas tasya priyam āsīt prajāpateḥ
yatosya dīvyato jātāstena devāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
dhāturdiviti yaḥ proktaḥ krīḍāyāṃ sa vibhāvyate
devānsṛṣṭvātha deveśastanumanyāmapadyata
utsṛṣṭā sā tanustena sadyohaḥ samajāyata
pitṛvanmanyamānasya putrāṃstāndhyāyataḥ prabhoḥ
tasmātte pitaro devāḥ pitṛtvaṃ tena teṣu tat
yayā sṛṣṭāstu pitarastanuṃ tāṃ sa vyapohata
yasmādahardevatānāṃ rātriryā sāsurī smṛtā
tayormadhye tu paitrī yā tanuḥ sā tu garīyasī
tasmāddevā surāḥ sarve ṛṣayo mānavās tathā
upāsaṃte mudāyuktā rātryahnormadhyamāṃ tanum
rajomā trātmikāyāṃ tu mānasā sosṛjatprabhuḥ
rajaḥ priyāṃstataḥ sotha mānasānasṛjatsutān
sṛṣṭvā punaḥ prajāścāpi svāṃ tanuṃ tāmapohata
yasmādbhavanti saṃhṛṣṭājyotsnāyā udbhave prajāḥ
jyotsnā saṃdhyā ahaścaiva sattvamātrātmakaṃ trayam
tamomātrātmikā rātriḥ sā vai tasmānniśātmikā
tasmāddevā divātanvā tuṣṭyā sṛṣṭā mukhāttu vai
yasmātteṣāṃ divā janma balinastena vai divā
tanvā yayāsurān rātrau jaghanādasṛjatprabhuḥ
etānyeva bhaviṣyāṇāṃ daṃvānāmasuraiḥ saha
pitṝṇāṃ mānavānāṃ ca atītānāgateṣu vai
jyotsnā rātryahanī saṃdhyā catvāryaṃbhāṃsi tāni vai
bhānti yasmāttatoṃbhāṃsi śabdoyaṃ sumanīṣibhiḥ
bhātirdīptau nigaditaḥ punaścātha prajāpatiḥ
so 'mbhāṃsyetāni sṛṣṭvā tu devamānuṣadānavān
pitṝṃścaiva sṛjattanvā ātmanā vividhānpunaḥ
tāmutsṛjya tanuṃ jyotsnāṃ tatonyāṃ prāpya sa prabhuḥ
mūrtiṃ tamorajaḥ prāyāṃ punarevābhyapūjayat
andhakāre kṣudhāviṣṭāṃstatonyasosṛjatprabhuḥ
tena sṛṣṭāḥ kṣudhātmāno aṃbhāṃsyādātumudyatāḥ
abhāṃsyetāni rakṣāma uktavantastu teṣu ye
rākṣasā nāma te yasmāt kṣudhāviṣṭā niśācarāḥ
yebruvanyakṣamombhāṃsi teṣāṃ hṛṣṭāḥ parasparam
tena te karmaṇā yakṣā guhyakā gūḍhakarmaṇā
rakṣeti pālane cāpi dhātureṣa vibhāṣyate
taṃ dṛṣṭvā hyapriyeṇāsya keśāḥ śīrṇāstu dhīmataḥ
te śīrṇāścotthitā hyūrdhvaṃ te caivārurudhuḥ prabhum
hīnāstacchiraso bālā yasmāccaivāvasarpiṇaḥ
vyālātmānaḥ smṛtā bālā hīnatvādahayaḥ smṛtāḥ
patatvātpannagāścaiva sarpāścaivāvasarpaṇāt
sa tu sarpān sahotpannānāviveśa viṣātmakaḥ
sarpānsṛṣṭvā tataḥ kruddhaḥ krodhātmāno vinirmame
varṇena kapiśenogrāste bhūtāḥ piśitāśanāḥ
bhūtatvātte smṛtā bhūtāḥ piśācāḥ piśitāśanāt
dhayatītyeṣa vai dhātuḥ pānatve paripaṭhyate
dhayanto jajñire vācaṃ gandharvāstena te smṛtāḥ
aṣṭasvetāsu sṛṣṭāsu devayoniṣu sa prabhuḥ
tataḥ svacchandatonyāni vayāṃsi vayasāsṛjat
paśūnsṛṣṭvā sa deveśo 'sṛjatpakṣigaṇānapi
mukhatojāḥ sasarjātha vakṣasaścāvayosṛjat
gāścaivāthodarādbrahmā pārśvābhyāṃ ca vinirmame
padbhyāṃ cāśvān samātaṅgān rāsabhānāvayānmṛgān
uṣṭrānaśvatarāṃścaiva tathānyāścaiva jātayaḥ
evaṃ paśvoṣadhīḥ sṛṣṭvāyūyujatsodhvare prabhuḥ
gaurajaḥ pūruṣo meṣo hyaśvośvataragardabhau
etāngrāmyānpaśūnāhurāraṇyānvai nibodhata
śvāpado dvikhuro hastī vānarāḥ pakṣipañcamāḥ
ādakāḥ paśavaḥ ṣaṣṭhāḥ saptamāstu sarīsṛpāḥ
mahiṣā gavayākṣāś ca plavaṅgāḥ śarabhā vṛkāḥ
siṃhastu saptamasteṣāmāraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ smṛtāḥ
gāyatraṃ ca ṛcaṃ caiva trivṛtsāma rathantaram
agniṣṭomaṃ ca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamān mukhāt
yajuṃṣi traiṣṭubhaṃ chandastomaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tathā
vṛhatsāma tathokthyaṃ ca dakṣiṇādasṛjanmukhāt
sāmāni jagatīcchandastomaṃ saptadaśaṃ tathā
vairūpamatirātraṃ ca paścimādasṛjanmukhāt
ekaviṃśamatharvāṇamāptoryā māṇameva ca
anuṣṭubhaṃ savairājamuttarādasṛjanmukhāt
vidyutośanimeghāṃś ca rohitendradhanūṃṣi ca
uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyastasya jajñire
sṛṣṭvā catuṣṭayaṃ pūrvaṃ devāsuranarānpitṝn
tato 'sṛjat sa bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
yakṣānpiśācān gandharvaṃstvathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇān
narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥ paśumṛgoragān
avyayaṃ ca vyayaṃ cāpi yadidaṃ sthāṇujaṅgamam
teṣāṃ vai yāni karmāṇi prāksṛṣṭyāṃ pratipedire
tānyeva pratipadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
hiṃsrāhiṃsre mṛdukrūre dharmādharme nṛtānṛte
mahābhūteṣu sṛṣṭeṣu indrīyārtheṣu mūrtiṣu
viniyogaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ dhātaiva vyādadhātsvayam
kecitpuruṣakāraṃ tu prāhuḥ karma sumānavāḥ
daivamityapare viprāḥ svabhāvaṃ bhūta cintakāḥ
karmasthā viṣamaṃ brūyuḥ sattvasthāḥ samadarśanāḥ
nāma rūpaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ kṛtānāṃ ca prapañcanam
ṛṣīṇāṃ nāmadheyāni yāś ca vedeṣu vṛttayaḥ
śarvaryante prasūtānāṃ tānyevaibhyo dadātyajaḥ
evaṃvidhāḥ sṛṣṭayastu brahmaṇovyaktajanmanaḥ
śarvaryante pradṛśyante siddhimāśritya mānasīm
evaṃbhūtāni sṛṣṭāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
yadāsya tāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭā na vyavardhanta sattamāḥ
tamomātrāvṛto brahmā tadā śokena duḥkhitaḥ
athātmani samadrākṣīttamomātrāṃ niyāmikām
tamaś ca vyanudatpaścādrajaḥ sattvaṃ tamāvṛṇot
adharmastamaso jajñe hiṃsā śokādajāyata
gatāsur bhagavān āsīt prītiś cainam aśiśriyat
svāṃ tanuṃ sa tato brahmā tāmapohata bhāsvarām
ardhena nārī sā tasya śatarūpā vyajāyata
prakṛtiṃ bhūtadhātriṃ tāṃ kāmādvai sṛṣṭavānprabhuḥ
sā divaṃ pṛthivīṃ caiva mahimnā vyāpyadhiṣṭhitā
brahmaṇaḥ sā tanuḥ pūrvā divamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati
yā tvardhātsṛjato nārī śatarūpā vyajāyata
sā devī niyutaṃ taptvā tapaḥ paramaduścaram
bhartāraṃ dīptayaśasaṃ puruṣaṃ pratyapadyata
sa vai svāyaṃbhuvaḥ pūrvaṃ puruṣo manurucyate
lebhe sa puruṣaḥ patnīṃ śatarūpā mayonijām
virājamasṛjadbrāhmā sobhavatpuruṣo virāṭ
samrāṭ ca śatarūpā vai verājaḥ sa manuḥ smṛtaḥ
sa vairājaḥ prajāsargaṃ sasarja puruṣo manuḥ
vairājātpuruṣā dvīrācchatarūpā vyajāyata
kanye dve ca mahābhāge yābhyāṃ jātā imāḥ prajāḥ
devī nāma tathākūtiḥ prasūtiścaiva te ubhe
svāyaṃbhuvaḥ prasūtiṃ tu dakṣāya pradadau prabhuḥ
prāṇo dakṣa iti jñeyaḥ saṃkalpo manurucyate
ruceḥ prajāpateḥ sotha ākūtiṃ pratyapādayat
ākūtyāṃ mithunaṃ jajñe mānasasya ruceḥ śubham
yajñaś ca dakṣiṇā caiva yamalau saṃbabhūvatuḥ
yajñasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ tu putrā dvādaśa jajñire
yāmā iti samākhyātā devāḥ svāyaṃbhuventare
etasya putrā yajñasya tasmādyāmāś ca te smṛtāḥ
ajitaścaiva śukraś ca gaṇau dvau brahmaṇā kṛtau
yāmāḥ pūrvaṃ prajātā ye te 'bhavaṃstu divaukasaḥ
svāyaṃbhuvasutāyāṃ tu prasūtyāṃ lokamātaraḥ
tasyāṃ kanyāścaturviśaddakṣastvajanayatprabhuḥ
sarvāstāś ca mahābhāgāḥ sarvāḥ kamalalocanāḥ
bhogavatyaś ca tāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāstā yogamātaraḥ
sarvāś ca brahmavādinyaḥ sarvā viśvasya mātaraḥ
śraddhā lakṣmīrdhṛtistuṣṭiḥ puṣṭirmedhā kriyā tathā
buddhirlajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtistrayodaśa
patnyarthaṃ pratijagrāha dharmo dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ
dārāṇyetāni vai tasya vihitāni svayaṃbhuvā
tābhyaḥ śiṣṭa yavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ
satī khyātyatha saṃbhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamā tathā
saṃnatiścānasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā
rudro bhṛgurmariciś ca aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
satīṃ bhavāya prāyacchat khyātiṃ ca bhṛgave tataḥ
prītiṃ caiva pulastyāya kṣamāṃ vai pulahāya ca
krateva saṃnatiṃ nāma anasūyāṃ tathātraye
ūrjāṃ dadau vasiṣṭhāya svāhāmapyagnaye dadau
etāḥ sarvā mahābhāgāḥ prajāsvanusṛtāḥ sthitāḥ
manvantareṣu sarveṣu yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam
śraddhā kāmaṃ vijajñe vai darpo lakṣmīsutaḥ smṛtaḥ
dhṛtyāstu niyamaḥ putrastuṣṭyāḥ saṃtoṣa eva ca
puṣṭyā lobhaḥ sutaścāpi medhāputraḥ śrutas tathā
lajjāyāṃ vinayaḥ putro vyavasāyo vasoḥ sutaḥ
kṣemaḥ śāntisutaścāpi sukhaṃ siddhervyajāyata
yaśaḥ kīrtisutaścāpi ityete dharmasūnavaḥ
kāmasya harṣaḥ putro vai devyāṃ prītyāṃ vyajāyata
jajñe hiṃsā tvadharmādvai nikṛtiṃ cānṛtaṃ sutam
nikṛtyāṃ tu dvayaṃ jajñe bhayaṃ naraka eva ca
bhūyo jajñetha vai māyā mṛtyuṃ bhūtāpahāriṇam
vedanāyāḥ sutaścāpi duḥkhaṃ jajñe ca rauravaḥ
mṛtyor vyādhijarāśokakrodhāsūyāś ca jajñire
duḥkhottarāḥ sutā hyete sarve cādharmalakṣaṇāḥ
naiṣāṃ bhāryāstu putrāś ca sarve hyete parigrahāḥ
ityeṣa tāmasaḥ sargo jajñe dharmaniyāmakaḥ
prajāḥ sṛjeti vyādiṣṭo brahmaṇā nīlalohitaḥ
sobhidhyāya satīṃ bhāryāṃ nirmame hyatmasaṃbhavān
nādhikānna ca hīnāṃstānmānasānātmanaḥ samān
sahasraṃ hi sahasrāṇāṃ sosṛjatkṛttivāsasaḥ
tulyānevātmanaḥ sarvān rūpatejobaluśrutaiḥ
piṅgalānsaniṣaṅgāṃś ca sakapardānsalohitān
viśiṣṭān harikeśāṃścadṛṣṭighnāṃś ca kapālinaḥ
mahārūpānvirūpāṃś ca viśvarūpānsvarūpiṇaḥ
rathinaścarmiṇaścaiva varmiṇaś ca varūthinaḥ
sahasraśatabāhuṃś ca divyānbhau māntarikṣagān
sthūlaśīrṣānaṣṭadaṃṣṭrāndvijihvāṃstāṃstrilocanān
annādānpiśitāśāṃś ca ājyapānsomapānapi
mīḍhuṣotikapālāṃś ca śitikaṇṭhordhvaretasaḥ
havyādāñchrutadharmaṃś ca dharmiṇo hyatha barhiṇaḥ
āsīnāndhāvataścaiva pañcabhūtānsahasraśaḥ
vṛddhānbuddhimataścaiva brahmiṣṭhāñśubhadarśanān
nīlagrīvānsahasrākṣānsarvāṃścātha kṣamākarān
adṛśyānsarvabhūtānāṃ mahāyogānmahaujasaḥ
ayātayāmānasṛjadrudrānetān surottamān
brahmā dṛṣṭvābravīdenaṃ māsrākṣīrīdṛśīḥ prajāḥ
sraṣṭavyā nātmanastulyāḥ prajā deva namostu te
anyāḥ sṛja tvaṃ bhadraṃ te prajā vai mṛtyusaṃyutāḥ
nārapsyante hi karmāṇi prajāvagatamṛtyavaḥ
evamukto 'bravīdenaṃ nāhaṃ mṛtyujarānvitāḥ
prajāḥ sakṣyāmi bhadraṃ te sthitoha tvaṃ sṛja prajāḥ
ete ye vai mayā sṛṣṭā virūpā nīlalohitāḥ
sahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ tu ātmano nissṛtāḥ prajāḥ
ete devā bhaviṣyanti rudrā nāma mahābalāḥ
pṛthivyāmantarikṣe ca dikṣu caiva pariśritāḥ
śatarudrāḥ samātmano bhaviṣyantitī yājñikāḥ
sārdhaṃ tairījyamānāste sthāsyantīhāyugakṣayāt
pratyuvāca namaskṛtya hṛṣyamāṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ
evaṃ bhavatu bhadraṃ te yathā te vyāhṛtaṃ vibho
brahmaṇā samanu jñāte tathā sarvamabhūtkila
tataḥ prabhṛti deveśo na cāsūyata vai prajāḥ
ūrdhvaretāḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇuryāvadābhūtasaṃplavam
yasmāduktaḥ sthitosmīti tasmātsthāṇuriti smṛtaḥ
svecchayāsau dvidhābhūtaḥ pṛthak strī puruṣaḥ pṛthak
tatra yā sā mahābhāgā śaṅkarasyārdhakāyinī
prāguktā tu mahādevī strī saiveha satī hyabhūt
hitāya jagatāṃ devī dakṣeṇārādhitā purā
kāryārthaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ tasyāḥ śuklaṃ vāmaṃ tathāsitam
ātmānaṃ vibhajasveti proktā devena śaṃbhunā
sā tathoktā dvidhābhūtā śuklā kṛṣṇā ca vai dvijāḥ
tasyā nāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇvantu ca samāhitāḥ
svāhā svadhā mahāvidyā medhā lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī
satī dākṣāyaṇī vidyā icchāśaktiḥ kriyātmikā
aparṇā caikaparṇā ca tathā caivaikapāṭalā
umā haimavatī caiva kalyāṇī caikamātṛkā
khyātiḥ prajñā mahābhāgā loke gaurīti viśrutā
gaṇāṃbikā mahādevī nandinī jātavedasī
ekarūpamathaitasyāḥ pṛthagdehavibhāvatān
sāvitrī varadā puṇyā pāvanī lokaviśrutā
ājñā āveśanī kṛṣṇā tāmasī sāttvikī śivā
prakṛtirvikṛtā raudrī durgā bhadrā pramāthinī
kālarātrirmahāmāyā revatī bhūtanāyikā
dvāparāntavibhāge ca nāmānīmānisuvratāḥ
gautamī kauśikī cāryā caṇḍī kātyāyanī satī
kumārī yādavī devī varadā kṛṣṇapiṅgalā
barhīdhvajā śūladharā paramā brahmacāriṇī
aparājitā bahubhujā pragalbhā siṃhavāhinī
śuṃbhādidaityahantrī ca mahāmahiṣamardinī
amoghā vindhyanilayā vikraāntā gaṇanāyikā
devyā nāmavikārāṇi ityetāni yathākramam
ye paṭhanti narāsteṣāṃ vidyate na ca pātakam
rakṣāmetāṃ prayuñjīta jale vātha sthalepi vā
vyāghrakuṃbhīnacorebhyo bhayasthāne viśeṣataḥ
āpatsvapi ca sarvāsu devyā nāmāni kīrtayet
āryakagrahabhūtaiś ca pūtanāmātṛbhis tathā
abhyarditānāṃ bālānāṃ rakṣāmetāṃ prayojayet
mahādevīkale dve tu prajñā śrīś ca prakīrtite
ābhyāṃ devīsahasrāṇī yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat
ātiṣṭhatsarvalokānāṃ hitāya parameśvaraḥ
rudraḥ paśupatiścāsītpurā dagdhaṃ puratrayam
devāś ca paśavaḥ sarve babhūvustasya tejasā
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi ādisargakramaṃ śubham
sa yāti brahmaṇo lokaṃ śrāvayedvā dvijottamān
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sṛṣṭivistāro nāma saptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
samāsādvistarāccaiva sargaḥ proktastvayā śubhaḥ
kathaṃ paśupatiścāsītpuraṃ dagdhuṃ maheśvaraḥ
kathaṃ ca paśavaścāsandevāḥ sabrahmakāḥ prabhoḥ
purasya saṃbhavaḥ sarvo varalābhaḥ purā śrutaḥ
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sūtāḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ
yathā śrutaṃ tathā prāha vyāsādviśvārthasūcakāt
sūta uvāca
trailokyasyāsya śāpāddhimanovākkāyasaṃbhavāt
vidyunmālī tārakākṣaḥ kamalākṣaś ca vīryavān
tapastepurmahātmāno mahābalaparākramāḥ
tapasā karśayāmāsurdehān svāndānavottamāḥ
teṣāṃ pitāmahaḥ prīto varadaḥ pradadau varam
daityā ūcuḥ
avadhyatvaṃ ca sarveṣā sarvabhūteṣu sarvadā
tān abravīt tadā devo lokānāṃ prabhur avyayaḥ
anyaṃ varaṃ vṛṇīdhvaṃ vai yādṛśaṃ saṃprarocate
vayaṃ purāṇi trīṇyeva samāsthāya mahīmimām
tathā varṣasahasreṣu sameṣyāmaḥ parasparam
ekībhāvaṃ gamiṣyanti purāṇyetāni cānagha
samāgatāniṃ caitāni yo hanyādbhagavaṃstadā
ekenaiveṣuṇā devaḥ sa no mṛtyurbhaviṣyati
tato mayaḥ svatapasā cakre vīraḥ purāṇyatha
kāñcanaṃ divī tatrāsīdantarikṣe ca rājatam
āyasaṃ cābhavadbhumau puraṃ teṣāṃ mahātmanām
ekaikaṃ yojanaśataṃ vistārāyāmataḥ samam
kāñcanaṃ tārakākṣasya kamalākṣasya rājatam
mayaś ca balavāṃstatra daityadānavapūjitaḥ
hairaṇye rājate caiva kṛṣṇāyasamaye tathā
ālayaṃ cātmanaḥ kṛtvā tavāste balavāṃstadā
evaṃ babhūvurdaityānāmatidurgāṇi suvratāḥ
purāṇi trīṇī viprendrāstrailokyamiva cāparam
nānāprasādasaṃkīrṇaṃ maṇijālaiḥ samāvṛtam
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśairvimānairviśvatomukhaiḥ
śobhitaṃ tripuraṃ teṣāṃ pṛthakpṛthaganuttamaiḥ
divyastrībhiḥ susaṃpūrṇaṃ gandharvaiḥ siddhacāraṇaiḥ
rudrālayaiḥ pratigṛhaṃ sāgnihotrairdvijottamāḥ
vāpīkūpataḍāgaiś ca dīrghikābhistu sarvataḥ
mattamātaṅgayūthaiś ca turaṅgaiś ca suśobhanaiḥ
sabhāprapādibhiś caiva krīḍāsthanaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak
vedādhyayanaśālābhir vividhābhiḥ samantataḥ
adhṛṣyaṃ manasāpyanyairmayasyaiva ca māyayā
pativratābhiḥ sarvatra sevitaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
kṛtvāpi sumahatpāpāmapāpaiḥ śaṅkarārcanāt
daityeśvarairmahābhāgaiḥ sadāraiḥ sasutairdvijāḥ
mahādevetaraṃ tyaktvā devaṃ tasyārcanaṃ sthitaiḥ
vyūḍhoraskairvṛṣaskandhaiḥ sarvāyudhadharaiḥ sadā
sarvadā kṣudhitaiścaiva dāvāgnisadṛśekṣaṇaiḥ
nīlādrimerusaṃkāśairnīradopamaniḥsvanaiḥ
mayena rakṣitaiḥ sarvaiḥ śikṣitairyuddhalālasaiḥ
seṃdrā devā dvijaśreṣṭhā drumā dāvāgninā yathā
athaivaṃ te tadā dagdhā devā deveśvaraṃ harim
sopi nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān cintayāmāsa cetasā
kiṃ kāryaṃ devakāryeṣu bhagavāniti sa prabhuḥ
tadā sasmāra vai yajñaṃ yajñamūrtirjanārdanaḥ
yajvā yajñabhugīśāno yajvanāṃ phaladaḥ prabhuḥ
devaṃ te puruṣaṃ caiva praṇemustuṣṭuvustadā
bhagavānapi taṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñaṃ prāha sanātanam
sanātanastadā sendrāndevāṃ nālokya cācyutaḥ
śrīviṣṇuruvāca
sūta uvāca
siṃhanādaṃ mahatkṛtvā yajñeśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ surāḥ
punaḥ prāha sa sarvāṃstāṃstridaśāṃstridaśeśvaraḥ
hatvā dagdhvā ca bhūtāni bhuktvā cānyāyato 'pi vā
yajedyadi mahādeva mapāpo nātra saṃśayaḥ
apāpā naiva hantavyāḥ pāpā eva na saṃśayaḥ
hantavyāḥ sarvayatnena kathaṃ vadhyāḥ surottamāḥ
asurā durmadāḥ pāpā api devairmahābalaiḥ
kohaṃ brahmāthavā devā daityā devārisūdanāḥ
munayaś ca mahātmānaḥ prasādena vinā prabhoḥ
yaḥ saptaviṃśako nityaḥ parātparataraḥ prabhuḥ
viśvāmareśvaro vandyo viśvādhāro maheśvaraḥ
sa eva sarvadeveśaḥ sarveṣāmapi śaṅkaraḥ
tasyāṃśame kaṃ sampūjya devā devatvam āgatāḥ
dharmaniṣṭhāś ca te sarve śrautasmārtavidhau sthitāḥ
rudramiṣṭvā yathānyāyaṃ jeṣyāmo daityasattamān
satārakākṣeṇa mayena guptaṃ svasthaṃ ca guptaṃ sphaṭikābhamekam
sūta uvāca
evamuktvā hariśceṣṭvā yajñenopasadā prabhum
upaviṣṭo dadarśātha bhūtasaṃghānsahasraśaḥ
śūlaśaktigadāhastān ṭaṅkopalaśilāyudhān
nānāpraharaṇopetānnānāveṣadharāṃstadā
kālāgnirudrasaṃkāśān kālarudropamāṃstadā
prāha devo hariḥ sākṣātpraṇipatyasthitān prabhuḥ
viṣṇuruvāca
tataḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ bhūtasaṃghāḥ puratrayam
praviśya naṣṭāste sarve śalabhā iva pāvakam
tatastu naṣṭāste sarve bhūtā deveśvarājñayā
tuṣṭuvurdevadeveśaṃ paramātmānamīśvaram
tataḥ parājitā devā dhvastavīryāḥ kṣaṇena tu
sendrāḥ saṃgamya deveśamupendraṃ dhiṣṭhitā bhayāt
tāndṛṣṭvā cintayāmāsa bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ
kiṃ kṛtyamiti saṃtaptaḥ saṃtaptānsendrakānkṣaṇam
kathaṃ tu teṣāṃ daityānāṃ balaṃ hatvā prayatnataḥ
devakāryyaṃ kariṣyāmi prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ
pāpaṃ vicārato nāsti dharmiṣṭhānāṃ na saṃśayaḥ
pāpaṃ nudati dharmeṇa dharmeṃ sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
dharmādaiśvaryamityeṣā śrutireṣā sanātanī
daityāścaite hi dharmiṣṭhāḥ sarve tripuravāsinaḥ
tasmādavadhyatāṃ prāptā nānyathā dvijapuṅgavāḥ
pūjasā bhogasaṃpattiravaśyaṃ jāyate dvijāḥ
tasmātte bhogino daityā liṅgārcanaparāyaṇāḥ
tasmātkṛtvā dharmavighnamahaṃ devāḥ svamāyayā
daityānāṃ devākāryārthaṃ jeṣyehaṃ tripuraṃ kṣaṇāt
sūta uvāca
vicāryainaṃ tatasteṣāṃ bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ
kartuṃ vyavasitaścābhūddharmavighnaṃ surāriṇām
asṛjacca mahātejāḥ puruṣaṃ cātmasaṃbhavam
māyī māyāmayaṃ teṣāṃ dharmavighnārthamacyutaḥ
śāstraṃ ca śāstā sarveṣāmakarotkāmarūpadhṛk
sarvasaṃmohanaṃ māyī dṛṣṭapratyayasaṃyutam
etatsvāṅgabhavāyaiva puruṣāyopadiśya tu
māyī māyāmayaṃ śāstraṃ granthaṣoḍaśalakṣakam
puratrayavināśāya prāhaunaṃ puruṣaṃ hariḥ
gantumarhasi nāśāya bho tūrṇaṃ puravā sinām
dharmās tathā pramaśyantu śrautasmārtā na saṃśayaḥ
tataḥ praṇamya taṃ māyī māyāśāstraviśāradaḥ
praviśya tatpuraṃ tūrṇaṃ munirmāyāṃ tadākarot
māyayā tasya te daityāḥ puratrayanivāsinaḥ
śraitaṃ smārtaṃ ca saṃtyajya tasya śiṣyāstadābhavan
tatyajuś ca mahādevaṃ śaṅkaraṃ parameśvaram
nāradopi tadā māyī niyogānmāyinaḥ prabhoḥ
praviśya tatpuraṃ tena māyinā saha dīkṣitaḥ
muniḥ śiṣyaiḥ praśiṣyaiś ca saṃvṛtaḥ sarvataḥ svayam
strīdharmaṃ cākarotstrīṇāṃ duścāraphalasiddhidam
janāsaktā babhūvustā vinindya patidevatāḥ
nāryaścaranti saṃtyajya bhartṝn svairaṃ vṛthādhamāḥ
strīṇāṃ mātā pitā bandhuḥ sakhā mitraṃ ca bāndhavaḥ
bhartā eva na saṃdehastathāpyāsahamāyayā
kṛtvāpi sumahatpāpaṃ yā bhartuḥ premasaṃyutā
puraikāmuniśārdūlāḥ sarvadharmān sadā patim
saṃtyajyāpūjayansādhvyo devānanyāñjagadgurūn
tāḥ svargalokamāsādya modante vigatajvarāḥ
narakaṃ ca jagāmānyā tasmādbhartā parā gatiḥ
tathāpi bhartṝn svāṃs tyaktvā babhūvuḥ svairavṛttayaḥ
māyayā devadevasya viṣṇostasyājñayā prabhoḥ
alakṣmīś ca svayaṃ tasya niyogāttripuraṃ gatā
yā lakṣmīstapasā deṣāṃ labdhā deveśvarādajāt
buddhi mohaṃ tathāmūtaṃ viṣṇumāyāvinirmitam
teṣāṃ dattvā kṣaṇaṃ devastāsāṃ māyī ca nāradaḥ
evaṃ naṣṭe tadā dharme śrautasmārte suśobhane
pāṣaṇḍe khyāpite tena viṣṇunā viśvayoninā
kṛtārtha iva deveśo devaiḥ sārdhamumāpatim
tapasā prāpya sarvajñaṃ tuṣṭāva puruṣottamaḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
nārāyaṇāya śarvāya brahmaṇe brahmarūpiṇe
śāśvatāya hyanantāya avyaktāya ca te namaḥ
sūta uvāca
evaṃ stutvā mahādevaṃ daṇḍavatpraṇipatya ca
jajāpa rudraṃ bhagavānkoṭivāraṃ jale sthitaḥ
devāś ca sarve te devaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ parameśvaram
seṃdrāḥ sasādhyāḥ sayamāḥ sarudrāḥ samarudgaṇāḥ
devā ūcuḥ
namaḥ sarvātmane tubhyaṃ śaṅkarāyārtihāriṇe
tvamādistvamanantaś ca anantaścākṣayaḥ prabhuḥ
prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ sākṣātsraṣṭā hartā jagadguro
trātā netā jagatyasmindvijānāṃ dvijavatsala
varado vāṅmayo vācyo vācyavācakavarjitaḥ
hṛtpuṇḍarīkasuṣire yogināṃ saṃsthitaḥ sadā
vadanti sūrayaḥ saṃtaṃ paraṃ brahmasvarūpiṇam
dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ sthitaṃ sarvaṃ jāyamānaṃ jagadguro
sarvataḥ pāṇipādaṃ tvāṃ sarvatokṣiśiromukham
sarvataḥ śrutimalloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhasi
mahādevamanirdeśyaṃ sarvajñaṃ tvāmanāmayam
viśvarūpaṃ virupākṣaṃ sadāśivam anāmayam
koṭibhāskarasaṃkāśaṃ koṭiśītāṃśusannibham
koṭikālāgnisaṃkāśaṃ ṣaḍviṃśakamanīśvaram
vadānti varadaṃ devaṃ sarvāvāsaṃ svayaṃbhuvam
śrutayaḥ śrutisāraṃ tvāṃ śrutisāravidojanāḥ
adṛṣṭamasmābhir anekamūrte vinā kṛtaṃ yadbhavatātha loke
tvameva daityāsurabhūtasaṃghāndevānnānsthāvarajaṅgamāṃś ca
pāhi nānyā gatiḥ śaṃbho vinihatyāsurottamān
māyayā mohitāḥ sarve bhavataḥ parameśvara
yathā taraṅgā laharīsamūhā yudhyanti cānyonyamapāṃnidhau ca
jalāśrayādeva jaḍīkṛtāś ca surāsurāstadvadajasya sarvam
sūta uvāca
ya idaṃ prātarutthāya sucirbhūtvā japennaraḥ
śṛṇuyādvā stavaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvakāmam avāpnuyāt
śṛṇuyādvā stavaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvakāmamavāpnuyāt
prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā devānālokya śaṅkaraḥ
jñātaṃ mayedamadhunā devakāryaṃ sureśvarāḥ
viṣmormāyābalaṃ caiva nāradasya ca dhīmataḥ
teṣāmadharmaniṣṭhānāṃ daityānāṃ devasattamāḥ
puratrayavināśaṃ ca kariṣyehaṃ surottamāḥ
sūta uvāca
atha sabrahmakā devāḥ seṃdrapendrāḥ samāgatāḥ
śrutvā prabhostadā vākyaṃ praṇemustuṣṭuvuś ca te
līlāṃbujena cāhatya kalamāha vṛṣadhvajam
krīḍamānaṃ vibho paśya ṣaṇmukhaṃ ravisānnibham
putraṃ putravatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bhūpitaṃ bhūṣaṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ
mukuṭaiḥ kaṭakaiścaiva kuṇḍalairvalayaiḥ śubhaiḥ
kalpakadrumajaiḥ puṣpaiḥ śobhitairalakaiḥ śubhaiḥ
hārairvārījarāgādimaṇicitraistathāṅgadaiḥ
tilakaiś ca mahādeva paśya putraṃ suśībhanam
aṅkitaṃ kuṅkumādyaiś ca vṛttaṃ bhasitanirmitam
vakravṛndaṃ ca paśyeśa vṛndaṃ kāmalakaṃ yathā
netrāṇi ca vibho paśya śubhāni tvaṃ śubhāni ca
añjanāni vicitrāṇi maṅgalārthaṃ ca mātṛbhiḥ
gaṅgādībhīḥ kṛttikādyaiḥ svāhayā ca viśeṣataḥ
ityevaṃ lokamātuś ca vāgbhiḥ saṃbodhitaḥ śivaḥ
na yayau tṛptimīśānaḥ pibanskandānanāmṛtam
na sasmāra ca tāndevāndaityaśastranipīḍitān
sopi līlālaso bālo nanartārtiharaḥ prabhuḥ
sahaiva nanṛtuścānve saha tena gaṇeśvarāḥ
trailokyamakhilaṃ tatra nanarteśājñayā kṣaṇam
nāgāś ca nanṛtuḥ sarve devāḥ seṃdrapurogamāḥ
tuṣṭuvurgaṇapāḥ skandaṃ mumodāṃbā ca mātaraḥ
sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi jagurgandharvakinnarāḥ
nṛtyāmṛtaṃ tadā pītvā pārvatīparameśvarau
avā patustadā tṛptiṃ nandinā ca gaṇeśvarāḥ
tataḥ sa nandī saha ṣaṇmukhena tathā ca sārdhaṃ girirājaputryā
viveśa divyaṃ bhavanaṃ bhavopi yathāṃ budo 'nyāṃbudamaṃbudābhaḥ
tuṣṭuvuś ca mahādevaṃ kiñcidudvignacetasaḥ
pāpā vayabhiti hyanye abhāgyāśceti cāpare
bhāgyavantaś ca daityendrā iti cānye sureśvarāḥ
pūjāphalamimaṃ teṣāmityanye neti cāpare
etasminnantare teṣāṃ śrutvā śabdānanekaśaḥ
kuṃbhodaro mahātejā daṇḍenātāḍayatsurān
dudruvuste bhayāviṣṭā devā hāhetivādinaḥ
apatanmunayaścānye devāś ca dharaṇītale
dṛṣṭvāpi devadeveśaṃ devānāṃ cāsuradviṣām
abhāgyānna samāptaṃ tu kāryamityapare dvijāḥ
procurnamaḥ śivāyeti pūjya cālpataraṃ hṛdi
tataḥ kapardi nandīśo mahādevāpriyo muniḥ
śūlī mālī tathā hālī kuṇḍalī valayī gadī
vṛṣamāruhya suśvetaṃ yayau tasyājñayā tadā
tato vai nandinaṃ dṛṣṭvā gaṇaḥ kuṃbhodaro 'pi saḥ
nandī bhāti mahātejā vṛṣapṛṣṭe vṛṣadhvajaḥ
sagaṇo gaṇasenānīrmeghapṛṣṭhe yathā bhavaḥ
daśayojanavistīrṇaṃ muktājālairalaṅkṛtam
sitātapatraṃ śailāderākāśamiva bhāti tat
tatrāntarbaddhamālā sā muktāphalamayī śubhā
gaṅgākāśānnipatitā bhāti mūrdhni vibhoryathā
atha dṛṣṭvā gaṇādhyakṣaṃ devadundubhayaḥ śubhāḥ
niyogādvajriṇaḥ sarve vinedurmunipuṅgavāḥ
tuṣṭuvuś ca gaṇeśānaṃ vāgbhir iṣṭapradaṃ śubham
yathā devā bhavaṃ dṛṣṭvā prītikaṇṭa kitatvacaḥ
niyogādvajriṇo mūrdhni puṣpavarṣaṃ ca khecarāḥ
vṛṣṭyā tuṣṭastadā reje tuṣṭyā puṣṭyā yathārthayā
nandī bhavaścāndrayā tu snātayā gandhavāriṇā
puṣpairnānāvidhaistatra bhāti pṛṣṭhaṃ vṛṣasya tat
saṃkīrṇaṃ tu divaḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ nakṣatrairiva suvratāḥ
kusumaiḥ saṃvṛto nandī vṛṣapṛṣṭhe rarāja saḥ
divaḥ pṛṣṭhe yathā candro nakṣatrairiva suvratāḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nandinaṃ devāḥ sendropendrās tathāvidham
tu ṣṭuvurgaṇapeśānaṃ devadevamivāparam
devā ūcuḥ
kūṣmāṇḍagaṇanāthāya yogināṃ pataye namaḥ
sarvadāya śaraṇyāya sarvajñāyārtihāriṇe
vajriṇe vajradaṃṣṭrāya vajrivajranivāriṇe
vajrālaṅkṛtadehāya vajriṇārādhitāya te
raktānāṃ bhavapādābje rudralokapradāyine
namaḥ senādhipataye rudrāṇāṃ pateya namaḥ
bhūtānāṃ bhuvane śānāṃ pataye pāpahāriṇe
namaḥ śivāya saumyāya rudrabhaktāya te namaḥ
sūta uvacā
tataḥ prīto gaṇādhyakṣaḥ prāha devāṃśchilātmajaḥ
rathaṃ ca sārathiṃ śaṃbhoḥ kārmukaṃ śaramuttamam
atha te brahmaṇā sārdhaṃ tathā vai viśvakarmaṇā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge puradāhe nandikeśvaravākyaṃ nāma ekasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
rathāṅgaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ sūryo vāmāṅgaṃ soma eva ca
dakṣiṇaṃ dvādaśāraṃ hi ṣoḍaśāraṃ tathottaram
areṣu teṣu viprendrāścādityā dvādaśaiva tu
śaśinaḥ ṣoḍaśāreṣu kalā vāmasya suvratāḥ
ṛkṣāṇi ca tadā tasya vamasyaiva tu bhūṣaṇam
nemyaḥ ṣaḍṛtavaścaiva tayorvai viprapuṅgavāḥ
puṣkaraṃ cāntarikṣaṃ vai rathanīḍaś ca mandaraḥ
adhiṣṭhānaṃ mahāmerurāśrayāḥ kesarācalāḥ
muhūrtā bandhurāstasya śamyāścaiva kalāḥ smṛtāḥ
tasya kāṣṭhāḥ smṛtā ghoṇā cākṣadaṇḍā kṣaṇāś ca vai
nimeṣāścānukarṣāś ca īṣā cāsya lavāḥ smṛtāḥ
dharmo virāgo daṇḍosya yajñāṃ daṇḍāśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ
dakṣiṇāḥ saṃdhayastasya lohāḥ pañcāśadagnayaḥ
īṣādaṇḍastathāvyaktaṃ buddhistasyaiva naḍvalaḥ
koṇas tathā hyahaṅkāro bhūtāni ca balaṃ smṛtam
indriyāṇi ca tasyaiva bhūṣaṇāni samantataḥ
kṣaddhā ca gatirasyaiva vedāstasya hayāḥ smṛtāḥ
padāni bhūṣaṇānyeva ṣaḍaṅgānyupabhūṣaṇam
purāṇanyāyamīmāṃsādharmaśāstrāṇi suvratāḥ
vālāśrayāḥ paṭāścaiva sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutāḥ
mantrā ghaṇṭāḥ smṛtāsteṣāṃ varṇāḥ pādāstathāśramāḥ
diśaḥ pādā rathasyāsya tathā copadiśaś ca ha
puṣkarādyāḥ patākāś ca sauvarṇā ratnabhūṣitāḥ
samudrāstasya catvāro rathakaṃbalikāḥ smṛtāḥ
gaṅgādyāḥ saritaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ
cāmarāsaktahastāgrāḥ sarvāḥ strīrūpaśobhitāḥ
tatratatra kṛtasthānāḥ śobhayāñcakrire ratham
āvahādyās tathā sapta sopānaṃ haimamuttamam
sārathirbhagavānbrahmā devābhīṣudharāḥ smṛtāḥ
viṣamaś ca tadābāhyo mānasādriḥ suśobhanaḥ
nāsāḥ samantatastasya sarva evācalāḥ smṛtāḥ
talāḥ kapotāḥ kāpotāḥ sarve talanivāsinaḥ
merureva mahāchatraṃ mandaraḥ pārśvaḍiṇḍimaḥ
śailendraḥ kārmukaṃ caiva jyā bhuñjagādhipaḥ svayam
kaṇṭā sarasvatī devī dhanuṣaḥ śrutirūpiṇī
iṣurviṣṇurmahātejāḥ śalyaṃ somaḥ śarasya ca
kālāgnistaccharasyaiva sākṣāttīkṣṇaḥ sudāruṇaḥ
anīkaṃ viṣasaṃbhūtaṃ vāyavo vājakāḥ smṛtāḥ
evaṃ kṛtvā rathaṃ divyaṃ kārmukaṃ ca śaraṃ tathā
sārathiṃ jagatāṃ caiva brahmāṇaṃ prabhumīśvaram
āruroha rathaṃ divyaṃ raṇamaṇḍanadhṛgbhavaḥ
ṛṣibhiḥ stūyamānaś ca vandyamānaś ca vandibhiḥ
upanṛtyaścāpsarasāṃ gaṇairnṛtyaviśāradaiḥ
śirobhiḥ patitā bhūmīṃ turagā vedasaṃbhavāḥ
athādhastādrathasyāsya bhagavān dharaṇīdharaḥ
vṛṣendrarūpī cotthāpya sthāpayāmāsa vai kṣaṇam
kṣaṇāntare vṛṣendropi jānubhyāmagamaddharām
tatośvāṃścodayāmāsa manomārutaraṃhasaḥ
purāṇyuddiśya khasthāni dānavānāṃ tarasvinām
athāha bhagavān rudro devānālokya śaṅkaraḥ
paśūnāmādhipatyaṃ me dattaṃ hanmi tato 'surān
pṛthakpaśutvaṃ devānāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ surottamāḥ
iti śrutvā vacaḥ sarvaṃ devadevasya dhīmataḥ
viṣādamagaman sarve paśutvaṃ prati śaṅkitāḥ
teṣāṃ bhāvaṃ tato jñātvā devastānidamabravīt
śrūyatāṃ paśubhāvasya vimokṣaḥ kriyatāṃ ca saḥ
paśutvāditi satyaṃ ca pratijñātaṃ samāhitāḥ
ye cāpyanye cariṣyanti vrataṃ pāśupataṃ mama
mokṣyanti te na saṃdehaḥ puśutvātsurasattamāḥ
naiṣṭhikaṃ dvādaśābdaṃvā tadardhaṃ varṣakatrayam
śuśrūṣāṃ kārayedyastu sa paśutvādvimucyate
tasmādvai paśavaḥ sarve devāsuranarāḥ prabhoḥ
rudraḥ paśupatiścaiva paśupāśavimocakaḥ
tatkṛtvā na ca pāpīyāniti śāstrasya niścayaḥ
tato vināyakaḥ sākṣādbālo 'bālaparākramaḥ
apūjitastadā devaiḥ prāha devānnivārayan
śrīvināyaka uvāca
māmapūjya jagatyasmin bhakṣyabhojyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ
kaḥ pumānsiddhimāpnoti devo vā dānavopi vā
tatastasmin kṣaṇādeva devakārye sureśvarāḥ
vighnaṃ kariṣye deveśa kathaṃ karttuṃ samudyatāḥ
tataḥ sendrāḥ surāḥ sarve bhītāḥ saṃpūjya taṃ prabhum
abruvaṃste gaṇeśānaṃ nirvighnaṃ cāstu naḥ sadā
āliṅgya cāghrāya sutaṃ tadānīmapūjayatsarvasurendramukhyaḥ
saṃpūjya pūjyaṃ saha devasaṃghairvināyakaṃ nāyakamīśvarāṇām
taṃ devadevaṃ surasiddhasaṃghā maheśvaraṃ bhūtagaṇāś ca sarve
gaṇeśvarā nandimukhāstadānīṃ svavāhanairanvayurīśamīśāḥ
agre surāṇāṃ ca gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ tadātha nandī girirājakalpam
vimānamāruhya puraṃ prahartuṃ jagāma mṛtyuṃ bhagavāniveśaḥ
yāntaṃ tadānīṃ tu śilādaputramāruhya nāgendravṛṣāśvavaryān
devāstadānīṃ gaṇapāś ca sarve gaṇā yayuḥ svāyudhacihnahastāḥ
surāsureśaṃ sahasraraśmirbhagavānsutīkṣṇaḥ
rarāja madhye bhagavānsurāṇāṃ vivāhano vārijapatravarṇaḥ
yathā sumeroḥ sikharādhirūḍhaḥ sahasraraśmirbhagavānsutīkṣṇaḥ
sahasranetraḥ prathamaḥ surāṇāṃ gajendramāruhya ca dakṣiṇe 'sya
samantatastuṣṭuvuriṣṭadaṃ te jayeti śakraṃ varapuṣpavṛṣṭyā
tadā hyahalyopapatiṃ sureśaṃ jagatpatiṃ diviṣṭhāḥ
apāṃ patistatheśāno bhavaṃ cānusamāgatāḥ
vṛṣabhendraṃ samāruhya romajaiś ca samāvṛtaḥ
mahākālo mahātejā mahādeva ivāparaḥ
vāyavyāṃ sagaṇaiḥ sārvaṃ sevāñcakre rathasya tu
ṣaṇmukhopi saha siddhacāraṇaiḥ senayā ca girirāja saṃnibhaḥ
devanāthagaṇavṛndasaṃvṛto vāraṇena ca tathāgnisaṃbhavaḥ
vighnaṃ gaṇeśopyasureśvarāṇāṃ kṛtvā surāṇāṃ bhagavānavighnam
vighneśvaro vighnagaṇaiś ca sārdhaṃ taṃ deśamīśānapadaṃ jagāma
kālī tadā kālaniśāprakāśaṃ śūlaṃ kapālābharaṇā kareṇa
prakaṃpayantī ca tadā suredrānmahāsurāsṛṅmadhupānamattā
mattebhagāmī madalolanetrā mattaiḥ piśācaiś ca gaṇaiś ca mattaiḥ
mattebhacarmāṃbaravoṣṭitāṅgī yayau purastācca gaṇeśvarasya
tāṃ siddhagandharvapiśācayakṣavidyādharāhīndrasurendramukhyāḥ
mātaraḥ suravarisūdanāḥ sādaraṃ suragaṇaiḥ surūjitāḥ
durgārūḍhamṛgādhipā duratigā dordaṇḍavṛndaiḥ śivā bibhrāṇāṅkuśaśulapāśaparaśuṃ cakraāsiśaṅkhāyudham
taṃ devamīśaṃ tripuraṃ nihantuṃ tadā tu devendraraviprakāśāḥ
gajairhayaiḥ siṃhavarai rathaiś ca vṛṣairyayuste gaṇarājamukhyāḥ
halaiś ca phaālairmusalairbhuśurṃbhuśuṇḍairgirīndrakūṭairgirisannibhāste
yayuḥ purastāddhi maheśvarasya sureśvarā bhūtagaṇeśvarāś ca
tathendrapadmodbhavaviṣṇumukhyāḥ surā gaṇeśāś ca gaṇeśamīśam
jayeti vāgbhir bhagavantamūcuḥ kirīṭadattāñjalayaḥ samantāt
nanṛturmunayaḥ sarve daṇḍahastā jaṭādharāḥ
vavṛṣuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
gaṇeśvarair devagaṇaiś ca bhṛṅgī sahāvṛtaḥ sarvagaṇendravaryaḥ
jagāma yogī tripuraṃ nihantuṃ vimānamāruhya yathā mahendraḥ
keśo vigatavāsāś ca mahākeśo mahājvaraḥ
somadhṛk sūryavācaś ca sūryapeṣaṇakas tathā
sūryākṣaḥ sūrināmā ca suraḥ suṃdara eva ca
prakṛdaḥ kakudantaś ca kaṃpanaś ca prakaṃpanaḥ
śatākṣaścaiva pañcākṣaḥ sahasrākṣo mahodaraḥ
yamajihvaḥ śatāśvaś ca kaṇṭhanaḥ kaṇṭhapūjanaḥ
dviśikhastriśikhaścaiva tathā pañcaśikho dvijāḥ
muṇḍordhamuṇḍo dīrghaś ca piśācāsyaḥ pinākadhṛk
pippalāyatanaścaiva tathā hyaṅgārakāśanaḥ
śithilaḥ śithilāsyaś ca akṣapādo hyajaḥ kujaḥ
ityādyāḥ parivāryeśaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitāḥ
vṛndaśastaṃ samāvṛtya jagmuḥ somaṃ gaṇairvṛtāḥ
sahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi rudrāṇāmūrdhvaretasām
samāvṛtya mahādevaṃ devadevaṃ maheśvaram
dagdhuṃ puratrayaṃ jagmuḥ koṭikoṭigaṇairvṛtāḥ
trayastriṃ śatsurāścaiva trayaś ca triśatās tathā
mātaraḥ sarvalokānāṃ gaṇānāṃ caiva mātaraḥ
bhūtānāṃ mātaraścaiva jagmurdevasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
bhāti madhye gaṇānāṃ ca rathamadhye gaṇeśvaraḥ
nabhasyamalanakṣatre tārāmadhya ivoḍurāṭ
rarāja devī devasya girijā pārśvasaṃsthitā
śubhāvatī tadā devī pārśvasaṃsthā vibhāti sā
cāmarāsaktahastāgrā sā hemāṃbujavarṇikā
bhātīndradhanuṣākāśaṃ meruṇā ca yathā jagat
hiraṇyadhanuṣā saumyaṃ vapuḥ śaṃbhoḥ śaśidyuti
sitātapatraṃ ratnāṃśumiśritaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
yathodaye śaśāṅkasya bhātyakhaṇḍaṃ hi maṇḍalam
sadukūlā śive raktā laṃbitā bhāti mālikā
chatrāntā ratnajākāśātpatantīva saridvarā
dagdhuṃ samartho manasā kṣaṇena carācaraṃ sarvamidaṃ triśūlī
kimatra dagdhuṃ tripuraṃ pinākī svayaṃ gataścātra gaṇaiś ca sārdham
rathena kiṃ ceṣuvareṇa tasya gaṇaiś ca kiṃ devagaṇaiś ca śaṃbhoḥ
manvāma nūnaṃ bhagavānpinākī līlārthametatsakalaṃ pravartum
vyavasthitaśceti tathānyathā cedāḍaṃbareṇāsya phalaṃ kimanyat
gaṇairgaṇeśastu rarāja devyā jagadratho merurivāṣṭaśṛṅgaiḥ
atha nirikṣya sureśvaramīśvaraṃ sagaṇamadrisutāsahitaṃ tadā
atha sajyaṃ dhanuḥ kṛtvā śarvaḥ saṃdhāya taṃ śaram
yuktvā pāśupatāstreṇa tripuraṃ samacintayat
babhūva tumulo harṣo devatānāṃ mahātmanām
tato devagaṇāḥ sarve siddhāś ca paramarpayaḥ
jayeti vāco mumucuḥ saṃstuvanto 'ṣṭamūrtinam
puṣyayogopi saṃprāpte līlāvaśamumāpatim
sthāne tava mahādeva ceṣṭeyaṃ parameśvara
pūrvadevāś ca devāś ca samāstava yataḥ prabho
tathāpi devā dharmiṣṭhāḥ pūrvadevāś ca pāpinaḥ
iṣuṇā bhūtasaṃghaiś ca viṣṇunā ca mayā prabho
dagdhumarhasi śīghraṃ tvaṃ trīṇyetāni purāṇi vai
puratrayaṃ virūpākṣastatkṣaṇādbhasma vai kṛtam
somaś ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ kālāgnirvāyureva ca
asmaddhitārthaṃ deveśa śaraṃ moktumihārhasi
mumoca bāṇaṃ viprendrā vyākṛṣyākarṇamīśvaraḥ
tatkṣaṇāttripuraṃ dagdhvā tripurāntakaraḥ śaraḥ
devadevaṃ samāsādya namaskṛtvā vyavasthitaḥ
ye pūjayanti tatrāpi daityā rudraṃ sabāndhavāḥ
gāṇapatyaṃ tadā śaṃbhoryayuḥ pūjāvidherbalāt
na kiñcidabruvandevāḥ seṃdropendrā gaṇeśvarāḥ
bhayāddevaṃ nirīkṣyaiva devīṃ himavataḥ sutām
dṛṣṭvā bhītaṃ tadānīkaṃ devānāṃ devapuṅgavaḥ
kiṃ cetyāha tadā devānpraṇemustaṃ samantataḥ
tuṣṭāva hṛdaye brahmā devaiḥ saha samāhitaḥ
viṣṇunā ca bhavaṃ devaṃ tripurārātimīśvaram
śrīpitāma uvāca
prasīda jagatāṃ nātha prasīdānandadāvyaya
pañcāsya rudrarudrāya pañcāśatkoṭimūrtaye
ātmatrayopaviṣṭāya vidyātattvāya te namaḥ
śivāya śivatattvāya aghorāya namonamaḥ
aghorāṣṭakatattvāya dvādaśātmasvarūpiṇe
vidyutkoṭipratīkāśamaṣṭakāśaṃ suśobhanam
rūpamāsthāya lokesmin saṃsthitāya śivātmane
agnivarṇāyaraudrāya aṃbikārdhaśarīriṇe
dhavalaśyāmaraktānāṃ muktidāyāmarāya ca
jyeṣṭhāya rudrarūpāya somāya varadāya ca
trilokāya tridevāya vaṣaṭkārāya vai namaḥ
aṣṭakṣetrāṣṭarūpāya aṣṭatattvāya te namaḥ
pañcadhā pañcadhā caiva pañcamantraśarīriṇe
catuḥṣaṣṭiprakārāya akārāya namonamaḥ
dvātriṃśattatvarūpāya ukārāya namonamaḥ
ṣoḍaśātmasvarūpāya makārāya namonamaḥ
aṣṭadhātmasvarūpāya ardhamātrātmane namaḥ
oṅkārāya namastubhyaṃ caturdhā saṃsthitāya ca
gaganeśāya devāya svargeśāya namo namaḥ
saptalokāya pātālanarakeśāya vai namaḥ
aṣṭakṣetrāṣṭarūpāya parātparatarāya ca
sahasrapādayuktāya śarvāya parameṣṭhine
navātmatattvarūpāya navāṣṭātmātmaśaktaye
punaraṣṭaprakāśāya tathāṣṭāṣṭakamūrtaye
catuḥṣaṣṭyātmatattvāya punaraṣṭavidhāya te
guṇāṣṭakavṛtāyaiva guṇine nirguṇāya te
mūlastāya namastubhyaṃ śāsvatasthānavāsine
nābhimaṇḍalasaṃsthāya hṛdi niḥsvanakāriṇe
candrabibasthitāyaiva śivāya śivarūpiṇe
vahnisomārkarūpāya ṣaṭtriṃśacchaktirūpiṇe
triprakāraṃ stitāyaiva tretāgnimayarūpiṇe
sadāśivāya śāntāya maheśāya pinākine
sarvajñāya śaraṇyāya sadyojātāya vai namaḥ
tatpuruṣāya namostu īśānāya namonamaḥ
namastriṃśatprakāśāya śāntātītāya vai namaḥ
ananteśāya sūkṣmāya uttamāya namostu te
namastrimūrtaye tubhyaṃ śrīkaṇṭhāya śikhaṇḍine
anantāsanasaṃsthāya anantāyāntakāriṇe
vimalāya viśālāya vimalāṅgāya te namaḥ
vimalāsanasaṃsthāya vimalārthārtharūpiṇe
yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthāya sadā nīvāraśūkavat
pratyāhārāya te nityaṃ pratyāhāraratāya te
pratyāhāraratānāṃ ca pratisthānasthitāya ca
dhāraṇāyai namastubhyaṃ dhāraṇābhiratāya te
dhāraṇābhyāsayuktānāṃ purastātsaṃsthitāya ca
dhyānāya dhyānarūpāya dhyānagamyāya te namaḥ
samādhānābhigamyāya samādhānāya te namaḥ
samādhānaratānāṃ tu nirvikalpārtharūpiṇe
kastotumicchetkathamīdṛśaṃ tvāṃ steṣyeha tuṣṭāya śivāya tubhyam
ete gaṇāḥ siddhagaṇaiḥ praṇāmaṃ kurvāti deveśa gaṇeśa tubhyam
līlālasenāṃbikayā kṣaṇena dagdhaṃ kileṣuś ca tadātha muktaḥ
kṛto rathaścaiṣuvaraś ca śubhraṃ śarasanaṃ te tripurakṣayāya
anekayatnaiś ca mayātha tubhyaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ phalaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ surasiddhasaṃghaiḥ
anaṃpāda stvamanantabāhuranantamūrdhāntakaraḥ śivaś ca
anantamūrtiḥ kathamīdṛśantvaṃ toṣyaṃ kathamīdṛśaṃ tvām
stūlāya sūkṣmāya susūkṣmasūkṣmasūkṣmāya sūkṣmārthavide vidhātre
sraṣṭre namaḥ sarvasurāsurāṇāṃ bhartre ca hartre jagatāṃ vidhātre
netre surāṇāmasureśvarāṇāṃ dātre praśāstre mama sarvaśāstre
ādyantaśūnyāya ca saṃsthitāya tathā tvaśūnyāya ca liṅgine ca
aliṅgine liṅgamayāya tubhyaṃ ligāya vedādimayāya sākṣāt
rudrāya mūrdhānanikṛntanāya mamādi devasya ca yajñamūrteḥ
vidhvāntabhaṅgaṃ mama kartumīśa dṛṣṭvaiva bhūmau karajāgrakoṭyā
dehīva devaiḥ saha devakāryaṃ kariṣyase nirgumīśa dṛṣṭvaiva bhūmau karajāgrakoṭyā
ekaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmamekaṃ susūkṣmaṃ sūrtāmūrtaṃ mūrtamekaṃ hyamūrtam
ekaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vāṅmayaṃ caikamīśaṃ dhyeyaṃ caikaṃ tattvamatrādbhutaṃ te
svapne dṛṣṭaṃ yatpadārthaṃ hyalakṣyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ nūnaṃ bhāti manye na cāpi
tathāpi bhaktyā vilapantamīśa pitāmahaṃ māṃ bhagavankṣamasva
sūta uvāca
ya imaṃ śṛṇuyāddvijottamā bhuvi devaṃ praṇipatya paṭhet
śrutvā ca bhaktyā caturānanena stuto hasañśailasutāṃ nirīkṣya
stavaṃ tadā prāha mahānubhāvaṃ mahābhujo mandaraśṛṅgavāsī
śiva uvāca
varān varaya bhadraṃ te devānāṃ ca yathopsitān
sūta uvāca
tataḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ bhagavānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā prāhedaṃ prītamānasaḥ
śrīpitāmaha uvāca
devānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ tvayī sarvārthadeśvara
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā prāha sāṃbaṃ triyaṃbakam
vāhanatvaṃ taveśāna nityamīhe prasīda me
sāmarthyaṃ ca sadā mahyaṃ bhavantaṃ voḍhumīśvaram
sūta uvāca
tayoḥ śrutvā mahādevo vijñaptiṃ parameśvaraḥ
sārdhaṃ devyā nandinā bhūsaṃghairantardhānaṃ kārayāmāsa śarvaḥ
tatastadā maheśvare gate raṇādgaṇaiḥ saha
sureśvarāḥ suvismitā bhavaṃ praṇamya pārvatīm
yayuś ca duḥkhavarjitāḥ svavāhanairdivaṃ tataḥ
sureśvarā munīśvarā gaṇeśvarāś ca bhāskarāḥ
tripurārerimaṃ puṇyaṃ nirmitaṃ brahmaṇā purā
yaḥ paṭhecchrāddhakāle vā daive karmaṇi ca dvijāḥ
mānasairvācikaiḥ kāpais tathā vai kāyikaiḥ punaḥ
sthūlaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ susūkṣmaiś ca mahāpātakasaṃbhavaiḥ
pātakaiś ca dvijaśreṣṭhā upapātakasaṃbhavaiḥ
pāpaiś ca mucyate jantuḥ śrutvādhyāyamimaṃ śubham
śatravo nāśamāyānti saṃgrāme vijayībhavet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge tripuradāhe brahmastavo nāma dvisaptitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
gate maheśvare deve dagdhvā ca tripuraṃ kṣaṇāt
sadasyāha suredrāṇāṃ bhagavānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ
pitāmaha uvāca
saṃtyajya deva deveśaṃ liṅgamūrti maheśvaram
tārakākṣopi ditijaḥ kamalākṣaś ca vīryavān
vidyunmālī ca daityeśaḥ anye cāpi sabāndhavāḥ
tyaktvā devaṃ mahādevaṃ māyayā ca hareḥ prabhoḥ
sarve vinaṣṭāḥ pradhvastāḥ svapuraiḥ purasaṃbhavaiḥ
tasmātsadā pūjanīyo liṅgamūrtiḥ sadāśivaḥ
yāvatpūjā sureśānāṃ tāvadeva sthitiryataḥ
pūjanīyaḥ śivo nityaṃ śraddhayā devapuṅgavaiḥ
tasmātsaṃpūjayelliṅgaṃ ya icchetsiddhimātmanaḥ
sarve liṅgārcanādeva devā daityāś ca dānavāḥ
yakṣā vidyādharāḥ siddhā rākṣasāḥ piśitāśanāḥ
pitaro munayaścāpi piśācāḥ kinnarādayaḥ
arcayitvā liṅgamūrti saṃsiddhā nātra saṃśayaḥ
tasmālliṅgaṃ yajennityaṃ yena kenāpi vā surāḥ
paśutvaṃ ca parityajya kṛtvā pāśupataṃ tataḥ
pūjanīyo mahādevo liṅgamūrtiḥ sanātanaḥ
viśodhya caiva bhūtāni pañcabhiḥ praṇavaiḥ samam
prāṇāyāmaiḥ samāyuktaiḥ pañcabhiḥ surapuṅgavāḥ
caturbhiḥ praṇavaiścaiva prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇaiḥ
tribhiś ca praṇavairdevāḥ prāṇāyāmaistathāvidhaiḥ
dvidhā nyasya tathoṅkāraṃ prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇaḥ
tataścoṅkāramuccārya prāṇāpānau niyamya ca
jñānāmṛtena sarvāṅgānyāpūrya praṇavena ca
guṇatrayaṃ caturdhākhyam ahaṅkāraṃ ca suvratāḥ
tanmātrāṇi ca bhūtāni tathā buddhīndriyāṇi ca
karmendriyāṇi saṃśodhya puruṣaṃ yugalaṃ tathā
cidātmānaṃ tanuṃ kṛtvā cāgnirbhasmeti saṃspṛśet
triyāyuṣaṃ trisaṃdhyaṃ ca dhūlayedbhasitena yaḥ
bhavena pāśamokṣārthaṃ kathitaṃ devasattamāḥ
evaṃ pāśupataṃ kṛtvā saṃpūjya parameśvaram
liṅge purā mayā dṛṣṭe viṣṇunā ca mahātmanā
paśavo naiva jāyante varṣamātreṇa devatāḥ
asmābhiḥ sarvakāryāṇāṃ devamabhyarcya yatnataḥ
pratijñā mama viṣṇoś ca divyaiṣā surasattamāḥ
munīnāṃ ca na saṃdehastasmātsaṃpūjayecchivam
sā hānistanmahacchidraṃ sa mohaḥ sā ca mūkatā
yatkṣaṇaṃ vā muhūrtaṃ vā śivamekaṃ na cintayet
bhavanāni manojñāni divyamābharaṇaṃ striyaḥ
dhanaṃ vā tuṣṭiparyantaṃ śivapūjāvidheḥ phalam
ye vāñchanti mahābhogān rājyaṃ ca tridaśālaye
ter'cayantu sadā kālaṃ liṅgamūrtiṃ maheśvaram
yajedekaṃ virūpākṣaṃ na pāpaiḥ sa pralipyate
śailaṃ liṅgaṃ madīyaṃ hi sarvadevanamaskṛtam
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhir devadevaṃ triyaṃbakam
tadāprabhṛti śakraādyāḥ pūjayāmāsurīśvaram
sākṣātpāśupataṃ kṛtvā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge brahmaproktaliṅgārcanavidhirnāma trisaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
liṅgāni kalpayitvaivaṃ svādhikārānurūpataḥ
viśvakarmā dadau teṣāṃ niyogādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ
indranīlamayaṃ liṅgaṃ viṣṇunā pūjitaṃ sadā
padmarāgamayaṃ śakro haimaṃ viśravasaḥ sutaḥ
viśvedevās tathā raupyaṃ vasavaḥ kāntikaṃ śubham
ārakūṭamayaṃ vāyuraśvinau pārthivaṃ sadā
sphaāṭikaṃ varuṇo rājā ādityāstāmranirmitam
mauktikaṃ somarāḍ dhīmāṃs tathā liṅgamanuttamam
anantādyā mahānāgāḥ pravālakamayaṃ śubham
daitya hyoyamayaṃ ligaṃ rākṣasāś ca mahātmanaḥ
trailohikaṃ guhyakāś ca sarvalohamayaṃ gaṇāḥ
cāmuṇḍā saikataṃ sākṣānmātaraś ca dvijottamāḥ
dārujaṃ nairṛtirbhaktyā yamo mārakataṃ śubham
nīlādyāś ca tathā rudrāḥ śuddhaṃ bhasmamayaṃ śubham
lakṣmīvṛkṣamayaṃ lakṣmīrguho vai gomayātmakam
munayo munisārdūlāḥ kuśāgramayamuttamam
vāmādyāḥ puṣpaliṅgaṃ tu gandhaliṅgaṃ manonmanī
ugrā piṣṭamayaṃ sarve mantrā hyājyamayaṃ śubham
vedāḥ sarve dadhimayaṃ piśācāḥ sīsanirmitam
ṣaḍvidhaṃ liṅgamityāhurdravyāṇāṃ ca prabhedataḥ
teṣāṃ bhedāścaturyuktacatvāriṃśaditi smṛtāḥ
tṛtīyaṃ dhātujaṃ liṅgamaṣṭadhā parameṣṭhinaḥ
turīyaṃ dārujaṃ liṅgaṃ tattu ṣoḍaśadhocyate
mṛnmayaṃ pañcamaṃ liṅgaṃ dvidhā bhinnaṃ dvijottamāḥ
ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu kṣaṇikaṃ liṅgaṃ saptadhā parikīrtitam
śrīprada ratnajaṃ liṅgaṃ śailajaṃ sarvasiddhidam
dhātujaṃ dhanadaṃ sākṣāddārujaṃ bhogasiddhidam
bahudhā liṅgabhejāś ca nava caiva samāsataḥ
mūle brahmā tathā madhye viṣṇustribhuvaneśvaraḥ
rudropari mahādevaḥ pramavākhyaḥ sadāśivaḥ
liṅgavedī mahādevī triguṇā trimayāṃbikā
śailajaṃ ratnajaṃ vāpi dhātujaṃ vāpi dārujam
mṛnmayaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ vāpi bhaktyā sthāpya phalaṃ śubham
suredrāṃbhojagarbhāgniyamāṃbupadhaneśvaraiḥ
stūyamānaḥ supuṇyātmā devadundubhiniḥsvanaiḥ
liṅgasthāpanasanmārganihitasvāyatāsinā
āśu brahmāṇḍamudbhidyanirgacchannirviśaṅkayā
śailajaṃ ratnajaṃ vāpi dhātujaṃ vāpi dārujam
mṛnmayaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ tyaktvā sthāpayetsakalaṃ vapuḥ
vidhinā caiva kṛtvā tu skandomāsahitaṃ śubham
kudagokṣīrasaṃkāśaṃ liṅgaṃ yaḥ sthāpayennaraḥ
nṛṇāṃ tanuṃ samāsthāya sthito rudro na saṃśayaḥ
darśanātsparśanāttasya labhante nirvṛtiṃ narāḥ
sarveṣāmeva martyānāṃ vibhordivyaṃ vapuḥ śubham
sakalaṃ bhāvanāyogyaṃ yogināmeva niṣkalam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivaliṅgabhedasaṃsthāpanādivarṇanaṃnāma catuḥsaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ yathā pūrvaṃ yathā śrutam
sūta uvāca
paramārthavidaḥ kecidūcuḥ praṇavarūpiṇam
vijñānamiti viprendrāḥ śrutvā śrutiśirasyajam
śabdādiviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ jñānamityabhidhīyate
yajjñānaṃ nirmalaṃ śuddhaṃ nirvikalpaṃ nirāśrayam
guruprakāśakaṃ jñānamityanye munayo dvijāḥ
dyaurmūrdhā tu vibhostasya khaṃ nābhiḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
somasūryāgnayo netre diśaḥ śrotraṃ mahātmanaḥ
caraṇau caiva pātālaṃ samudrastasya cāṃbaram
devāstasya bhujāḥ sarve nakṣatrāṇi ca bhūṣaṇam
vattrādvai brāhmaṇāḥ sarve brahmā ca bhagavānprabhuḥ
indropendrau bhujābhyāṃ tu kṣatriyāś ca mahātmanaḥ
vaiśyāścorupradeśāttu śūdrāḥ pādātpinākinaḥ
puṣkarāvartakādyāstu keśāstasya prakīrtitāḥ
vāyavo ghrāṇajāstasya gatiḥ śrautaṃ smṛtis tathā
puṃsāṃ tu puruṣaḥ śrīmān jñānagamyo na cānyathā
dhyānayajñātparo nāsti dhyānaṃ jñānasya sādhanam
yadā samarase niṣṭho yogī dhyānena paśyati
dhyānayajñaratasyāsya tadā saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ
nāsti vijñānināṃ śaucaṃ prāyaścittādi codanā
viśuddhā vidyayā sarve brahmavidyāvido janāḥ
nāsti kriyā ca lokeṣu sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ vicārataḥ
dharmādharmau japo homo dhyānināṃ saṃnidhiḥ sadā
parānandātmakaṃ liṅgaṃ viśuddhaṃ śivamakṣaram
niṣkalaṃ sarvagaṃ jñeyaṃ yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthitam
liṅgaṃ tu dvividhaṃ prāhurbāhyamābhyantaraṃ dvijāḥ
bāhyaṃ sthūlaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sūkṣmamābhyantaraṃ dvijāḥ
karmayajñaratāḥ sthūlāḥ sthūlaliṅgārcaneratāḥ
asatāṃ bhāvanārthāya nānyathā sthūlavigrahaḥ
ādhyātmikaṃ ca yalliṅgaṃ pratyakṣaṃ yasya no bhavet
jñānināṃ sūkṣmamamalaṃ bhavetpratyakṣamavyayam
yatā sthūlamayuktānāṃ mṛtkāṣṭhādyauḥ prakalpitam
niṣkalaḥ sakalaśceti sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ tataḥ
vyomaikamapi dṛṣṭaṃ hi śarāvaṃ prati suvratāḥ
pṛthaktvaṃ cāpṛthaktvaṃ ca śaṅkarasyeti cāpare
ekopi bahudhā dṛṣṭo jalādhāreṣu suvratāḥ
jantavo divi bhūmā ca sarve vai pāñcabhautikāḥ
tathāpi bahulā dṛṣṭā jātivyaktivibhedataḥ
bhedo janānāṃ lokesminpratibhāso vicārataḥ
duḥkhī ca bhegaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca nānubhūtaṃ vicārataḥ
hṛdi saṃsāriṇāṃ sākṣātsakalaḥ parameśvaraḥ
yogināṃ niṣkalo devo jñānināṃ ca jaganmayaḥ
tṛtīyaṃ sakalaṃ caiva nānyatheti dvijottamāḥ
sakalaṃ munayaḥ kecitsadā saṃsāravartinaḥ
evamabhyarcayantyeva sadārāḥ sasutānarāḥ
yathā śivas tathā devī yathā devī tathā śivaḥ
daśāre dvādaśāre ca ṣoḍaśāre trirasrake
sa svecchayā śivaḥ sākṣāddevyā sārdhaṃ sthitaḥ prabhuḥ
saṃtāraṇārthaṃ ca śivaḥ sadasadvyaktivarjitaḥ
ūcus tathā taṃ ca śivaṃ tathānye saṃsāriṇaṃ vedavido vadanti
bhaktyā ca yogena śubhena yuktā viprāḥ sadā dharmaratā viśiṣṭāḥ
te yānti cainaṃ na ca yogino 'nye tayā ca devyā puruṣaṃ purāṇam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivādvaitakathanaṃ nāma pañcasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
pratiṣṭhāyāḥ phalaṃ sarvaṃ sarvalokahitāya vai
skandomāsahitaṃ devamāsīnaṃ paramāsane
kṛtvā bhakyā pratiṣṭhāpya sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt
skandomāsahitaṃ devaṃ saṃpūjya vidhinā sakṛt
sūryakoṭipratikāśairvimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ
rudrakanyāsamākīrṇairgayanāṭyasamanvitaiḥ
śivavatkrīḍate yogī yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ
aumaṃ kaumāramaiśānaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmameva ca
prājāpatyaṃ mahātejā janalokaṃ mahas tathā
eendramāsādya caidratvaṃ kṛtvā varṣāyutaṃ punaḥ
merumāsādya devānāṃ bhavaneṣu pramodate
ekapādaṃ caturbāhuṃ trinetraṃ śūlasaṃyutam
sṛṣṭvā sthitaṃ harīṃ vāme dakṣiṇe caturānanam
aṣṭāviṃśatirudrāṇaāṃ koṭiḥ sarvāṅgasuprabham
pañcaviṃśatikaṃ sākṣātpuruṣaṃ hṛdayāttathā
prakṛtiṃ vāmataścaiva buddhiṃ vai buddhideśataḥ
ahaṅkāramahaṅkārāttanmātrāṇi tu tatra vai
indriyāṇīndriyādeva līlayā parameśvaram
pṛthivīṃ pādamūlāttu guhyadeśājjakaṃ tathā
nābideśāttathā vahniṃ hṛdayādbhāskaraṃ tathā
kaṇṭhātsomaṃ tathātmānaṃ bhrūmadhyānmastakāddivam
sṛṣṭaivaṃ saṃsthitaṃ sākṣājjagatsarvaṃ carācaram
sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ devaṃ kṛtvā vidyāvidhānataḥ
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
tripādaṃ saptahastaṃ ca catuḥśṛṅgaṃ dviśīrṣakam
kṛtvā yajñeśamīśānaṃ viṣṇuloke mahīyate
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogānkalpalakṣaṃ sukhīnaraḥ
vṛṣārūḍhaṃ tu yaḥ kuryātsomaṃ somārdhabhūṣaṇam
hayamedhāyutaṃ kṛtvā yatpuṇyaṃ tadāvāpya saḥ
kāñcanena vimānene kiṅkiṇījālamālinā
nandinā sahitaṃ devaṃ sābaṃ sarvagaṇairvṛtam
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśairvimānaivṛṣasaṃyutaiḥ
apsaro gaṇasaṃkīrṇairdevadānavadurlabhaiḥ
nṛtyādbhir apsaraḥ saṃghaiḥ sarvataḥ sarvaśaubhitaiḥ
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt
nṛtyantaṃ devadeveśaṃ śailajāsahitaṃ prabhum
sahasrabāhuṃ sarvajñaṃ caturbāhumathāpi vā
bhṛgvādyairbhūtasaṃghaiś ca saṃvṛtaṃ parameśvaram
śailajāsahitaṃ sākṣādvṛṣabhadhvajamīśvaram
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya yatphalaṃ tadvadāmyaham
tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ labdhvā yāti śivaṃ padam
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvadā bhūtasaṃplavam
sṛṣṭyantare punaḥ prāpte mānavaṃ padamāpnuyāt
kapālahastaṃ deveśaṃ kṛṣṇakuñcitamūrdhajam
kṛtvā bhakyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
ibhendradārakaṃ devaṃ sāṃbaṃ siddhārthadaṃ prabhum
sudhūmravarṇaṃ raktākṣaṃ trinetraṃ candrabhūṣaṇam
kākapakṣadharaṃ mūrdhnā nāgaṭaṅkadharaṃ haram
siṃhājinottarīyaṃ ca mṛgacarmāṃbaraṃ prabhum
tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ gadāhastaṃ kapālodyatapāṇinam
huṃphaṭkāre mahāśabdaśabditākhiladiṅmukham
puṇḍarīkājinaṃ dorbhyāṃ bibhrantaṃ kaṃbukaṃ tathā
hasaṃtaṃ ca nadantaṃ ca pibantaṃ kṛṣṇasāgaram
nṛtyantaṃ bhūtasaṃghaiś ca gaṇasaṃghaistvalaṅkṛtam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvibhava vistaram
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam
strīpuṃbhāvena saṃsthānaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivaloke mahīyate
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogānaṇimādiguṇairyutaḥ
ācandratārakaṃ jñānaṃ tato labdhvā vimucyate
yaḥ kuryāddevadeveśaṃ sarvajñaṃ lakulīśvaram
vṛtaṃ śiṣyapraśiṣyaiś ca vyākhyānodyatapāṇinam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivalokaṃ sa gacchati
bhuktvā tu vipulāṃstatra bhogān yugaśataṃ naraḥ
pūrvadevāmarāṇāṃ ca yatsthānaṃ sakalepsitam
tripuṇḍradhāriṇasteṣāṃ śiromālādharasya ca
brahmaṇaḥ keśakenaikamupavītaṃ ca bibhrataḥ
viṣṇoḥ kalevaraṃ caiva bibhrataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya mucyate bhavasāgarāt
oṃnamo nīlakaṇṭhāya iti puṇyākṣarāṣṭakam
mantramāha sakṛdvā yaḥ pātakaiḥ sa vimucyate
mantreṇānenaṃ gandhādyairbhaktyā vittānusārataḥ
saṃpūjya devadeveśaṃ śivaloke mahīyate
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya dvidhābhūtaṃ jalandharam
prayāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
sudarśanapradaṃ devaṃ sākṣātpūrvoktalakṣaṇam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivaloke mahīyate
tiṣṭhatotha nikuṃbhasya pṛṣṭhataścaraṇāṃbujam
vāmetaraṃ suvinyasya vāme cāliṅgya cādrijām
śūlāgre kūrparaṃ sthāpya kiṅkiṇī kṛtapannagam
saṃprekṣya cāndhakaṃ pārśve kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam
rūpaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
yaḥ kuryāddevadeveśaṃ tripurāntakamīśvaram
dhanurbāṇasamāyuktaṃ somaṃ somārdhabhūṣaṇam
tadākāratayā sopi gatvā śivapuraṃ sukhī
krīḍate nātra saṃdeho dvitīya iva śaṅkaraḥ
gaṅgādharaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ candraśekharameva ca
gaṅgayā sahitaṃ caiva vāmotsaṃgeṃbikānvitam
vināyakaṃ tathā skandaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ durgāṃ suśobhanām
bhāskaraṃ ca tathā somaṃ brahmāṇīṃ ca maheśvarīm
kaumārīṃ vaiṣṇavaīṃ devaīṃ vārāhīṃ vāradāṃ tathā
indrāṇīṃ caiva cāmuṇḍāṃ vīrabhadrasamanvitām
vighneśena ca yo dhīmān śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
liṅgamūrtiṃ mahājvālamālāsaṃvṛtamavyayam
vyomnikuryāttathā liṅgaṃ brahmāṇaṃ haṃsarūpiṇam
viṣṇuṃ varāharūpeṇa liṅgasyādhastvadhomukham
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe tasya kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
kṣetrasaṃrakṣakaṃ devaṃ tathā pāśupataṃ prabhum
kṛtvā bhaktyā yathānyāyaṃ śivaloke mahīyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivamūrtipratiṣṭhāphalakathanaṃ nāma ṣaṭsaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
liṅgapratiṣṭhāpuṇyaṃ ca liṅgasthāpanameva ca
liṅgānāṃ caiva bhedāś ca śrutaṃ tava mukhādiha
mṛdādiratnaparyantairdravyaiḥ kṛtvā śivālayam
sūta uvāca
tathāpi bhaktāḥ parameśvarasya kṛtveṣṭaloṣṭairapi rudralokam
bālyāttu loṣṭena ca kṛtvā mṛdāpi vā pāṃsubhir ādidevam
gṛhaṃ ca tādṛgvidhamasya śaṃbhoḥ saṃpūjya rudratvamavāpnuvanti
kesaraṃ nāgaraṃ vāpi drāvīḍaṃ vā tathāparam
kṛtvā rudrālayaṃ bhaktyā śivaloke mahīyate
kailāsākhyaṃ ca yaḥ kuryātprāsādaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
kailāsaśikharākārair vimānair modate sukhī
mandaraṃ vā prakurvīta śivāya vidhipūrvakam
mandarādripratīkāśairvimānairviśvatomukhaiḥ
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇairdevadānavadurlabhaiḥ
gatvā śivapuraṃ ramyaṃ bhuktvā bhogān yathepsitān
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya gāṇapatyaṃ labhennaraḥ
yaḥ kuryānmerunāmānaṃ prāsādaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
niṣadhaṃ nāma yaḥ kuryātprāsādaṃ bhaktitaḥ sudhīḥ
kuryādvā yaḥ śubhaṃ viprā himaśailamanuttamam
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt
nīlādriśikharākhyaṃ vā prāsādaṃ yaḥ suśobhanam
kṛtvā vittānusāreṇa bhaktyā rudrāya śaṃbhave
mahendraśailanāmānaṃ prāsādaṃ rudrasaṃmatam
mahendraparvatākārairvimānairvṛṣasaṃyutaiḥ
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ bhuktvā bhogānyathepsitān
jñānaṃ vicāritaṃ rudraiḥ saṃprāpya munipuṅgavāḥ
viṣayān viṣapattyaktvā śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
hemnā yastu prakṛrvīta prāsādaṃ ratnaśobhitam
dravīḍaṃ nāgaraṃ vāpi kesaraṃ vā vidhānataḥ
kūṭaṃ vā maṇḍapaṃ vāpi samaṃ vā dīrgham eva ca
jīrṇaṃ vā patitaṃ vāpi khaṇḍitaṃ sphuṭitaṃ tathā
pūrvavatkārayedyastu dvārādyaiḥ suśubhaṃ dvijāḥ
prasādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ vāpi prākāraṃ gopuraṃ tu vā
karturapyadhikaṃ puṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
vṛttyarthaṃ vā prakurvīta naraḥ karma śivālaye
yaḥ sa yāti na saṃdehaḥ svargalokaṃ sabāndhavaḥ
tasmād āyatanaṃ bhaktyā yaḥ kuryān munisattamāḥ
kāṣṭheṣṭakādibhir martyaḥ śivaloke mahīyate
prasādārtha maheśasya prāsāde munipuṅgavāḥ
aśaktaścenmuniśreṣṭhāḥ prāsādaṃ kartumuttamam
saṃmārjanādibhir vāpi sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt
saṃmārjanaṃ tu yaḥ kuryānmārjanyā mṛdusūkṣmayā
yaḥ kuryādvastrapūtena gandhagomayavāriṇā
ālepanaṃ yathānyāyaṃ varṣacāndrāyaṇaṃ labhet
ardhakrośaṃ śivakṣetraṃ śivaliṅgātsamantataḥ
yas tyajed dustyajān prāṇāñ śivasāyujyam āpnuyāt
svāyaṃbhuvasya mānaṃ hi tathā bāṇasya suvratāḥ
svāyaṃbhuve tadardhaṃ syātsyādārṣe ca tadardhakam
mānuṣe ca tadardhaṃ syātkṣetramānaṃ dvijottamāḥ
evaṃ yatīnāmāvāse kṣetramānaṃ dvijottamāḥ
rudrāvatāre cādyaṃ yacchiṣye caiva praśiṣyake
narāvatāre tacciṣye catchiṣye ca praśīṣyake
śrīparvate mahāpuṇye tasya prānte ca vā dvijāḥ
tasminvā yastyajetprāṇāñchivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
vārāṇasyāṃ tathāpyevamavimukte viśeṣataḥ
kedāre ca mahākṣetre prayāge ca viśeṣataḥ
kurukṣetra ca yaḥ prāṇānsaṃtyajedyāti nirvṛtim
prabhāse puṣkare 'vantyāṃ tathā caivāmareśvare
vaṇīśelākule caiva mṛto yāti śivātmatām
vārāṇasyāṃ mṛto janturna jātu jantutāṃ vrajet
śālake vā tyajetprāṇāṃs tathā vai jaṃbukeśvare
śukreśvare vā gokarṇe bhāskareśe guheśvare
hiraṇyagarbhe nandīśe sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
sa yāti śivatāṃ yogī mānuṣe devīkepi vā
ārṣe vāpi muniśreṣṭhās tathā svāyaṃbhuvepi vā
svayaṃbhūte tathā deve nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
ādhāyāgniṃ śivakṣetre saṃpūjya parameśvaram
svadeha piṇḍaṃ juhuyādyaḥ sa yāti parāṃ gatim
yāvattāvannirāhāro bhūtvā prāmānparityajet
śivakṣetre muniśreṣṭhāḥ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
chittvā pādadvayaṃ cāpi śivakṣetre vasettu yaḥ
sa yāti śivatāṃ caiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
kṣetrasya darśanaṃ puṇyaṃ praveśastaccha tādhikaḥ
tasmācchataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ sparśanaṃ ca pradakṣiṇam
tasmācchataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ jalasnānamataḥ param
kṣīrasnānaṃ tato viprāḥ śatādhikamanuttamam
ghṛtasnānena cānantaṃ śārkare tacchatādhikam
śivakṣetrasamīpasthāṃ nadīṃ prāpyāvagāhya ca
tyajeddehaṃ vihāyānnaṃ śivaloke mahīyate
śivakṣetrasamīpasthā nadyaḥ sarvāḥ suśobhanāḥ
vāpīkūpataḍāgāś ca śivatīrthā iti smṛtāḥ
snātvā teṣu naro bhaktyā tīrtheṣu dvijasattamāḥ
brahmahatyādibhiḥ pāpairmucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
prātaḥ snātvā muniśreṣṭhāḥ śivatīrtheṣu mānavaḥ
madhyāhne śivatīrtheṣu snātvā bhaktyā sakṛnnaraḥ
gaṅgāsnānasamaṃ puṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
pāpakañcukamutsṛjya śivatīrtheṣu mānavaḥ
dvijās triṣavaṇaṃ snātvā śivatīrthe sakṛ naraḥ
śivasāyujyamāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
purātha sūkaraḥ kaścit śvānaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhayātpathi
prasaṃgādvāramekaṃ tu śivatīrthe 'vagāhya ca
mṛtaḥ svayaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhā gāṇapatyamavāptavān
yaḥ prātardevadeveśaṃ śivaṃ liṅgasvarūpiṇam
madhyāhne ca mahādevaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñaphalaṃ labhet
sāyāhne sarvayajñānāṃ phalaṃ prāpya vimucyate
mānasairvācikaiḥ pāpaiḥ kāyikaiś ca mahattaraiḥ
tathopapātakaiścaiva pāpaiścaivānupātakaiḥ
saṃkrame devamīśānaṃ dṛṣṭvā liṅgākṛtiṃ prabhum
māsena yatkṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tyaktvā yāti śivaṃ padam
ayane cārdhamāsena dakṣiṇe cottarāyaṇe
viṣuve caiva saṃpūjya prayāti paramāṃ gatim
pradakṣiṇātrayaṃ kuryādyaḥ prāsādaṃ samantataḥ
savyāpasavyanyāyena mṛdugatyā śucirnaraḥ
vācā yastu śivaṃ nityaṃ saṃrauti parameśvaram
sopi yāti śivaṃ sthānaṃ prāpya kiṃ punareva ca
kṛtvā maṇḍalakaṃ kṣetraṃ gandhagomayavāriṇā
padmarāgamayaiścaiva sphaāṭikaiś ca suśobhanaiḥ
ālikhyā kamalaṃ bhadrandaśahastapramāṇataḥ
sakarṇikaṃ mahābhāgā mahādevasamīpataḥ
pañcabhicca tathā ṣaḍbhir aṣṭābhiśceṣṭadaṃ param
punaraṣṭābhir īśānaṃ daśāre daśabhis tathā
punarbāhye ca daśabhiḥ saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca
śālipiṣṭādibhir vāpi padmamālikhya nirdhanaḥ
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ puṇyaṃ labhate nātra śaṃśayaḥ
dvādaśāraṃ tathālikhya maṇḍalaṃ padammuttamam
ratnacūrṇādibhiścūrṇais tathā dvādaśamūrtibhiḥ
grahaiś ca saṃvṛtaṃ vāpi sūryasāyujyamuttamam
evaṃ prākṛtamapyāryāṃ ṣaḍasraṃ parikalpya ca
madhyadeśe ca deveśīṃ prakṛtiṃ brahmarūpiṇīm
dakṣiṇe sattvamūrtiṃ ca vāmataś ca rajoguṇam
agratastu tamomūrtiṃ madhye devīṃ tathāṃbikām
pañcabhūtāni tanmātrāpañcakaṃ caiva dakṣiṇe
ātmānaṃ cāntarātmānaṃ yugalaṃ buddhimeva ca
ahaṅkāraṃ ca mahatā sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet
evaṃ vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ prākṛtaṃ maṇḍalaṃ param
ato vakṣyāmi viprendrāḥ sarvakāmārthasādhanam
alaṅkṛtya vitānādyaiśchatrairvāpi manoramaiḥ
sitamṛtpātrakaiścaiva suślakṣṇaiḥ pūrṇakuṃbhakaiḥ
pañcāśaddīpamālābhir dhūpaiḥ pañcavidhais tathā
tattadvarṇais tathā cūrṇaiḥ śvetacūrṇairathāpi vā
ekahastapramāṇena kṛtvā padmaṃ vidhānataḥ
karṇikāyāṃnyeseddevaṃ devyā deveśvaraṃ bhavam
praṇavādinamontāni sarvavarṇāni suvratāḥ
saṃpūjyaivaṃ muniśreṣṭhā gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra pañcāśadvidhipūrvakam
akṣamālopavītaṃ ca kuṇḍalaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum
āsanaṃ ca tathā daṇḍamuṣṇīṣaṃ vastrameva ca
datvā teṣāṃ munīndrāṇāṃ devadevāya śaṃbhave
mahācaruṃ nivedyaivaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ gomithunaṃ tathā
ante ca devadevāya dāpayeccūrṇamaṇḍalam
oṅkārādyaṃ japeddhīmānprativarṇamanukramāt
sāṃgānvedānyathānyāyamadhītya vidhipūrvakam
iṣṭvā yajñairyathānyāyaṃ jyotiṣṭomādibhiḥ kramāt
tato viśvajidantaiś ca putrānutpādya tādṛśān
vānaprasthāśramaṃ gatvā sadāraḥ sāgnireva ca
cāndrāyaṇādikāḥ sarvāḥ kṛtvā nyasya kriyā dvijāḥ
brahmavidyāmadhītyaiva jñānamāsādya yatnataḥ
jñānena jñenamālokya yogī yatkāmamāpnuyāt
tatphalaṃ labhate sarvaṃ varṇamaṇḍaladarśanāt
yena kenāpi vā martyaḥ pralipyāyatanāgrataḥ
uttare dakṣiṇe vāpi pṛṣṭhato vā dvijottamā
catuṣkoṇaṃ tu vā cūrṇairalaṅkṛtya samantata
puṣpākṣatādibhiḥ pūjya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
prārthayeddevamīśānaṃ śivalokaṃ sa gacchati
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogānkalpakoṭiśataṃ naraḥ
kramādgāndharvamāsādya gandharvaiś ca supūjitaḥ
kramādāgatya loke 'smin rājā bhavati vīryavān
sargaś ca bhuvanādhīśaḥ śarvavyāpī sadāśivaḥ
śivabrahmāmṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ mokṣasādhana muttamam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge upalepanādikathanaṃ nāma saptasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
śivakṣetra muniśreṣṭhā nānyathā siddhiriṣyate
āpaḥ pūtā bhavantyetā vastrapūtāḥ samuddhṛtāḥ
aphenā munisārdūlā nādeyāś ca viśeṣataḥ
tasmādvai sarvakāryāṇi daivikāni dvijottamāḥ
adbhiḥ kāryāṇi pūtābhiḥ sarvakāryaprasiddhaye
jantubhir miśritā hyāpaḥ sūkṣmābhistānnihatya tu
yatpāpaṃ sakalaṃ cādbhir apūtābhiściraṃ labhet
saṃmārjane tathā nṝṇāṃ mārjane ca viśeṣataḥ
hiṃsā sadā sṛhasthānāṃ tasmāddhiṃsāṃ vivarjayet
ahiṃseyaṃ paro dharmaḥ sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ dvijāḥ
manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvadāhiṃsakaṃ naram
tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ labhate 'hiṃsako naraḥ
manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ
kāryamabhyukṣaṇaṃ nityaṃ snapanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
śivāryaṃ sarvadā kāryā puṣpahiṃsā dvijottamāḥ
yajñārthaṃ paśuhiṃsā ca kṣatriyairduṣṭaśāsanam
vihitāvihitaṃ nāsti yogināṃ brahmavādinām
yatastasmānna hantavyā niṣiddhānāṃ niṣevaṇāt
na hantavyāḥ sadā pūjyāḥ pāpakarmaratā api
pavitrāstu striyaḥ sarvā atreś ca kulasaṃbhavāḥ
brahmahatyāsamaṃ pāpamātreyīṃ vinihatya ca
striyaḥ sarvā na hantavyāḥ pāpakarmaratā api
na yajñārthaṃ striyo grāhyāḥ sarvaiḥ sarvatra sarvadā
sarvavarṇeṣu viprendrāḥ pāpakarmaratā api
malinā rūpavatyaś ca virupā malināṃbarāḥ
na hantavyāḥ sadā martyaiḥ śivavaccaṅkayā tathā
vedabāhyavratācārāḥ śrautasmārtabahiṣkṛtāḥ
pāṣaṇḍina iti khyātā na saṃbhāṣyā dvijātibhiḥ
na spṛṣṭavyā na draṣṭavyā dṛṣṭvā bhānuṃ samīkṣate
prasaṃgādvāpi yo martyaḥ satāṃ sakṛdaho dvijāḥ
bhavānti duḥkhitāḥ sarve nirdayā munisattamāḥ
putreṣu dāreṣu gṛheṣu nṝṇāṃ bhaktaṃ yathā cittamathādideve
sakṛtprasaṃgādyatitāpasānāṃ teṣāṃ na dūraḥ parameśalokaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge bhaktimahimāvarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
saṃvatsarasahasraiś ca tapasā pūjya śaṅkaram
na paśyanti surāścāpi kathaṃ devaṃ yajanti te
sūta uvāca
kathitaṃ tathya mevātra yuṣmābhir munipuṅgavāḥ
tathāpi śraddhayā dṛśyaḥ pūjyaḥ saṃbhāṣya eva ca
prasaṃgāccaiva saṃpūjya bhaktihīnairapi dvijāḥ
bhāvānurūpaphalado bhagavāniti kīrtitaḥ
ucchiṣṭaḥ pūjayanyāti paiśācaṃ tu dvijādhamaḥ
saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ sthānaṃ prāpnuyānmūḍhadhīrdvijāḥ
abhakṣyabhakṣī saṃpūjya yākṣaṃ prāpnoti durjanaḥ
gānaśīlaś ca gāndharvaṃ nṛtyaśīlastathaiva ca
khyātiśīlas tathā cāndraṃ strīṣu sakto narādhamaḥ
madārtaḥ pūjayan rudraṃ somasthānamavāpnuyāt
brāhmaṃ hi praṇavenaiva vaiṣṇavaṃ cābhinandya ca
saṃśodhya ca śubhaṃ liṅgam amarāsurapūjitam
jalaiḥ pūtaistatā pīṭhe devamāvāhya bhaktitaḥ
dṛṣṭvā devaṃ yathānyāyaṃ praṇipatya ca śaṅkaram
pādyamācamanaṃ cārghyaṃ dattvā rudrāya śaṃbhave
tataḥ śuddhāṃbunā snāpya candanādyaiś ca pūjayet
rocanādyaiś ca saṃpūjya divyapuṣpaiś ca pūjayet
nīlotpalaiś ca rājīvairnadyāvartaiś ca mallikaiḥ
caṅkapairjātipuṣpaiścavakulaiḥ karavīrakaiḥ
apāmārgakadaṃbaiś ca bhūṣaṇairapi śobhanaiḥ
dattvā pañcavidhaṃ dhūpaṃ pāyasaṃ ca nivedayet
śuddhānnaṃ caiva mudgānnaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ ca nivedayet
kevalaṃ cāpi śuddhānnamāḍhakaṃ taṇḍulaṃ pacet
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ cānte namaskṛtya muhurmuhuḥ
stutvā ca devamīśānaṃ punaḥ saṃpūjya śaṅkaram
īśānaṃ puruṣaṃ caiva aghoraṃ vāmameva ca
sadyojātaṃ japaṃścāpi pañcabhiḥ pūjayecchivam
vṛkṣāḥ puṣpādipatrādyairupayuktāḥ śivārcane
gāvaścaiva dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ prayānti paramāṃ gatim
pūjayedyaḥ śivaṃ rudraṃ śarvaṃ bhavamajaṃ sakṛt
arcitaṃ parameśānaṃ bhavaṃ śarvamumāpatim
sakṛtprasaṃgādvā dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
pūjitaṃ vā mahādevaṃ pūjyamānamathāpi vā
dṛṣṭvā prayāti vai martyo brahmalokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
śrutvānumodayeccāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
yo dadyāddhṛtadīpaṃ ca sakṛlliṅgasya cāgrataḥ
sa tāṃ gatim avāpnoti svāśramair durlabhāṃ sthirām
dīpavṛkṣaṃ pārthivaṃ vā dāravaṃ vā śivālaye
dattvā kulaśataṃ sāgraṃ sivaloke mahīyate
āyasaṃ tāmrajaṃ vāpi raupyaṃ sauvarṇikaṃ tathā
śivāya dīpaṃ yo dadyādvidhinā vāpi bhaktitaḥ
sūryāyutasamaiḥ ślakṣṇairyānaiḥ śivapuraṃ vrajet
kārtike māsi yo dadyaddhṛtadīpaṃ śivāgrataḥ
saṃpūjyamānaṃ vā paśyedvidhinā parameśvaram
sa yāti brahmaṇo lokaṃ śraddhayā munisāttamāḥ
āvāhanaṃ susānnidhyaṃ sthāpanaṃ pūjanaṃ tathā
saṃproktaṃ rudragāyatryā āsanaṃ praṇavena vai
pañcabhiḥ snapanaṃ proktaṃ rudrādyaiś ca viśeṣataḥ
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe tasya praṇavena samarcayet
uttare devadeveśaṃ viṣṇuṃ gāyatriyā yajet
vahnau hutvā yathānyāyaṃ pañcabhiḥ praṇavena ca
sa yāti śivasāyujyamevaṃ saṃpūjya śaṅkaram
vyāsena kathitaḥ pūrvaṃ śrutvā rudramukhātsvayam
iti śrīlaṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivārcanavidhirnāmaikānāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ paśupatiṃ dṛṣṭvā paśupāśavimokṣaṇam
sūta uvāca
hitāya sarvadevānāṃ brahmaṇā ca janārdanaḥ
seṃdrāḥ sasādhyāḥ sayamāḥ praṇemur girimuttamam
bhagavān vāsudevo 'sau garuḍād garuḍadhvajaḥ
sakaladuritahītaṃ sarvadaṃ bhogamukhyaṃ muditakuraravṛndaṃ nāditaṃ nāgavṛndaiḥ
madhuraraṇitagītaṃ sānukūlāndhakāraṃ padaracitavanāntaṃ kāntavātāntatoyam
gireḥ pṛṣṭhe paraṃ śārvaṃ kalpitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
krīḍārthaṃ devadevasya bhavasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
apaśyaṃstatpuraṃ devāḥ seṃdropendrāḥ samāhitāḥ
praṇemurdūrataścaiva prabhāvādeva śūlinaḥ
jagāma kailāsagiriṃ mahātmā meruprabhāge puramādidevaḥ
gaṇairgaṇeśaiś ca girīndrasannibhaṃ mahāpuradvāramajo hariś ca
atha jāṃbūnadamayairbhavanairmaṇibhūṣitaiḥ
vimānairvividhākāraiḥ prākāraiś ca samāvṛtam
dṛṣṭvā śaṃbhoḥ puraṃ bāhyaṃ devaiḥ sabrahmakairhariḥ
prahṛṣṭavadano bhūtvā praviveśa tataḥ puram
harmyaprāsādasaṃbādhaṃ mahāṭṭālasamanvitam
vajravaiḍūryamāṇikyamaṇijālaiḥ samāvṛtam
dolāvikṣepasaṃyuktaṃ ghaṇṭācāmarabhūṣitam
mṛdaṅgamurajairjuṣṭaṃ vīṇāveṇunināditam
nṛtyadbhir apsaraḥsaṃghair bhūtasaṃghaiś ca saṃvṛtam
prāsādaśṛṅgeṣvatha pauranāryaḥ sahasraśaḥ puṣpaphalākṣatādyaiḥ
dṛṣṭvā nāryastadā viṣṇuṃ madāghūrṇitalocanāḥ
viśālajaghanāḥ sadyo nanṛturmumudurjaguḥ
kāściddṛṣṭvā hariṃ nāryaḥ kiñcitprahasitānanāḥ
kiñcidvasrastavastrāś ca srastakāñcīguṇājaguḥ
caturthaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca saptamaṃ tathā
aṣṭamaṃ navamaṃ caiva daśamaṃ ca purottamam
atītyāsādya devasya puraṃ śaṃbhoḥ suśobhanam
suvṛttaṃ sutarāṃ śubhraṃ kailāsaśikhare śubhe
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśairvimānaiś ca vibhūṣitam
sphaāṭikairmaḍapaiḥ śubhrairjāṃbūnadamayais tathā
nānāratnamayaiścaiva digvidikṣu vibhūṣitam
gopurairgopateḥ śaṃbhornānābhūṣaṇabhūṣitaiḥ
prākārairvividhākārairaṣṭāviṃśatibhir vṛtam
upadvārairmahādvārairvidikṣu vividhairdṛḍhaiḥ
grāmyair anyair mahābhāgā mauktikair dṛṣṭimohanaiḥ
candanairvividhākāraiḥ puṣpodyānaiścaśaubhanaiḥ
taḍāgairdirghikābhiś ca hemasopānapaṅktibhiḥ
strīṇāṅgatijitairhaṃsaiḥ sevitābhiḥ samantataḥ
mayūraiścaiva kāraṇḍaiḥ kokilaiścakravākakaiḥ
śobhitābhiś ca vāpībhir divyāmṛtajalais tathā
saṃlāpālāpakuśalaiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ
stanabārāvanamraiś ca madāghūrṇitalocanaiḥ
rudrastrīgamasaṃkīrṇairjalakrīḍāratais tathā
dṛṣṭvā vismayamāpannāstasthurdevāḥ samantataḥ
tatraiva dadṛśurdevā vṛndaṃ rudragaṇasya ca
gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ vīrāṇāmapi vṛndaṃ sahasraśaḥ
suvarṇakṛtasopānān vajravaiḍūrya bhūṣitān
sphaāṭikān devadevasya dadṛśuste vimānakān
teṣāṃ śṛṅgeṣu hṛṣṭāś ca nāryaḥ kamalalocanāḥ
viśālajaghanā yakṣā gandharvāpsarasas tathā
kinnaryaḥ kiṃnarāścaiva bhujaṅgāḥ siddhakanyakāḥ
nānaveṣadharāścānyā nānābhūṣaṇabhūṣitāḥ
nānāprabhāva saṃyuktā nānābhogaratipriyāḥ
nīlotpaladalaprakhyāḥ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇāḥ
padmakiñjalkasaṃkāśairaṃśukairatiśobhanāḥ
valayairnūpurairhāraiśchatraiścitraistathāṃśukaiḥ
bhūṣitā bhūṣitaiścānyairmāṇḍitā maṇḍanapriyāḥ
dṛṣṭvātha vṛndaṃ surasuṃdarīṇāṃ gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ surasuṃdarīṇām
jagmurgaṇeśasya puraṃ sureśāḥ puradviṣaḥ śakrapurogamāś ca
dṛṣṭvā ca tasthuḥ surasiddhasaṃghāḥ purasya madhye puruhūtapūrvāḥ
nandinaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarve devāḥ sakrapurogamāḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nandinaṃ sarve pramamyāhurgaṇeśvaram
jayeti devāstaṃ dṛṣṭvā sopyāha ca gaṇaiśvaraḥ
bho bho devā mahābhāgāḥ sarve nirdhūtakalmaṣāḥ
saṃprāptāḥ sarvalokesā vaktumarhatha suvratāḥ
paśupāśavimokṣārthaṃ darśayāsmān maheśvaram
purā puratrayaṃ dagdhuṃ paśutvaṃ paribhāṣitam
śaṅkitāś ca vayaṃ tatra paśutvaṃ prati suvrata
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ proktaṃ bhavena parameṣṭhinā
atha dvādaśavarṣaṃ vā māsadvādaśakaṃ tu vā
dinadvādaśakaṃ vāpi kṛtvā tadbratamuttamam
darśayāmāsa tāndevānnārāyaṇapurogamān
nandī śilādatanayaḥ sarvabhūtagaṇāgraṇīḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā devamīśānaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyayam
praṇemustuṣṭuvuśvaiva prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ
vijñāpya śitikaṇṭhāya paśupāśavimokṣaṇam
tasthustadāgrataḥ śaṃbhoḥ praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ
tataḥ saṃprekṣya tān sarvāndevadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ
viśodhya teṣāṃ devānāṃ paśutvaṃ parameśvaraḥ
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caiva svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ
upadiśya munīnāṃ ca sahāste cāṃbayā bhavaḥ
tadāprabhṛti te devāḥ sarve pāśupatāḥ smṛtāḥ
paśūnāṃ ca patiryasmātteṣāṃ sākṣāddhi devatāḥ
tasmātpāśupatāḥ proktāstapastepuś ca te punaḥ
tato dvādaśavarṣānte mukta pāśāḥ surottamāḥ
yayuryathāgataṃ sarve brahmaṇā saha viṣṇunā
purā sanatkumāreṇa tasmādvyāsena dhīmatā
yaḥ śrāvayecchrucirviprāñchṛṇuyādvā śucirnaraḥ
sa dehabhedamāsādya paśupāśaiḥ pramucyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pāśupatavratamāhātmyaṃ nāmāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vratametattvayā proktaṃ paśupāśavimokṣaṇam
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ laiṅgaṃ purā devair anuṣṭhitam
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ tvayā śrutam
sūta uvāca
purā sanatkumāreṇa pṛṣṭaḥ śailādirādarāt
vrataṃ dvādaśaliṅgākhyaṃ paśupāśavimokṣaṇam
aviyogakaraṃ puṇyaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhayanāśanam
ṣaḍaṅgasahitān vedānmathitvā tena nirmitam
sarvadānottamaṃ puṇyamaśvamedhāyutādhikam
sarvamaṅgaladaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvaśatruvināśanam
saṃsārarṇavamagnānāṃ jantūnāmapi mokṣadam
devairanuṣṭhitaṃ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā
kṛtvākanīyasaṃ liṅgaṃsnāpya candanavāriṇā
caitramāsādi viprendrāḥ śivaliṅgavrataṃ caret
kṛtvā haimaṃ śubhaṃ padmaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam
karṇikāyāṃ nyaselliṅgaṃ sphaāṭikaṃ pīṭhasaṃyutam
śvetārkakarṇikāraiś ca karavīrairbakairapi
etairanyair yathālābhaṃ gāyatryā tasya suvratāḥ
saṃpūjya caiva gandhādyairdhūpairdīpaiś ca maṅgalaiḥ
nīrājanādyaiścānyaiś ca liṅgamūrti maheśvaram
agaruṃ dakṣiṇe dadyādaghoreṇa dvijottamāḥ
paścime sadyamantreṇa divyāṃ caiva manaḥśilām
puruṣeṇa muniśreṣṭhā haritālaṃ ca pūrvataḥ
sitāgarūdbhavaṃ viprās tathā kṛṣṇāgarūdbhavam
sitāraṃ nāma dhūpaṃ ca dadyadīśāya bhaktitaḥ
mahācarurnivedyaḥ syādāḍhakānnamathāpi vā
etadvāḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ śivaliṅgamahāvratam
sarvamāseṣu sāmānyaṃ viśeṣopi ca kīrtyate
vaiśākhe vajraliṅgaṃ ca jyeṣṭhe mārakataṃ tathā
āṣāḍhaṃ mauktikaṃ liṅgaṃ śrāvaṇe nīlanirmitam
māsi bhādrapade liṅgaṃ padmarāgamayaṃ śubham
āśvine caiva viprendrāḥ gomedakamayaṃ śubham
pravalenaiva kārtikyāṃ tathā vai mārgaśīrṣake
vaiḍūlyanirmitaṃliṅgaṃ puṣparāgeṇa puṣyake
alābhe rājataṃ vāpi ke valaṃ kamalaṃ tu vā
ratnānāmpayalābhe tu hemnā vā rājatena vā
śailaṃ vā dārujaṃ vāpi mṛnmayaṃ vā savedikam
sarvagandhamayaṃ vāpi kṣāṇikaṃ parikalpayet
haimantike mahādevaṃ śrīpatreṇaiva pūjayet
tadardhārdhena vā rudramaṣṭottaraśatena vā
bilvapatre sthitā lakṣmīrdevī lakṣaṇasaṃyutā
nīlotpaleṃbikā sākṣādutpale ṣaṇmukhaḥ svayam
padmāśritā mahādevaḥ sarvadevapatiḥ śivaḥ
nīlotpalaṃ cotpalaṃ ca kamalaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
sarvavaśyakaraṃ padmaṃ śilā sarvārthasiddhidā
kṛṣṇāgarusamudbhutaṃ sarvapāpanikṛntanam
gugguluprabhṛtīnāṃ caiva dīpānāṃ ca nivedanam
saugandhikaṃ tathā dhūpaṃ sarvakāmārthasādhakam
śvetagarūdbhavaṃ caiva tathā kṛṣṇāgarūdbhavam
saumyaṃ sītāridhūpaṃ ca sākṣānnirvāṇasiddhidam
śvetārkakusume sākṣāccaturvattraḥ prajāpatiḥ
karṇikārasya kusume medhā sākṣādvyavasthitā
karavīre gaṇādhyakṣo bake nārāyaṇaḥ svayam
tasmādetairyathālābhaṃ puṣpadhūpādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ
pūjayeddevadeveśaṃ bhaktyā vittānusārataḥ
śuddhānnaṃ vāpi mudgānnamāḍhakaṃ cārdhakaṃ tu vā
upahārāṇi puṇyāni nyāyenaivārjitānyapi
nānāvidhāni cārhāṇi prokṣitānyaṃbhasā punaḥ
kṣīrādvai sarvadevānāṃ sthityarthamamṛtaṃ dhruvam
viṣṇunā jiṣṇunā sākṣādanne sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
bhūtānāmannadānena prītirbavati śaṅkare
tasmātsaṃpūjayeddevamanne prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
upahāre tathā tuṣṭirvyañjane pavanaḥ svayam
pīṭhe vai prakṛtiḥ sākṣānmahadādyairvyavasthitā
paurṇamāsyāṃvrataṃ kāryaṃ sarvakāmārthasiddhaye
satyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā śāntiḥ saṃtoṣo dānameva ca
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāmupavāsaṃ ca kārayet
saṃvatsarānte godānaṃ vṛṣotsargaṃ viśeṣataḥ
bhojayedbrāhmaṇānbhaktyā śrotriyān vedapāragān
sthāpayed vā śivakṣetre dāpayed brāhmaṇāya vā
ya evaṃ sarvamāseṣu śivaliṅgamahāvratam
kuryādbhaktyā muniśreṣṭhāḥ sa eva tapatāṃ varaḥ
sūryakoṭipratīkāśairvimānai ratnabhūṣitaiḥ
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ nehāyāti kadācana
śivalokamavāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
varṣamekaṃ caredevaṃ tāṃstānprāpya śivaṃvrajet
devatvaṃ vā pitṛtvaṃ vā devarājatvameva ca
vidyārthī labhate vidyāṃ bhogārthi bhogamāpnuyāt
dravyārthī ca nidhiṃ paśyedāyuḥkāmaścirāyuṣam
yānyāṃścintayate kāmāṃstāṃstānprāpyeha modate
idaṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ rahasyaṃ vratottamaṃ viśvasṛjāpi sṛṣṭam
hitāya devāsurasiddhamartyavidyādharāṇāṃ paramaṃ śivena
saṃpūjya pūjyaṃ vidhinaivamīśaṃ praṇamya mūrdhnā saha bhṛtyaputraiḥ
vyapohanaṃ nāma japetstavaṃ ca pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtya śivaṃ prayatnāt
purākṛtaṃ viśvasṛjā stavaṃ ca hitāya devena jagattrayasya
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge paśupāśavimocanaliṅgapūjādikathanaṃ nāmaikāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
nandinaś ca mukhācchrutvā kumāreṇa mahātmanā
vyāsāya kathitaṃ tasmādbahumānena vai mayā
namaḥ śivāya śuddhāya nirmalāya yaśasvine
duṣṭāntakāya sarvāya bhavāya paramātmane
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
sarvajña sarvagaḥ śāntaḥ sarvopari susaṃsthitaḥ
padmāsanasthaḥ someśaḥ pāpamāśu vyapohatu
īśānaḥ puruṣaścaiva aghoraḥ sadya eva ca
vāmadevaś ca bhagavānpāpamāśu vyapohatu
anantaḥ sarvavidyeśaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvadaḥ prabhuḥ
śivadhyānaikasaṃpannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
sūkṣmaḥ surāsureśāno viśveśo gaṇapūjitaḥ
śivadhyānaikasaṃpannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
śivottamo mahāpūjyaḥ śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
sarvagaḥ sarvadaḥ śāntaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
ekāśro bhagavānīśaḥ śivārcanaparāyaṇaḥ
