śivadhyānaikasaṃpannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
trimūrtir bhagavān īśaḥ śivabhaktiprabodhakaḥ
śivadhyānaikasaṃpannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
śrīkaṇṭhaḥ śrīpatiḥ śrīmāñśivadhyānarataḥ sadā
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
trailokyanamitā devī solkākārā purātanī
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
trailokyanamiti devī solkākārā purātanī
dākṣāyaṇī mahādevī bhaurī haimavatī śubhā
ekaparṇāgrajā saumyā tathā vai caikapāṭalā
aparṇāvaradā devī varadānaikatatparā
umā suraharā sākṣātkauśikī vā kapardinī
khaṭvāṅgadhāriṇī divyā karāgratarupallavā
menāyā nandinī devī vārijā vārijekṣaṇā
aṃbāyā vītaśokasya nandinaś ca mahātmanaḥ
śubhāvatyāḥ sakhī śāntā pañcacūḍā varapradā
sṛṣṭyarthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ prakṛtitvaṃ gatāvyayā
manonmanī mahādevī māyāvī maṇḍanapriyā
māyayā yā jagatsarvaṃ brahmādyaṃ sacarācaram
kṣobhiṇī mohinī nityaṃ yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthitā
ekānekasthitā loke indīvaranibhekṣaṇā
saṃstutā jananī teṣāṃ sarvopadravanāśinī
bhaktānāmārtihā bhavyā bhavabhāvavināśanī
sā me sākṣānmahādevī pāpāmāśu vyapohatu
caṇḍaḥ sarvagaṇeśāno mukhācchaṃbhorvinirgataḥ
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
śālaṅkāyanaputrastu halamārgotthitaḥ prabhuḥ
jāmātā marutāṃ devaḥ sarvabhūtamaheśvaraḥ
sarvagaḥ sarvadṛk śarvaḥ sarveśasadṛśaḥ prabhuḥ
sanārāyaṇakairdevaiḥ seṃdracandradivākaraiḥ
uragairṛṣibhiścaiva brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā
sarvadā pūjitaḥ sarvairnandī pāpaṃ vyapohatu
mahākāyo mahā tejā mahādeva ivāparaḥ
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmānsa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
merumandārakailāsataṭakūṭaprabhedanaḥ
saptapātālapādaś ca saptadvīporujaṅghakaḥ
saptārṇavāṅkuśaścaiva sarvatīrthodaraḥ śivaḥ
ākāśadeho digbāhuḥ somasūryāgnilocanaḥ
hatāsuramahāvṛkṣo brahmavidyāmahotkaṭaḥ
baddho hṛtpuṇḍarīkākhyestaṃbhe vṛttiṃ nirudhya ca
nāgendravattro yaḥ sākṣādgaṇakoṭiśatairvṛtaḥ
śivadhyānaikasaṃpannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
bhṛṅgīśaḥ piṅgalākṣosau bhasitāśastu dehuyuk
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmānsa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
skandaḥ śaktidharaḥ śāntaḥ senānīḥ śikhivāhanaḥ
devasenāpatiḥ śrīmānsa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
bhavaḥ śarvastatheśāno rudraḥ paśupatis tathā
ugro bhīmo mahādevaḥ śivārcanarataḥ sadā
etāḥ pāpaṃ vyapohantu mūrtayaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
mahādevaḥ śivo rudraḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ
kapālīśaś ca vijñeyo rudrā rudrāṃśasaṃbhavāḥ
śivapraṇāmasaṃpannā vyapohantu malaṃ mama
vikartano vivasvāṃś ca mārtaṇḍo bhāskaro raviḥ
lokaprakāśakaścaiva lokasākṣītrivikramaḥ
ādityaś ca tathā sūryaścāṃsumāṃś ca divākaraḥ
gaganaṃ sparśanaṃ tejo rasaś ca pṛthivī tathā
candraḥ sūryastathātmā ca tanavaḥ śivabhāṣitāḥ
varuṇo vāyusomau ca īśāno bhagavān hariḥ
pitāmahaś ca bhagavān śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
prāṇaḥ prāṇeśajīveśau mārutaḥ śivabhāṣitāḥ
suṣeṇaḥ śāśvataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ supuṣṭaścamahābalaḥ
ete vai cāraṇāḥ śaṃbhoḥ pūjayātīva bhāvitāḥ
vyapohantu malaṃ sarvaṃ pāpaṃ caiva mayā kṛtam
mantrajño mantravit prājño mantrarāṭ siddhapūjitaḥ
vyapohantu malaṃ sarve siddhāḥ śivapadārcakāḥ
yakṣo yakṣeśa dhanado jṛṃbhako maṇibhadrakaḥ
pūrṇabhadreśvaro mālī śitikuṇḍalireva ca
karkoṭako mahāpadmaḥ śaṅkhapālo mahābalaḥ
śivapraṇāmasaṃpannāḥ śivadehaprabhūṣaṇāḥ
mama pāpaṃ vyapohantu viṣaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam
vīṇājñaḥ kinnaraścaiva surasenaḥ pramardanaḥ
atiśayaḥ sa prayogī gītajñaścaiva kinnarāḥ
śivapraṇāmasaṃpannā vyopohantu malaṃ mama
vidyādharaś ca vibudho vidyārāśirvidāṃ varaḥ
vibuddho vibudhaḥ śrīmānkṛtajñaś ca mahāyaśāḥ
ete vidyādharāḥ sarve śivadhyānaparāyaṇāḥ
vāmadevī mahājaṃbhaḥ kālanemirmahābalaḥ
prahrādaścāpyanuhrādaḥ saṃhrādaḥ kila bāṣkalau
jaṃbhaḥ kuṃbhaś ca māyavī kārtavīryaḥ kṛtañjayaḥ
ete 'surā mahātmāno mahādevaparāyaṇāḥ
garutmān khagatiścaiva pakṣirāṭ nāgamardanaḥ
nāgaśatrurhiraṇyāṅgo vainateyaḥ prabhañjanaḥ
nāgāśīrviṣanāśaś ca viṣṇuvāhana eva ca
ete hiraṇyavarṇābhā garuḍā viṣṇuvāhanāḥ
nānābharaṇasaṃpannā vyapohantu malaṃ mama
agastyaś ca vasiṣṭhaś ca aṅgirābhṛgureva ca
kāśyapo nāradaścaiva dadhīcaścyavanas tathā
upamanyustathānye ca ṛṣayaḥ śivabhāvitāḥ
pitaraḥ pitāmahāś ca tathaiva prapitāmahāḥ
agniṣvāttā barhiṣadas tathā mātāmahādayaḥ
vyapohantu bhayaṃ pāpaṃ śivadhyānaparāyaṇāḥ
lakṣmīś ca dharaṇī caiva gāyatrī ca sarasvatī
durgā uṣā śacī jyeṣṭhā mātaraḥ surapūjitāḥ
devānāṃ mātaraś caiva gaṇānāṃ mātaras tathā
bhūtānāṃ mātaraḥ sarvā yatra yā gaṇamātaraḥ
urvaśī menakā caiva raṃbhā ratitilottamāḥ
sumukhī durmukhī caiva kāmukhī kāmavardhanī
tathānyāḥ sarvalokeṣu divyāścāpsarasas tathā
śivāya tāṇḍavaṃ nityaṃ kurvantyotīva bhāvitāḥ
arkaḥ somoṅgārakaś ca budhaścaiva bṛhaspatiḥ
śukraḥ śanaiścaraścaiva rāhuḥ ketustathaiva ca
vyapohantu bhayaṃ ghoraṃ grahapīḍāṃ śivārcakāḥ
meṣo vṛṣotha mithunas tathā karkaṭakaḥ śubhaḥ
siṃhaś ca kanyā vipulā tulā vai vṛścikas tathā
rāśayo dvādaśa hyete śivapūjāparāyaṇāḥ
vyapohantu bhayaṃ pāpaṃ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ
aśvinī bharaṇī caiva kṛttikā rohiṇī tathā
śrīmanmṛgaśiraścārdrā punarvasupuṣyasārpakāḥ
maghā vai pūrvaphaālgunya uttarāphaālgunī tathā
hastaścitrā tathā svātī viśākhā cānurādhikā
jyeṣṭhā mūlaṃ mahābhāgā pūrvāṣāḍhā tathaiva ca
uttarāṣāḍhikā caiva śravaṇaṃ ca śraviṣṭhikā
śatabhiṣak pūrvabhadrā tathā proṣṭhapadā tathā
jvaraḥ kuṃbhodaraścaiva śaṅkukarṇo mahābalaḥ
mahākarṇaḥ prabhātaś ca mahābhūtapramardanaḥ
śyenajicchivadūtaś ca pramathāḥ prītivardhanāḥ
koṭikoṭiśataiścaiva bhūtānāṃ mātaraḥ sadā
vyapohantu bhayaṃ pāpaṃ mahādevaprasādataḥ
śivadhyānaikasaṃpanno himarāḍaṃbusannibhaḥ
kundendusadṛśākāraḥ kuṃbhakundendubhūṣaṇaḥ
vaḍavānalaśatruryo vaḍavāmukhabhedanaḥ
catuṣpādasamāyuktaḥ kṣīroda iva pāṇḍuraḥ
rudraloke sthito nityaṃ rudraiḥ sārdhaṃ gaṇeśvaraiḥ
vṛṣendro viśvadhṛgdevo viśvasya jagataḥ pitā
gaṅgā mātā jaganmātā rudraloke vyavasthitā
śivabhaktā tu yā nandā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
mātā gavāṃ mahābhāgā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
surabhiḥ sarvatobhadrā sarvapāpapraṇāśanī
rudrapūjāratā nityaṃ sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
suśīlā śīlasaṃpannā śrīpradā śivabhāvitā
śivaloke sthitā nityaṃ sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
vedasāstrārthatattvajñaḥ sarvakāryābhicintakaḥ
samastaguṇasaṃpannaḥ sarvadevaśvarātmajaḥ
jyeṣṭhaḥ sarveśvaraḥ saumyo mahā viṣṇutanuḥ svayam
āryaḥ senāpatiḥ sākṣādgahano makhamardanaḥ
airāvatagajārūḍhaḥ kṛṣṇakuñcitamūrdhajaḥ
kṛṣṇāṅgo raktanayanaḥ śaśipannagabhūṣaṇaḥ
bhūtaiḥ pretaiḥ piśācaiś ca kūṣmāṇḍaiś ca samāvṛtaḥ
śivārcanarataḥ sākṣātsa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
brahmāṇī caiva māheśī kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā
vārāhī caiva māhendrī cāmuṇḍāgneyikā tathā
etā vai mātaraḥ sarvāḥ sarvalokaprapūjitāḥ
yoginībhīrmahāpāpaṃ vyapohantu samāhitāḥ
rudrasya tanayo raudraḥ śūlāsaktamahākaraḥ
mātṝṇāṃ rakṣako nityaṃ mahāvṛṣabhavāhanaḥ
trailokyanamitaḥ śrīmānśivapādārcane rataḥ
yajñasya ca śiraśchettā pūṣṇo dantavināśanaḥ
pādāṅguṣṭhena somāṅgapeṣakaḥ prabhusaṃjñakaḥ
upendredrayamādīnāṃ devānāmaṅgarakṣakaḥ
sarasvatya mahādevyā nāsikoṣṭhāvakartanaḥ
gaṇeśvaroyaḥ senānīḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā varadā varābharaṇabhūṣitā
mahālakṣmīrjaganmātā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
mahāmohā mahābhāgā mahābhūtagaṇairvṛtā
śivārcanaratā nityaṃ sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
lakṣmīḥ sarvaguṇopetā sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutā
sarvadā sarvagā devī sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
siṃhārūḍhā mahādevī pārvatyāstanayāvyayā
viṣṇornidrā mahāmāyā vaiṣṇavī surapūjitā
śivārcanaratā durgā sā me pāpaṃ vyavohatu
brahmāṇḍadhārakā rudrāḥ sarvalokaprapūjitāḥ
satyāś ca mānasāḥ sarve vyapohantu bhayaṃ mama
bhūtāḥ pretāḥ piśācāś ca kūṣmāṇḍagaṇanāyakāḥ
kūṣmāṇḍakāś ca te pāpaṃ vyapohantu samāhitāḥ
praṇamya śirasā bhūmau pratimāse dvijottamāḥ
vyapohanastavaṃ divyaṃ yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādapi
vidyārthī labhate vidyāṃ bhogārthī bhogamāpnuyāt
yānyānprārthayate kāmānmānavaḥ śravaṇādiha
tānsarvān śīghramāpnoti devānāṃ ca priyo bhavet
paṭhyamānamidaṃ puṇyaṃ yamuddiśya tu paṭhyate
tasya rogā na bādhante vātapittādisaṃbhavāḥ
yatpuṇyaṃ caiva tīrthānāṃ yajñānāṃ caiva yatphalam
dānānāṃ caiva yatpuṇyaṃ vratānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
tatpuṇyaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ japtvā cāpnoti mānavaḥ
śaraṇāgataghātī ca mitraviśvāsaghātakaḥ
duṣṭaḥ pāpasamācāro mātṛhā pitṛhā tathā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vyapohanastavanirūpaṇaṃ nāma dvyaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vyapohanastavaṃ puṇyaṃ śrutamasmābhir ādarāt
sūta uvāca
vratānī vaḥ pravakṣyāmi śubhāni munisattamāḥ
tāni vyāsādupaśrutya yuṣmākaṃ pravadāmyaham
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ pakṣayorubhayorapi
varṣamekaṃ tu bhuñjāno naktaṃ yaḥ pūjayecchivam
sarvayajñaphalaṃ prāpya sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
pṛthivīṃ bhājanaṃ kṛtvā bhuktvā parvasu mānavaḥ
kṣīpadhārāvrataṃ kuryātsośvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ tu naktena yāvatkṛṣṇacaturdaśī
brahmacārī jitakrodhaḥ śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
sa yāti śāṅkaraṃ lokaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
upavāsāt paraṃ bhaikṣyaṃ bhaikṣyātparamayācitam
devairbhuktaṃ tu pūrvāhṇe madhyāhne ṛṣibhis tathā
aparāhṇe ca pitṛbhiḥ saṃdhyāyāṃ guhyakādibhiḥ
haviṣyabhojanaṃ snāṃna satyamāhāralāghavam
agnikāryamadhaḥśayyāṃ naktabhojī samācaret
dharmakāmārthamokṣārthaṃ sarvapāpaviśuddhaye
satyavādī jitakrodhaḥ śāligodhūmagorasaiḥ
pakṣayoraṣṭamīṃ yatnādupavāsena vartayet
bhūmiśayyāṃ ca māsāṃte paurṇamāsyāṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ
snāpya rudraṃ mahādevaṃ saṃpūjya vidhipūrvakam
yāvakaṃ caudanaṃ dattvā sakṣīraṃ saghṛtaṃ dvijāḥ
bhījayedbrāhmaṇāñśiṣṭāñjapecchāntiṃ viśeṣataḥ
bhavāya devadevāya śivāya parameṣṭhine
māghamāse tu saṃpūjya yaḥ kuryān naktabhojam
kṛśaraṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ bhuñjānaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ
sopavāsaṃ caturdaśyāṃ bhavedubhayapakṣayoḥ
rudrāya paurṇamāsyāṃ tu dadyādvai ghṛtakaṃbalam
kṛṣṇaṃ gomithunaṃ dadyātpūjayeccaiva saṃkaram
śyāmākānnaghṛtakṣīrairjitakrodho jitendriyaḥ
caturdaśyāmathāṣṭamyāmupavāsaṃ ca kārayet
paurṇamāsyāṃ mahādevaṃ snāpya saṃpūjya śaṅkaram
dadyādgomithunaṃ vāpi tāmrābhaṃ śūlapāṇaye
sa yāti candrasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
śālyannaṃ payasā yuktaṃ ghṛtena ca yathāsukham
goṣṭhaśāyī muniśreṣṭhāḥ kṣitau niśi bhavaṃ smaret
paurṇamāsyāṃ śivaṃ snāpya dadyādgomithunaṃ sitam
brāhmaṇān bhojayeccaiva nirṛteḥ sthānamāpnuyāt
vaiśākhe ca tathā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam
paurṇamāsyāṃ bhavaṃ snāpyaṃ pañcagavyaghṛtādibhiḥ
jyeṣṭhe māse ca deveśaṃ bhavaṃ śarvamumāpatim
saṃpūjya śraddhayā bhaktyā kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam
raktaśālyannamadhvā ca ādbhiḥ pūtaṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ
vīrāsanī niśārdhaṃ ca gavāṃ śuśrūpaṇe rataḥ
paurṇamāsyāṃ tu saṃpūjya devadevamumāpatim
snāpya śaktyā yathānyāyaṃ caruṃ dadyāc ca śūline
dhūmraṃ gomithunaṃ dattvā vāyuloke mahīyate
āṣāḍhe māsi cāpyevaṃ naktabhojanatatparaḥ
bhūrikhaṇḍājyasaṃmiśraṃ saktubhiścaiva gorasam
paurṇamāsyāṃ ghṛtādyaistu snāpya pūjya yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śrotriyān vedapāragān
dadyādgomithunaṃ gauraṃ vāruṇaṃ lokamāpnuyāt
śrāvaṇeca dvijā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam
kṣīraṣaṣṭikabhaktena saṃpūjya vṛṣabhadhvajam
paurṇamāsyāṃ ghṛtādyaistu snāpya pūjya yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śrotriyān vedapāragān
śvetāgrapādaṃ pauḍraṃ ca dadyādgomithunaṃ punaḥ
hutaśeṣaṃ ca viprandrānvṛkṣamūlāśrito divā
paurṇamāsyāṃ tu deveśaṃ snāpya saṃpūjya śaṅkaram
nīlaskandhaṃ vṛṣaṃ gāṃ ca dattvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca vedavedāṅgapāragān
tataścāśvayuje māsi kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam
saghṛtaṃ śaṅkaraṃ pūjya paurṇamāsyāṃ ca pūrvavat
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śivabhaktān sadā śucīn
vaṣabhaṃ nīlavarṇābhamurodeśasamunnatam
gāṃ ca datvā yathānyāya maiśānaṃ lokamāpnuyāt
paurṇamāsyāṃ ca vidhivatsnāpya dattvā caruṃ punaḥ
dattvā gomithunaṃ caiva kāpilaṃ pūrva vaddvijāḥ
sūryasāyujyamāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
mārgasīrṣe ca māsepi kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam
yavānnena yathānyāyamājyakṣīrādibhiḥ samam
paurṇamāsyāṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ kṛtvā śarvāya śaṃbhave
brāhmaṇān bhojayittvā ca daridrānvedapāragān
dattvā gomithunaṃ caiva pāṇḍuraṃ vidhipūrvakam
ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ kṣamā dayā
triḥsnānaṃ cāgnihotraṃ ca bhūśayyā naktabhojanam
pakṣayorupavāsaṃ ca caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca
kuryādvarṣaṃ krameṇaiva vyutkrameṇāpi vā dvijāḥ
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ jñānayogamavāpnuyāt
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivavratakathanaṃ nāma tryaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
umāmaheśvaraṃ vakṣye vratamīśvarabhāṣitam
naranāryādijantūnāṃ hitāya munisattamāḥ
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ caturdasyaṣṭamīṣu ca
umāmaheśapratimāṃ hemnā kṛtvā suśobhanām
rājatīṃ vātha varṣānte pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dattvā śaktyā ca dakṣiṇām
rathādyairvāpi devaśaṃ nītvā rudrālayaṃ prati
sarvātiśayasaṃyuktaiś chatracāmarabhūṣaṇaiḥ
sa yāti śivāsāyujyaṃ nārī devyā yadi prabho
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ niyatā brahmacāriṇī
varṣamekaṃ na bhuñjati kanyā vā vidhavāpi vā
varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā pūrvoktavidhinā tataḥ
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ dattvā rudrālaye punaḥ
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca bhavānyā saha modate
yā nāryevaṃ caredabdaṃ kṛṣṇāmekāṃ caturdaśīm
varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā yena kenāpi vā dvijāḥ
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate
amāvāsyāṃ nirāhārā bhavedabdaṃ suyantritā
śūlaṃ ca vidhinā kṛtvā varṣānte vinivedayet
snāpyeśānaṃ yajedbhaktyā sahasraiḥ kamalaiḥ sitaiḥ
rājataṃ kamalaṃ caiva jāṃbūnadasukarṇikam
dattvā bhavāya viprebhyaḥ pradadyād dakṣiṇām api
kāmatopi kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhrūṇahatyādikaṃ ca yat
tatsarvaṃ śūladānena bhindyānnārī na saṃśayaḥ
sāyujyaṃ caivamāpnoti bhavānyā dvijasattamāḥ
kuryādyadvā naraḥ sopi rudrasāyujyamāpnuyāt
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ varṣamekamatandritā
upavāsaratā nārī naropi dvijasattamāḥ
niyogādeva tatkāryaṃ bhartṝṇāṃ dvijasattamāḥ
japaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ sarvamasvatantrā yataḥ striyaḥ
varṣānte sarvagandhāḍhyāṃ pratimāṃ saṃnivedayet
sā bhavānyāś ca sāyujyaṃ sārūyaṃ cāpi suvratā
kārtikyāṃ vā tu yā nārī ekabhaktena vartate
kṣamāhiṃsādiniyamaiḥ saṃyuktā brahmacāriṇī
dadyātkṛṣṇatilānāṃ ca bhāramekamatandriyā
saghṛtaṃ saguḍaṃ caiva odanaṃ parameṣṭhine
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyā mupavāsaratā ca sā
bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ sārūpyaṃ prāpya suvratā
kṣamā satyaṃ dayā dānaṃ śaucamindriyanigrahaḥ
samāsādvaḥ pravakṣyāmi pratimāsamanukramāt
mārgaśīrṣakamāsādi kārtikyāntaṃ yatākramam
vrataṃ suvipulaṃ puṇyaṃ nandinā paribhāṣitam
mārgaśīrṣakamāsetha vṛṣaṃ pūrṇāṅgamuttamam
alaṅkṛtya yathānyāyaṃ śivāya vinivedayet
sā ca sārdhaṃ bhavānyā vai modate nātra saṃśayaḥ
puṣyamāse tu vai śūlaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya nivedayet
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate
māghamāse rathaṃ kṛtvā sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam
dadyātsaṃpūjya deveśaṃ brāhmaṇāṃścaiva bhojayet
sā ca devyā mahābhāga modate nātra saṃśayaḥ
phaālgune pratimāṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyena yathāvidhi
sā ca sārdhaṃ mahādevyā modate nātra saṃśayaḥ
caitre bhavaṃ kumāraṃ ca bhavānīṃ ca yathāvidhi
tāmrādyairvidhivatkṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi
bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ dattvā rudrāya śaṃbhave
kṛtvālayaṃ hi kauberaṃ rājataṃ rajatena vai
īśvaromāsamāyuktaṃ gaṇeśaiś ca samantataḥ
jyeṣṭhe māsi mahādevaṃ liṅgamūrtimumāpatim
kṛtāñjali puṭenaiva brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā
haṃsena ca varāheṇa kṛtvā tāmrādibhiḥ śubhām
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayettataḥ
śivāya śivamāsādya śivasthāne yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇaiḥ sahitāṃ sthāpya devyāḥ sāyujyamāpnuyāt
āṣāḍhe ca śubhe māse gṛhaṃ kṛtvā suśobhanam
sarvabījarasaiścāpi saṃpūrṇaṃ sarvaśobhanaiḥ
gṛhopakaraṇaiścaiva musalolūkhalādibhiḥ
dāsīdāsādibhiścaiva śayanairaśanādibhiḥ
saṃpūrṇaiś ca gṛhaṃ vastrairācchādya ca samantataḥ
devaṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ snāpya mahādevamumāpatim
brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayitvā yathāvidhi
vidyāvinayasaṃpannaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam
prathamāśramiṇaṃ bhaktyā saṃpūjya ca yathāvidhi
kanyāṃ sumadhyamāṃ yāvat kālajīvanasaṃyutām
bhavānyā sadṛśībhūtvā sarvakalpeṣu sāvyayā
bhavānyāścaiva sāyujyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
nivedayīta śarvāya śrāvaṇe tilaparvatam
kṛtvā bhādrapade māsi śobhanaṃ śāliparvatam
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dāpayecca yathāvidhi
sā ca sūryāṃśusaṃkāśā bhavānyā saha modate
kṛtvā cāśvayuje māsi vipulaṃ dhānyaparvatam
suvarṇavastrayaṃyuktaṃ dattvā saṃpūjya śaṅkaram
sarvadhānyasamāyuktaṃ sarvabījarasādibhiḥ
śṛṅgaiścaturbhiḥ saṃyuktaṃ vitānacchatraśobhitam
gandhamālyais tathā dhūpaiścitraiścāpi suśobhitam
vicitrairnṛtyageyaiś ca śaṅkhavīṇādibhis tathā
brahmaghoṣairmahāpuṇyaṃ maṅgalaiś ca viśeṣataḥ
dakṣiṇe ca yathānyāyaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca caturmukham
uttare devadeveśaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam
indrādilokapālāṃś ca kṛtvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi
devasya dakṣiṇe haste śūlaṃ tridaśapūjitam
vāme pāśaṃ bhavānyāś ca kamalaṃ hemabhūṣitam
viṣṇoś ca śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ ca gadāmabjaṃ prayatnataḥ
brahmaṇaścākṣasūtraṃ ca kamaṇḍalumanuttamam
yamasya daṇḍaṃ nirṛteḥ khaḍgaṃ niśicarasya tu
varuṇasya mahāpāśaṃ nāgākhyaṃ rudramadbhutam
vāyoryāṣṭiṃ kuberasya gadāṃ lokaprapūjitām
ṭaṅkaṃ ceśānadevasya nivedyaivaṃ krameṇa ca
śivasya mahatīṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā carusamānvitām
brāhmaṇānbhojayitvā ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ
mahāmeruvrataṃ kṛtvā mahādevāya dāpayet
ciraṃ sāyucyamāpnoti mahādevyā na saṃśayaḥ
kārtikyāmapi yā nārī kṛtvā devīmumāṃ śubhām
sarvābharaṇa saṃpūrṇāṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitām
hematāmrādibhiścaiva pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānataḥ
devaṃ ca kṛtvā deveśaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam
nārāyaṇaṃ ca dātāraṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
lokapālais tathā siddhaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ sthāpya yatnataḥ
mārgaśīrṣakamāsādikārtikāntaṃ pravartitam
naranāryādijantūnāṃ hitāya munisattamāḥ
naraḥ kṛtvā vrataṃ caiva śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
nārī devyā na saṃdehaḥ śivena paribhāṣitam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge umāmaheśvaravrataṃ nāma caturaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
japetpañcākṣarīṃ vidyāṃ vidhinaiva dvijottamāḥ
japādeva na saṃdeho vratānāṃ vai viśeṣataḥ
samāptirnānyathā tasmājjapetpañcākṣarīṃ śubhām
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ pañcākṣarī vidyā prabhāvo vā kathaṃ vada
kramopāyaṃ mahābhāga śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ
sūta uvāca
pārvatyāḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ pravadāmi samāsataḥ
śrīdevyuvāca
pañcākṣarasya mahātmyaṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
pañcākṣarasya mahātmyaṃ varṣakoṭiśatairapi
na śakyaṃ kathituṃ devi tasprātsaṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu
naṣṭe devāsure caiva naṣṭe coragarākṣase
sarvaṃ prakṛtimāpannaṃ tvayā pralayameṣyati
tasminvedāś ca śāstrāṇi mantre pañcākṣare sthitāḥ
te nāśaṃ naiva saṃprāptā macchaktyā hyanupālitāḥ
sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ śete devo māyāmayīṃ tanum
tannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ
sisṛkṣamāṇo lokānvai trīnaśakto 'sahāyavān
daśa brahmā sasarjādau mānasānamitaujasaḥ
teṣāṃ sṛṣṭiprasiddhyarthaṃ māṃ provāca pitāmahaḥ
matputrāṇāṃ mahādeva śaktiṃ dehi maheśvara
pañcākṣarānpañcamukhaiḥ proktavān padmayonaye
tānpañcavadanairgṛhṇan brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
vācyavācakabhāvena jñātavānparameśvaram
vācyaḥ pañcākṣarairdevi śivastrailokyapūjitaḥ
vācakaḥ paramo mantrastasya pañcākṣaraḥ sthitaḥ
jñātvā prayogaṃ vidhinā ca siddhiṃ labdhvā tathā pañcamukho mahātmā
te labdhvā mantraratnaṃ tu sākṣāllokapitāmahāt
tamārādhayituṃ devaṃ parātparataraṃ śivam
tatastutoṣa bhagavān trimūrtīnāṃ paraḥ śivaḥ
dattavānakhilaṃ jñānamaṇimādiguṇāṣṭakam
tepi labdhvā varānviprāstadārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
matpriyaḥ satataṃ śrīmānmadbhūtaiḥ parirakṣitaḥ
tasyābhyāśe tapastīvraṃ lokasṛṣṭisamutsukāḥ
divyavarṣasahasraṃ tu vāyubhakṣāḥ samācaran
tiṣṭhantonugrahārthāya devi te ṛṣayaḥ purā
teṣāṃ bhaktimahaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadyaḥ pratyakṣatāmiyām
pañcākṣaramṛṣicchandau daivataṃ śaktibījavat
nyāsaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ digbandhaṃ viniyogamaśeṣataḥ
proktavānahamāryāṇāṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
tacchrutvā mantramāhātmyamṛṣayaste tapodhanāḥ
mantrasya viniyogaṃ ca kṛtvā sarvamanuṣṭhitāḥ
tanmāhātyāttadālokānsadevāsuramānuṣān
varṇānvarṇavibhāgāṃś ca sarvadharmāṃś ca śobhanān
pañcākṣaraprabhāvācca lokā vedā maharṣayaḥ
tiṣṭhanti śāśvatā dharmā devāḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat
taditānīṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu cāvahitākhilam
alpākṣaraṃ mahārthaṃ ca vedasāraṃ vimuktidam
ājñāsiddhamasaṃdigdhaṃ vākyametacchivātmakam
nānāsiddhiyutaṃ divyaṃ lokacittānurañjakam
suniścitārthaṃ gaṃbhīraṃ vākyaṃ me pārameśvaram
tadbījaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ mantramādyaṃ suśojakam
atisūkṣmaṃ mahārthaṃ ca jñeyaṃ tadvaṭabījavat
vedaḥ sa triguṇātītaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvakṛtprabhuḥ
omityekākṣaraṃ mantraṃ sthitaḥ sarvagataḥ śivaḥ
mantreṣaḍakṣare sūkṣme pañcākṣaratanuḥ śivaḥ
vācyavācakabhāvena sthitaḥ sākṣātsvabhāvataḥ
vācyaḥ śivaḥ prameyatvānmantrastadvācakaḥ smṛtaḥ
vācyavācakabhāvoyamanādiḥ saṃsthitastayoḥ
vede śivāgame vāpi yatrayatra ṣaāḍakṣaraḥ
mantraḥ sthitaḥ sadā mukhyo loke pañcākṣaro mataḥ
yasyaivaṃ hṛdi saṃsthoyaṃ mantraḥ syātpārameśvaraḥ
tenādhītaṃ śrutaṃ tena tena sarvamanuṣṭhitam
etāvaddhi śivajñānametāvatparamaṃ padam
pañcākṣaraiḥ sapraṇavo mantroyaṃ hṛdayaṃ mama
guhyādguhyataraṃ sākṣānmokṣajñānamanuktamam
bījaṃ śaktiṃ svaraṃ varṇaṃ sthānaṃ caivākṣaraṃ prati
vāmadevo nāma ṛṣiḥ paṅktiśchanda udāhṛtaḥ
devatā śiva evāhaṃ mantrasyāsya varānane
nakārādīni bījāni pañcabhūtātmakāni ca
tvadīyaṃ praṇavaṃ kiñcinmadīyaṃ praṇavaṃ tathā
tvadīyaṃ deviṃ mantrāṇāṃ śaktibhūtaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
akārokāramakārā madīye praṇave sthitāḥ
ukāraṃ ca makāraṃ ca akāraṃ ca krameṇa vai
oṅkārasya svarodātta ṛṣirbrahma sitaṃ vapuḥ
chando devī ca gāyatrī paramātmādhidevatā
pañcamaḥ svaritaścaiva madhyamo niṣadhaḥ smṛtāḥ
nakāraḥ pītavarṇaś ca sthānaṃ pūrvamukhaṃ smṛtam
indrodhidaivataṃ chando gāyatrī gautamo ṛṣiḥ
makāraḥ kṛṣmavarṇosya sthānaṃ vai dākṣiṇāmukham
chandonuṣṭup ṛṣiścātrī rudro daivatamucyate
śikāro dhūmravarṇosya sthānaṃ vai paścimaṃ mukham
viśvāmitra ṛṣistriṣṭup chando viṣṇustu daivatam
brahmādhidaivataṃ chando bṛhatī cāṅgirā ṛṣiḥ
yakāro raktavarṇaś ca sthānum ūrdhvaṃ mukhaṃ virāṭ
brahmacārigṛhasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ kramaśo bhavet
utpattirbrahmacārīṇāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ sthitiḥ sadā
yatīnāṃ saṃhṛtir nyāsaḥ siddhir bhavati nānyathā
aṅganyāsaḥ karanyāso dehanyāsa iti tridhā
aṅganyāsaṃ tataḥ paścādakṣarāṇāṃ vidhikramāt
pādādimūrdhaparyantaṃ saṃhāro bhavati priye
hṛdayāsyagalanyāsaḥ sthitinyāsa udāhṛtaḥ
brahmacārigṛhasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ caiva śobhane
saśiraskaṃ tato dehaṃ sarvamantreṇa saṃspṛśet
dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhamārabhya vāmāṅguṣṭhānta eva hi
aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ nyasyate hastayordviyoḥ
atīva bhogado devī sthitinyāsaḥ kuṭuṃbinām
karanyāsaṃ purā kṛttvā dehanyāsamanaṃ taram
aṅganyāsaṃ nyasetpaścādeṣa sādhāraṇo vidhiḥ
oṅkāraṃ saṃpuṭīkṛtya sarvāṅgeṣu ca vinyaset
karayorubhayoścaiva daśāgrāṃ guliṣu kramāt
prakṣālya pādāvācamya śucirbhūtvā samāhitaḥ
prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi nyāsakarma samācaret
smaretpūrvamṛṣiñchando daivataṃ bījameva ca
śaktiṃ ca paramātmānaṃ guruṃ caiva varānane
mantreṇa pāṇī saṃmṛjya talayoḥ praṇavaṃ nyaset
aṅgulīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ tathā cādyantaparvasu
ubhābhyāmeva pāṇibhyāmāpādatalamastakam
mantreṇa saṃspṛśeddehaṃ praṇavenaiva saṃpuṭam
kṛtvāṅganyāsamevaṃ hi mukhāni parikalpayet
ṣaḍaṅgāni nyasetpaścādyathāsthānaṃ ca śobhanam
namaḥ svāhā vaṣaḍḍhuṃ ca vaiṣaṭphaṭkārakaiḥ saha
praṇavaṃ hṛdayaṃ vidyān nakāraḥ śira ucyate
śikhā makāra ākhyātaḥ śikāraḥ kavacaṃ tathā
vākāro netramastraṃ tu yakāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ
vighneśo mātaro durgā kṣetrajño devatā diśaḥ
āgneyādiṣu koṇeṣu caturṣvapi yathākramam
aṅguṣṭhatarjanyagrābhyāṃ saṃsthāpya sumukhaṃ śubham
gale madhye tathāṅguṣṭhe tarjanyādyāṅgulīṣu ca
aṅguṣṭhena karanyāsaṃ kuryādeva vicakṣaṇaḥ
evaṃ nyāsamimaṃ proktaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham
sarvasiddhikaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvarakṣākaraṃ śivam
janmāntarakṛtaṃ pāpamapi naśyati tatkṣaṇāt
evaṃ vinyasya medhāvī śuddhakāyo dṛḍhavrataḥ
japetpañcākṣaraṃ mantraṃ labdhvācāryaprasādataḥ
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi mantrasaṃgrahaṇaṃ śubhe
yaṃ vinā niṣphalaṃ nityaṃ yena vā saphalaṃ bhavet
ājñāhīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnamamānasam
ājñaptaṃ dakṣiṇāhīnaṃ sadā japtaṃ ca niṣphalam
ājñāsiddhaṃ kriyāsiddhaṃ śraddhāsiddhaṃ sumānasam
evaṃ ca dakṣiṇāsiddhaṃ mantraṃ siddhaṃ yatastataḥ
jñāninaṃ sadguṇopetaṃ dhyānayogaparāyaṇam
ācāryaṃ pūjayecchiṣyaḥ sarvadātiprayatnataḥ
hastyaśvaratharatnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca
bhūṣaṇāniṃ ca vāsāṃsi dhānyāni vividhāni ca
vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchetsiddhimātmanaḥ
ādadīta gurormantraṃ jñānaṃ caiva krameṇa tu
evaṃ tuṣṭo guruḥ śiṣyaṃ pūjitaṃ vatsaroṣitam
śuśrūṣumanahaṅkāramupavāsakṛśaṃ śucim
snāpayitvā tu siṣyāya brāhmaṇānapi pūjya ca
samudratīre nadyāṃ ca goṣṭhe devālayepi vā
śivaṃ cāstu śubhaṃ cāstu śobhanostu priyostviti
evaṃ labdhvā paraṃ mantraṃ jñānaṃ caiva gurostataḥ
anaśraṃstatparo bhūtvā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
japedakṣaralakṣaṃ vai caturguṇitamādarāt
naktāsī saṃyamī yaś ca pauraścaraṇikaḥ smṛtaḥ
puraścaraṇajāpī vā api vā nityajāpakaḥ
yaḥ puraścaraṇaṃ kṛtvā nityajāpī bhavennaraḥ
āsanaṃ ruciraṃ baddhvā maunī caikāgramānasaḥ
ādyāntayorjapasyāpi kuryādvai prāṇasaṃyamān
tathā cānte japedbījaṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ śubham
catvāriṃśatsamāvṛtti prāṇānāyamya saṃsmaret
pañcākṣarasya mantrasya prāṇāyāma udāhṛtaḥ
prāṇāyāmādbhavetkṣipraṃ sarvapāpaparikṣayaḥ
indriyāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ ca tasmātprāṇāṃś ca saṃyamet
gṛhe japaḥ samaṃ vidyādgoṣṭhe śataguṇaṃ bhavet
nadyāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu anantaḥ śivasannidhau
puṇyāśrameṣu sarveṣu japaḥ koṭiguṇo bhavet
aṅgulījapasaṃkhyānamekamekaṃ śubhānane
śataṃ vai śaṅkhamaṇibhiḥ pravalaiś ca sahasrakam
padmākṣairdaśalakṣaṃ tu sauvarṇaiḥ koṭirucyate
pañcaviṃśati mokṣārthaṃ saptaviṃśati pauṣṭikam
triṃśacca dhanasaṃpattyai pañcāśaccābhicārikam
tatpūrvābhimukhaṃ vaśyaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ cābhicārikam
paścimaṃ dhanadaṃ vidyāduttaraṃ śāntikaṃ bhavet
aṅguṣṭhaṃ mokṣadaṃ vidyāttarjanī śatrunāśanī
madhyamā dhanadā śāntiṃ karotyeṣā hy anāmikā
kaniṣṭhā rakṣaṇīyā sā japakarmaṇiśobhane
aṅguṣṭhena vinā karma kṛtaṃ tadaphalaṃ yataḥ
śṛṇuṣva sarvayajñebhyo japayajño viśiṣyate
yāvantaḥ karmayajñāḥ syuḥ pradānāni tapāṃsi ca
sarve te japayajñasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm
tasmācchataguṇopāṃśuḥ sahasro mānasaḥ smṛtaḥ
yaduccanīcasvaritaiḥ śabdaiḥ spaṣṭapadākṣaraiḥ
mantramuccārayedvācā japayajñaḥ sa vācikaḥ
śanairuccārayenmantramīṣadeṣṭhau tu cālayet
kiñcitkarṇāntaraṃ vidyādupāṃśuḥ sa japaḥ smṛtaḥ
dhiyā yadakṣaraśreṇyā varṇādvarṇaṃ padātpadam
śabdārthaṃ cintayedbhūyaḥ sa tūkto mānaso japaḥ
trayāṇāṃ japayajñānāṃ śreyān syāduttarottaraḥ
bhavedyajñaviśeṣeṇa vaiśiṣṭyaṃ tatphalasya ca
japena devatā nityaṃ stūyamānā prasīdati
prasannā vipulān bhogāndadyānmuktiṃ ca śāśvatīm
yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāś ca grahāḥ sarve ca bhīṣaṇāḥ
jāpinaṃ nopasarpanti bhayabhītāḥ samantataḥ
japena pāpaṃ śamayedaśeṣaṃ yattatkṛtaṃ janmaparaṃparāsu
evaṃ labdhvā śivaṃ jñānaṃ jñātvā japavidhikramam
sadācārī japannityaṃ dhyāyan bhadraṃ samaśnute
yasmādācārahīnasya sādhanaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet
ācāraḥ paramo dharma ācāraḥ paramantapaḥ
ācāraḥ paramā vidyā ācāraḥ paramā gatiḥ
sadācāravatāṃ puṃsāṃ sarvatrāpyabhayaṃ bhavet
tadvadācārahīnānāṃ sarvatraivabhayaṃ bhavet
sadācāreṇa devatvamṛṣitvaṃ ca varānane
ācārahīnaḥ puruṣo loke bhavatininditaḥ
durvṛtto śuddhibhūyiṣṭho pāpīyān jñānadūṣakaḥ
varṇāśramavidhānoktaṃ dharmaṃ kurvīta yatnataḥ
saṃdhyopāsanaśīlaḥ syātsāyaṃ prātaḥ prasannadhīḥ
udayāstamayātpūrvamāramya vidhinā śuciḥ
kāmānmohādbhayāllobhātsaṃdhyāṃ nātikrameddvijaḥ
saṃdhyātikramaṇādvipro brāhmaṇyātpatate yataḥ
anṛtaṃ paruṣaṃ śāṭhyaṃ paiśunyaṃ pāpahetukam
paradārānparadravyaṃ parahiṃsāṃ ca sarvadā
kvaciccāpi na kurvīta vācā ca manasā tathā
śūdrānnaṃ yātayāmānnaṃ naivedyaṃ śrāddhameva ca
gaṇānnaṃ samudāyānnaṃ rājānnaṃ ca vivarjayet
rājapratigrahair dagdhān brāhmaṇān brahmavādinaḥ
svinnānāmapi bījānāṃ punarjanma na vidyate
asnātvā na ca bhuñjīyādajapognimapūjya ca
parṇapṛṣṭhe na bhuñjīyādrātrau dīpaṃ vinā tathā
bhinnabhāṇḍe ca rathyāyāṃ patitānāṃ ca saṃnidhau
śūdraśeṣaṃ na bhuñjīyātsahānnaṃ śisukairapi
śuddhānnaṃ snigdhamaśrīyātsaṃskṛtaṃ cābhimantritam
bhoktā śiva iti smṛtvā maunī caikāgramānasaḥ
āsyena na pibettoyaṃ tiṣṭhannañjalināpi vā
vāmahastena śayyāyāṃ tathaivānyaṃkareṇa vā
vibhītakārkakārañjasnuhicchāyāṃ na cāśrayet
staṃbhadīpamanuṣyāṇāmanyeṣāṃ praṇināṃ tathā
nāvaroheta kūpādiṃ nāroheduccapādapān
sūryāgnijaladevānāṃ gurūṇāṃ vimukhaḥ śubhe
na kuryādiha kāryāṇi japakarma śubhāni vā
agnau na tāpayetpādau hastaṃ padbhyāṃ na saṃspṛśet
na jalaṃ tāḍayetpadbhyāṃ nāṃbhasyaṅgamalaṃ tyajet
malaṃ prakṣālayettī re prakṣālya snānamācaret
aśrīkaraṃ manuṣyāṇāmasuddhaṃ saṃspṛśedyadi
ajāśvānakharoṣṭrāṇāṃ mārjanāttupareṇukān
saspṛśīdyādi mūḍhātmā śriyaṃ hanti harerapi
taccāṇḍālasamaṃ jñeyaṃ nātra kāryāvicāraṇā
sphigvātaṃ śūrpavātaṃ ca vātaṃ prāṇamukhānilam
sukṛtāni harantyete saṃspṛṣṭāḥ puruṣasya tu
uṣṇīṣī kañcukī nagno muktakeśo malāvṛtaḥ
krodho madaḥ kṣudhā tandrā niṣṭhīvanavijṛṃbhaṇe
śvanīcadarśanaṃ nidrā pralāpāste japadviṣaḥ
eteṣāṃ saṃbhave vāpi kuryātsūryādidarśanam
ācamya vā japec cheṣaṃ kṛtvā vā prāṇasaṃyamam
sūryogniścandramāścaiva grahanakṣatratārakāḥ
ete jyotīṃṣi proktāni vidvadbhir bāhmaṇais tathā
anāsanaḥ śayāno vā rathyāyāṃ śūdrasannidhau
raktabhūmyāṃ ca khaṭvāyāṃ na japejjāpakas tathā
kauśeyaṃ vyāghracarmaṃ vā cailaṃ taulamathāpi vā
dāravaṃ tālaparṇaṃ vā āsanaṃ parikalpayet
trisaṃdhyaṃ tu guroḥ pūjā kartavyā hitamicchatā
yo guruḥ sa śivaḥ prokto yaḥ śivaḥ sa guruḥ smṛtaḥ
yathā śivas tathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ
saguṇo nirguṇo vāpi tasyājñāṃ śirasā vahet
śreyorthi yastu gurvājñāṃ manasāpi na laṅghayet
gurvājñāpālakaḥ samyak jñānasaṃpattimaśnute
gurordevasamakṣaṃ vā na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet
gururdevo yataḥ sākṣāttadgṛhaṃ devamandiram
pāpinā ca yatāsaṃgāttatpāpaiḥ patanaṃ bhavet
tathaiva gurusaṃparkātpāpaṃ tyajati mānavaḥ
tathā pāpaṃ vilīyeta ācāryasya samīpataḥ
yathā prajvalito vahnirviṣṭhā kāṣṭhaṃ ca nirdahet
gurustuṣṭo dahatyevaṃ pāpaṃ tanmantratejasā
kurvantyanugrahaṃ tuṣṭā gurau tuṣṭe na saṃśayaḥ
karmaṇā manasā vācā guroḥ krodhaṃ na kārayet
tasya krodhena dahyante āyuḥśrījñonasatkriyāḥ
tatkrodhaṃ ye kariṣyanti teṣāṃ yajñāś ca niṣphalāḥ
japānyaniyamāścaiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
gurorhitaṃ priyaṃ kuryādādiṣṭo vā na vā sadā
asamakṣaṃ samakṣaṃ vā guroḥ kāryaṃ samācaret
evamācāravān bhakto nityaṃ japaparāyaṇaḥ
yasya yena viyuñjīta kāryeṇa tu viśeṣataḥ
rājyaiśvaryaṃ ca vijñānaṃ svargo nirvāṇa eva ca
prokṣaṇaṃ cābhiṣekaṃ ca aghamarṣaṇameva ca
snāne ca saṃdhyayoścaiva kuryādekādaśena vai
mahānadyāṃ dvilakṣaṃ tu dīrghamāyuravāpnuyāt
dūrvāṅkurāstilā vāṇī guḍūcī ghuṭikā tathā
teṣāṃ tu daśasāhasraṃ homamāyuṣyavardhanam
aśvatthavṛkṣamāśritya japellakṣadvayaṃ sudhīḥ
śanaiścaradine spṛṣṭvā dīrghayuṣyaṃ labhennaraḥ
śanaiścaradine 'śvatthaṃ pāṇibhyāṃ saṃspṛśetsudhīḥ
ādityābhimukho bhūtvā japellakṣamananyadhīḥ
samastavyādhiśāntyarthaṃ palāśasamidairnaraḥ
ekādaśena bhuñjīyādannaṃ caivābhimantritam
bhakṣyaṃ cānyattathā peyaṃ viṣamapyamṛtaṃ bhavet
japel lakṣaṃ tu pūrvāhṇe hutvā cāṣṭaśatena vai
nadītoyena saṃpūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ saṃspṛśya śobhanam
japtvāyutaṃ ca tatsnānādrogāṇāṃ bheṣajaṃ bhavet
aṣṭāviṃśajjapitvānnamaśrīyādanvahaṃ śuciḥ
hutvā ca tāvatpālaśairevaṃ vārogyam aśnute
candrasūryagrahe pūrvam upoṣya vidhinā śuciḥ
yāvadgrahaṇamokṣaṃ tu tāvannadyāṃ samāhitaḥ
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa pibedbrāhmīrasaṃ dvijāḥ
ehikāṃ labhate medhāṃ sarvaśāstradharāṃ śubhām
sārasvatī bhaveddevī tasya vāgatimānuṣī
grahanakṣatrapīḍāsu japedbhaktyāyutaṃ naraḥ
hutvā cāṣṭasahasraṃ tu grahapīḍāṃ vyapohati
duḥsvapnadarśane snātvā japedvai cāyutaṃ naraḥ
ghṛte nāṣṭaśataṃ hutvā sadyaḥ śāntirbhaviṣyati
saṃnidhā vasya devasya śuciḥ saṃyatamānasaḥ
sarvānkāmānavāpnoti puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ
gajānāṃ turagāṇāṃ tu gojātīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ
vyādhyāgame śucirbhūtvā juhuyātsamidhāhutim
teṣāmṛddhiś ca śāntiś ca bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
utpāte śatrubādhāyāṃ juhuyādayutaṃ śuciḥ
pālāśasamidhairdevi tasya śāntirbhaviṣyati
ābhicārikabādhāyāmetaddevi samācaret
pratyag bhavati tacchaktiḥ śatroḥ pīḍā bhaviṣyati
vidveṣaṇārthaṃ juhuyādvaibhītasamidhāṣṭakam
viṣeṇa rudhirābhyakto vidveṣāṇakaraṃ nṛṇām
prayāścittaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpāviśuddhaye
pāpaśuddhirna cetpuṃsaḥ kriyāḥ sarvāścaniṣphalāḥ
jñānaṃ ca hīyate tasmātkartavyaṃ pāpaśodhanam
vidyālakṣmīviśuddhyarthaṃ māṃ dhyātvāñjalinā śubhe
śivenaikā daśenādbhir abhiṣiñcetsamantataḥ
aṣṭottaraśatenaiva snāyātpāpaviśuddhaye
saṃdhyopāsanavicchede japedaṣṭaśataṃ naraḥ
viḍvarāhaiś ca cāṇḍālairdurjanaiḥ kukkuṭairapi
spṛṣṭamannaṃ na bhuñjīta bhuktvā cāṣṭaśataṃ japet
brahmahatyā viśuddhyarthaṃ japellakṣāyutaṃ naraḥ
pātakānāṃ tadardhaṃ syānnātra kāryā vicāraṇā
upapātakaduṣṭānāṃ tadardhaṃ parikīrtitam
śeṣāṇāmapi pāpānāṃ japetpañcasahasrakam
ātmabodhaparaṃ guhyaṃ śivabodhaprakāśakam
śivaḥ syātsa japenmantraṃ pañcalakṣamanākulaḥ
japecca pañcalakṣaṃ tu vigṛhītendriyaḥ śuciḥ
pañcendriyāṇāṃ vijayo bhaviṣyati varānane
viṣayāṇāṃ ca pañcānāṃ jayaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
bhūtānāmiha pañcānāṃ vijayaṃ manujo labhet
samyagvijayamāpnoti karaṇānāṃ varānane
pañcaviṃśatilakṣāṇāṃ japena kamalānane
pañcaviṃśatitattvānāṃ vijayaṃ manujo labhet
madhyarātre ca śivayoḥ paśyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
andhakāravināśaś ca dīpasyeva prakāśanam
hṛdayāntarbahirvāpi bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
sabījasaṃpuṭaṃ mantraṃ śatalakṣaṃ japecchuciḥ
iti te sarvamākhyātaṃ pañcākṣaravidhikramam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
śravayecca dvijāñchuddhānpañcākṣaravidhikramam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pañcākṣaramāhātmyaṃ nāma pañcāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
japācchreṣṭhātamaṃ prāhurbrāhmaṇā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
viraktānāṃ prabuddhānāṃ dhyānayajñaṃ suśobhanam
tasmādvadasva sūtādya dhyānayajñamaśeṣataḥ
vistārātsarvayatnena viraktānāṃ mahātmanām
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ dīrghasattriṇām
rudreṇa kathitaṃ prāha guhāṃ prāpya mahātmanām
saṃhṛtya kālakūṭākhyaṃ viṣaṃ vai viśvakarmaṇā
sūta uvāca
guhāṃ prāpya sukhāsīnaṃ bhavānyā saha śaṅkaram
munayaḥ saṃśitātmānaḥ preṇamustaṃ guhāśrayam
astuvaṃś ca tataḥ sarve nīlakaṇṭhamumāpatim
atyugraṃ kālakūṭākhyaṃ saṃhṛtaṃ bhagavaṃstvayā
ataḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ sarvaṃ tvayā deva vṛṣadhvaja
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
kimanena dvijaśreṣṭhā viṣaṃ vakṣye sudāruṇam
na viṣaṃ kālakūṭākhyaṃ saṃsāro viṣamucyate
saṃsāro dvividhaḥ proktaḥ svādhikārānurūpataḥ
puṃsāṃ saṃmūḍhacittānāmasaṃkṣīṇaḥ sudāruṇaḥ
īṣaṇārāgadoṣema sargo jñānena suvratāḥ
tadvaśādeva sarveṣāṃ dharmādharmau na saṃśayaḥ
asannikṛṣṭe tvarthepi śāstraṃ tacchravaṇātsatām
buddhimutpādayatyeva saṃsāre viduṣāṃ dvijāḥ
tasmāddṛṣṭānuśravikaṃ duṣṭamityubhayātmakam
śāstramityucyate 'bhāgaṃ śruteḥ karmasu taddvijāḥ
mūrdhānaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sāramṛṣīṇāṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam
nanu svabhāvaḥ sarveṣāṃ kāmo dṛṣṭo na cānyathā
śrutuḥ pravartikā teṣāmiti karmaṇyatādvidaḥ
nivṛttilakṣaṇo dharmaḥ samarthānā mihocyate
tasmādajñānamūlo hi saṃsāraḥ sarvadehinām
kalā saṃśoṣamāyāti karmaṇānyasvabhāvataḥ
nārakī pāpakṛtsvargī puṇyakṛtpuṇyagairavāt
vyatimiśreṇa vai jīvaścaturdhā saṃvyavasthitaḥ
udbhijaḥ svedajaścaiva aṇḍajo vai jarāyujaḥ
evaṃ vyavasthito dehī karmaṇājño hyanirvṛtaḥ
evamajñānadoṣeṇa nānākarmavaśena ca
ṣaṭkauśikaṃ samudbhūtaṃ bhajatyeṣa kalevaram
vicārataḥ satāṃ duḥkhaṃ strīsaṃsargādibhīrdvijāḥ
duḥkhenaikena vai duḥkhaṃ praśāmyantīha duḥkhinaḥ
na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānamupabhogena śāmyati
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate
tasmādvicārato nāsti saṃyogādapi vai nṛṇām
paiśāce rākṣase duḥkhaṃ yākṣe caiva vacāritaḥ
prājāpatye tathā brāhme prākṛte pauruṣe tathā
kṣayasātiśayādyaistu duḥkhairduḥkhāni suvratāḥ
tāni bhāgyānyaśuddhāni saṃtyajecca dhanāni ca
tasmādaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhogaṃ tathā ṣoḍaśadhā sthitam
caturviśatprakāreṇa saṃsthitaṃ cāpi suvratāḥ
dvātriṃśadbhedamanaghāścatvāriṃśadguṇaṃ punaḥ
tathāṣṭacatvāriṃścca ṣaṭpañcaṭāśatprakārataḥ
catuḥṣaṣṭividhaṃ caiva duḥkhameva vivekinaḥ
pārthivaṃ ca tathāpyaṃ ca taijasaṃ ca vicārataḥ
ābhimānikamapyevaṃ bauddhaṃ prākṛtameva ca
duḥkhameva na saṃdeho yogināṃ brahmavādinām
gauṇaṃ gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ ca duḥkhameva vicārataḥ
vartamānāni duḥkhāni bhaviṣyāṇi yathātatham
doṣaduṣṭeṣu deśeṣu duḥkhāni vividhāni ca
na bhāvayantyatītāni hyajñāne jñānamāninaḥ
kṣudvyādheḥ parihārārthaṃ na sukhāyānnamucyate
yathetareṣāṃ rogāṇāmauṣadhaṃ na sukhāya tat
śītoṣṇavātavarṣādyaistattatkāleṣu dehinām
duḥkhameva na saṃdeho na jānānti hyapaṇḍitāḥ
svargepyevaṃ muniśreṣṭhā hyaviśuddhakṣayādibhiḥ
rogaurnānāvidhairgrastā rāgadveṣabhayādibhiḥ
puṇyavṛkṣakṣayāttadvadgāṃ patanti divaukasaḥ
duḥkhābhilāṣaniṣṭhānāṃ duḥkhabhogādisaṃpadām
asmāttu patatāṃ duḥkhaṃ kaṣṭaṃ svargāddivaukasām
narake duḥkhamevātra nākāṇāṃ niṣevaṇāt
vihitākaraṇāccaiva varṇināṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
evaṃ yatirdhyānaparo mahātmā saṃsārabhīto na labheta nidrām
kīṭapakṣimṛgāṇāṃ ca paśūnāṃ gajavājinām
dṛṣṭamevāsukhaṃ tasmāt tyajataḥ sukhamuttamam
vaimānikānāmapyevaṃ duḥkhaṃ kalpādhikāriṇām
sthānābhimānināṃ caiva manvādīnāṃ ca suvratāḥ
devānāṃ caiva daityānāmanyonyavijigīṣayā
duḥkhameva nṛpāṇāṃ ca rākṣasānāṃ jagattraye
śramārthamāśramaścāpi varṇānāṃ paramārthataḥ
āśramairna ca devaiś ca yajñaḥ sāṃkhyairvratais tathā
bhasmaśāyī bhavennityaṃ vrate pāśupate budhaḥ
pañcārthajñānasaṃpannaḥ śivatattve samāhitaḥ
pañcārthayogasaṃpanno duḥkhāntaṃ vrajate sudhīḥ
śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ chanda eva ca
jyotiṣaṃ cāparā vidyā parākṣaramiti sthitam
tadadṛśyaṃ tadagrāhyamagotraṃ tadavarṇakam
tadacakṣustadaśrotraṃ tadapāṇi apādakam
tadajātamabhūtaṃ ca tadaśabdaṃ dvijottamāḥ
avyayaṃ cāpratiṣṭhaṃ ca tannityaṃ sarvagaṃ vibhum
mahāntaṃ tadgṛhaṃ taṃ ca tadajaṃ cinmayaṃ dvijāḥ
asaṃvṛtaṃ tadātmaikaṃ parā vidyā na cānyathā
matto nānyaditīkṣeta manovākpāṇibhis tathā
sarvamātmani saṃpaśyetsaccāsacca samāhitaḥ
adhodṛṣṭyā vitastyāṃ tu nābhyāmuparitiṣṭhati
hṛdayaṃ tadvijānīyādviśvasyāyatanaṃ mahat
dharmakandasamudbhūtaṃ jñānanālaṃ suśobhanam
aiśvaryāṣṭadalaṃ śvetaṃ paraṃ vairāgyakarṇikam
chidrāṇi ca diśo yasya prāṇādyāś ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ
prāṇādyaiścaiva saṃyuktaḥ paśyate bahudhā kramāt
daśaprāṇavahā nāḍyaḥ pratyekaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
dvgisaptatisahasrāṇi nāḍyaḥ saṃparikīrtitāḥ
netrasthañjāgrataṃ vidyātkaṇṭhe svapnaṃ samādiśet
suṣuptaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ tu turīyaṃ mūrdhani sthitam
jāgre brahmā ca viṣṇuś ca svapne caiva yathākramāt
īśvarastu suṣupte tu turīye ca maheśvaraḥ
ṇanobuddhirahaṅkāraṃ cittaṃ coti catuṣṭayam
karaṇāni vilīnāni yadā svātmani suvratāḥ
parasturīyātītosau śivaḥ paramakāraṇam
buddhīndriyāṇi viprendrās tathā karmendriyāṇi ca
manobuddirahaṅkāraścittaṃ ceti catuṣṭayam
adhyātmaṃ pṛthagevedaṃ caturdaśavidhaṃsmṛtam
draṣṭavyaṃ caiva śrotavyaṃ ghrātavyaṃ ca yathākramam
rasitavyaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sparśitavyaṃ tathaiva ca
tathā cetayitavyaṃ ca vaktavyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
ādityopi diśaścaiva pṛthivī varuṇas tathā
vāyuścandras tathā brahmā rudraḥ kṣetrajña eva ca
rājñī sudarśanā caiva jitā saumyā yathākramam
moghā rudrāmṛtā satyā madhyamā ca dvijottamāḥ
nāḍī rāśiśukā caiva asurā caiva kṛttikā
bhāsvatī nāḍayaścaitāścaturdaśanibandhanāḥ
vāyavo nāḍimadhyasthā vāhakāś ca caturdaśa
prāṇo vyānastvapānaś ca udānaś ca samānakaḥ
kūrmakaś ca tathā śyenaḥ śvetaḥ kṛṣmastathānilaḥ
yaścakṣuṣvatha draṣṭavye tathāditye ca suvratāḥ
nāḍyāṃ prāṇe ca vijñāne tvānande ca yathākramam
ātmā ekaś ca carati tamupāsīta māṃ prabhum
eṣa sarvādhipo devastvantaryāmī mahādyutiḥ
upāsyamāno vedaiś ca śāstrairnānāvidhairapi
na vaiṣa vedaśāstrāṇi sarvajñe yāsyati prabhuḥ
svātmanā rakṣitaṃ cādyādannabhūtaṃ na kutracit
sarvatra prāṇināmannaṃ prāṇināṃ granthirasmyaham
praśāstā nayanaścaiva pañcātmā sa vibhāgaśaḥ
prāṇamayaścendriyātmā saṃkalpātmā manomayaḥ
kālātmā soma eveha vijñānamaya ucyate
sadānandamayo bhūtvā maheśaḥ parameśvaraḥ
na prajñānaghanastvevaṃ na prājño jñānapūrvakaḥ
viditaṃ nāsti vedyaṃ ca nirvāṇaṃ paramārthataḥ
nirvāṇaṃ caiva kaivalyaṃ niḥśreyasamanāmayam
amṛtaṃ cākṣaraṃ brahma paramātmā parāparam
nirvikalpaṃ nirābhāsaṃ jñānaṃ paryāyavācakam
prasannaṃ ca yadekāgraṃ tadā jñānamiti smṛtam
ajñānamitaratsarvaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
rāgadveṣānṛtakrodhaṃ kāmatṛṣṇādibhiḥ sadā
aparāmṛṣṭamadyaiva vijñeyaṃ muktidaṃ tvidam
ajñānamalapūrvatvātpuruṣo malinaḥ smṛtaḥ
jñānamekaṃ vinā nāsti puṇyapāpaparikṣayaḥ
jñānābhyāsāddhi vai puṃsāṃ buddhirbhavati nirmalā
tasmātsadābhyasejjñānaṃ tanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ
jñānābhyāsarato nityaṃ jñānatattvārthavitsvayam
varṇāśramābhimānī yastyaktakrodho dvijottamāḥ
anyatra ramate mūḍhaḥ so 'jñānī nātra saṃśayaḥ
saṃsāraheturajñānaṃ saṃsārastanusaṃgrahaḥ
mokṣahetus tathā jñānaṃ muktaḥ svātmanyavasthitaḥ
ajñāne sati viprendrāḥ krodhādyā nātra saṃśayaḥ
dharmādharmau hi teṣāṃ ca tadvaśāttanusaṃgrahaḥ
śarīre sati vai kleśaḥ sovidyāṃ saṃtyajedbudhaḥ
krodhādyā nāśamāyānti dharmādharmau ca vai dvijāḥ
tatkṣayācca śarīreṇa na punaḥ saṃprayujyate
sa eva muktaḥ saṃsārādduḥkhatrayavivarjitaḥ
evaṃ jñānaṃ vinā nāsti dhyānaṃ dhyātur dvijarṣabhāḥ
jñānaṃ gurorhi saṃparkānna vācā paramārthataḥ
caturvyūhamiti jñātvā dhyātā dhyānaṃ samabhyaset
sahajāgantukaṃ pāpamasthivāgudbhavaṃ tathā
jñānāgnirdahate kṣipraṃsuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ
jñānātparataraṃ nāsti sarvapāpavināśanam
abhyasecca sadā jñānaṃ sarvasaṃgavivarjitaḥ
jñāninaḥ sarvapāpāni jīryante nātra saṃśayaḥ
jñānaṃ yathā tathā dhyānaṃ tasmāddhyānaṃ samabhyaset
dhyānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ proktam ādau saviṣayaṃ tathā
ṣaṭprakāraṃ samabhyasya cutaḥṣaṭdaśabhis tathā
tathā dvādaśadhā caiva punaḥ ṣoḍaśadhā kramāt
śuddhajāṃbūnadākāraṃ vadhūmāṅgārasannibham
ahiṃsakaḥ satyavādī asteyī sarvayatnataḥ
saṃtuṣṭaḥ śaucasaṃpannaḥ svādhyāyanirataḥ sadā
na budhyati tathā dhyātā sthāpya cittaṃ dvijottamāḥ
na ghrāti na śṛṇotyeva līnaḥ svātmani yaḥ svayam
na ca sparśaṃ vijānāti sa vai samarasaḥ smṛtaḥ
vāhnena kālarudrākhyo vāyutattve maheśvaraḥ
suṣire sa śivaḥ sākṣātkramādevaṃ vicintayet
kṣitau śarvaḥ smṛto devo hy apāṃ bhava iti smṛtaḥ
bhīmaḥ suṣiranāke 'sau bhāskare maṇḍale sthitaḥ
īśānaḥ somabiṃve ca mahādeva iti smṛtaḥ
puṃsā paśupatirdevaścāṣṭadhāhaṃ vyavasthitaḥ
kāṭhinyaṃ yattanau sarvaṃ pārthivaṃ parigīyate
yatsaṃcarati tadvāyuḥ suṣiraṃ yaddvijottamāḥ
tadākāśaṃ ca vijñānaṃ śabdajaṃ vyomasaṃbhavam
tathaiva viprā vijñānaṃ sparśākhyaṃ vāyusaṃbhavam
rūpaṃ vāhneyamityuktamāpyaṃ rasamayaṃ dvijāḥ
gandhākhyaṃ pārthivaṃ bhūyaścintayedbhāskaraṃ kramāt
netre ca dakṣiṇe vāme somaṃ hṛdī vibhuṃ dvijāḥ
ājānu pṛthivītattvamānābhervārimaṇḍalam
ākaṇṭhaṃ vahnitattvaṃ syāllalāṭāntaṃ dvijottamāḥ
vāyavyaṃ vai lalāṭādyaṃ vyomākhyaṃ vā śikhāgrakam
na jīvaḥ prakṛtiḥ sattvaṃ rajaścātha tamaḥ punaḥ
mahāṃstathābhimānaś ca tanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca
vyomādīni ca bhūtāni naiveha paramārthataḥ
vyāpya tiṣṭhadyato viśvaṃ sthāṇurityabhidhīyate
dadhāti bhūmirākāśamavakāśaṃ dadāti ca
tadājñayā tataṃ sarvaṃ tasmādvai cintayeddvijāḥ
tenaivādhiṣṭhitaṃ tasmādetatsarvaṃ dvijottamāḥ
saṃsāraviṣataptānāṃ jñānadhyānāmṛtena vai
pratīkāraḥ samākhyāto nānyathā dvijasattamāḥ
jñānaṃ dharmodbhavaṃ sākṣajjñānādvairāgyasaṃbhavaḥ
vairāgyātparamaṃ jñānaṃ paramārthaprakāśakam
yogasiddhyā vimuktiḥ syātsattvaniṣṭhasya nānyathā
sattvaśaktiṃ samāsthāya śivamabhyarcayeddvijāḥ
sarvato dharmaniṣṭhaś ca sadotsāhī samāhitaḥ
ṛjusvabhāvaḥ satataṃ svasthacitto mṛduḥ sadā
amānī buddhimāñchāntastyaktaspardho dvijottamāḥ
sadā mumukṣurdharmajñaḥ svātmalakṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ
ṛṇatrayavinirmuktaḥ pūrvajanmani puṇyabhāk
jarāyukto dvijo bhūtvā śraddhayā ca guroḥ kramāt
anyathā vāpi śuśrūṣāṃ kṛtvā kṛtrimavarjitaḥ
āsādya bhārataṃ varṣaṃ brahmavijjāyate dvijāḥ
saṃparkājjñānamāsādya jñānino yogavidbhavet
kramoyaṃ malapūrṇasya jñānaprāpterdvijottamāḥ
tasmādanena mārgeṇa tyaktasaṃgo dṛḍhavrataḥ
saṃsārakālakūṭākhyānmucyate munipuṅgavāḥ
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ mayā yuṣmākamacyutam
jñānasyaiveha māhātmyaṃ prasaṃgādiha śobhanam
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ kathitaṃ tvīśvareṇa tu
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi śivoktaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi saṃsāraśamanaṃ naraḥ
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge saṃsāraviṣakathanaṃ nāma ṣaḍaśītimo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
niśamya te mahāprājñāḥ kumārādyāḥ pinākinam
procuḥ praṇamya vai bhītāḥ prasannaṃ parameśvaram
sūta uvāca
evamuktaḥ prahasyeśaḥ pinākī nīlalohitaḥ
prāhatāmaṃbikāṃ prekṣya praṇipatya sthitān dvijān
akārtajñaḥ paśurjīvo vibhurbhoktā hyaṇuḥ pumān
māyī ca māyayā baddhaḥ karmabhir yujyate tu saḥ
jñānaṃ dhyānaṃ ca bandhaś ca mokṣo nāstyātmano dvijāḥ
eṣā vidyā hyahaṃ vedyaḥ prajñaiṣā ca śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ
dhṛtireṣā mayā niṣṭhā jñānaśaktiḥ kriyā tathā
icchākhyā ca tathā hyajñā dve vidye na ca saṃśayaḥ
na hyeṣā prakṛtirjaivī vikṛtiś ca vicārataḥ
purā mamājña madvaktrātsamutpannā sanātanī
pañcavaktrā mahābhāgā jagatāmabhayapradā
tāmājñāṃ saṃpraviśyāhaṃ cintayan jagatāṃ hitam
saptaviṃśatprakāreṇa sarvaṃ vyāpyānayā śivaḥ
sūta uvāca
evamuktvā tadāpaśyadbhavānīṃ parameśvaraḥ
bhavānī ca tamālokya māyāmaharadavyayā
te māyāmalanirmuktā munayaḥ prekṣya pārvatīm
prītā babhūvurmuktāś ca tasmādeṣā parā gatiḥ
umāśaṅkarayorbhedo nāstyeva paramārthataḥ
dvidhāsau rūpamāsthāya sthita eva na saṃśayaḥ
yadā vidvānasaṃgaḥ syādājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ
tadā muktiḥ kṣaṇādeva nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ
kramo 'vivakṣito bhūtavivṛddhaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
prasādena kṣaṇānmuktiḥ pratijñaiṣā na saṃśayaḥ
garbhastho jāyamāno vā bālo vā taruṇopi vā
vṛddho vā mucyate jantuḥ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ
prasādāddevadevasya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
eṣa eva jagannātho bandhamokṣakaraḥ śivaḥ
bhūrbhūvaḥsvarmahaścaiva janaḥ sākṣāttapaḥ svayam
satyaloka stathāṇḍānāṃ koṭikoṭiśatāni ca
vigrahaṃ devadevasya tathāṇḍāvaraṇāṣṭakam
tathānyeṣu ca lokeṣu vasaṃti ca carācarāḥ
sarve bhavāṃśajā nūnaṃ gatistveṣāṃ sa eva vai
viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ tathā jātaṃ bahudhā rudra eva saḥ
rudrājñaiṣā sthitā devī hyanayā muktiraṃbikā
ityevaṃ khecarāḥ siddhā jajalpuḥ prītamānasāḥ
yadāvalokya tān sarvānprasādādanayāṃbikā
tadā tiṣṭhanti sāyujyaṃ prāptāste khecarāḥ prabhoḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge munimohaśamanaṃ nāma saptāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
sūta uvāca
ṣaḍviṃśacchaktisaṃyuktamaṣṭadhā ca dvijottamāḥ
tataḥ ṣoḍaśadhā caiva punardvādaśadhā dvijāḥ
aṣṭaśaktisamāyuktamaṣṭamūrtimajaṃ prabhum
tābhiścāṣṭavidhā rudrāścatuḥṣaṣṭividhāḥ punaḥ
śaktayaś ca tathā sarvā guṇāṣṭakasamanvitāḥ
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ mokṣasiddhipradāyakam
tasyāṇinādayo viprā nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ
tatrāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryaṃ yogināṃ samudāhṛtam
prākāmyaṃ caiva sarvatra īśitvaṃ caiva sarvataḥ
taccāpi trividhaṃ jñeyamaiśvaryaṃ sārvakāmikam
sāvadyaṃ nāma yattatra pañcabhūtātmakaṃ smṛtam
indriyāṇi manaścaiva ahaṅkāraś ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ
tatra sūkṣmapravṛttistu pañcabhūtātmikā punaḥ
indriyāṇi manaścittabuddhyahaṅkārasaṃjñitam
punaraṣṭaguṇaścāpi sūkṣmeṣveva vidhīyate
tasya rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāha bhagavānprabhuḥ
aṇimādyaṃ tathāvyaktaṃ sarvatraiva pratiṣṭhitam
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ duṣprāpyaṃ samudāhṛtam
śīghratvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu dvitīyaṃ tu padaṃ smṛtam
prākāmān viṣayān bhuṅkte tathāpratihataḥ kvacit
vaśyāni cāsya bhūtāni trailokye sacarācare
aṇutvāttu paraḥ sūkṣmaḥ sūkṣmatvādapavargikaḥ
vyāpakastvapavargācca vyāpakātpuruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ
puruṣaḥ sūkṣmabhāvāttu aiśvarye parame sthitaḥ
aiśvaryaṃ cāpratīghātaṃ prāpya yogamanuttamam
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ jñātavyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
svargāpavargaphaladaṃ śivasāyujyakāraṇam
athavā gatavijñāno rāgātkarma samācaret
rājasaṃ tāsamaṃ vāpi bhuktvā tatraiva mucyate
tasmātsthānātpunaḥ śreṣṭho mānuṣyamupapadyate
pariśramo hi yajñānāṃ mahatārthena vartate
bhūyo mṛtyuvaśaṃ yāti tasmānmokṣaḥ paraṃ sukham
dṛṣṭvā tu puruṣaṃ divyaṃ viśvākhyaṃ viśvatomukham
viśvapādaśirogrīvaṃ viśveśaṃ viśvarūpiṇam
viśvagandhaṃ viśvamālyaṃ viśvāṃbaradharaṃ prabhum
kaviṃ purāṇamanusāsitāraṃ sūkṣmācca sūkṣmaṃ mahato mahāntam
aliṅginaṃ nirguṇaṃ cetanaṃ ca nityaṃ sadā sarvagaṃ sarvasāram
paśyanti yuktyā hyacalaprakāśaṃ tadbhāvitāstejasā dīpyamānam
apāṇipādodarapārśvajihvo hyatīndriyo vāpi susūkṣma ekaḥ
paśyatyacakṣuḥ sa śṛṇotyakarṇo na cāstyabuddhaṃ na ca buddhirāsti
ace tanāṃ sarvagatāṃ sūkṣmāṃ prasavadharmiṇīm
prakṛtiṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ yuktāḥ paśyanti yoginaḥ
sarvataḥ pāṇipādaṃ tatsarvatokṣiśiromukham
sarvataḥ śrutimaṃlloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati
puruṣaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ taṃ vidvānna vimuhyati
bhūtātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ paramātmānamavyayam
strīpuṃsoḥ saṃprayoge hi jāyate hi tataḥ prabhuḥ
kālena kalalaṃ cāpi budvudaṃ saṃprajāyate
mṛtpiṇḍastu yathā cakre cakraāvartena pīḍitaḥ
evamādhyātmikairyuktā vāyunā saṃprapūritaḥ
yāvaddhi vaiṣṇavo vāyurjātamātraṃ na saṃspṛśet
tāvatkālaṃ mahādevamarcayāmīti cintayet
jāyate mānuṣastatra yathārūpaṃ yathāvayaḥ
jalātsaṃbhavati prāṇaḥ prāṇācchukraṃ vivardhate
raktabhāgāstrayastriṃśadretobhāgāścaturdaśa
pituḥ śarīrātpratyaṅgaṃ rūpamasyopajāyate
tato 'sya māturāhārāt pītalīḍhapraveśanāt
nābhideśena vai prāṇāste hyādhārā hi dehinām
navamāsātparīkliṣṭaḥ saṃveṣṭitaśirodharaḥ
veṣṭitaḥ sarvagātraiś ca aparyāpta praveśanaḥ
navamāsoṣitaścāpi yonicchidrādavāṅmukhaḥ
tāḍanaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ caiva pūyaśoṇitabhakṣaṇam
yathā hyāpastu saṃchinnāḥ saṃśleṣmamupayānti vai
tathā chinnāś ca bhinnāścayātanāsthānamāgatāḥ
evaṃ jīvāstu taiḥ pāpaistapyamānāḥ svayaṅkṛtaiḥ
prāpnuyuḥ karmabhiḥ śeṣairduḥkhaṃ vā yadi vetarat
te nityaṃ yamaviṣyeṣu saṃpravṛttāḥ krośantaḥ satatamaniṣṭasaṃprayogaiḥ
śuṣyante parigatavedanāśarīrābahvībhiḥ subhṛśamanantayātanābhiḥ
karmaṇa manasā vācā yadabhīkṣṇaṃ niṣevate
tadabhyāso haratyenaṃ tasmātkalyāṇamācaret
anādimānprabandhaḥ syātpūrvakarmaṇi dehinaḥ
saṃsāraṃ tāmasaṃ ghoraṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ pratipadyate
mānuṣyātpaśubhāvaś ca paśubhāvānmṛgo bhavet
mṛgatvātpakṣibhāvaś ca tasmāccaiva sarīsṛpaḥ
sarīsṛpatvādgacchedvai sthāvaratvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
ityevaṃ hi manuṣyādiḥ saṃsāraḥ sthāvarātikaḥ
sāttvikaścāpi saṃsāro brahmādiḥ parikīrtitaḥ
piśācāntaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ svargasthāneṣu dehinām
caturdaśānāṃ sthānānāṃ madhye viṣṭaṃbhakaṃrajaḥ
saṃsāraḥ pūrvadharmasya bhāvanābhiḥ praṇoditaḥ
mānuṣaṃ bhajate nityaṃ tasmāddhyānaṃ samācaret
nityaṃ samārabheddharmaṃ saṃsārabhayapīḍitaḥ
tathā samārabhedyogaṃ yathātmānaṃ sa paśyati
eṣa āpaḥ paraṃ jyotireṣa seturanuttamaḥ
vivṛtyā hyeṣa saṃbhedādbhutānāṃ caiva śāśvataḥ
hṛdisthaṃ sarvabhūtānāmupāsīta maheśvaram
tathāntaḥ saṃsthitaṃ devaṃ svaśaktyā parimaṇḍitam
aṣṭadhā cāṣṭadhā caiva tathā cāṣṭavidhena ca
sṛṣṭyarthaṃ saṃsthitaṃ vahniṃ saṃkṣipya ca hṛdi sthitam
dhyātvā yathāvaddeveśaṃ rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam
hutvā pañcāhutīḥ samyak taccintāgatamānasaḥ
vaiśvānaraṃ hṛdisthaṃ tu yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
āpaḥ pūtāḥ sakṛtprāśya tūṣṇīṃ hutvā hyupāviśan
prāṇāyeti tatastasya prathamā hyāhutiḥ smṛtāḥ
apānāya dvitīyā ca vyānāyeti tathā parā
udānāya caturthi syātsamānāyoti pañcamī
svāhākāraiḥ pṛthag hutvā śeṣaṃ bhuñjīta kāmataḥ
apaḥ punaḥ sakṛtprāśya ācamya hṛdayaṃ spṛśet
prāṇānāṃ granthirasyātmā rudro hyātmā viśāntakaḥ
prāṇe niviṣṭo vai rudrastasmātprāṇamayaḥ svayam
śivāviśeha māmīśa svāhā brahmātmane svayam
evaṃ pañcāhutīścaiva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ
tvaṃ devānāmasi cyeṣṭho rudrastvaṃ ca purovṛṣā
ityevaṃ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ guṇaprāptiviśeṣataḥ
savasya jagataścaiva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ
tvaṃ devānāmasi jyeṣṭho rudrastvaṃ ca puro vṛṣā
ityevaṃ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ guṇaprāptiviśeṣataḥ
yogācāraḥ svayaṃ tena brahmaṇā kathitaḥpurā
evaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ jñātavyaṃ ca prayatnataḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge 'ṇimādyaṣṭasiddhitriguṇasaṃsāraprāgnau homādivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi śaucācārasya lakṣaṇam
yadanuṣṭhāya śuddhātmā paretya gatimāpnuyāt
brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ sarvabhūtahitāya vai
saṃkṣepātsarvavedārthaṃ saṃcayaṃ brahmavādinām
udayārthaṃ tu śaucānāṃ munīnāmuttamaṃ padam
mānāvamānau dvāvetau tāvevāhurviṣāmṛte
prāpyānujñāṃ tataścaiva jñānayogamanuttamam
cakṣuḥpūtaṃ carenmārgaṃ vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ pibet
satyapūtaṃ vadedvākyaṃ manaḥpūtaṃ samācaret
matsyagṛhyasya yatpāpaṃṣaṇmāsābhyantare bhavet
ekāhaṃ tatsamaṃ jñeyamapūtaṃ yajjalaṃ bhavet
aghoralakṣaṇaṃ mantraṃ tataḥ śuddhimavāpnuyāt
athavā pūjayecchaṃbhuṃ ghṛtasrānādivistaraiḥ
tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya śuddhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
tathā yuktaṃ caredbhaikṣyaṃ satāṃ dharmamadūṣayan
bhaikṣyaṃ caredvanastheṣu yāyāvaragṛheṣu ca
śreṣṭhā tu prathamā hīyaṃ vṛttirasyopajāyate
ata ūrdhvaṃ gṛhastheṣu śīlīneṣu careddvijāḥ
śraddadhāneṣu dānteṣu śrotriyeṣu mahātmasu
ata ūrdhvaṃ punaścāpi aduṣṭāpatiteṣu ca
bhaikṣyaṃ yavāgūstakraṃ vā payo yāvakameva ca
phalamūlādi pakvaṃ vā kaṇapiṇyākasaktavaḥ
āhārāsteṣu siddheṣu śreṣṭhaṃ bhaikṣyamiti smṛtam
abvinduṃ yaḥ kuśāgreṇa māsimāsi samaśnute
nyāyato yaścaredbhaikṣyaṃ pūrvoktātsa viśiṣyate
dadhibhakṣāḥ payobhakṣā ye cānye jīvakṣīṇakāḥ
sarve te bhaikṣyabhakṣasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm
bhasmaśāyī bhavennityaṃ bhikṣācārī jitendriyaḥ
ya icchet paramaṃ sthānaṃ vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caret
yogināṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ bhavet
ekaṃ dve trīṇi catvāri śaktito vā samācaret
vratāni pañca bhikṣūṇāmahiṃsā paramā tviha
akrodho guruśuśruṣā śaucamāhāralāghavam
nityaṃ svādhyāya ityete niyamāḥ parikīrtitāḥ
yathā dvipa ivāraṇye manuṣyāṇāṃ vidhīyate
devaistulyāḥ sarvayajñakriyāstu yajñājjāpyaṃ jñānamāhuś ca jāpyāt
jñānaddhyānāṃ saṃgarāgādapetaṃ tasminprāpte śāśvatasyopalaṃbhaḥ
damaḥ śamaḥ satyamakalmaṣatvaṃ maunaṃ ca bhūteṣvakhileṣu cārjavam
atindriyaṃ jñānamidaṃ tathā śivaṃ prāhus tathā jñānaviśuddhabuddhayaḥ
samāpnuyādyogamimaṃ mahātmā maharṣayaścaivamaninditāmalāḥ
prāpyate 'bhimatān deśānaṅkuśena nivāritaḥ
etanmārgeṇa śuddhena dagdhabījo hyakalmaṣaḥ
sadācāraratāḥ śāntāḥ svadharmaparipālakāḥ
pitāmahenopadiṣṭo dharmaḥ sākṣātsanātanaḥ
sarvalokopakārārthaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ pravadāmi vaḥ
gurūpadeśayuktānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ kramavarttinām
abhyutthānādikaṃ sarvaṃ praṇāmaṃ caiva kārayet
aṣṭāṅgapraṇipātenatridhā nyastena suvratāḥ
jyeṣṭhānyepi ca te sarve vandanīyā vijānatā
ājñābhaṅgaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchatsiddhimuttamām
viṣagrahaviḍaṃbādīnvarjayetsarvayatnataḥ
kaitavaṃ vittaśāṭhyaṃ ca paiśunyaṃ varjayetsadā
atihāsamavaṣṭaṃbhaṃ līlāsvecchāpravartanam
yatīnāmāsanaṃ vastraṃ daṇḍādyaṃ pāduke tathā
mālyaṃ ca śayanasthānaṃ pātrañchāyāṃ ca yatnataḥ
yajñopakaraṇāṅgaṃ ca na spṛśed vai padena ca
kṛtvā pramādato viprāḥ praṇavasyāyutaṃ japet
saṃdhyālope kṛte vipraḥ trirāvṛttyaiva śuddhyati
laṅghane samayānāṃ tu abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇe
kākolūkakapotānāṃ pakṣiṇāmapi ghātane
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ japtvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
smaraṇācchuddhimāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
naivamātmavidāmasti prāyaścittāni codanā
yogadhyānaikaniṣṭhāś ca nirlepāḥ kāñcanaṃ yathā
śuddhānāṃ śodhanaṃ nāsti viśuddhā brahmavidyayā
uddhṛtānuṣṇapenābhiḥ pūtābhir vastracakṣuṣā
paṅkāśmadūṣitaṃ caiva sāmudraṃ palvalodakam
saśaivālaṃ tathānyairvā doṣairduṣṭaṃ vivarjayet
vastraśaucānvitaḥ kuryātsarvakāryāṇi vai dvijāḥ
namaskārādikaṃ sarvaṃ guruśuśrūṣaṇādikam
vastraśaucavihīnātmā hyaśucirnātra saṃśayaḥ
devakāryopayuktānāṃ pratyahaṃ śaucamiṣyate
itareṣāṃ hi vastrāṇāṃ śaucaṃ kāryaṃ malāgame
kauśayāvikayo rukṣaiḥ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ
śrīphalairaṃśupaṭṭānāṃ kutapānāmariṣṭakaiḥ
carmaṇāṃ vidalānāṃ ca vetrāṇāṃ vastravanmatam
valkalānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ chatracāmarayorapi
bhasmanā śuddhyate kāṃsyaṃ kṣāreṇāyasam ucyate
haimamadbhiḥ śubhaṃ pātraṃ raupyapātraṃ dvijottamāḥ
maṇyaśmaśaṅkhamuktānāṃ śaucaṃ taijasavatsmṛtam
rasānāmiha sarvaṣāṃ śuddhirutplavanaṃ smṛtam
tṛṇakāṣṭhādivastūnāṃ śubhenābhyukṣaṇaṃ smṛtam
uṣṇena vāriṇā śuddhis tathā sruksruvayorapi
tathaiva yajñapātrāṇāṃ muśalolūkhalasya ca
śṛṅgāsthidārudantānāṃ takṣaṇenaiva śodhanam
saṃhatānāṃ mahābhāgā dravyāṇāṃ prokṣaṇaṃ smṛtam
asaṃhatānāṃ dravyāṇaṃ pratyekaṃ śaucamucyate
abhuktarāśidhānyānāmekadeśasya dhūṣaṇe
tāvanmātraṃ samuddhṛtya prokṣayedvai kuśāṃbhasā
śākamūlaphalādīnāṃ dhānyavacchuddhiriṣyate
gonivāsena vai śuddhā secanena dharā smṛtā
bhūmisthamudakaṃśuddhaṃ vaitṛṣṇyaṃ yatra gaurvrajet
vatsaḥ śuciḥ prasravaṇe śakuniḥ phalapātane
svādārāsyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ ratau bhāryābhikāṅkṣayā
hastābhyāṃ kṣālitaṃ vastraṃ kāruṇā ca yathāvidhi
kuśāṃbunā susaṃprokṣya gṛhṇīyāddharmavittamaḥ
paṇyaṃ prasāritaṃ caiva varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ
śucirākarajaṃ teṣāṃ śvā mṛgagrahaṇe śuciḥ
chāyā ca vipluṣo viprā makṣikādyā dvijottamāḥ
rajobhūrvāyuragniś ca medhyāni sparśane sadā
suptvā bhuktvā ca vai viprāḥ kṣuttvā pītvā ca vai tathā
ṣṭhīvitvādhyayanādau ca śucirapyācametpunaḥ
pādau spṛśanti ye cāpi parācamanabindavaḥ
kṛtvā ca maithunaṃ spṛṣṭvā patitaṃ kukkuṭādikam
sūkaraṃ caiva kākādi śvānamuṣṭraṃ kharaṃ tathā
yūpaṃ cāṇḍālakādyāṃś ca spṛṣṭvā snānena śudhyati
rajasvalāṃ sūtikāṃ ca na spṛśedantyajāmapi
sūtikāśaucasaṃyuktaḥ śāvāśaucasamanvitaḥ
saṃspṛśenna rajastāsāṃ spṛṣṭvā snātvaiva śudhyati
naivāśaucaṃ yatīnāṃ ca vanasthabrahmacāriṇām
naiṣṭhikānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca maṇḍalīnāṃ ca suvratāḥ
tataḥ kāryavirodhāddhi nṛpāṇāṃ nānyathā bhavet
vaikhānasānāṃ viprāṇāṃ patitānāmasaṃbhavāt
asaṃcayadvijānāṃ ca snānamātreṇa nānyathā
tathā saṃnihitānāṃ ca yajñārthaṃ dīkṣitasya ca
ekāhādyajñayājīnāṃ śuddhiruktā svayaṃbhuvā
tatastvadhītaśākhānāṃ caturbhiḥ sarvadehinām
avārgekādaśāhāntaṃ bāndhavānāṃ dvijottamāḥ
tata ṛtutrayādarvāgekāhaḥ parigīyate
saptavarṣāttataścārvāk trirātraṃ hi tataḥ param
daśāhaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ vai prathame 'hani vā pituḥ
daśāhaṃ sūtikāśaucaṃ māturapyevamavyayāḥ
arvāk trivarṣātsnānena bāndhavānāṃ pituḥ sadā
aṣṭabdādekarātreṇa śuddhiḥ syādbrāndhavasya tu
dvādaśābdāttataścārvāk trirātraṃ strīṣu suvratāḥ
ātikraānte daśāhe tu trirātramaśucirbhavet
tataḥ saṃnihito vipraścārvāk pūrvaṃ tadeva vai
saṃvatsare vyatīte tu snānamātreṇa śudhyati
spṛṣṭvā pretantrirātreṇa dharmārthaṃ snānamucyate
dāhakānāṃ ca netṝṇāṃ snānamātramabāndhave
anugamya ca vai snātvā ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyati
ācāryamaraṇe caiva trirātraṃ śrotriye mṛte
pakṣiṇī mātulānāṃ ca sodarāṇāṃ ca vā dvijāḥ
bhūpānāṃ maṇḍalīnāṃ ca sadyo nīrāṣṭravāsinām
kevalaṃ dvādaśāhena kṣattriyāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ
nābhiṣiktasya cāśaucaṃ saṃpramādeṣu vai raṇe
vaiśyaḥ pañcadaśāhena śūdro māsena śudhyati
aśaucaṃ cānupūrvyeṇa yatīnāṃ naiva vidyate
tretāprabhṛti nārīṇāṃ māsi māsyārtavaṃ dvijāḥ
prayānti ca mahābhāgā bhāryābhiḥ kuravo yathā
varṇāśramavyavasthā ca tretāprabhṛti suvratāḥ
bhārate dakṣiṇe varṣe vyavasthā netareṣvatha
mahāvīte suvīte ca jaṃbūdvīpe tathāṣṭasu
śākadvīpādiṣu prokto dharmo vai bhārate yathā
rasollāsā kṛte vṛttistretāyāṃ gṛhavṛkṣajā
saivārtavakṛtāddoṣādrāgadveṣādibhir nṛṇām
yavādyāḥ saṃprajāyante grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa
oṣadhyaś ca rajodoṣāḥ strīṇāṃ rāgādibhir nṛṇām
akālakṛṣṭā vidhvastāḥ punarutpāditās tathā
prathame 'hani cāṇḍālī yathāvajyā tathāṅganā
snātvārdhamāsātsaṃśuddhā tataḥ śuddhirbhaviṣyati
āṣoḍaśāttataḥ strīṇāṃ mūtravacchaucamiṣyate
pañcarātraṃ tathāspṛśyā rajasā vartate yadi
sā viṃśaddivasādūrdhvaṃ rajasā pūrvavattathā
snāne śaucaṃ tathā gānaṃ rodanaṃ hasanaṃ tathā
yānamabhyañjanaṃ nārī dyūtaṃ caivānulepanam
divāsvapnaṃ viśeṣeṇa tathā vai dantadhāvanam
maithunaṃ mānasaṃ vāpi vācikaṃ devatārcanam
rajasvalāṅganāsparśasaṃbhāṣe ca rajasvalā
saṃtyāgaṃ caiva vastrāṇāṃ varjayetsarvayatnataḥ
snātvānyapuruṣaṃ nārī na spṛśettu rajasvalā
īkṣayedbhāskaraṃ devaṃ brahmakūrcaṃ tataḥ vibet
kevalaṃ pañcagavyaṃ vā kṣīraṃ vā cātmaśuddhaye
caturthyāṃ strī na gamyā tu gatolpāyuḥ prasūyate
vidyāhīnaṃ vratabhraṣṭaṃ patitaṃ pāradārikam
dāridryārṇavamagnaṃ ca tanayaṃ sā prasūyate
raktādhikyādbhavennārī śukraādhikye bhavetpumān
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ gamyā mahābhāgā satputrajananī bhavet
pumiti narakasyākhyā duḥkhaṃ ca narakaṃ viduḥ
puṃsastrāṇānvitaṃ putraṃ tathābhūtaṃ prasūyate
aṣṭamyāṃ sarvasaṃpannaṃ tanayaṃ saṃprasūyate
navamyāṃ dārikā yārthi daśamyāṃ paṇḍitā bhavet
ekādaśyāṃ tathā nārīṃ janayetsaiva pūrvavat
dvādaśyāṃ dharmatattvajñaṃ śrautasmārtapravartakam
trayodaśyāṃ jaḍāṃ nārīṃ sarvasaṃkarakāriṇīm
caturdaśyāṃ yadā gaccetsā putrajananī bhavet
pañcadaśyāṃ ca dharmiṣṭhāṃ ṣoḍaśyāṃ jñānapāragam
strīṇāṃ vai mathune kāle vāmapārśve prabhañjanaḥ
caredyadi bhavennārī pumāṃsaṃ dakṣiṇe labhet
strīṇāṃ maithunakāle tu pāpagrahavivarjite
uktakāle śucirbhūtvā śuddhāṃ gacchecchucismitām
ityevaṃ saṃprasaṃgena yatīnāṃ dharmasaṃgrahe
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ sadācāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchūṇuyādvāpi sadācāraṃ śucirnaraḥ
śrāvayedvā yathānyāyaṃ brāhmaṇān dagdhakilbiṣān
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sadācārakathanaṃ nāmaukonanavati tamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
atha ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yatīnāmiha niścitam
prāyaścittaṃ śivaproktaṃ yatīnāṃ pāpaśodhanam
pāpaṃ hi trividhaṃ jñeyaṃ vāṅmanaḥ kāyasaṃbhavam
satataṃ hi divā rātrau yenedaṃ veṣṭyate jagat
tatkarmaṇā vināpyeṣa tiṣṭhatīti parā śrutiḥ
kṣaṇamevaṃ prayojyaṃ tu āyuṣyaṃ tu vidhāraṇam
na hi yogātparaṃ kiñcinnarāṇāṃ dṛśyate śubham
tasmā dyogaṃ praśaṃsaṃti dharmayuktā manīṣiṇaḥ
dṛṣṭvāparāvaraṃ dhīrāḥ paraṃ gacchanti tatpadam
vratāni yāni bhīkṣūṇāṃ tathaivopavratāni ca
ekaikātikrame teṣāṃ prāyāścittaṃ vidhīyate
upetya tu striyaṃ kāmātprāyaścittaṃ vinirdiśet
prāṇāyāmasamāyuktaṃ caretsāṃtapanaṃ vratam
tataścarati nirdeśātkṛcchraṃ cānte samāhitaḥ
punārāśramamāgatya caredbhikṣuratandritaḥ
na dharmayuktamanṛtaṃ hinastīti manīṣiṇaḥ
tathāpi na ca kartavyaṃ prasaṃgo hyeṣa dāruṇaḥ
ahorātrapavāsaś ca prāmāyāmaśataṃ tathā
hiṃsā hyeṣā parā sṛṣṭā stainyaṃ vai kathitaṃ tathā
yadetaddraviṇaṃ nāma prāṇā hyete bahiścarāḥ
evaṃ kṛtvā suduṣṭātmā bhinnavṛtto vratāccyutaḥ
bhūyo nirvedamāpannaścareccāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam
vidhinā śāstradṛṣṭena saṃvatsaramiti śrutiḥ
tataḥ saṃvatsarasyānte bhūyaḥ prakṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ
ahiṃsā sarvabhūtānāṃ karmaṇā manasā girā
akāmādapi hiṃseta yadi bhikṣuḥ paśūn kṛmīn
kṛcchrātikṛcchraṃ kurvīta cāndrāyaṇamathāpi vā
tena dhārayitavyā vai prāṇāyāmāstu ṣoṭaśa
trirātramupavāsāś ca prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā
rātrau skannaḥ śuciḥ snātvā dvādaśaiva tu dhāraṇā
prāṇāyāmena śuddhātmā virajā jāyate dvijāḥ
ekānnaṃ madhumāṃsaṃ vā aśṛtānnaṃ tathaiva ca
abhojyāni yatīnāṃ tu pratyakṣalavaṇāni ca
ekaikātikramātteṣāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate
prājāpatyena kṛcchreṇa tataḥ pāpātpramucyate
vyatikramāś ca ye kecidvāṅmanaḥ kāyasaṃbhavāḥ
careddhi śuddhaḥ samaloṣṭhakāñcanaḥ samastabhūteṣu ca satsamāhitaḥ
sthānaṃ dhruvaṃ śāśvatamavyayaṃ tu paraṃ hi gatvā na punarhi jāyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge yatiprāyāścittaṃ nāma navatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ariṣṭāni nibodhata
yena jñānaviśeṣeṇa mṛtyuṃ paśyanti yoginaḥ
arundhatīṃ dhruvaṃ caiva somacchāyāṃ mahāpatham
ariśmavantamādityaṃ raśmivantaṃ ca pāvakam
yaḥ paśyati na jīvedvai māsādekādaśātparam
vamenmūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tathā
pratyakṣamathavā svapne daśamāsānna jīvati
paśyetpratorpaśācāṃś ca navamāsān sa jīvati
prakṛteś ca nivarteta cāṣṭau māsaṃś ca jīvati
agrataḥ pṛṣṭhato vāpi khaṇḍaṃ yasya padaṃ bhavet
pāṃsuke kardame vāpi saptamāsānsa jīvati
kākaḥ kapoto gṛdhro vā nilīyedyasya mūrdhani
kravyādo vā khago yasya ṣaṇmāsānnativartate
gacchedvāyasapaṅktībhiḥ pāṃsuvarṣeṇa vā punaḥ
svacchāyāṃ vikṛtāṃ paśyeccatuḥ pañca sa jīvati
anabhre vidyutaṃ paśyeddakṣiṇāṃ diśamāsthitām
udake dhanur aidraṃ vā trīṇi dvau vā sa jīvati
apsu vā yadi vādarśe yo hyātmānaṃ na paśyati
aśiraskaṃ tathā paśyenmāsādvardhvaṃ na jīvati
yasya vai snātamātrasya hṛdayaṃ pariśuṣyati
dhūmaṃ vā mastakātpaśyeddaśāhānna sa jīvati
ādbhiḥ spṛṣṭo na hṛṣyeta tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
ṛkṣavānarayuktena rathenāśāṃ ca dakṣiṇām
kṛṣṇāṃbaradharā śyāmā gāyantī vāpyathāṅganā
yaṃ nayeddakṣiṇāmāśāṃ svapne sopi na jīvati
chidraṃvā svasya kaṇṭhasya svapne yo vīkṣate naraḥ
nagnaṃ vā śramaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidyānmṛtyumupasthitam
dṛṣṭvā tu tādṛśaṃ svapnaṃ sadya eva na jīvati
bhasmāṅgārāṃś ca keśāṃś ca nadīṃ śuṣkāṃ bhujaṅgamān
paśyedyo daśarātraṃ tu na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ
kṛṣṇaiś ca vikaṭaiścaiva puruṣairudyatāyudhaiḥ
pāṣāṇaistāḍyate svapne yaḥ sadyo na sa jīvāti
sūryodaye pratyuṣasi pratyakṣaṃ yasya vai śivāḥ
yasya vā snātamātrasya hṛdayaṃ pīḍyate bhṛśam
jāyate dantaharṣaś ca taṃ gatāyuṣamādiśet
bhūyobhūyastrasedyastu rātrau vā yadi vā divā
rātrau cendradhanuḥ paśyeddivā nakṣatramaṇḍalam
paranetreṣu cātmānaṃ na paśyenna sa jīvati
vakraā ca nāsā bhavati vijñeyo gatajīvitaḥ
yasya kṛṣṇā kharā jihvā padmābhāsaṃ ca vai mukham
gaṇḍevā piṇḍikārakte tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
muktakeśo hasaṃścaiva gāyannṛtyaṃś ca yo naraḥ
yasya śvetavanābhāsā śvetasarṣapasaṃnibhā
uṣṭrā vā rāsabhā vābhiyuktāḥ svapne rathe śubhāḥ
dve vātha parame 'riṣṭe ekībhūtaḥ paraṃ bhavet
ghoṣaṃ na śṛṇuyātkarṇejyotirnetre na paśyati
na cottiṣṭhati yaḥ śvabhrāttadantaṃ tasya jīvatam
ūrdhvā ca dṛṣṭirna ca saṃpratiṣṭhā raktā punaḥ saṃparivartamānā
mukhasya śoṣaḥ suṣirā ca nābhiratyuṣṇamūtro viṣamastha eva
divā vā yadi vā rātrau pratyakṣaṃ yo nihanyate
yastu prāvaraṇaṃ śuklaṃ svakaṃ paśyati mānavaḥ
tyaktvā khedaṃ viṣādaṃ ca upekṣedbruddhimānnaraḥ
prācīṃ vā yadi vodīcīṃ diśaṃ niṣkramyavai śuciḥ
udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukho vā svaśthaścācānta eva ca
yathā dīpo nivātastho neṅgate sopamā smṛtā
prāgudakpravaṇe deśe tathā yuñjīta śāstravit
kāmaṃ vitarkaṃ prītiṃ ca sukhaduḥkhe ubhe tathā
ghrāṇe ca rasane nityaṃ cakṣuṣī sparśane tathā
kālakarmāṇi vijñāya samūheṣveva nityaśaḥ
dvādaśādhyātmamityevaṃ yogadhāraṇamucyate
śatamardhaśataṃ vāpi dhāraṇāṃ mūrdhni dhārayet
khinnasya dhāraṇāyogādvāyurūrdhvaṃ pravartate
tataścāpūrayeddehamoṅkāreṇa samanvitaḥ
tathoṅkāramayo yogī akṣare tvakṣarī bhavet
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi oṅkāraprāptilakṣaṇam
eṣa trimātro vijñeyo vyañjanaṃ cātra ceśvaraḥ
prathamā vidyutī mātrā dvitīyā tāmasī smṛtā
tṛtīyāṃ nirguṇāṃ caiva mātrāmakṣaragāminīm
gāndhārī caiva vijñeyā gāndharasvarasaṃbhavā
pipīlikāgatisparśā prayuktā mūrdhni lakṣyate
yathā prayukta oṅkāraḥ pratiniryāti mūrdhani
praṇavo dhanuḥ śaro hyātmā brahmalakṣaṇamucyate
omityekākṣaraṃ hyetadguhāyāṃ nihitaṃ padam
viṣṇukramāstrayastvete ṛksāmāni yajūṃṣi ca
mātrā cārdhaṃ ca tisrastu vijñeyāḥ paramārthataḥ
akāro hyakṣaro jñeya ukāraḥ sahitaḥ smṛtaḥ
makārasahitoṅkārastrimātra iti saṃjñitaḥ
oṅkārastu trayo lokāḥ śirastasya triviṣṭapam
mātrāpādo rudraloko hyamātraṃ tu śivaṃ padam
evaṃ jñānaviśeṣeṇa tatpadaṃ samupāsyate
upāsyaṃ hi prayatnena śāśvataṃ sukhamicchatā
tataḥ plutavatī caiva tṛtīyā copadiśyate
etāstu mātrā vijñeyā yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
indriyāṇi mano buddhiṃ dhyāyannātmani yaḥ sadā
māsemāse 'śvamedhena yo yajeta śataṃ samāḥ
tena yatprāpyate puṇyaṃ mātrayā tadavāpnuyāt
na tathā tapasogreṇa na yajñairbhūridakṣiṇaiḥ
yatphalaṃ prāpyate samyaṅmātrayā tadavāpnuyāt
tatra caiṣā tu yā mātrā plutā nāmopadiśyate
eṣā eva bhavetkāryā gṛhasthānāṃ tu yoginām
eṣaā caiva viśeṣeṇa aiśvarye hyaṣṭalakṣaṇe
aṇimādye tu vijñeyā tasmādyuñjīta tāṃ dvijāḥ
evaṃ hi yogasaṃyuktaḥ śucirdāto jitendriyaḥ
ātmānaṃ vidyate yastu sa sarvaṃ vindate dvijāḥ
tasmātpāśupatairyogairātmānaṃ cintayedbudhaḥ
ātmānaṃ jānate ye tu śucayaste na saṃśayaḥ
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni vedopaniṣadas tathā
yogajñānādavāpnoti brāhmaṇo 'dhyātmacintakaḥ
yonisaṃkramaṇaṃ tyaktvā yāti vai śāśvataṃ padam
yathā vṛkṣāt phalaṃ pakvaṃ pavanena samīritam
namaskāreṇa rudrasya tathā pāpaṃ praṇaśyati
tasmāttriḥpravaṇaṃ yogī upāsīta maheśvaram
avimukteśvaraṃ gatvā vārāṇasyāṃ tu śodhanam
śrīparvate vā viprendrāḥ saṃtyajetsvatanuṃ naraḥ
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
avimuktaṃ paraṃ kṣetraṃ jantūnāṃ muktidaṃ sadā
seveta satataṃ dhīmān viśeṣānmaraṇāntike
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ariṣṭakathanaṃ nāma ekanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
evaṃ vārāṇasī puṇyā yadi sūta mahāmate
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ tatprabhāvaṃ hi sāṃpratam
vistareṇa yatānyāyaṃ śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ
sūta uvāca
vakṣye saṃkṣepataḥ samyak vārāṇasyāḥ suśobhanam
vistareṇa mayā vaktuṃ brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā
devaḥ purā kṛtodvāhaḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ
vārāṇasīmanuprāpya darśayāmāsaśaṅkaraḥ
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ vāsaṃ tatra cakāra saḥ
vārāṇasīkurukṣetraśrīparvatamahālaye
haimavatyāḥ svayaṃ devaḥ sanandī parameśvaraḥ
uktavānparameśānaḥ pārvatyāḥ prīyate bhavaḥ
praphullanānāvidhagulmaśobhitaṃ latāprātānādimanoharaṃ bahiḥ
virūḍhapuṣpaiḥ paritaḥ priyaṅgubhiḥ supuṣpitaiḥ kaṇṭakitaiś ca ketakaiḥ
aśokapunnāgaśataiḥ supuṣpitairdvirephamālākulapuṣpasaṃcayaiḥ
kvacitpraphullāmbujareṇubhūṣitairvihaṅgamaiścānukalapraṇādibhiḥ
vināditaṃ sārasacakravākaiḥ pramattadātyūhavaraiś ca sarvataḥ
kvacicca kekāruta nāditaṃ śubhaṃ kvacicca kāraṇḍavanādanāditam
kvacicca mattālikulākulīkṛtaṃ madākulābhir bhramarāṅganādibhīḥ
niṣevitaṃ cārusugāndhipuṣpakaiḥ kvacitsupaṣpaiḥ sahakāravṛkṣaiḥ
latopagūḍhaistilakaiś ca gūḍhaṃ pragītavidyādharasiddhacāraṇam
pravṛttanṛttānugatāpsarogaṇaṃ prahṛṣṭanānāvidhapakṣisevitam
pranṛttahārītakulopanāditaṃ mṛgendranādākulamattamānasaiḥ
viṭapanicayalīnaṃ nīlakaṇṭhābhirāmaṃ madamuditavihaṅgaṃ prāptanādābhīrāmam
kusumitataruśākhālīnamattadvirephaṃ navakisalayaśobhāśobhitaṃ prāṃśuśākham
kvacicca dantakṣatacāruvīrudhaṃ kvacillatāliṅgi tacāruvṛkṣakam
kvacidvilāsālasagāminībhir niṣevitaṃ kiṃpuruṣāṅganābhiḥ
pārāvatadhvanivikūjitacāruśṛṅgairabhraṅkaṣaiḥ sitamanohara cārurūpaiḥ
tuṅgāgrairnilapuṣpaistabakabharanataprāṃśuśākhairaśokairdelāprāntāntalīnaśrutisukhajanakairbhāsitāntaṃ manojñaiḥ
haṃsānāṃ pakṣavātapracalitakamalasvacchavistīrṇatoyaṃ coyānāṃ tīrajātapracakitakadalīcāṭunṛtyanmayūram
māyūraiḥ pakṣacandraiḥ kvacidavanigatai rañjitakṣmāpradeśaṃ deśedeśe vilīnapramuditavilasanmattahārītavṛndam
hṛṣṭabhiḥ kvacidapi kinnarāṅganābhir viṇābhiḥ samadhuragītanṛttakaṇṭham
saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacidupaliptakīrṇapuṣpairāvāsaiḥ parivṛtapādapaṃ munīnām
ramyaṃ priyaṅgutarumañjarisaktabhṛṅgaṃ bhṛṅgāvalīkavalitāmrakadaṃbapuṣpam
gulmāntaraprasabhabhītamṛgīsamūhaṃ vāteritaṃ tanubhṛtāmapavargadātṛ
candrāṃśujālaśablaistilakairmanojñaiḥ siṃdūrakuṅkumakusuṃbhanibhairaśokaiḥ
cāmīkaradyutisamairatha karṇikāraiḥ puṣpotkarairupacitaṃ suviśālaśākhaiḥ
kvacitkāñcanasaṃkāśaiḥ puṣpairācitabhūtalam
sakalabhuvanabhartā lokanāthastadānīṃ tuhinaśikharaputryā sārdhamiṣṭairgaṇeśaiḥ
vividhataruviśālaṃ mattahṛṣṭānnapuṣṭairupavanamatiramyaṃ darśayāmāsa devyāḥ
puṣpairvanyaiḥ śubhaśubhatamaiḥ kalpitairdivyabhūṣairdevīṃ divyāmupavanagatāṃ bhūṣayāmāsa śarvaḥ
sā cāpyenaṃ tuhināgirisutā śaṅkaraṃ devadevaṃ puṣpairdivyaiḥ śubhataratamairbhūṣayāmāsa bhaktyā
saṃpūjya pūjyaṃ tridaśesvarāṇāṃ saṃprekṣya codyāna matīva ramyam
gaṇeśvarairnādimukhaiś ca sārdhamuvāca devaṃ praṇipatya devī
śrīdevyuvāca
udyānaṃ darśitaṃ deva prabhayā parayā yutam
sūta uvāca
āghrāya vadanāṃbhojaṃ tadāha girijāṃ hasan
śrībhagavānuvāca
idaṃ guhyatamaṃ kṣetraṃ sadā vārāṇasī mama
sarveṣāmeva jantūnāṃ heturmokṣasya sarvadā
asminsiddhāḥ sadā devi madīyaṃ vratamāsthitāḥ
nānāliṅgadharā nityaṃ mama lokābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ
nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇe nānāvihagasobhite
kamalotpalapuṣpāḍhyaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṅkṛte
rocate me sadā vāso yena kāryeṇa tacchṛṇu
kāmaṃ hyatra mṛto devī janturmokṣāya kalpate
ataḥ paramidaṃ kṣetraṃ parā ceyaṃ gatirmama
vimuktaṃ na mayā yasmānmokṣyate vā kadācana
naimiṣe ca kurukṣetre gaṅgādvāre ca puṣkare
snānātsaṃsevanādvāpi na mokṣaḥ prāpyate yataḥ
prayāgādapi tīrthāgryādavimuktamidaṃ śubham
kāmaṃ bhuñjan svapan krīḍan kurvan hi vividhāḥ kriyāḥ
kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi piśācatvaṃ varaṃ nṛṇām
na tu śakrasahasratvaṃ svarge kāśīpurīṃ vinā
jaigīṣavyaḥ parāṃ siddhiṃ gato yatra mahātapāḥ
asya kṣetrasya māhātmyādbhaktyā ca mama bhāvitaḥ
jaigīṣavyaguhā śreṣṭhā yogināṃ sthānamiṣyate
dhyāyantastatra māṃ nityaṃ yogāgnirdīpyate bhṛśam
ātmanaścaiva sāyujyamīpsitaṃ sthānameva ca
kṣetrasaṃsevanādeva gaṇeśatvamavāpa ha
ihaivārādhya māṃ devi siddhiṃ yāsyatyanuttamām
parāśarasutau yogī ṛṣirvyāso mahātapāḥ
brahmā devarṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ viṣṇurvāpi divākaraḥ
anyepi yogino divyāśchannarūpā mahātmanaḥ
ye punarnirmamā dhīrāḥ sattvasthā vijitendriyāḥ
vratinaś ca nirāraṃbhāḥ sarve te mayi bhāvitāḥ
devadevaṃ samāsādya dhīmantaḥ saṃgavarjitāḥ
gatā iha paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate
janmāntarasahasreṣu yaṃ na yogī samāpnuyāt
goprekṣakamidaṃ kṣetraṃ brahmaṇā sthāpitaṃ purā
kailāsabhavanaṃ cātra paśya divyaṃ varānane
goprekṣakamayāgamya dṛṣṭvāmāmatra mānavaḥ
kapilāhrahamityevaṃ tathā vai brahmaṇā kṛtam
atrāpi svayamevāhaṃ vṛṣadhvaja iti smṛtaḥ
sānnadhyaṃ kṛtavān devi sadāhaṃ dṛśyate tavyā
gacchopaśamamīśoti upaśāntaḥ śivas tathā
atrāhaṃ brahmaṇānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā
brahmaṇā cāpi saṃgṛhya viṣṇunā sthāpitaḥ punaḥ
brahmaṇāpi tato viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvignacetasā
mayānītamidaṃ liṅgaṅkasmātsthāpitavānasi
tamuvāca punarviṣṇurbrahmaṇaṃ kupitānanam
dṛṣṭvainamapi deveśaṃ mama lokaṃ vrajennaraḥ
sthāpayāmāsa vidhivadbhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ
svarlīneśvara ityevamatrāhaṃ svayamāgataḥ
ananyā sā gatistasya yogināṃ caiva yā smṛtā
vyāghrarūpaṃ samāsthāya nihato darpito balī
na punardurgatiṃ yāti dṛṣṭvainaṃ vyāghramīśvaram
ādāvatrāhamāgamya prasthito gaṇapaiḥ saha
jyeṣṭhasthānamidaṃ tasmādetanme puṇyadarśanam
devaiḥ saṃmatādetāni liṅgāni stāpitānyataḥ
mama priyahitaṃ sthānaṃ jñātvā liṅgaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
śaileśvaramiti khyātaṃ dṛśyatāmiha cādarāt
nadyeṣā varuṇā devi puṇyā pāpapramocanī
kṣetrametadalaṅkṛtya jāhnavyā saha saṃgatā
sthāpitaṃ brahmaṇā cāpi saṃgame liṅgamuttamam
sagameśvaramityevaṃ khyātaṃ jagati dṛśyatām
saṃgame devanadyā hi yaḥ snātvā manujaḥ śuciḥ
idaṃ manye mahākṣetraṃ nivāso yogināṃ param
kṣetramadhye ca yatrāhaṃ svayaṃ bhūtvāgramāsthitaḥ
siddhānāṃ sthānametaddhi madīyavratadhāriṇām
yogināṃ mokṣalipsūnāṃ jñānayogaratātmanām
dṛṣṭvainaṃ madhyameśānaṃ janmaprati na śocati
sthāpitaṃ liṅgametattu śukreṇa bhṛgusūnunā
nāmnā śukreśvaraṃ nāma sarvasiddhāmarārcitam
mṛtaś ca na punarjantuḥ saṃsārī tu bhavennaraḥ
purā jaṃbukarūpeṇa asuro devakaṇṭakaḥ
brahmaṇo hi varaṃ labdhvā gomāyurbandhaśaṅkitaḥ
dṛṣṭvainamapi deveśaṃ sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt
grahaiḥ śukrapurogaiś ca etāni sthāpitāni ha
paśya puṇyāni liṅgāni sarvakāmapradāni tu
evametāni puṇyāni mannivāsāni pārvati
kathitāni mama kṣetre guhyaṃ cānyadidaṃ śṛṇu
yojanaṃ viddhi cārvaṅgi mṛtyukāle 'mṛtapradam
gaṇatvaṃ labhate dṛṣṭvā hyasminmokṣo hyavāpyate
gāṇapatyaṃ labhedyasmādyataḥ sā muktiruttamā
tato mahālayāttasmātkedārānmadhyamādapi
smṛtaṃ puṇyatamaṃ kṣetramavimuktaṃ varānane
kedāraṃ madhyamaṃ kṣetraṃ sthānaṃ caiva mahālayam
mama puṇyāni bhūrloke tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamaṃ tvidam
yataḥ sṛṣṭāstvime lokāstataḥ kṣetramidaṃ śubham
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ mama dṛṣṭveha mānavaḥ
sadyaḥ pāpavinirmuktaḥ paśupāśairvimucyate
śaileśaṃ saṃgameśaṃ ca svarlīnaṃ madhyameśvaram
hiraṇyagarbham īśānaṃ goprekṣaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam
upaśāntaṃ śivaṃ caiva jyeṣṭhasthānanivāsinam
śukreśvaraṃ ca vikhyātaṃ vyāghreśaṃ jaṃbukeśvaram
dṛṣṭvā na jāyate martyaḥ saṃsāre duḥkhasāgare
sūta uvāca
tataḥ pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmābhyaṅgasitaprabhāḥ
māheśvarā mahātmānas tathā vai niyatavratāḥ
punarnirīkṣya yogeśaṃ dhyānayogaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ
tasthurātmānamāsthāya līyamānā iveśvare
sthitānāṃ sa tadā teṣāṃ devadeva umāpatiḥ
sa bibhratparamāṃ mūrti babhūva puruṣaḥ prabhuḥ
tasya tāṃ paramāṃ mūrtimāsthitasya jagatprabhoḥ
na śaśāka punardraṣṭuṃ hṛṣṭaromā girindrajā
tatastvadṛṣṭamākāraṃ budhvā sā prakatisthitam
prakṛtermūrtimāsthāya yogena parameśvarī
taṃ śaśāka punardraṣṭuṃ harasyaca mahātmanaḥ
viviśurhṛdayaṃ sarve dagdhasaṃsārabījinaḥ
pañcākṣarasya vai bījaṃ saṃsmarantaḥ suśobhanam
sarvapāpaharaṃ divyaṃ purā caiva prakāśitam
taṃ dṛṣṭvā śailajā prāha hṛṣṭasarvatanūruhā
tāmuvāca suraśreṣṭhastadā devīṃ giradrijām
śrībhagavānuvāca
yairyairyogā ihābhyastā steṣāmekena janmanā
tasmā detanmahatkṣetraṃ brahmādyaiḥ sevitaṃ tathā
pratimāsaṃ tathāṣṭamyāṃ pratimāsaṃ caturdaśīm
ubhayoḥ pakṣayordevi vārāṇasyāmupāsyate
śaśibhānūparāge ca kārtikyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
pṛthivyāṃ sarvatīrthāni vārāṇasyāṃ tu jāhnavīm
uttarapravahāṃ puṇyāṃ mama mauliviniḥsṛtām
pituste girirājasya śubhāṃ himavataḥ sutām
puṇyasthānasthitāṃ puṇyāṃ puṇyadikpravahāṃ sadā
saṃnihatya kurukṣetraṃ sārdhaṃ tīrthaśatais tathā
puṣkaraṃ nimipaṃ caiva prayāgaṃ ca pṛthūdakam
drumakṣetraṃ kurukṣetraṃ naimiṣaṃ tīrthasaṃyutam
kṣetrāṇi sarvato devī devatā ṛṣayas tathā
saṃdhyā ca ṛtavaścaiva sarvā nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ca
samudrāḥ sapta caivātra devatīrthāni kṛtsnaśaḥ
avimukteśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā caiva triviṣṭapam
kālabhairavamāsādya dhūtapāpāni sarvaśaḥ
pṛthivyāṃ yāni puṇyāni mahāntyāyatanāni ca
avimuktaṃ kṣetravaraṃ mahāpāpanibarhaṇam
kedāre caiva yalliṅgaṃ yacca liṅgaṃ mahālaye
madhyamesvarasaṃjñaṃ ca tathā pāśupateśvaram
śaṅkukarṇeśvaraṃ caiva gokarṇau ca tathā hyubhau
sthāneśvaraṃ tathaikāgraṃ kāleśvaramajeśvaram
bhairaveśvaramīśānaṃ tathoṅkārakasaṃjñitam
amareśaṃ mahākālaṃ jyotiṣaṃ bhasmagātrakam
yāni cānyāni puṇyāni sthānāni mama bhūtale
aṣṭaṣaṣṭisamākhyāni ruḍhānyanyāni kṛtsnaśaḥ
tāni sarvāṇyaśeṣāṇi vārāṇasyāṃ viśanti mām
snātasya caiva gaṅgāyāṃ dṛṣṭena ca mayā śubhe
sarvayajñaphalaistulyamiṣṭaiḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
sudṛṣṭaṃ kuru deveśi avimuktaṃ gṛhaṃ mama
darśayāmāsa bhagavān śrīparvatamanuttamam
śrīparvatamanuprāpyadevyā deveśvaro haraḥ
kṣetrāṇi darśayāmāsa sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ
kuṇḍiprabhe ca paramaṃ divyaṃ vaiśravaṇeśvaram
āśāliṅgaṃ ca deveśaṃ divyaṃyacca bileśvaram
rāmeśvaraṃ ca paramaṃ viṣṇunā yatpratiṣṭhitam
dakṣiṇadvārapārśve tu kuṇḍaleśvaramīśvaram
vivṛddhaṃ giriṇā sārdhaṃ devadevanamaskṛtam
amareśvaraṃ ca varadaṃ devaiḥ pūrvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
karmeśvaraṃ ca vipulaṃ kāryārthaṃ brahmaṇā kṛtam
śrīmatsiddhavaṭañcaiva sadāvāso mamāvyaye
ajena nirmitaṃ divyaṃ sākṣādajabilaṃ śubham
tatra śṛṅgāṭakākāraṃ śṛṅgāṭācalamadhyame
śṛṅgāṭakeśvaraṃ nāma śrīdevyā tu pratiṣṭhitam
rajeśvaraṃ ca paryāye rajasā supratiṣṭhitam
gajeśvaraṃ ca vaiśākhaṃ kapoteśvaramavyayam
koṭīśvaraṃ mahātīrthaṃ rudrakoṭigaṇaiḥ purā
dvidevakulasaṃjñaṃ ca brahmaṇā dakṣiṇe śubham
uttare sthāpitaṃ caiva viṣṇunā caiva śailajam
mahāpramāṇaliṅgaṃ ca mayā pūrvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
ityuktvā tadgṛhe tiṣṭhad alaṅgṛhamiti smṛtam
tatrāpi tīrthaṃ tīrthajñe vyomaliṅgaṃ ca paśya me
gomaṇḍaleśvaraṃ caiva nandādyaiḥ supratiṣṭhitam
devaiḥ sarvaistu śakraādyaiḥ stāpitāni varānane
śrīmaddevahradaprānte sthānānīmāni pasya me
tvayā hitāya jagatāṃ hārakuṇḍamidaṃ kṛtam
alaṅkṛtaṃ mayā brahmapurastānmunibhaḥ siha
caṇḍikeśvarakaṃ devi caṇḍikeśā tavātmajā
caṇḍikānirmitaṃ sthānamaṃbikātīrthamuttamam
rucikeśvarakaṃ caiva dhāraiṣā kapilā śubhā
eteṣu devi sthāneṣu tīrtheṣu vividheṣu ca
pūjayenmāṃ sadā bhaktyā mayā sārdhaṃ hi modate
śrīśaile saṃtyajeddaṃhaṃ brāhmaṇo dagdhakilbiṣaḥ
mahāsnānaṃ ca yaḥ kuryādghṛtena vidhinaiva tu
sa yāti mama sāyujyaṃ sthāneṣveteṣu suvrate
snānaṃ palaśataṃ jñeyamabhyaṅgaṃ pañcaviṃśati
palānāṃ dve sahasre tu mahāsnānaṃ prakīrtitam
snāpya liṅgaṃ madīyaṃ tu gavyenaiva ghṛtena ca
saṃmārjya śatayajñānāṃ snānena prayutaṃ tathā
pūjayā śatasāhasramanantaṃ gītavādinām
mahāsnāne prasaktaṃ tu snānamaṣṭaguṇaṃ smṛtam
śamipuṣpaṃ ca vidhinā bilvapatraṃ ca paṅkajam
anyānyapi ca puṣpāṇi bilvapatraṃ na saṃtyajet
caturdroṇair mahādevam aṣṭadroṇairathāpi vā
daśadroṇais tu naivedyam aṣṭadroṇairathāpi vā
śatadroṇasamaṃ puṇyamāḍhakepi vidhīyate
vittahīnasya viprasya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
bherīmṛdaṅgamurajatimirāpaṭahādibhiḥ
sa bhṛtyaputradāraiś ca tathā saṃbandhibāndhavaiḥ
sārdhaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā pārthayelliṅgamuttamam
dravyahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnaṃ sureśvara
kṛtaṃ vā na kṛtaṃ vāpi kṣantumarhasi śaṅkara
japitvaivaṃ mahābījaṃ tathā pañcākṣarasya vai
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti vārāṇasyāṃ yathā mṛtaḥ
tathaiva mama sāyujyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
sūta uvāca
niśamya vacanaṃ devī gatvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ payasā ca ghṛtena ca
arcayāmāsa deveśaṃ rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam
tatrāndhakaṃ mahādaityaṃ hiraṇyākṣasutaṃ prabhuḥ
anugṛhya gaṇatvaṃ ca prāpayāmāsa līlayā
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi kṣetramāhātmyamuttamam
śrāvayedvā dvijānsarvān kṛtaśaucān jitendriyān
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vārāṇasīśailamāhātmyakathanaṃ nāmadvinavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
damitastu kathaṃ lebhe gāṇapatyaṃ maheśvarāt
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ yathāśrutam
sūta uvāca
andakānugrahaṃ caiva mandare śoṣaṇaṃ tathā
varalābhamaśeṣaṃ ca pravadāmi samāsataḥ
prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ sākṣādavadhyatvamavāpya ca
līlayā cāprayatnena trāsayāmāsa vāsavan
bādhitāstāḍitā baddhāḥ pātitāstena te surāḥ
viviśurmandaraṃ bhītā nārāyaṇapurogamāḥ
evaṃ saṃpīḍya vai devānandhakopi mahāsuraḥ
tataste samāstāḥ suredrāḥ sasādhyāḥ sureśa maheśaṃ puretyāhurevam
drutaṃ cālpavīryaprabhinnāṅgabhinnā vayaṃ daityarājasya śastrairnikṛttāḥ
jayeti vācā bhagavandamūcūḥ kirīṭabaddhāñjalayaḥ samantāt
athāśeṣāsurāṃstasya koṭikoṭisataistataḥ
bhasmīkṛtya mahādevo nirbibhedāndhakaṃ tadā
śūlena śūlinā protaṃ dagdhakalmaṣakañcukam
dṛṣṭvāndhakaṃ nanādeśaṃ praṇamya sa pitāmahaḥ
tannādaśravaṇānnedurdevā devaṃ praṇamya tam
nanṛturmunayaḥ sarve mumudurgaṇapuṅgavāḥ
sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi devāḥ śaṃbhostadopari
dagdhogninā ca śūlena protaḥ preta ivāndhakaḥ
sāttvikaṃ bhāvamāsthāya cintayāmāsa cetasā
ārādhito mayā śaṃbhuḥ purā sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ
yaḥ smarenmanasā rudraṃ prāṇānte sakṛdeva vā
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ kiṃ punarbahuśaḥ smaran
brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ
śaraṇaṃ prāpya tiṣṭhanti tameva śaraṇaṃ vrajet
evaṃ saṃcintya tuṣṭātmā soṃdhakaścāndhakārdanam
sagaṇaṃ śivamīśānamastuvatpuṇyagauravāt
hiraṇyanetratanayaṃ śūlāgrasthaṃ sureśvaraḥ
provāca dānavaṃ prekṣya ghṛṇayā nīlalohitaḥ
tuṣṭosmi vatsa bhadraṃ te kāmaṃ kiṃ karavāṇi te
śrutvā vākyaṃ tadā śaṃbhorhiraṇyanayanātmajaḥ
harṣagadgadayā vācā provācedaṃ maheśvaram
pradadau durlabhāṃ śraddhāṃ daityendrāya mahādyutiḥ
praṇemustaṃ suredrādyā gāmapatye pratiṣṭhitam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvebhāge andhakagāṇapatyātmako nāma trinavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathamasya pitā daityo hiraṇyākṣaḥ sudāruṇaḥ
viṣṇunā sūdito viṣṇurvārāhatvaṃ kathaṃ gataḥ
tasya śṛṅgaṃ maheśasya bhūṣaṇatvaṃ kathaṃ gatam
etatsarvaṃ viśeṣeṇa sūta vaktumihārhasi
sūta uvāca
hiraṇyakaśiporbhrātā hiraṇyākṣa iti smṛtaḥ
purāndhakāsureśasya pitā kālāntakopamaḥ
devāñjitvātha daityandro baddhvā ca dharaṇīmimām
nītvā rasātalaṃ cakre bandīmindīvaraprabhām
tataḥ sabrahmakā devāḥ parimlānamukhaśriyaḥ
bādhitāstāḍitā baddhva hiraṇyākṣeṇa tena vai
praṇamya śirasā viṣṇuṃ daityakoṭivimardanam
sarve vijñāpayāmāsurdharaṇībandhanaṃ hareḥ
śrutvaitadbhagavān viṣṇurdharaṇībandhanaṃ hariḥ
bhūtvā yajñavarāhosau yathā liṅgodbhave tathā
daityaiś ca sārdhaṃ daityendraṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ mahābalam
daṃṣṭrāgrakoṭyā hatvainaṃ reje daityāntakṛtprabhuḥ
kalpādiṣu yathāpūrvaṃ praviśya ca rasātalam
ānīya vasudhāṃ devīmaṅkasthāmakarodbahiḥ
tatastuṣṭāvadeveśaṃ devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ
śakraādyaiḥ sahito bhūtvā harṣagadgadaya girā
śāśvatāya varāhāya daṃṣṭriṇe daṇḍine namaḥ
nārāyaṇāya sarvāya brahmaṇe paramātmane
kartre netre suredrāṇāṃ śāstre ca sakalasya ca
tavyā kṛtaṃ sarvamidaṃ prasīda sureśa lokeśa varāha viṣṇo
tathaikadaṃṣṭrāgramukhāgrakoṭibhāgaikabhāgārdhatamena viṣṇo
hatāḥ kṣaṇātkāmadadaityamukhyāḥ svadaṃṣṭrakoṭyā saha putrabhṛtyaiḥ
tvayoddhṛtā deva dharā dhareśadharādharākāra dhṛtāgradaṃṣṭre
tvayaiva deveśa vibho kṛtaś ca jayaḥ surāṇāmasureśvaṇām
aho vasuṃdharā tava pṛṣṭhataḥ sakalatārakādayaḥ
nihitā rasātalagatā vasuṃdharā tava pṛṣṭhataḥ sakalatārakādayaḥ
jagatāṃ hitāya bhavatā vasuṃdharā bhagavān rasātasapuṭaṅgatā tadā
atha tāmuddhṛtāṃ tena dharāṃ devā munīśvarāḥ
mūrdhnyāropya namaścakruś cakriṇaḥ saṃnidhau tadā
kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakāryeṇa śatahastena viṣṇunā
lokānāṃ dhāriṇī tvaṃ hi mṛttike hara pātakam
manasā karmaṇā vācāvarade vārijekṣaṇe
tvayā hatena pāpena jīvāmastvatprasādataḥ
ityuktā sā tadā devī dharā devairadhābravīt
varāhadaṃṣṭrābhinnāyāṃ dharāyāṃ mṛttikāṃ dvijāḥ
vārāharūpamanaghaṃ cacāla ca dharā punaḥ
tasya daṃṣṭrābharākraāntā devadevasya dhīmataḥ
yadṛcchayā bhavaḥ paśyan jagāmajagadīśvaraḥ
daṃṣṭrāṃ jagrāha dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhūṣaṇārthamathātmanaḥ
devāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ seṃdrā devadevasya vaibhavam
dharā pratiṣṭhitā hyevaṃ devadevena līlayā
bhūtānāṃ saṃplave cāpi viṣṇoścaiva kalevaram
brahmaṇaś ca tathānyeṣāṃ devānāmapi līlayā
