kathaṃ vimuktirviprāṇāṃ tasmāddaṃṣṭrī maheśvaraḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge varāhaprādurbhāvo nāma caturnavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nṛsiṃhena hataḥ pūrvaṃ hiraṇyākṣāgrajaḥ śrutam
sūta uvāca
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putraḥ prahrāda iti viśrutaḥ
dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃpannastapasvī cābhavatsudhīḥ
janmaprabhṛti deveśaṃ pūjayāmāsa cāvyayam
tamādipuruṣaṃ bhaktyā parabrahmasvarūpiṇam
brahmaṇodhipatiṃ sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārakāraṇam
sopi viṣṇostathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā putraṃ samāhitam
stuvantaṃ prāha devārīḥ pradahanniva pāpadhīḥ
prahrāda vīra duṣputra dvijadevārtikāraṇam
ko viṣṇuḥ padmajo vāpi śakraś ca varuṇothavā
vāyuḥ somastatheśānaḥ pāvako mama yaḥ samaḥ
māmevārcaya bhaktyā ca svalpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ sadā
prahrāda jīvite vāñchā tavaiṣā śṛṇu cāsti cet
śrutvāpi tasya vacanaṃ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sudhīḥ
prahrādaḥ pūjayāmāsa namo nārāyaṇeti ca
namo nārāyaṇāyeti sarvadaityakumārakān
adhyāpayāmāsa ca tāṃ brahmavidyāṃ suśobhanām
durlaṅghyāṃ cātmano dṛṣṭvā śakrādibhir api svayam
putreṇa laṅghitāmājñāṃ hiraṇyaḥ prāhadānavān
kṣīravārinidhiśāyinaḥ prabhorniṣphalaṃ tvatha babhūva tejasā
tatraivāvirabhūddhantuṃ nṛsiṃhākṛtimāsthitaḥ
jaghāna ca sutaṃ prekṣya pitaraṃ dānavādhamam
bibheda tatkṣaṇādeva karajaurniśitaiḥ śataiḥ
pīḍayāmāsa daityendraṃ yugāntāgnirivāparaḥ
ābrahmabhuvanādviprā pracacāla ca suvratāḥ
dṛṣṭvā surāsuramahoragasiddhasādhyāstasmin kṣaṇe hariviriñcimukhā nṛsiṃham
dhairyaṃ balaṃ ca samavāpya yayurvisṛjya ādiṅmukhāntamasurākṣaṇatatparāś ca
tatastairgataiḥ saiṣa devonṛsiṃhaḥ sahasrākṛtiḥ sarvapātsarvabāhuḥ
sahasrekṣaṇaḥ somasūryāgninetrastadā saṃsthitaḥ sarvamāvṛtya māyī
taṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ suraśreṣṭhā lokā lokācale stitāḥ
sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sayamāḥ samarūdgaṇāḥ
jyotiṣāṃ tu parañjyotiḥ paramātmā jaganmayaḥ
sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ susūkṣmaṃ ca śabdabrahmamayaḥ śubhaḥ
yajñabhugyajñamūrtistvaṃ yajñināṃ phaladaḥ prabhuḥ
bhavānmatsyākṛtiḥ kaurmamāsthāya jagati sthitaḥ
vārāhiṃ caiva tāṃ saiṃhīmāsthāyehavyavasthitaḥ
devānāṃ devarakṣārthaṃ nihatya ditijeśvaram
dvijaśāpacchalenaivamavatīrṇosi līlayā
na dṛṣṭaṃ yattvadanyaṃ hi bhavānsarvañcarācaram
bhavānviṣṇurbhavān rudro bhavāneva pitāmahaḥ
māyayā bahudhā saṃsthamadvitīyamayaṃ prabho
stoṣyāmastvāṃ kathaṃ bhāsi devadeva mṛgādhipa
na jagāma dvijāḥ śāntiṃ mānayanyonimātmanaḥ
yo nṛsiṃhastavaṃ bhaktyā paṭhedvārthaṃ vicārayet
śravayedvā dvijānsarvān viṣṇuloke mahīyate
tadantare śivaṃ devāḥ seṃdrāḥ sabrahmakāḥ prabhum
saṃprāpya tuṣṭavuḥ sarvaṃ vijñāpya mṛgarūpiṇaḥ
tato brahmādayastūrṇaṃ saṃstūya parameśvaram
ātmatrāṇāya śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ paramakāraṇam
mandarasthaṃ mahādevaṃ krīḍamānaṃ sahomayā
sevitaṃ gaṇagandharvaiḥ siddhairapsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
praṇamya daṇḍavadbhūmau tuṣṭāva parameśvaram
namaḥ śivāya rudrāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te
ugrosi sarvabhūtānāṃ niyantāsi śivosi naḥ
namaḥ śivāya śarvāya śaṅkarāyārttihariṇe
mayaskarāya viśvāya viṣṇave brahmaṇe namaḥ
hiraṇyabāhave sākṣāddhiraṇyapataye namaḥ
śarvāya sarvarūpāya puruṣāya namonamaḥ
sadasadvyaktihīnāya mahataḥ kāraṇāya te
nityāya viśvarūpāya jāyamānāya te namaḥ
jātāya bahudhā loke prabhūtāya namonamaḥ
kālāya kālapūpāya namaḥ kālāṅgahāriṇe
mīḍhuṣṭamāya devāya śitikaṇṭhāya te namaḥ
mahīyase namastubhyaṃ hantre devāriṇāṃ sadā
tārāya ca sutārāya tāraṇāya namonamaḥ
harikeśāya devāya śaṃbhave paramātmane
devānāṃ śaṃbhave tubhyaṃ bhūtānāṃ śaṃbhave namaḥ
śaṃbhave haimavatyāś ca manyave rudrarūpiṇe
kapardine namastubhyaṃ kālakaṇṭhāya te namaḥ
hiraṇyāya maheśāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namonamaḥ
bhasmadigdhaśarīrāya daṇḍamuṇḍīśvarāya ca
namo hrasvāya dīrghāya vāmanāya namonamaḥ
bhīmāya bhīmarūpāya bhīmakarmaratāya te
sadyāya sadyarūpāya sadyojātāya te namaḥ
vāmāya vāmarūpāya vāmanetrāya te namaḥ
aghorarūpāya vikaṭāya vikaṭaśarīrāya te nāmaḥ
puruṣarūpāya puruṣaikatatpuruṣāya vai namaḥ
puruṣārthapradānāya pataye parameṣṭhine
īśānāya namastubhyamīśvarāya namonamaḥ
brahmaṇe brahmarūpāya namaḥ sākṣācchivāya te
sarvaviṣṇurnṛsiṃhasya rūpamāsthāya viśvakṛt
daityendrairbahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ hitārthaṃ jagatāṃ prabhuḥ
saiṃhīṃ samānayanyoniṃ bādhate nikhilaṃ jagat
ugrosi sarvaduṣṭānāṃ niyantāsi śivosi naḥ
kālakūṭādivapuṣā trāhi naḥ śaraṇāgatān
śukraṃ tu vṛttaṃ viśveśakrīḍā vai kevalaṃ vayam
tavonmeṣanimeṣābhyāmasmākaṃ pralayodayau
saṃtaptāsmovayaṃ deva hariṇāmitatejasā
sūta uvāca
vijñāpitas tathā devaḥ prahasanprāha tān surān
abhayaṃ ca dadau teṣāṃ haniṣyāmiti taṃ prabhuḥ
sopi śakraḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ praṇipatya yathāgatam
jagāma bhagavān brahmā tathānye ca surottamāḥ
athotthāya mahādevaḥ śārabhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ
yayau prānte nṛsiṃhasya garvitasya mṛgāśinaḥ
apahṛtya tadā prāṇānśarabhaḥ surapūjitaḥ
siṃhāttato naro bhūtvā jagāma ca yathākramam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyadvāpi saṃstavaṃ śārvamuttamam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge nārasiṃhe pañcanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ devo mahādevo viśvasaṃhārakārakaḥ
śarabhākhyaṃ mahāghoraṃ vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ
kiṅkiṃ dhairyaṃ kṛtaṃ tena brūhi sarvamaseṣataḥ
sūta uvāca
ātmano bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ mahāpralayakārakam
ājagāma purā sadyo gaṇānāmagrato hasan
nṛsiṃharūpairatyugraiḥ koṭibhiḥ parivāritaḥ
krīḍadbhiś ca mahādhīrairbrahmādyaiḥ kundukairiva
adṛṣṭapūrvairanyaiś ca veṣṭito vīravanditaḥ
āttaśastro jaṭājūṭe jvaladbālendumaṇḍitaḥ
bālendudvitayākāratīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāṅkuradvayaḥ
ākhaṇḍaladhanuḥkhaṇḍasaṃnibhabhrūlatāyutaḥ
mahāpracaṇḍahuṅkārabadhirīkṛtadiṅmukhaḥ
nīlameghāñjanākārabhīṣaṇaśmaśruradbhutaḥ
vādakhaṇḍamakhaṇḍābhyāṃ bhrāmayaṃstriśikhaṃ muhuḥ
vīrabhadropi bhagavān vīraśaktivijṛṃbhitaḥ
svayaṃ vijñāpayāmāsa kimatra smṛtikāraṇam
ājñāpaya jagatsvāmin prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ mayi
śrībhagavānuvāca
jvalitaḥ sa nṛsiṃhāgniḥ śamayainaṃ durāsadam
sāṃtvayan bodhayādau taṃ tena kiṃ nopaśāmyati
sūkṣmaṃ sūkṣmeṇa saṃhṛtya sthūlaṃ sthūlena tejasā
vaktramānaya kṛttiṃ ca vīrabhadra mamājñayā
ityādiṣṭo gaṇādhyakṣaḥ praśāntavapurāsthitaḥ
uvāca vākyamīśānaḥ pitāputramivaurasam
śrīvīrabhadra uvāca
jantucakraṃ bhagavatā rakṣitaṃ matsyarūpiṇā
bibharṣi kūrmarūpeṇa vārāheṇoddhṛtā mahī
tvam eva sarvabhūtānāṃ prabhāvaḥ prabhur avyayaḥ
yadāyadā hi lokasya duḥkhaṃ kiñcitprajāyate
tadātadāvatīrṇastvaṃ kariṣyasi nirāmayam
tvayā dharmāś ca vedāś ca śubhe mārge pratiṣṭhitāḥ
sūta uvāca
ityukto vīrabhadreṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ śāntayā girā
śrīnṛsiṃha uvāca
idānīṃ saṃhariṣyāmi jagadetaccarācaram
saṃhartturna hi saṃhāraḥ svato vā paratopi vā
ahaṃ hi sarvaśaktīnāṃ pravartakanivarttakaḥ
devatāparamārthajñā mamaiva paramaṃ viduḥ
madaṃśāḥ śaktisaṃpannā brahmaśakraādayaḥ surāḥ
mannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ purā brahmā caturmukhaḥ
rajasādhiṣṭhitaḥ sraṣṭā rudrastāmasa ucyate
viśvādhikaḥ svatantraś ca kartā hartākhileśvaraḥ
idaṃ tu matparaṃ tejaḥ kaḥ punaḥ śrotumicchati
ato māṃ śaraṇaṃ prāpya gaccha tvaṃ vigatajvaraḥ
avehi paramaṃ bhāvamidaṃ bhūtamaheśvaraḥ
kālesmyahaṃ kālavināśaheturlokān samāharttumahaṃ pravṛttaḥ
mṛtyormṛtyuṃ viddhi māṃ vīrabhadra jīvantyete matprasādena devāḥ
sūta uvāca
sāhaṅkāramidaṃ śrutvā harerāmatavikramaḥ
vihasyovāca sāvajñaṃ tato visphuritādharaḥ
śrīvīrabhadra uvāca
kiṃ na jānāsi viśveśaṃ saṃhartāraṃ pinākinam
asadvādo vivādaś ca vināśastvayi kevalaḥ
tavānyonyāvatārāṇi kāni śeṣāṇi sāṃpratam
kṛtāniyena kenāpi kathāśeṣo bhaviṣyati
doṣaṃ tvaṃ paśya etattvamavasthāmīdṛśīṃ gataḥ
tena saṃhāradakṣeṇa kṣaṇātsaṃkṣayameṣyasi
tvannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ
sṛṣṭyarthena jagatpūrvaṃ śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam
tallalāṭādabhūcchaṃbhoḥ sṛṣṭyarthaṃ tanna dūṣaṇam
aṃśohaṃ devadevasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ
evaṃ rakṣo vidāryaiva tvaṃ śaktikalayā yutaḥ
upakāro hyasādhūnāmapakārāya kevalam
adyāpi tava nikṣiptaṃ kapālaṃ kūrmarūpiṇaḥ
vismṛtaṃ kiṃ tadaṃśena daṃṣṭrotpātanapīḍitaḥ
vārāhavigrahaste 'dya sākrośaṃ tārakāriṇā
dakṣayajñe śiraśchinnaṃ mayā te yajñarūpiṇaḥ
adyāpi tava putrasya brahmaṇaḥ pañcamaṃśiraḥ
chinnaṃ tamenābhisaṃdhaṃ tadaṃśaṃ tasya tadvalam
kaṇḍūyamāne śirasi kathaṃ tadvismṛtaṃ tvayā
kutaḥ prāptaṃ kṛtaṃ kena tvayā tadapi vismṛtam
te mayā sakalā lokā gṛhītāstvaṃ payonidhau
nidrāparavaśaḥ śeṣe sa kathaṃ sāttviko bhavān
tvadādistaṃvaṣaryantaṃ rudraśaktivijṛṃbhitam
tattejasopi mahātmyaṃ yuvāṃ draṣṭuṃ na hi kṣamau
sthūlā ye hi prapaśyanti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
dyāvāpṛthivyā indrāgniyamasya varuṇasya ca
dhvāntodare śaśāṅkasya janitvā parameśvaraḥ
kālosi tvaṃ mahākālaḥ kālakālo maheśvaraḥ
sthiradhanvā kṣayo vīro vīro viśvādhikaḥ prabhuḥ
upahastā jvaraṃ bhīmo mṛgapakṣihiraṇmayaḥ
śāstāśeṣasya jagato na tvaṃ naivacaturmukhaḥ
itthaṃ sarvaṃ samālokya saṃhārātmānamātmanā
no cedidānīṃ krodhasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ
vajrāśaniriva sthāṇostvevaṃ mṛtyuḥ patiṣyati
sūta uvāca
atrāntare mahāghoraṃ vipakṣabhayakāraṇam
vīrabhadrasya tadrūpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva dṛśyate
na tāddhiraṇmayaṃ saumyaṃ na sauraṃ nāgnisaṃbhavam
tadā tejāṃsi sarvāṇi tasmin līnāni śāṅkare
rudrasādhāraṇaṃ caiva cihnita vikṛtākṛti
tataḥ saṃhārarūpeṇa suvyaktaḥ parameśvaraḥ
paśyatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ jayaśabdādimaṅgalaiḥ
sahasrabāhurjaṭilaścandrārdhakṛtaśekharaḥ
sa mṛgārdhaśarīreṇa pakṣābhyāṃ cañcunā dvijāḥ
atitīkṣṇamahādaṃṣṭro vajratulyanakhāyudhaḥ
kaṇṭhe kālo mahābāhuścatuṣpādvahnisaṃbhavaḥ
yugāntodyatajīmūtabhīmagaṃbhīraniḥsvanaḥ
samaṃ kupitavṛttāgnivyāvṛttanayanatrayaḥ
spaṣṭadaṃṣṭrodharoṣṭhaś ca huṅkāreṇa yuto haraḥ
atha vibhramya pakṣābhyāṃ nābhipādebhyudārayan
pādāvābadhya pucchena bāhubhyāṃ bāhumaṇḍalam
uḍḍīyoḍḍīya bhagavān pakṣāghātavimohitam
hariṃ harantaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ viśveśānaṃ tamīśvaram
anuyānti surāḥ sarve namovākyena tuṣṭuvuḥ
nīyamānaḥ paravaśo dīnavaktraḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
tuṣṭāva parameśānaṃ haristaṃ lalitākṣaraiḥ
śrīnṛsiṃha uvāca
namorudrāya śarvāya mahāgrāsāya viṣṇave
namo bhavāya śarvāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te
kālakālāya kālāya mahākālāya mṛtyave
vīrāya vīrabhadrāya kṣayadvīrāya śūline
mahādevāya mahate paśūnāṃ pataye namaḥ
ekāya nīlakaṇṭhāya śrīkaṇṭhāya pinākine
parāya parameśāya parātparatarāya te
parātparāya viśvāya namaste viśvamūrttaye
namo viṣṇukalatrāya viṣṇukṣetrāya bhānave
kaivartāya kirātāya mahāvyādhāya śāśvate
bhairavāya śaraṇyāya mahābairavarūpiṇe
namo nṛsiṃhasaṃhartre kāmakālapurāraye
mahāpāśaughasaṃhartre viṣṇumāyāntakāriṇe
tryaṃbakāya tryakṣarāya śipiviṣṭāya mīḍhuṣe
mṛtyuñjayāya śarvāya sarvajñāya makhāraye
makheśāya vareṇyāya namaste vahnirūpiṇe
mahāghrāṇāya jihvāya prāṇāpānapravarttine
triguṇāya triśūlāya guṇātītāya yogine
saṃsārāya pravāhāya mahāyantrapravartine
varadāyāvatārāya sarvakāraṇahetave
amoghāyāgninetrāya lakulīśāya śaṃbhave
bhiṣaktamāya muṇḍāya daṇḍine yogarūpiṇe
meghavāhāya devāya pārvatīpataye namaḥ
sthāṇave kṛttivāsāya namaḥ pañcārthahetave
yogīśvarāya nityāya satyāya parameṣṭhine
sūta uvāca
nāmnāmaṣṭaśatenaivaṃ stutvāmṛtamayena tu
punastu pārthayāmāsa nṛsiṃhaḥ śarabheśvaram
yadāyadā mamājñānamatyahaṅkāradūṣitam
evaṃ vijñāpayanprītaḥ śaṅkaraṃ narakesarī
nanvaśakto bhavān viṣṇo jīvitāntaṃ parājitaḥ
tadvaktraśeṣamātrāntaṃ kṛtvā sarvasya vigraham
śuktiśityaṃ tadā maṅgaṃ vīrabhadraḥ kṣaṇāttataḥ
devā ūcuḥ
atha brahmādayaḥ sarve varībhadratvayā dṛśā
jīvitāḥ smo vayaṃ devāḥ parjanyeneva pādapāḥ
vāto vāti ca sositvaṃ mṛtyurdhāvati pañcamaḥ
yadavyaktaṃ paraṃ vyoma kalātītaṃ sadāśivam
na viddhi paramaṃ dhāma rūpalāvaṇyavarṇane
upasargeṣu sarveṣu trāyasvāsmān gaṇādhipa
ekādasātman bhagavānvartate rūpavān haraḥ
īdṛśān te 'vatārāṇi dṛṣṭvā śiva bahūṃstamaḥ
kadācitsaṃdihennāsmāṃstvaccintāstamayā tathā
guñjagirivarataṭāmitarūpāṇi sarvaśaḥ
abhyasaṃhara gamyaṃ te na nītavyaṃ parāparā
dve tanū tava tudrasya vedajñā brāhmaṇā viduḥ
ghorāpyanyā śivāpyanyā te pratyekamanekadhā
ihāsmānpāhi bhagavannityāhatamahābalaḥ
brahmaviṣṇvīndracandrādi vayaṃ ca pramukhāḥ surāḥ
surāsurāḥ saṃprasūtāstvattaḥ sarve maheśvara
brahmā ca indro viṣṇuś ca yamādyā na surāsurān
atosmānpāhi bhagavansurādānairabhīpsitaiḥ
uvāca tān surāndevo maharṣiś ca purātanān
yathā jale jalaṃ kṣiptaṃ kṣīraṃ kṣīre ghṛtaṃ ghṛte
eka eva tadā viṣṇuḥ śivalīno na cānyathā
eṣa eva nṛsiṃhātmā sadarpaś ca mahābalaḥ
jagatsaṃhārakāreṇa pravṛtto narakesarī
etāvaduktvā bhagavānvīrabhadro mahābalaḥ
apaśyan sarvabhūtānāṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata
nṛsiṃhakṛttivasanastadāprabhṛti śaṅkaraḥ
vaktraṃ tanmuṇḍamālāyāṃ nāyakatvena kalpitam
tato devā nirātaṅkāḥ kīrtayantaḥ kathāmimām
ya idaṃ paramākhyānaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiḥ samanvitam
paṭhitvā śṛṇute caiva sarvaduḥkhavināśanam
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyam ārogyaṃ puṣṭivardhanam
apamṛtyupraśamanaṃ mahāśāntikaraṃ śubham
tato duḥsvapnaśamanaṃ sarvabhūtanivāraṇam
śeṣalokasya sopānaṃ vāñchitārthaikasādhanam
viṣṇumāyānirasanaṃ devatāparamārthadam
vāñchasiddhipradaṃ caiva ṛddhiprajñādisādhanam
idaṃ tu śarabhākāraṃ paraṃ rūpaṃ pinākinaḥ
prakāśītavyaṃ bhakteṣu cireṣudyamiteṣu ca
taireva paṭhitavyaṃ ca śrotavyaṃ ca śivātmabhiḥ
śivotsaveṣu sarveṣu caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca
paṭhetpratiṣṭhākāleṣu śivasannidhikāraṇam
coravyāghrahisiṃhāntakṛto rājabhayeṣu ca
atrānyotpātabhūkaṃpadavāgnipāṃsuvṛṣṭiṣu
ulkāpāte mahāvāte vinā vṛṣṭyātivṛṣṭiṣu
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi stavaṃ sarvamanuttamam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śarabhaprādurbhāvo nāma ṣaṇṇavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
sūta uvāca
āsīdantakasaṃkāśastapasā labdhavikramaḥ
tena devāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ
jitvaiva devasaṃghātaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vai jalandharaḥ
jagāma devadevaśaṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvaharaṃ gurum
provācedaṃ diteḥ putrān nyāyadhīrjetumīśvaram
taṃ jitvā sarvamīśānaṃ gaṇapairnadinā kṣaṇāt
vāsavatvaṃ ca yuṣmākaṃ dāsye dānavapuṅgavāḥ
jalandharavacaḥ śrutvā sarve te dānavādhamāḥ
jagarjuruccaiḥ pāpiṣṭhā mṛtyudarśanatatparāḥ
bhavopi dṛṣṭvā daityendraṃ merukūṭamiva sthitam
brahmaṇo vacanaṃ rakṣan rakṣako jagatāṃ prabhuḥ
sāṃbaḥ sanandī sagamaḥ provāca prahasanniva
kiṃ kṛtyamasureśāna yuddhenānena sāṃpratam
jalandharopi tadvākyaṃ śrutvā śrotravidāraṇam
vākyenālaṃ mahābāho devadeva vṛṣadhvaja
candrāṃśusannibhaiḥ śastrairhara yoddhumihāgataḥ
niśamyāsyavacaḥ śūlī pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā
mahāṃbhasi cakārāśu rathāṅgaṃ raudramāyudham
kṛtvārṇavāṃbhasi sitaṃ bhagavān rathāṅgaṃ smṛtvā jagattrayamanena hatāḥ surāś ca
balavān yadi coddhartuṃ tiṣṭha yoddhuṃ na cānyathā
gadāmuddhṛtya hatvā ca nandinaṃ tvāṃ ca śaṅkara
hatvā lokānsuraiḥ sārdhaṃ ḍuṇḍubhān garuḍo yathā
indrāgniyamavitteśavāyuvārīśvarādayaḥ
samastānparvatānprāpya gharṣitāś ca gaṇeśvara
girīndro mandaraḥ śrīmānnalo meruḥ suśobhanaḥ
gharṣito bāhudaṇḍena kaṇḍūnodārthamāpatat
gaṅgā niruddhā bāhubhyāṃ līlārthaṃ himavadgirau
nārīṇāṃ mama bhṛtyaiś ca vajro baddho divaukasām
vaḍavāyā mukhaṃ bhagnaṃ gṛhītvā vai kareṇa tu
tatkṣaṇādeva sakalaṃ caikārṇavamabhūdidam
airāvatādayo nāgāḥ kṣiptaḥ siṃdhujalopari
garuḍopi mayā baddho nāgapāśena viṣṇunā
urvaśyādyā mayā nītā nāryaḥ kāragṛhāntaram
kathañcillabdhavān śakraḥ śacīmekāṃ praṇamya mām
māṃ na jānāsi daityendraṃ jalandharamumāpate
sūta uvāca
nāgādvaiśasamanusaṃvṛtaś ca nāgairdeveśaṃ vacanamuvāca cālpabuddhiḥ
yattasmādbhayamihanāsti yoddhamīśa vāñchaiṣā vipulatarā na saṃśayotraḥ
ityuktvātha mahādevaṃ mahādevārinandanaḥ
durmadenāvinītātmā dorbhyāmāsphoṭya dorbalāt
durdhareṇa rathāṅgena kucchreṇāpi dvijottamāḥ
papāta daityo balavānañjanādririvāparaḥ
tasya raktena raudreṇa saṃpūrṇamabhavatkṣaṇāt
mahārauravamāsādya raktakuṇḍamabhūdaho
jalandharaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā devagandharvapārṣadāḥ
siṃhanādaṃ mahatkṛtvā sādhu deveti cābruvan
śrāvayedvā yathānyāyaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge jalandharavadho nāma saptanavititamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
sudarśanākhyaṃ vai labdhaṃ vaktumarhasi viṣṇunā
sūta uvāca
devānāmasuredrāṇāmabhavacca sudāruṇaḥ
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ vināśakaraṇo mahān
te devāḥ śaktimuśalaiḥ sāyakairnataparvabhiḥ
parājitāstadā devā devadeveśvaraṃ harim
praṇemustaṃ sureśānaṃ śokasaṃvignamānasāḥ
tān samīkṣyātha bhagavān devadeveśvaro hariḥ
vatsāḥ kimiti vai devāś cyutālaṅkāravikramāḥ
samāgatāḥ sasaṃtāpā vaktumarhatha suvratāḥ
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tathābhūtāḥ surottamāḥ
praṇamyāhuryathāvṛttaṃ devadevāya viṣṇave
bhagavandevadeveśa viṣṇo jiṣṇo janārdana
dānavaiḥ pīḍitāḥ sarve vayaṃ śaraṇamāgatāḥ
tvameva bhartā hartā ca bhoktā dātā janārdana
hantumarhasi tasmāttvaṃ dānavāndānavārdana
daityāś ca vaiṣṇavairbrāhmai raudrairyāmyaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ
kauberaiścaiva saumyaiś ca nairṛtyairvāruṇairdṛḍhaiḥ
vāyavyaiś ca tathāgnoyairaiśānairvārṣikaiḥ śubhaiḥ
saurai raudraus tathā bhīmaiḥ kaṃpanairjūṃbhaṇairdṛḍhaiḥ
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃbhūtaṃ tvadīyaṃ cakramudyutam
daṇḍaṃśārṅgaṃ tavāstraṃ ca labdhaṃ daityaiḥ prasādataḥ
purā jalandharaṃ hantuṃ nirmitaṃ tripurāriṇā
rathāṅgaṃ suśitaṃ ghoraṃ tena tān hantum arhasi
tato niśamya teṣāṃ vai vacanaṃ vārījekṣaṇaḥ
śriviṣṇuruvāca
saṃprāpya sāṃprataṃ sarvaṃ kariṣyāmi divaukasām
devā jalandharaṃ hantuṃ nirmitaṃhi purāriṇā
sarvāndhundhumukhāndaityānaṣṭaṣaṣṭiśatān surān
sabāndhavānkṣaṇādeva yuṣmān saṃtārayāmyaham
sūta uvāca
evamuktā suraśreṣṭhān suraśreṣṭhān suraśreṣṭhamanusmaran
suśreṣṭhastadā śreṣṭhaṃ pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram
liṅgaṃ sthāpya yathānyāyaṃ himavacchikhare śubhe
meruparvatasaṃkāśaṃ nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
snāpya saṃpūjya gandhādyairjvālākāraṃ manoramam
tuṣṭāva ca tadā rudraṃ saṃpūjyāgnau praṇamya ca
devaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa bhavādyena yathākramam
pūjayāmāsa ca śivaṃ praṇavādyaṃ namontakam
devaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa bhavādyena maheśvaram
pratināma sapadmena pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram
tuṣṭāva ca punaḥ śaṃbhuṃ bhavādyairbhavamīśvaram
śrīviṣṇuruvāca
bhavaḥ śivo haro rudraḥ puruṣaḥ padamlocanaḥ
arthitavyaḥ sadācāra sarvaśaṃbhurmaheśvaraḥ
īśvaraḥ sthāṇurīśānaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt
varīyān varado vandhyaḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ
gaṅgādharaḥ śūladharaḥ parārthaikaprayojanaḥ
sarvajñaḥ sarvadevādigiridhanvā jaṭādharaḥ
candrāpīḍaścandramaulirvidvānviśvāmareśvaraḥ
vedāntasārasaṃdohaḥ kapālī nīlalohitaḥ
dhyānādhāroparicchedyo gaurībhartā gaṇeśvaraḥ
aṣṭamūrtirviśvamūrtistrivargaḥ svargasādhanaḥ
jñānagamyo dṛḍhaprajño devadevastrilocanaḥ
vāmadevo mahādevaḥ pāṇḍuḥ paridṛḍho dṛḍhaḥ
viśvarūpo virūpākṣo vāgīśaḥ śucirantaraḥ
sarvapraṇayasaṃvādī vṛṣāṅko vṛṣavāhanaḥ
īśaḥ pinākī khaṭvāṅgī citraveṣaścirantanaḥ
tamoharo mahāyogī goptā brahmāṅgahṛjjaṭi
kālakālaḥ kṛttivāsāḥ subhagaḥ praṇavātmakaḥ
unmattaveṣaścaśruṣyo durvāsāḥ smaraśāsanaḥ
dṛḍhāyudhaḥ skandaguruḥ parameṣṭhī parāyaṇaḥ
kuberabandhuḥ śrīkaṇṭho lokavarṇottamottamaḥ
sāmānyadevaḥ kodaṇḍī nīlakaṇṭhaḥ paraśvadhī
viśālākṣo mṛgavyādhaḥ sureśaḥ sūryatāpanaḥ
ugraḥ paśupatistārkṣyapriyabhaktaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ
dātā dayākaro dakṣaḥ kapardī kāmaśāsanaḥ
śmaśānanilayaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śmaśānastho maheśvaraḥ
lokakartā bhūtapatirmahākartā mahauṣadhī
uttaro gopatirgoptā jñānagamyaḥ purātanaḥ
nītiḥ sunītiḥ śuddhātmā somasomarataḥ sukhī
somapomṛtapaḥ somo mahānītirmahāmatiḥ
ajataśatrurālokaḥ saṃbhāvyo havyavāhanaḥ
lokakāro vedakāraḥ sūtrakāraḥ sanātanaḥ
maharṣiḥ kapilācāryo viśvadīptistrilocanaḥ
pinākapāṇibhūrdevaḥ svastidaḥ svastikṛtsadā
tridhāmā saubhagaḥ śarvaḥ savajñaḥ sarvagocaraḥ
brahmadhṛgviśvasṛksvargaḥ karṇikāraḥ priyaḥ kaviḥ
śākho viśākho gośākhaḥ śivo naikaḥ kratuḥ samaḥ
vijitātmā vidheyātmā bhūtavāhanasārathiḥ
sagaṇo gaṇakāryaś ca sukīrti śchinnasaṃśayaḥ
kāmadevaḥ kāmapālo bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaḥ
bhasmapriyo bhasmaśāyī kāmī kāntaḥ kṛtāgamaḥ
samāyukto nivṛttātmā dharmayuktaḥ sadāśivaḥ
caturmukhaścaturbāhurdurāvāso durāsadaḥ
subhāṅgo lokasāraṅgo jagadīśo 'mṛtāśanaḥ
hiraṇyaretāstaraṇirmarīcirmahimālayaḥ
mahāhrado mahāgarbhaḥ siddhavṛndāravānditaḥ
vyāghracarmadharo vyālī mahābhūto mahānidhiḥ
amṛtāṅgo 'mṛtavapuḥ pañcayajñaḥ prabhañjanaḥ
pañcaṃ viṃśatitattvajñaḥ pārijātaḥ parāvaraḥ
varṇāśramagururvarṇī śatrujicchatrutāpanaḥ
āśramaḥ kṣapaṇaḥ kṣāmo jñānavānacalācalaḥ
pramāṇabhūto durjñeyaḥ suparṇo vāyuvāhanaḥ
dhanurdharo dhanurvedo guṇarāśirguṇākaraḥ
anantadṛṣṭirānando daṇḍo damayitā damaḥ
abhivādyo mahācāryo viśvakarmā viśāradaḥ
vītarāgo vinītātmā tapasvī bhūtabhāvanaḥ
kalyāṇaprakṛtiḥ kalpaḥ sarvalokaprajāpatiḥ
lokapālo 'ntarhitātmā kalpādiḥ kamalekṣaṇaḥ
vedaśāstrārthatattvajño niyamo niyamāśrayaḥ
candraḥ sūryaḥ śaniḥ keturvirāmo vidrumacchaviḥ
bhaktigasyaḥ paraṃbrahmamṛgabāṇārpaṇo 'naghaḥ
adrirājālayaḥ kāntaḥ paramātmā jagadguruḥ
sarvakarmācalastvaṣṭā maṅgalyo maṅgalāvṛtaḥ
mahātapā dīrghatapāḥ sthaviṣṭhaḥ sthaviro dhruvaḥ
ahaḥ saṃvatsaro vyāptiḥ pramāṇaṃ parama tapaḥ
ajaḥ sarveśvaraḥ snigdho mahoratā mahābalaḥ
amṛtaḥ śāśvataḥ śānto bāṇahastaḥ pratāpavān
kamaṇḍaludharo dhanvī vedāṅgo vedavinmuniḥ
bhrajiṣṇurbhojanaṃ bhoktā lokanetā durādharaḥ
atīndriyo mahāmāyaḥ sarvāvāsaścatuṣpathaḥ
kālayogī mahānādo mahotsāho mahābalaḥ
mahābuddhirmahāvīryo bhūtacārī purandaraḥ
niśācaraḥ pretacārimahāśaktirmahādyutiḥ
anirdeśyavapuḥ śrīmān sarvahāryamito gatiḥ
nṛtyapriyo nṛtyanṛtyaḥ prakāśātmā pratāpanaḥ
buddhaspaṣṭākṣaro mantraḥ sanmānaḥ sārasaṃplavaḥ
yugādikṛdyugāvarto gaṃbhīro vṛṣavāhanaḥ
iṣṭo viśiṣṭaḥ śiṣṭeṣṭaḥ śarabhaḥ śarabho dhanuḥ
apāṃ nidhiradhiṣṭhānaṃ vijayo jayakālavit
pratiṣṭhitaḥ pramāṇajño hiraṇyakavaco hariḥ
virocanaḥ suragaṇo vidyeśo vibudhāśrayaḥ
karaṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ kartā sarvabandhavimocanaḥ
vidvattamo vītabhayo viśvabhartā niśākaraḥ
vyavasāyo vyavasthānaḥ sthānado jagadādijaḥ
vīreśvaro vīrabhadro vīrahā vīrabhṛdvirād
vīracūḍāmaṇirvettā tīvranādo nadīdharaḥ
ājñādharastriśūlī ca śipiviṣṭaḥ śivālayaḥ
vālakhilyo mahācāpastigmāṃśur nidhir avyayaḥ
abhirāmaḥ suśaraṇaḥ subrahmaṇyaḥ sudhāpatiḥ
maghavānkauśiko gomān viśrāmaḥ sarvaśāsanaḥ
lalāṭākṣo viśvadehaḥ sarāḥ saṃsāracakrabhṛt
paramārthaḥ paramayaḥ śaṃbaro vyāghrako 'nalaḥ
yuktirunnatakīrtiś ca śāntarāgaḥ parājayaḥ
kailāsapatikāmāriḥ savitā ravilocanaḥ
nityo niyatakalyāṇaḥ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanaḥ
dūraśravā viśvasaho dhyeyo duḥsvapnunāśanaḥ
uttārako duṣkṛtihā durdharṣo duḥsaho 'bhayaḥ
anādirbhūrbhuvolakṣmīḥ kirīṭitridaśādhipaḥ
viśvagoptā viśvabhartā sudhīro rucirāṅgadaḥ
janano janajanmādiḥ prītimānnītimānnayaḥ
viśiṣṭaḥ kāśyapo bhānurbhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
praṇavaḥ saptadhācāro mahākāyo mahādhanuḥ
janmādhipo mahādevaḥ sakalāgamapāragaḥ
tattvātattvavivekātmā vibhūṣṇurbhūtibhūṣaṇaḥ
ṛṣirbrāhmaṇavijjiṣṇurjanmamṛtyujarātigaḥ
mahendro durbharaḥ senī yajñāṅgo yajñavāhanaḥ
ātmayoniranādyanto ṣaḍviṃśatsaptalokadhṛk
gāyatrīvillabhaḥ prāṃśurviśvāvāsaḥ prabhākaraḥ
śiśurgirirataḥ samrāṭsuṣeṇaḥ suraśatruhā
piṅgalaḥ kapilaśmaśruḥ śāstranetrastrayītanuḥ
jñānaskandho mahājñānī nirutpattirupaplavaḥ
bhago vivasvānādityo yogācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ
nakṣatramālī rākeśaḥ sādhiṣṭhānaḥ ṣaḍāśrayaḥ
pavitrapāṇiḥ pāpārirmaṇipūro manogatiḥ
hṛtpuṇḍarīkamāsīnaḥ śuklaḥ śānto vṛṣākapiḥ
viṣṇurgrahapatiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ samartho 'narthanāśanaḥ
adharmaśatrurakṣayyaḥ puruhūtaḥ puruṣṭutaḥ
jagaddhitaipisugataḥ kumāraḥ kuśalāgamaḥ
hiraṇyavarṇo jyotiṣmānnānābhūtadharo dhvaniḥ
bṛhajjyotiḥ sudhāmā ca mahājyotiranuttamaḥ
mātāmaho mātīraśvā nabhasvānnāgahāradhṛk
pulastyaḥ pulaho 'gastyo jātūkarṇyaḥ parāśaraḥ
nirāvaraṇadharmajño viriñco viṣṭaraśravāḥ
ātmabhūraniruddhotrijñānamūrtirmahāyaśāḥ
lokacūḍāmaṇirvīraḥ caṇḍasatyaparākramaḥ
vyālakalpo mahākalpo mahāvṛkṣaḥ kalādharaḥ
alaṅkariṣṇustvacalo rociṣṇurvikramottamaḥ
āśuśabdapatirvegī plavanaḥ śikhisārathiḥ
asaṃsṛṣṭo 'tithi śakraḥ pramāthī pāpanāśanaḥ
vasuśravāḥ kavyavāhaḥ pratapto viśvabhojanaḥ
pṛṣadaśvo nabhoyoniḥ supratīkastamistrahā
nidāghastapano meghaḥ pakṣaḥ parapurañjayaḥ
mukhānilaḥ suniṣpannaḥ surabhiḥ śiśirātmakaḥ
vasaṃto mādhavo grīṣmo nabhasyo bījavāhanaḥ
aṅgirāmunirātreyo vimalo viśvavāhanaḥ
mano buddhirahaṅkāraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetrapālakaḥ
adharo 'nuttaro jñeyo jyeṣṭho niḥśreyasālayaḥ
cārudhirjanakaścāruviśalyo lokaśalyakṛt
āmnoyotha samāmnāyastīrthadevaśivālayaḥ
bahurūpo mahārūpaḥ sarvarūpaścarācaraḥ
nyāyanirvāhako nyāyo nyāyagamyo nirañjanaḥ
sahasramūrdhā devendrāḥ sarvaśastraprabhañjanaḥ
muṇḍo virūpo vikṛto daṇḍī dānto guṇottamaḥ
piṅgalākṣotha haryakṣo nīlagrīvo nirāmayaḥ
sahasrabāhuḥ sarveśaḥ śaraṇyaḥ sarvalokabhṛt
padmāsanaḥ parañjyotiḥ parāvaraṃparaṃphalaḥ
parāvarajño bījeśaḥ sumukhaḥ sumahāsvanaḥ
devāsuramahāmātro devāsuramahāśrayaḥ
īḍyo 'nīśaḥ suravyāghro devasiṃho divākaraḥ
śivajñānarataḥ śrīmān śikhiśrīparvatapriyaḥ
jayastaṃbho viśiṣṭaṃbho narasiṃhanipātanaḥ
brahmacārī lokacārī dharmacārī dhanādhipaḥ
liṅgādhyakṣaḥ surādhyakṣo yugādhyakṣo yugāvahaḥ
svavaśaḥ savaśaḥ svargaḥ svaraḥ svaramayasvanaḥ
bījādhyakṣo bījakartā dhanakṛddharmavardhanaḥ
daṃbho 'daṃbho mahādaṃbhaḥ sarvabhūtamaheśvaraḥ
śmaśānanilayastiṣyaḥ seturapratimākṛtiḥ
lokottarasphuṭālokastryaṃbako nāgabhūṣaṇaḥ
andhakārirmakhadveṣī viṣṇukandharapātanaḥ
vītadoṣo 'kṣayaguṇo dakṣāriḥ pūṣadantahṛt
dhūrjaṭiḥ khaṇḍaparaśuḥ sakalo niṣkalo 'naghaḥ
ādhāraḥ sakalādhāraḥ pāṇḍurābho mṛḍo naṭaḥ
pūrṇaḥ pūrayitā puṇyaḥ sukumāraḥ sulocanaḥ
sāmageyaḥ priyakaraḥ puṇyakīrtiranāmayaḥ
sadgatiḥ satkṛtiḥ saktaḥ kālakaṇṭhaḥ kalādharaḥ
mānī mānyo mahākālaḥ sadbhutiḥ satparāyaṇaḥ
candrasaṃjīvanaḥ śāstā lokagūḍhomarādhipaḥ
lokabandhurlokanāthaḥ kṛtajñaḥ kṛtibhūṣaṇaḥ
anapāyyakṣaraḥ kāntaḥ sarvaśāstrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
tuṃbavīṇī mahākāyo viśokaḥ śokanāśanaḥ
trilokātmā trilokeśaḥ śuddhaḥ śuddhī rathākṣajaḥ
avyaktalakṣaṇo vyakto vyaktāvyakto viśāṃpatiḥ
brahmā vuṣṇuḥ prajāpālo haṃso haṃsagatiryamaḥ
vedhā dhātā vidhātā ca attā hartā caturmukhaḥ
kailāsaśikharāvāsī sarvāvāsī satāṃ gatiḥ
hiraṇyagarbho harimaḥ puruṣaḥ pūrvajaḥ pitā
bhūtālayo bhūtapatirbhūtido bhuvaneśvaraḥ
viṣamākṣaḥ kalādhyakṣo vṛṣāṅko vṛṣavardhanaḥ
saptajihvaḥ sahasrarciḥ srigdhaḥ prakṛtidakṣiṇaḥ
bhūtabhavyabhavannāthaḥ prabhavo bhrāntināśanaḥ
arthonartho mahākośaḥ parakāryaikapaṇḍitaḥ
niṣkaṇṭakaḥ kṛtānando nirvyājo vyājamardanaḥ
sattvavān sāttvikaḥ satyakīrtistaṃbhakṛtāgamaḥ
akaṃpito guṇagrāhī naikātmā naikakarmakṛt
suprītaḥ sumukhaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sukaro dakṣiṇo 'nalaḥ
adhṛtaḥ svadhṛtaḥ sādhyaḥ pūrvamūrtiryaśodharaḥ
varāhaśṛṅgadhṛgvāyurbalavānekanāyakaḥ
śrutiprakāśaḥ śrutimānekabandhuranekadhṛk
śrīvallabhaśivāraṃbhaḥ śāntabhadraḥ samañjasaḥ
bhūśayo bhūtikṛdbhūtirbhūṣaṇo bhūtavāhanaḥ
akāyo bhaktakāyasthaḥ kālajñānī kalāvapuḥ
satyavatamahātyāgī niṣṭhāśāntiparāyaṇaḥ
parārthavṛttirvarado viviktaḥ śrutisāgaraḥ
anirviṇṇo guṇagrāhī kalaṅkāṃlaḥ kalaṅkahā
śikhaṇḍī kavacī śūlī candī muṇḍī ca kuṇḍalī
mekhalī kavacī khaḍgī māyī saṃsārasārathiḥ
amṛtyuḥ sarvadṛk siṃhastejorāśirmahāmaṇiḥ
asaṃkhyeyoprameyātmā vīryavān kāryakovidaḥ
vedyo vedārthavidgoptā sarvācāro munīśvaraḥ
sureśaḥ śaraṇaṃ sarvaḥ śabdabrahmasatāṅgatiḥ
kālabhakṣaḥ kalaṅkāriḥ kaṅkaṇīkṛtavāsukiḥ
maheṣvāso mahībhartā niṣkalaṅko viśṛṅkhalaḥ
nivṛttaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ śilpo vyūḍhorasko mahābhujaḥ
ekajyotirnirātaṅko naro nārāyaṇapriyaḥ
nirlepo niṣprapañcātmā nirvyagro vyagranāśanaḥ
praśāntabuddhirakṣudraḥ kṣudrahānityasuṃdaraḥ
dhairyāgryadhuryo dhātrīśaḥ śākalyaḥ śarvarīpatiḥ
paramārthagururdṛṣṭirgururāśritavatsalaḥ
raso rasajñaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvasattvāvalaṃbanaḥ
sūta uvāca
evaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa tuṣṭāva vṛṣabhadhvajam
snāpayāmāsa ca vibhuḥ pūjayāmāsa paṅkajaiḥ
parīkṣārthaṃ hareḥ pūjākamaleṣu maheśvaraḥ
gopayāmāsa kamalaṃ tadaikaṃ bhuvaneśvaraḥ
pūjayāmāsa bhāvena nāmnā tena jagadgurum
tatastatra vibhurdṛṣṭvā tathābhūtaṃ haro harim
tasmādavatatārāśu maṇḍalātpāvakasya ca
koṭibhāskarasaṃkāśaṃ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitam
jvālāmālāvṛtaṃ divyaṃ tīkṣṇandaṃṣṭraṃ bhayaṅkaram
śūlaṭaṅkagadācakrakuntapāśadharaṃ haram
itthaṃbhūtaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā bhavaṃ bhasmavibhūṣitam
hṛṣṭo namaścakārāśu devadevaṃ janārdanaḥ
tadā prāha mahādevaḥ prahasanniva śaṅkaraḥ
saṃprekṣya praṇayādviṣṇuṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam
jñātaṃ mayedamadhunā devakāryaṃ janārdana
sudarśanākhyaṃ cakraṃ ca dadāmi tava śobhanam
yadrūpaṃ bhavatā dṛṣṭaṃ sarvalokabhayaṃkaram
śāntaṃ raṇājire viṣṇo devānāṃ duḥkhasādhanam
śāntasya cāstraṃ śāntasyācchāntenāstrema kiṃ phalam
śāntasya samare cāstraṃ śāntireva tapasvinam
yoddhuḥ śāntyā balacchedaḥ parasya balavṛddhidaḥ
devairaśāntairyadrūpaṃ madīyaṃ bhāvayāvyayam
kimāyudhena kāryaṃ vai yoddhuṃ devārisūdana
kṣamā yudhi na kāryaṃ vai yoddhuṃ devārisūdana
tadāprabhṛti taṃ prāhuḥ padmākṣamiti suvratam
dattvainaṃ nayanaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇave nīlalohitaḥ
pasparśa ca karābhyāṃ vai suśubhābhyāmuvāca ha
varadohaṃ varaśreṣṭha varānvaraya cepsitān
bhaktyā vaśīkṛto nūnaṃ tvayāhaṃ puruṣottama
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasya dayāvān sutarāṃ bhavaḥ
pasparśa ca dadau tasmai śraddhāṃ śītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ
prāha caivaṃ mahādevaḥ paramātmānamacyutam
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ dakṣaṃ bhaviṣyati sureśvarī
bhaginīṃ tava kalyāṇīṃ devīṃ haimavatīmumām
matsaṃbandhī ca lokānāṃ madhye pūjyo bhaviṣyasi
māṃ divyena ca bhāvena tadāprabhṛti śaṅkaram
ayācata mahādevaṃ brahmaṇaṃ munibhiḥ samam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān
ghṛtādyau snāpayedrudraṃ stālyā vai kalaśaiḥ śubhaiḥ
nāmnāṃ sahasreṇānena śraddhayā śivamīśvaram
tasmānnāmnāṃ sahasreṇa pūjayenadagho dvijāḥ
japennāmnāṃ sahasraṃ ca sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sahasranāmabhiḥ pūjanādviṣṇucakralābho nāmāṣṭanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
saṃbhavaḥ sūcito devyāstvayā sūta mahāmate
menājatvaṃ mahādevyā dakṣayajñavimardanam
viṣṇunā ca kathaṃ dattā devadevāya śaṃbhave
kalyāṇaṃ vā kathaṃ tasya vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ
saṃbhavaṃ ca mahādevyāḥ prāha teṣāṃ mahātmanām
sūta uvāca
yuṣmābhir vai kumārāya tena vyāsāya dhīmate
vacanādvo mahābhāgāḥ praṇamyomāṃ tathā bhavam
sā bhagākhyā jagaddhātrī liṅgamūrtestrivedikā
liṅgastu bhagavāndvābhyāṃ jagatsṛṣṭirdvijottamāḥ
liṅgavedisamāyogādardhanārīśvarobhavat
prāhiṇoti sma tasyaiva jñānaṃ jñānamayo haraḥ
viśvādhikosau bhagavānardhanārīśvaro vibhuḥ
hiraṇyagarbhaṃ taṃ devo jāyamānamapaśyata
sopi rudraṃ mahādevaṃ brahmāpaśyata śaṅkaram
taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃsthitaṃ devamardhanārīśvaraṃ prabhum
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhir varadaṃ vārijodbhavaḥ
vibhajasveti viśveśaṃ viśvātmānamajo vibhuḥ
sasarjadevīṃ vāmāṅgātpatnīṃ caivātmanaḥ samām
śraddhā hyasya śubhā patnī tataḥ puṃsaḥ surātanī
saivājñayā vibhordevī dakṣaputrī babhūva ha
satīsaṃjñā tadā sā vai rudramevāśritā patim
dakṣaṃ vinindya kālena devī mainā hyabhūtpunaḥ
nāradasyaiva dakṣopi śāpādevaṃ vinindyaca
anādṛtya kṛtiṃ jñātvā satī dakṣeṇa tatkṣaṇāt
bhasmīkṛtvātmano dehaṃ yogamārgeṇasā punaḥ
babhūva pārvatī devī tapasā ca gireḥ prabhoḥ
jñātvaitadbhagavān bhargo dadāha ruṣitaḥ prabhuḥ
viṣṇunā lokapālaṃś ca śaśāpa ca munīśvaraḥ
vināśovai kṣaṇādeva māyayā śaṅkarasya vai
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge devīsaṃbhavo nāma navanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vijitya viṣṇunā sārdhaṃ bhagavānparameśvaraḥ
sūta uvacā
dakṣayajñe suvipule devān viṣṇupurogamān
dadāha bhagavān rudraḥ sarvān munigaṇān api
bhadro nāma gaṇastena preṣitaḥ parameṣṭhinā
sosṛjadvīrabhadraś ca gaṇeśānromajāñchubhān
gaṇeśvaraiḥ samāruhya rathaṃ bhadraḥ pratāpavān
gaṇeśvarāś ca te sarve vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ
yajñavāṭas tathā tasya gaṅgādvārasamīpataḥ
taddeśe caiva vikhyātaṃ śubhaṃ kanakhalaṃ dvijāḥ
dagdhuṃ vai preṣitaścasau bhagavān parameṣṭhinā
tadotpāto babhūvātha lokānāṃ bhayaśaṃsanaḥ
parvatāś ca vyaśīryanta pracakaṃpe vasuṃdharā
marutaścāpyaghūrṇanta cukṣubhe makarālayaḥ
grahāś ca na prakāśyante na devā na ca dānavāḥ
tataḥ kṣaṇāt praviśyaiva yajñavāṭaṃ mahātmanaḥ
romajaiḥ sahito bhadraḥ kālāgnirivacāparaḥ
saṃparkādeva dakṣādyamunīndevān pinākinā
dagdhuṃ saṃproṣitaścāhaṃ bhavantaṃ samunīśvaraiḥ
ityuktvā yajñaśālāṃ tāṃ dadāha gaṇapuṅgavaḥ
gaṇeśvarāś ca saṃkruddhā yūpānutpāṭya cikṣipuḥ
gṛhītvā gaṇapāḥ sarvān gaṅgāsrotasi cikṣipuḥ
vyaṣṭaṃbhayadadīnātmā tathānyeṣāṃ divaukasām
bhagasya netre cotpāṭya karajāgreṇa līlayā
nihatya muṣṭinā dantān pūṣṇaścaivaṃ nyapātayat
tathā candramasaṃdevaṃ pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā
gharṣayāmāsa bhagavān vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān
vahnerhastadvayaṃ chittvā jihvāmutpāṭya līlayā
jaghāna mūrdhni pādena vīrabhadro mahābalaḥ
jaghāna devamīśānaṃ triśūlena mahābalam
trayaś ca triśataṃ teṣāṃ trisāhasraṃ ca līlayā
trayaṃ caiva suredrāṇāṃ jaghāna ca munīśvarān
anyāṃś ca devāndevosau sarvānyuddhāya saṃsthitān
jaghāna bhagavānnudraḥ khaḍgamuṣṭyādisāyakaiḥ
atha viṣṇurmahādejāścakramudyamya mūrcchitaḥ
viṣṇoryogabalāttasya divyadehāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
śaṅkhacakragadāhastā asaṃkhyātāś ca jajñire
tānsarvānapi devosaunārāyaṇasamaprabhrān
nihatya gadayā viṣṇuṃ tāḍayāmāsa mūrdhani
tataścorasi taṃ devaṃ līlayaiva raṇājire
papāta ca tadā bhūmau visaṃjñaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
krodharaktekṣamaḥ śrīmānatiṣṭhatpuruṣarṣabhaḥ
vyaṣṭaṃbhayadadīnātmā karasthaṃ na cacāla saḥ
atiṣṭhatstaṃbhitastena śṛṅgavāniva niścalaḥ
tribhiś ca dharṣitaṃ śārṅgaṃ tridhābhūtaṃ prabhostadā
śārṅgaṅkoṭiprasaṃgādvai ciccheda ca śiraḥ prabhoḥ
vāyunā preritaṃ caiva prāṇajena pinākinā
pradīpitamahāśālaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñopi dudruve
te tadā mṛgarūpeṇa dhāvantaṃ gaganaṃ prati
vīrabhadraḥ samādhāya viśiraskamathākarot
ariṣṭaneminaṃ vīro bahuputraṃ munīśvaram
munīmaṅgirasaṃ caiva kṛṣṇāśvaṃ ca mahābalaḥ
nikṛtya karajāgreṇa varibhadraḥ pratāpavān
bhadramāha mahātejāḥ prārthayanpraṇataḥ prabhuḥ
sopi bhadraḥ prabhāveṇa brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
śamaṃ jagāma śanakaiḥ śāntastasthau tadājñayā
sagaṇaḥ sarvadaḥ śarvaḥ sarvalokamaheśvaraḥ
hatānāṃ ca tadā teṣāṃ pradadau pūrvavattanum
dakṣasya ca munīndrasya tathānyeṣāṃ maheśvaraḥ
vāgīśyāścaiva nāsāgraṃ devamātustathaiva ca
naṣṭānāṃ jīvitaṃ caiva varāṇi vividhāni ca
kalpayāmāsa vai vaktraṃ līlayā ca mahān bhavaḥ
dakṣopi labdhasaṃjñaś ca samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ
tuṣṭāva devadeveśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam
stutastena mahātejāḥ pradāya vividhānvarān
gāmapatyaṃ dadau tasmai dakṣāyākliṣṭakarmaṇe
devāś ca sarve deveśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ parameśvaram
nārāyaṇaś ca bhagavān tuṣṭāva ca kṛtāñjaliḥ
tuṣṭuvurdevardeveśaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ vṛṣadhvajam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivakṛddakṣayajñavidhvaṃsano nāma śatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ himavataḥ putrī babhūvāṃbā satī śubhā
kathaṃ vā devadeveśamavāpa patimīśvaram
sūta uvāca
sā menā tanum āśritya svecchayaiva varāṅganā
tadā haimavatī jajñe tapasā ca dvijottamāḥ
jātakarmādikāḥ sarvāścakāra ca giriśvaraḥ
dvādaśe ca tadā varṣe pūrṇe haimavatī śubhā
tapastepe tayā sārdhamanujā ca śubhānanā
ṛṣayaś ca tadā sarve sarvalokamaheśvarīm
tuṣṭuvus tapasā devīṃ samāvṛtya samantataḥ
jyeṣṭhā hyaparṇā hyanujā caikaparṇā śabhānanā
tṛtīyā ca vārārohā tathā caivaikapāṭalā
tapasā ca mahādevyāḥ parvātyāḥ parameśvaraḥ
vaśīkṛto mahādevaḥ sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ
tārātmajo mahātejā babhūva ditinandanaḥ
tasya putrāstrayaścāpi tārakākṣo mahāsuraḥ
vidyunmālī ca bhagavān kamalākṣaś ca vīryavān
pitāmahas tathā caiṣāṃ tāro nāma mahābalaḥ
tapasā labdhavīryaś ca prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ
vijitya samare pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca jitavān asau
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu divārātram aviśramam
sarathaṃ viṣṇumādāya cikṣepa śatayojanam
tāreṇa vijitaḥ saṃkhye dudrāva garuḍadhvajaḥ
tāro varāñchataguṇaṃ labdhvā śataguṇaṃ balam
devendrapramukhāñjitvā devāndeveśvareśvaraḥ
vārayāmāsa tairdevansarvalokeṣu māyayā
devatāś ca sahendreṇa tārakādbhayapīḍitāḥ
na śāntiṃ lebhire śūrāḥ śaraṇaṃ vā bhayārditāḥ
tadāmarapatiḥ śrīmān saṃnipatyamaraprabhuḥ
uvācāṅgirasaṃ devo devānāmapi saṃnidhau
bhagavaṃstārako nāma tārajo dānavottamaḥ
asamākaṃ yāny amoghāni āyudhāny aṅgirovara
tāni moghāni jāyante prabhāvādamaradviṣaḥ
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi dviguṇāni bṛhaspate
viṣṇunā yodhito yuddhe tenāpi na ca sūditaḥ
yastenānirjito yuddhe viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
evam uktas tu śakreṇa jīvaḥ sārdhaṃ surādhipaiḥ
sahasrākṣeṇa ca vibhuṃ saṃprāpyāha kuśadhvajam
sopi tasya mukhācchrutvā praṇayātpraṇatārtihā
devairaśeṣaiḥ seṃdraistu jīvamāha pitāmahaḥ
jāne vortiṃ suredrāṇāṃ tathāpi śṛṇu sāṃpratam
vinindyadakṣa yā devī satī rudrāṅgasaṃbhavā
tasyāścaiveha rūpeṇa yūyaṃ devāḥ surottamāḥ
tayoryogena saṃbhūtaḥ skandaḥ śaktidharaḥ prabhuḥ
ṣaḍāsyo dvādaśabhujaḥ senānīḥ pāvakiḥ prabhuḥ
svāheyaḥ kārtikeyaś ca gāṅgeyaḥ śaradhāmajaḥ
devaḥ śākho viśākhaś ca naigameśaś ca vīryavān
senāpatiḥ kumārākhyaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ
līlayaiva mahāsenaḥ prabalaṃ tārakāsuram
evam uktas tadā tena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā
mero śikharamāsādya smaraṃ sasmāra suvrataḥ
ratyā samaṃ samāgamya namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ
saśakramāha taṃ jīvaṃ jagajjīvo dvijottamāḥ
smṛto yadbhavatā jīva saṃprāptohaṃ tavāntikam
śaṅkareṇāṃbikāmadya saṃyojaya yathāsukham
tena mārgeṇa mārgasva patnyā ratyānayā saha
sopi tuṣṭo mahādevaḥ pradāsyati śubhāṃ gatim
viprayuktastayā pūrvaṃ labdvā tāṃ girijāmumām
devadevāśramaṃ gantuṃ matiṃ cakre tayā saha
gatvā tadaśraye śaṃbhoḥ saha ratyā mahābalaḥ
nayanena tṛtīyena sāvajñaṃ tamevaikṣata
adahattatkṣaṇādeva lalāpa karuṇaṃ ratiḥ
ratyāḥ pralāpamākarṇya devadevo vṛpadhvajaḥ
kṛpayā parayā prāha kāmapatnīṃ nirībhya ca
yadā viṣṇuś ca bhavitā vāsudevo mahāyaśāḥ
śāpādbhṛgormahātejāḥ sarvalokahitāyavai
sā praṇamya tadā rudraṃ kāmapatnī śucismitā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge madanadāho nāmaikādhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
hitāya cāśramāṇāṃ ca krīḍārthaṃ bhagavānbhavaḥ
jagāma sa svayaṃ brahmā marīcyādyairmaharṣibhiḥ
tapovanaṃ mahādevyāḥ pārvatyāḥ padamsaṃbhavaḥ
pradakṣiṇīkṛtya ca tāṃ devīṃ sa jagatoraṇīm
kīmarthaṃ tapasā lokānsaṃtāpayasi śailaje
tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ jagatsarvaṃ mātastvaṃ mā vimāśaya
tvaṃ hi saṃdhāraye lokānimānsarvānsvatejasā
sa evaṃ parameśānaḥ svayaṃ ca varayiṣyati
varade yena sṛṣṭāsi na vinā yastvayāṃbike
ityuktvā tāṃ namaskṛtya muhuḥ saṃprekṣya pārvatīm
jagāmānugrahaṃ karttuṃ dvijarūpeṇa cāśramam
sā ca dṛṣṭvā māhadevaṃ dvijarūpeṇa saṃsthitam
pratibhādyaiḥ prabhuṃ jñātvā nanāma vṛṣabhadhvajam
saṃpūjya varadaṃ devaṃ brāhmaṇacchadmanāgatam
tuṣṭāva parameśānaṃ pārvatī parameśvaram
kuladharmāśrayaṃ rakṣan bhūdharasya mahātmanaḥ
krīḍārthaṃ ca saṃtāṃ madhye sarvadevapatirbhavaḥ
āsthāya rūpaṃ yatsaumyaṃ sameṣyehaṃ saha tvayā
ityuktvā tāṃ samālokya devo divyena cakṣuṣā
jagāmeṣṭaṃ tadā divyaṃ svapuraṃ prayayauca sā
dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭastadā devīṃ menayā tuhinācalaḥ
āliṅgyāghrāya saṃpūjya putrīṃ sākṣāttapasvinīm
svayaṃvaraṃ tadā devyāḥ sarvalokeṣvaghoṣayat
atha brahmā ca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sākṣājjanārdanaḥ
tvaṣṭāryamā vivasvāṃś ca yamo varuṇa eva ca
vāyuḥ somastatheśāno rudrāś ca munayas tathā
aśvinau dvādaśādityā gandharvā garuḍas tathā
yakṣāḥ siddhāstatā sādhyā daityāḥ kiṃpuruṣoragāḥ
samudrāś ca nadā vedā mantrāḥ stotrādayaḥ kṣaṇāḥ
nāgāś ca parvatāḥ sarve yajñāḥ sūryādayo grahāḥ
trayastriṃśacca devānāṃ trayaś ca triśataṃ tathā
apsarobhiḥ pranṛttābhiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ
vandibhiḥ stūyamānā ca sthitā śailasutā tadā
sitātapatraṃ ratnāṃśumiśritaṃ cāvahattathā
mālinī giriputryāstu saṃdhyāpūrṇendumaṇḍalam
cāmarāsaktahastābhir divyastrībhiś ca saṃvṛtā
vijayā vyajanaṃ gṛhya sthitā devyāḥ samīpagā
mālāṃ prahṛhya devyāṃ tu sthitāyāṃ devasaṃsadi
śiśurbhūtvā mahādevaḥ krīḍārthaṃ pṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
atha dṛṣṭvā śiśuṃ devāstasyā utsaṃgavarttinam
staṃbhitaḥ śiśurūpeṇa devadevena līlayā
vajraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka bāhuṃ cālayituṃ tathā
vahniṃ śaktiṃ tathā kṣeptaṃ na śaśāka tathā sthitaḥ
yamopi daṇḍaṃ khaḍgaṃ ca nirṛtirmunipuṅgavāḥ
varuṇo nāgapāśaṃ ca dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samīraṇaḥ
somo gadāṃ dhaneśaś ca daṇḍaṃ daṇḍabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
īśānaś ca tathā śūlaṃ tīvramudyamya saṃsthitaḥ
rudrāś ca śūlamādityā muśalaṃ vasavas tathā
śiraḥprakaṃpayanviṣṇuścakramudyamya saṃsthitaḥ
tasyāpi śiraso bālaḥ sthiratvaṃ pracakāra ha
cakraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka bāhūṃścālayituṃ na ca
pūṣā dantāndaśandantairbālamaikṣata mohitaḥ
tasyāpi daśanāḥ peturdṛṣṭamātrasya śaṃbhunā
brahmā paramasaṃvigno dhyānamāsthāya śaṅkaram
sa buddhvā devamīśānaṃ śīghrāmutthāya vismitaḥ
sa buddhva devamīśānaṃ śīghramutthāya vismitaḥ
buddhistvaṃ sarvalokānā mahaṅkārastvamīśvaraḥ
bhūtānāmindriyāṇāṃ ca tvameveśa pravarttakaḥ
tavāhaṃ dakṣiṇāddhastātsṛṣṭaḥ pūrvaṃ purātanaḥ
vāmahastānmahā bāho devo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
iyaṃ ca prakṛtirdevī sadā te sṛṣṭikāraṇa
patnīrūpaṃ samāsthāya jagatkāraṇamāgatā
prasādāttava deveśa niyogācca mayā prajāḥ
devādyāstu imāḥ sṛṣṭā mūḍhāstvadyogamohitāḥ
kuru prasādameteṣāṃ yathāpūrvaṃ bhavantvime
sūta uvāca
vijñāpyaivaṃ tadā brahmā devadevaṃ maheśvaram
saṃstantitāṃstadā tena bhagavānāhapadmajaḥ
mūḍhāstha devatāḥ sarvā naiva budhyata śaṅkaram
gacchadhvaṃ śaraṇaṃ śīghraṃ devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ
sanārāyaṇakāḥ sarve munibhiḥ śaṅkaraṃ prabhum
sārdhaṃ mayaiva deveśaṃ paramātmānamīśvaram
praṇemur manasā sarve sanārāyaṇakāḥ prabhum
yathāpūrvaṃ cakārāśu vacanādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
tejasā tasya devāste seṃdracandradivākarāḥ
sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sanārāyaṇakās tathā
sayamāś ca sarudāś ca cakṣura prāthayanvibhum
tebhyaś ca paramaṃ cakṣuḥ sarvadṛṣṭau ca śaktimat
dadāvaṃbāpatiḥ śarvo bhavānyāś ca calasya ca
labdhvā cakṣustadā devā indraviṣṇupurogamāḥ
brahmādyā nemire tūrṇaṃ bhavānī ca giriśvaraḥ
munayaś ca mahādevaṃ gaṇeśāḥ śivasaṃmatāḥ
sasarjuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
jagurgandharvamukhyāś ca nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ
mumuhurgaṇapāḥ sarvaṃ mumodāṃbā ca pārvatī
tasya devī tadā hṛṣṭā samakṣaṃ tridivaukasām
pādayoḥ stāpayāmāsa mālāṃ divyāṃ sugandhinīm
saha devyā namaścakruḥ śirobhir bhūtalāśritaiḥ
sarve sabrahmakā devāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge umāsvayaṃvaro nāma dvyadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
atha brahmā mahādevamabhivandya kṛtāñjaliḥ
udvāhaḥ kriyatāṃ deva ityuvāca maheśvaram
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
yatheṣṭamiti lokeśaṃ prāha bhūtapatiḥ prabhuḥ
udvāhārthaṃ maheśasya tatkṣaṇādeva suvratāḥ
brahmaṇā kalpitaṃ divyaṃ puraṃ ratnamayaṃ śubham
athāditirditiḥ sākṣāddanuḥ kadruḥ sukālikā
siddhirmāyā kriyā durgā devī sākṣātsudhā svadhā
sāvitrī vedamātā ca rajanī dakṣiṇā dyutiḥ
svāhā svāhā matirvuddhirṛddhirvṛddhiḥ sarasvatī
rākā kuhūḥ sinīvālī devī anumati tathā
dharaṇī dhāraṇī celā śacī nārāyaṇī tathā
etāścānyāś ca devānāṃ mātaraḥ patnayas tathā
udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyeti jagmuḥ sarvā mudānvitāḥ
uragā garuḍā yakṣā gandharvāḥ kinnarā gaṇāḥ
sāgarā girayo meghā māsāḥ saṃvatsarā tathā
vedā mantrās tathā yajñāḥ stomā dharmāś ca sarvaśaḥ
huṅkāraḥ praṇavaścaiva pratihārāḥ sahasraśaḥ
koṭirapsaraso divyāstāsāṃ ca paricārikāḥ
yāś ca sarveṣu dvīpeṣu devalokeṣu nimnagāḥ
tāś ca strīvigrahāḥ sarvāḥ saṃjagmurhṛṣṭamānasāḥ
gaṇapāś ca mahā bhāgāḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtāḥ
udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyeti tatrājagmurmudānvitāḥ
abhyayuḥ śaṅkhavarṇāś ca gaṇakoṭyo gaṇeśvarāḥ
daśabhiḥ kekarākṣaś ca vidyutoṣṭābhir eva ca
catuḥṣaṣṭyā viśākhāś ca navabhiḥ pārayātrikaḥ
ṣaḍbhiḥ sarvātakaḥ śrīmān tathaiva vikṛtānanaḥ
jvālākeśo dvādaśabhiḥ koṭibhir gaṇapuṅgavaḥ
saptabhiḥ samadaḥ śrīmāndundubhoṣṭābhir eva ca
pañcabhiś ca kapālīśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ saṃdārakaḥ śubhaḥ
koṭikoṭibhir eveha gaṇḍakaḥ kuṃbhakas tathā
viṣṭaṃbhoṣṭābhir eveha gaṇapaḥ sarvasattamaḥ
pipalaś ca sahasreṇa saṃnādaś ca tathā dvijāḥ
āveṣṭanastathāṣṭābhiḥ saptabhiścandratāpanaḥ
mahākeśaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnāṃ gaṇapo vṛtaḥ
kuṇḍī dvādaśabhir vīras tathā parvatakaḥ śubhaḥ
kālaś ca kālakaścaiva mahākālaḥ śatena vai
āgnikaḥ śatakoṭyā vai koṭyāgnimukha eva ca
āditya mūrdhā koṭyā ca tathā caiva dhanāvahaḥ
sannāmaś ca śatenaiva kumudaḥ koṭibhis tathā
amoghaḥ kokilaścaiva koṭikoṭyā sumantrakaḥ
kākapāṭo 'paraḥ ṣaṣṭyā ṣaṣṭyā saṃtānakaḥ prabhuḥ
mahābalaś ca navabhir madhupiṅgaś ca piṅgalaḥ
koṭīnāṃ caiva saptatyā caturvaktro mahābalaḥ
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇāṃ śatairviśātibhir vṛtāḥ
vīrabhadraścatuḥṣaṣṭyā romajāścaiva koṭibhiḥ
karaṇaścaiva viṃśatyā navatyā kevalaḥ śubhaḥ
kāṣṭhakūṭaścatuḥ ṣaṣṭyā sukeśo vṛṣabhas tathā
virupākṣaś ca bhagavān catuḥṣaṣṭyā sanātanaḥ
tāluketuḥ ṣaḍāsyaś ca pañcāsyaś ca sanātanaḥ
saṃvarttakas tathā caitro lakulīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ
lokāntakaś ca diptāsyo tathā daityāntakaḥ prabhuḥ
mṛtyuhṛtkālahā kālo mṛtyuñjayakaras tathā
viṣādo viṣadaścaiva vidyutaḥ kāntakaḥ prabhuḥ
devo bhṛṅgī riṭiḥ śrīmān devadevapriyas tathā
aśanīrbhāsakaścaiva catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahasrapāt
ete cānye ca gaṇapā asaṃkhyātā mahābalāḥ
sarve sahasrahastāś ca jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇaḥ
candrarekhāvataṃsāś ca nīlakaṇṭhāstrilocanāḥ
hārakuṇḍalakeyūramukuṭādyairalaṅkṛtāḥ
brahmendraviṣṇusaṃkāśā aṇimādiguṇairvṛtāḥ
sūryakoṭipratīkāśāstatrājagmurgaṇeśvarāḥ
pātālacāriṇaścaiva sarvalokanivāsinaḥ
tuṃbarurnārado hāhā hūhūścaiva tu sāmagāḥ
ratnānyādāya vādyāṃś ca tatrājagmustadā puram
ṛṣayaḥ kṛtsnaśastatra devagītāstapodhanāḥ
puṇyān vaivāhikān mantrān japur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ
girijāṃ tāmalaṅkṛtya svayameva śucismitām
puraṃ praveśayāmāsa svayamādāyakeśavaḥ
sadasyāha ca deveśaṃ nārāyaṇamajo harim
vāmāṅgādasya rudrasya dakṣiṇāṅgādahaṃ prabho
manmūrtistuhinādrīśo yajñārthaṃ sṛṣṭa eva hi
eṣā haimavatī jajñe māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ
śrautasmārtapravṛttyarthamudvāhārtha mihāgataḥ
atosau jagatāṃ dhātrī dhātā tava mamāpi ca
kṣmābagnikhendusūryātmapavanātmā yato bhavaḥ
eṣā hy ajā śuklakṛṣṇā lohitā prakṛtirbhavān
śreyopi śailarājena saṃbandho 'yaṃ tavāpi ca
madaṃśasyāsya śailasya mamāpi ca gururbhavān
sūta uvāca
devāś ca munayaḥ sarve devadevaś ca śaṅkaraḥ
tataścotthāya vidvānsaḥ padmanābhaḥ praṇamya tām
pādau prakṣālya devasya karābhyāṃ kamalekṣaṇaḥ
tvadīyaiṣā vivāhārthaṃ menajā hyanujā mama
ityuktvā sodakaṃ datvā devīṃ deveśvarāya tām
atha sarve muniśreṣṭhāḥ sarvavedārthapāragāḥ
ūcurdātā gṛhītā ca phalaṃ dravyaṃ vicārataḥ
eṣa devo haro nūnaṃ māyayā hi tato jagat
ityuktvā taṃ praṇemuś ca prītikaṇṭākitatvacaḥ
sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
devadundubhayo nedurnanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ
brahmaṇā munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ devadevamumāpatim
devopi devīmālokya salajjāṃ himaśailajām
na tṛpyatyanavadyāṅgī sā ca devaṃ vṛṣadhvajam
varadosmīti taṃ prāha hariṃ sopyāha śaṅkaram
dadāsi mama yadyājñāṃ karttavyo hyakṛto vidhiḥ
yadyadiṣṭaṃ suraśreṣṭha tatkuruṣva yathepsitam
tataḥ praṇamya hṛṣṭāmā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
ānītānviṣṇunā viprāsaṃpūjya vividhairvaraiḥ
triś ca taṃ jvalanaṃ devaṃ kārayitvā pradakṣiṇam
suraiś ca mānavaiḥ sarvaiḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
tataḥ pādyaṃ tayordatvā śaṃbhorācamanaṃ tathā
madhuparkaṃ tathā gāṃ ca praṇamya ca punaḥ śivam
bhṛgvādya munayaḥ sarve cākṣataistilataṇḍulaiḥ
sūryādayaḥ samabhyarcya tuṣṭuvurvṛṣabhadhvajam
śivaḥ samāpya devoktaṃ vahnimāropya cātmani
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi bhavodvāhaṃ śucismitaḥ
śrāvayedvā dvijāñchuddhānvedavedāṅgapāragān
yatrāyaṃ kīrtyate vipraistāvadāste tadā bhavaḥ
tasmātsaṃpūjya vidhivatkīrtayennāyathā dvijāḥ
udvāhe ca dvijendrāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ
kṛtodvāhastadā devyā haimavatyā vṛṣadhvajaḥ
sagaṇo nandinā sārdhaṃ sarvadevagaṇairvṛtaḥ
purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ divyāmājagāma mahādyutiḥ
avimukte sukhāsīnaṃ praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam
apṛcchatkṣetramāhātmyaṃ bhavānī harṣitānanā
vaktuṃ mayā sureśāni ṛṣisaṃghabhipūjitam
pāpināṃ yatra muktiḥ syānmṛtānāmekajanmanā
anyatra tu kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ vyapohati
vārāṇasyāṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paiśācyanarakāvaham
kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi piśācatvaṃ varaṃ nṛṇām
na tu śakrasahasratvaṃ svarge kāśīpurīṃ vinā
oṅkāreśaḥ kṛttivāsā mṛtānāṃ na punarbhavaḥ
uktvā kṣetrasya māhātmyaṃ saṃkṣepācchaśiśekharaḥ
darśayāmāsa codyānaṃ parityajya gaṇeśvarān
yathāśrutaṃ mayā sarvaṃ prasādādvaḥ suśobhanam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pārvatīvivāhavarṇanaṃ nāma tryadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ vināyako jāto gajavaktro gaṇeśvaraḥ
sūta uvāca
dharmavighnaṃ tadā karttuṃ daityānāmabhavandvijāḥ
asurā yātudhānāś ca rākṣasāḥ krūrakarmiṇaḥ
tāmāsāś ca tathā cānye rājasāś ca tathā bhuvi
brahmāṇaṃ ca hariṃ viprā labdhepsitavarā yataḥ
tato 'smākaṃ suraśreṣṭhāḥ sadā vijayasaṃbhavaḥ
putrārthaṃ caiva nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ karmasiddhaye
vighneśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ sraṣṭuṃ gaṇapaṃ stotumarhatha
ityuktvānyonyamanaghaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ śivamīśvaram
namaḥ sarvātmane tubhyaṃ sarvajñāya pinākine
anaghāyaviriñcāya devyāḥ kāryārthadāyine
akāyāyārthakāyāya hareḥ kāyāpahāriṇe
kāyāntasthāmṛtādhāramaṇḍalāvasthitāya te
kṛtādibhedakālāya kālavegāya te namaḥ
kālāgnirudrarupāya dharmādyaṣṭapadāya ca
kālīviśuddhadehāya kālikākāraṇāya te
kālakaṇṭhāya mukhyāya vāhanāya varāya te
hiraṇyaretase caiva namaḥ śarvāya śūline
kapāladaṇḍapāśāsicarmāṅkuśadharāyaca
pītaśuklāya rakṣārthaṃ surāṇāṃ kṛṣṇavartmane
pañcamāya mahāpañcayajñināṃ phaladāya ca
pañcāsyaphaṇihārāya pañcākṣaramayāya te
pañcākṣaradṛśe tubhyaṃ parātparātarāya te
ṣoḍaśasvaravajrāṅgavaktrāyākṣayarūpiṇe
kādipañcakahastāya cādihastāya te namaḥ
ṭādipādāya rudrāya tādipādāya te namaḥ
pādimeṇḍhrāya yadyaṅgadhātusaptakadhāriṇe
śāntatmarūpiṇe sākṣātkṣadantakrodhine namaḥ
lavarephahalāṅgāya niraṅgāya ca te namaḥ
sarvaṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ hṛdi niḥsvanakāriṇe
bhruverante sadā sadbhir dṛṣṭāyātyantabhānave
bhānusomāgninetrāya paramātmasvarūpiṇe
guṇatrayoparisthāya tīrthapādāya te namaḥ
tīrthatattvāya sārāya tasmādapi parāya te
ṛgjayuḥsāmavedāya oṃkārāya namo namaḥ
oṅkāre trividhaṃ rūpamāsthāyoparivāsine
pītāya kṛṣṇavarṇāya raktāyātyantatejase
sthānapañcakasaṃsthāya pañcadhāṇḍabahiḥ kramāt
brahmaṇe viṣṇave tubhyaṃ kumārāya namonamaḥ
aṃbāyāḥ parameśāya sarvoparicāraya te
mūlasūkṣmasvarūpāya sthūlasūkṣmāya te namaḥ
sarvasaṃkalpaśūnyāya sarvasmādrakṣitāya te
ādimadhyāntaśūnyāya citsaṃsthāya namonamaḥ
yamāgnivāyurudrāṃbusomaśakraniśācaraiḥ
diṅmukhodiṅmukhe nityaṃ sagaṇaiḥ pūjitāya te
sarvaṣu sarvadā sarvamārge saṃpūjitāya te
maheśvarāya dhīrāya namaḥ sākṣācchivāya te
makhamadanayamāgnidakṣayajñakṣapaṇavicitravicoṣṭitaṃ kṣamasva
sūta uvāca
yaḥ paṭhettu stavaṃ bhakyā śakraāgnipramukhaiḥ suraiḥ
kīrtitaṃ śrāvayedvidvān sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge devastutirnāma caturadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
yadā sthitāḥ sureśvarāḥ praṇamya caivamīśvaram
tadāṃ bikāpatirbhavaḥ pinākadhṛṅ maheśvaraḥ
dadau nirīkṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇādbhavaḥ sa tānsurottamān
praṇemurādarāddharaṃ surā mudārdralocanāḥ
bhavaḥ sudhāmṛtopamairnirīkṣaṇairnirīkṣaṇāt
tadāha bhadramastu vaḥ sureśvarān maheśvaraḥ
varārthamīśa vīkṣyate surā gṛhaṃ gatāstvime
praṇamya cāha vākpatiḥ patiṃ nirīkṣya nirbhayaḥ
surāpakārakāriṇāmihaiṣa eva no varaḥ
tatastadā niśamya vai pinākadhṛk sureśvaraḥ
gaṇeśvaraṃ sureśvaraṃ vapurdadhāra saḥ śivaḥ
gaṇeśvarāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ surevarā maheśvaram
samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ bhavārttihāriṇaṃ śubham
ibhānanāśritaṃvaraṃ triśulapāśadhāriṇam
samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ gajānanaṃ tadāṃbikā
daduḥ puṣpavarṣaṃ hi siddhā munīndrās tathā khecarā devasaṃghāstadānīm
tadā tuṣṭuvuścaikadantaṃ sureśāḥ praṇemurgaṇeśaṃ maheśaṃ vitandrāḥ
vicitravastrabhūṣaṇairalaṅkṛto gajānano
jātamātraṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā cakāra bhagavānbhavaḥ
gajānanāya kṛtyāṃstu sarvānsarveśvaraḥ svayam
ādāya ca karābhyāṃ ca susukhābhyāṃ bhavaḥ svayam
āliṅgyāghrāya mūrdhānaṃ mahādevo jagadguruḥ
tavāvatāro daityānāṃ vināśāya mamātmaja
devānāmupakārārthaṃ dvijānāṃ brahmavādinām
yajñaś ca dakṣiṇāhīnaḥ kṛto yena mahītale
adhyāpanaṃ cādhyayanaṃ vyākhyānaṃ karma eva ca
yo 'nyāyataḥ karotyasmin tasya prāṇānsadā hara
varṇāccyutānāṃ nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ narapuṅgava
svadharmarahitānāṃ ca prāṇānapahara prabho
yāḥ striyastvāṃ sadā kālaṃ puruṣāś ca vināyaka
yajanti tāsāṃ teṣāṃ ca tvatsāmyaṃ dātumarhasi
yauvanasthāṃś ca vṛddhāṃś ca ihāmutra ca pūjitaḥ
saṃpūjyo vandanīyaś ca bhaviṣyasi na saśaṃyaḥ
māṃ ca nārāyaṇaṃ vāpi brahmaṇamapi putraka
tvām anabhyarcya kalyāṇaṃ śrautaṃ smārtaṃ ca laukikam
kurute tasya kalyāṇam akalyāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaiḥ śūdraiścaiva gajānana
saṃpūjya sarvasiddhyarthaṃ bhakṣyabhojyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ
te cārcanīyāḥ śakraādyairbhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
ajaṃ hariṃ ca māṃ vāpi śakramanyānsurānapi
sasarja ca tadā vighnagaṇaṃ gaṇapatiḥ prabhuḥ
gaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ namaskṛtvāpyatiṣṭhattasya cāgrataḥ
daityānāṃ dharmavighnaṃ ca cakārāsau gaṇeśvaraḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā sukhībhavet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vināyakotpattirnāma pañcādhi kaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nṛtyāraṃbhaḥ kathaṃ śaṃbhoḥ kimarthaṃ vā yathātatham
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ śrutaḥ skandāgrajodbhavaḥ
sūta uvāca
sūdayāmāsa kālāgniriva devāndvijottamān
dārukeṇa tadā devāstāḍitāḥ pīḍitā bhṛśam
brahmāṇaṃ ca tatheśānaṃ kumāraṃ viṣṇumeva ca
bādhitāstena te sarve brahmāṇaṃ prāpya vai dvijāḥ
saṃprāpya tuṣṭuvuḥ sarve pitāmahapurogamāḥ
brahmā prāpya ca deveśaṃ praṇamya bahudhānataḥ
dāruṇo bhagavāndāruḥ pūrvaṃ tena vinirjitāḥ
vijñaptiṃ brahmaṇaḥ śrutvā bhagavān bhaganetrahā
bhavatīṃ prārthayāmyadya hitāya jagatāṃ śubhe
ekenāṃśena deveśaṃ praviṣṭā devasattamam
na viveda tadā brahmā devāścendrapurogamāḥ
girijāṃ pūrvavacchaṃbhordṛṣṭvā pārśvasthitāṃ śubhām
māyayā mohitastasyāḥ sarvajñopi caturmukhaḥ
sā praviṣṭātanuṃ tasya devadevasya pārvatī
kaṇṭhasthena viṣeṇāsya tanuṃ cakre tadātmanaḥ
tāṃ ca jñātvā tathābhūtāṃ tṛtīyenekṣaṇena vai
sasarja kālīṃ kāmāriḥ kālakaṇṭhīṃ kapardinīm
jātā yadā kālikālakaṇṭhī jātā tadānīṃ vipulā jayaśrīḥ
devetarāṇāmajayastvasiddhyā tuṣṭirbhavānyāḥ parameśvarasya
jātāṃ tadānīṃ surasiddhasaṃghā dṛṣṭvā bhayāddudruvurāgnikalpām
kālīṃ garālaṅkṛtakālakaṇṭhīmupedandrapadmodbhavaśakramukhyāḥ
tathaiva jātaṃ nayanaṃ lalāṭe sitāṃśulekhā ca sirasyudagrā
kaṇṭhe karālaṃ niśitaṃ triśūlaṃ kare karālaṃ ca vibhūṣaṇāni
sārdhaṃ divyāṃbarā devyāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ
siddhendrasiddhāś ca tathā piśācā jajñire punaḥ
ājñayā dārukaṃ tasyāḥ pārvatyāḥ parameśvarī
dānavaṃ sūdayāmāsa sūdayantaṃ surādhipān
saṃraṃbhātiprasaṃgādvai tasyāḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat
krodhāgninā ca viprendrāḥ saṃbabhūva tadāturam
bhavopi bālarūpeṇa śmaśāne pretasaṃkule
ruroda māyayā tasyāḥ krodhāgniṃ pātumīsvaraḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bālamīśānaṃ māyayā tasya mohitā
utthāpyāghrāya vakṣojaṃ stanaṃ sā pradadau dvijāḥ
stanajena tadā sārdhaṃ kopamasyāḥ papau punaḥ
krodhenānena vai bālaḥ kṣetrāṇāṃ rakṣako 'bhavat
mūrtayo 'ṣṭau ca tasyāpi kṣetrapālasya dhīmataḥ
evaṃ vai tena bālena kṛtā sā krodhamūrcchitā
kṛtamasyāḥ prasādārthaṃ devadevena tāṇḍavam
saṃdhyāyāṃ sarvabhūtendraiḥ pretaiḥ prītena śūlinā
pītvā nṛtyāmṛtaṃ śaṃbhor ākaṇṭhaṃ parameśvarī
tatra sabrahmakā devāḥ seṃdropendrāḥ samantataḥ
praṇemustuṣṭuvuḥ kālīṃ punardevīṃ ca pārvatīm
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ tāṇḍavaṃ śūlinaḥ prabhoḥ
yogānandena ca vibhostāṇḍavaṃ ceti cāpare
iti śrīliṅgadṛ pūrvadṛ śivatāṇḍavakathanaṃ nāma ṣaḍadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
puropamanyunā sūta gāṇapatyaṃ maheśvarāt
kṣīrārṇavaḥ kathaṃ labdho vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam
sūta uvāca
kumāra iva tejasvī krīḍamāno yadṛcchayā
kadācitkṣaramalpaṃ ca pītavānmātulāśrame
īrṣyayā mātulasuto hy apibat kṣīram uttamam
pītvā sthitaṃ yathākāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā provāca mātaram
gavyaṃ kṣīramatisvādu nālpamuṣṇaṃ namāmyaham
sūta uvāca
upalālitaivaṃ putreṇa putram āliṅgya sādaram
duḥkhitā vilalāpārtā smṛtvā nairdhanyamātmanaḥ
smṛtvāsmṛtvāpunaḥ kṣīramupamanyurapi dvijāḥ
dehidehīti tāmāha rodamāno mahādyutiḥ
uñchavṛttyājintānvījānsvayaṃ viṣṭvā ca sā tadā
vījapiṣṭaṃ tadāloḍya toyena kalabhāṣiṇī
āliṅgyādāya duḥkhārtā pradadau kṛtrimaṃ payaḥ
pītvā ca kṛtrimaṃ kṣīraṃ mātrā dattaṃ dvijottamaḥ
naitatkṣīramiti prāha mātaraṃ cātivihvalaḥ
duḥkhitā sā tadā prāha saṃprekṣyāghrāyamūrdhani
taṭinī ratnapūrṇāste svargapātālagocarāḥ
bhāgyahīnā na paśyanti bhaktihināś ca ye śive
rājyaṃ svargaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca bhojanaṃ kṣīrasaṃbhavam
na labhante priyāṇyeṣāṃ no tuṣyati sadā bhavaḥ
kṣīraṃ tatra kuto 'smākaṃ mahādevo na pūjitaḥ
bālopi mātaraṃ prāha praṇipatya tapasvinīm
cirādvā hyacirādvāpi kṣīrodaṃ sādhayāmyaham
sūta uvāca
tamāha mātā śuśubhaṃ kurvīti sutarāṃ sutam
himavatparvataṃ prāpya vāyubhakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ
śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ
kimidantviti saṃcintya jñātvā tatkāraṇaṃ ca saḥ
jagāma mandaraṃ tūrṇaṃ maheśvaradidṛkṣayā
dṛṣṭvā devaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ provācedaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ
kṣīrārthamadahatsarvaṃ tapasā taṃ vivāraya
śakrarūpaṃ samāsthāya gantuṃ cakre matiṃ tadā
vāmena śacyā sahitaṃ surendraṃ kareṇa cānyena sitātapatram
rarāja bhagavān somaḥ śakrarūpī sadāśivaḥ
āsthāyaivaṃ hi śakrasya svarūpaṃ parameśvaraḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā parameśānaṃ śakrarūpadharaṃ śivam
praṇamya śirasā prāha munirmunivarāḥ svayam
pāvitaścāśramaścāyaṃ mama deveśvaraḥ svayam
prāptaḥ śakro jagannātho bhagavānbhānunā prabhuḥ
evamuktvā sthitaṃ vīkṣya kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ dvijam
prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā śakrarūpadharo haraḥ
varayāmi śive bhaktimityuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ
prāha savyagramīśānaḥ śakrarūpadharaḥ svayam
māṃ na jānāsi devarṣe devarājānamīśvaram
tataḥ śakrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā śrotravidāraṇam
upamanyuridaṃ prāha japanpañcākṣara śubham
bhavāntarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śrutā nindā bhavasya tu
śrutvā nindāṃ bhavasyātha tatkṣaṇādeva saṃtyajet
svadehaṃ taṃ nihatyāśu śivalokaṃ sa gacchati
yo vācotpāṭayojjihvāṃ śivanindāratasya tu
āstāṃ tāvanmamecchāyāḥ kṣīraṃ prati surādhamam
purā mātrā tu kathitaṃ tatthyameva na saṃśayaḥ
bhasmādhārānmahātejā bhasmamuṣṭiṃ pragṛhya ca
dagdhuṃ svadeha māgneyīṃ dhyātvā vai dhāraṇāṃ tadā
atiṣṭhacca mahātejāḥ śuṣkendhanamivāvyayaḥ
vārayāmāsa saumyena dhāraṇāṃ tasya yoginaḥ
atharvāstraṃ tadā tasya saṃhṛtaṃ candrikeṇa tu
kālāgnisadṛśaṃ cedaṃ niyogānnandinas tathā
svarūpameva bhagavānāsthāya parameśvaraḥ
darśayāmāsa viprāya bālendukṛtaśekharam
kṣīradhārāsahasraṃ ca kṣīrodārṇavameva ca
dadhyāderarṇavaṃ caiva ghṛtodārṇavameva ca
phalārṇavaṃ ca bālasya bhakṣyabhojyārṇavaṃ tathā
apūpagirayaścaiva tathātiṣṭhan samantataḥ
girijāvalokya sasmitāṃ saghṛṇaṃ prekṣyatu taṃ tadā ghṛṇī
bhuṅkṣva bhogānyathākāmaṃ bāndhavaiḥ paśya vatsa me
upamanyo mahābhāga tavāṃbaiṣā hi pārvatī
mayā putrīkṛtosyadya dattaḥ kṣīrodadhis tathā
madhunaścārṇavaścaiva dadhnaścārṇava eva ca
ājyodanārṇavaścaiva phalalohyārṇavas tathā
apūpagirayaścaiva bhakṣyabhojyārṇavaḥ punaḥ
pitā tava mahādevaḥ pitā vai jagatāṃ mune
mātā tava mahābhāgā jaganmātā na saṃśayaḥ
amaratvaṃ mayā dattaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ ca śāśvatam
varānvaraya dāsyāmi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
evamuktvā mahādevaḥ karābhyāmupagṛhya tam
yogaiśvaryaṃ tadā tuṣṭā brahmavidyāṃ dvijottamāḥ
sopi labdhvā varaṃ tasyāḥ kumāratvaṃ ca sarvadā
tuṣṭāva ca mahādevaṃ harṣagadgadayā girā
varayāmāsa ca tadā vareṇyaṃ virajekṣaṇam
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ
prasīda devadeveśa tvayi cāvyabhicāriṇī
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge upamanyucaritaṃ nāma saptādhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
dṛṣṭo 'sau vāsudevena kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā
kathaṃ labdhaṃ tadā jñānaṃ tasmātkṛṣṇena dhīmatā
vaktumarhasi tāṃ sūta kathāṃ pātakanāśinīm
sūta uvāca
svecchayā hyavatīrṇopi vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ
nindayanneva mānuṣyaṃ dehaśuddhiṃ cakāra saḥ
āśramaṃ copamanyorvai dṛṣṭavāṃstatra taṃ munim
namaścakāra taṃ dṛṣṭvā dhaumyāgrajamaho dvijāḥ
bahumānena vai kṛṣṇastriḥ kṛtvāvai pradakṣiṇam
tasyāvalokanādeva muneḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ
naṣṭameva malaṃ sarvaṃ kāyajaṃ karmmajaṃ tathā
divyaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ pradadau prītamānasaḥ
muneḥ prasādānmānyo 'sau kṛṣṇaḥ pāśupate dvijāḥ
tapasā tvekavarṣānte dṛṣṭvā devaṃ maheśvaram
sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyagraṃ labdhavānputramātmanaḥ
tadāprabhṛti taṃ kṛṣṇaṃ munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
divyāḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve tasthuḥ saṃvṛtya sarvadā
anyaṃ ca kathayiṣyāmi muktyarthaṃ prāṇināṃ sadā
sauvarṇīṃ mekhalāṃ kṛtvā ādhāraṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam
sauvarṇaṃ piṇḍikaṃ cāpi vyajanaṃ daṇḍameva ca
naraiḥ striyātha vā kāryaṃ maṣībhājanalekhanīm
kṣurākarttarikā cāpi atha pātramathāpi vā
pāśupatāya dātavyaṃ bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaiḥ
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi tāmraṃvātha nivedayet
ātmavittānusāreṇa yoginaṃ pūjayedbudhaḥ
te sarve pāpanirmuktāḥ samastakulasaṃyutāḥ
yānti rudrapadaṃ divyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
yogināṃ saṃpradānena śivaḥ kṣipraṃ prasīdati
rājyaṃ putraṃ dhanaṃ bhavyamaśvaṃ yānamathāpi vā
adhruveṇa śarīreṇa dhruvaṃ sādhyaṃ prayatnataḥ
bhavyaṃ pāśupataṃ nityaṃ saṃsārārṇavatārakam
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkṣepānna ca saṃśayaḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge 'ṣṭottaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
samāptaścāyaṃ pūrvabhāgaḥ
śrīśaṅkarārpaṇamastu
iti śrīsaṭīkaliṅgamahāpurāṇapūrvabhāgaḥ samāptaḥ
